40001001	Ndaa , inɗe kaakaaji Yeesu Almasiihu , danyaaɗo nder asŋgol Daawuda e Ibrahiima .
40001002	Ibrahiima danyi Isiyaaku , Isiyaaku danyi Yakubu , Yakubu danyi Yahuuda e deerɗum'en .
40001003	Yahuuda danyi Fares e Jara , Tamar woni daada maɓɓe . Fares danyi Hesruunu , Hesruunu danyi Aram .
40001004	Aram danyi Aminadabu , Aminadabu danyi Naasunu , Naasunu danyi Salmuuna ,
40001005	Salmuuna danyi Bo'es , Rahab woni daada maako . Bo'es danyi Obed , Ruut woni daada maako . Obed danyi Yessa ,
40001006	Yessa danyi Daawuda , laamiiɗo . Daawuda danyi Suleymaanu , laatinooɗo debbo Uriya woni daada maako .
40001007	Suleymaanu danyi Robo'am , Robo'am danyi Abiya , Abiya danyi Asa ,
40001008	Asa danyi Yusafat , Yusafat danyi Yoram . Yoram danyi Ujiya ,
40001009	Ujiya danyi Yotam , Yotam danyi Akas , Akas danyi Hejekiya ,
40001010	Hejekiya danyi Manassa , Manassa danyi Amos , Amos danyi Yusiya ,
40001011	Yusiya danyi Yekuniya e deerɗum'en , saa'i ɓe eggini Isra'iila'en haa lesdi Baabila .
40001012	Ɓaawo eggineeki Isra'iila'en haa lesdi Baabila , Yekuniya danyi Salaatiyel , Salaatiyel danyi Jorobaabila ,
40001013	Jorobaabila danyi Abihuda , Abihuda danyi Eliyakim , Eliyakim danyi Ajora ,
40001014	Ajora danyi Sadok , Sadok danyi Akim , Akim danyi Eliyuda , Eliyuda danyi Eliyajaaru ,
40001015	Eliyajaaru danyi Matta , Matta danyi Yakubu ,
40001016	Yakubu danyi Yusufu , gorko Mariyama mo danyi Yeesu bi'eteeɗo Almasiihu .
40001017	Tokkindirki asli man diga Ibrahiima haa Daawuda waɗi sappo e nayi , diga Daawuda haa saa'i ɓe eggini Isra'iila'en haa lesdi Baabila waɗi asli sappo e nayi , diga eggineeki Isra'iila'en haa Baabila haa Almasiihu danya , waɗi asli sappo e nayi .
40001018	Ndaa ni danyeeki Yeesu Almasiihu laatori . Daadafa maako Mariyama laati muuyaaɗo Yusufu , ammaa diga ɓe ngondaay tawon , Mariyama reedi bee baawɗe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo .
40001019	Yusufu muuyɗo mo o tokkiiɗo Allah , kakkilɗo , o yiɗaa waŋgingo ɗum yeeso yimɓe , o yiɗino accugo mo bee sirri .
40001020	Nde o ɗonno numta haala man , ndaa malaa'ikaajo Jawmiraawo waŋgani mo nder koyɗol , wi'i mo : " Yusufu , goɗɗo asŋgol Daawuda , taa hul ɓaŋgugo Mariyama muuyaaɗo maaɗa , ngam ko reeda nder maako iwi haa baawɗe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo .
40001021	O tammi danyugo ɓiɗɗo gorko , a ewno innde maako Yeesu , ngam o hisnan yimɓe maako e hakkeeji maɓɓe . "
40001022	Ɗum fuu ɗum laati ngam gooŋɗingo ko Jawmiraawo wi'no bee hunduko annaboojo :
40001023	" Paanyo debbo reedan , danyan ɓiɗɗo gorko ,
40001024	Nde Yusufu fini , o huuwi bana no malaa'ikaajo Jawmiraawo umri mo , o hoo'i debbo maako ,
40001025	ammaa o hawtaay bee maako haa o danyi ɓiiyiiko gorko . Yusufu ewni mo Yeesu .
40002001	Too , Yeesu danyaama haa Baytilaama , wuro nder lesdi Yahudiya , nder jamanu laamiiɗo Hirudus . Ɓaawo danyeeki maako marɓe anndal linyugo koode ngari diga fuunaaŋge haa Urusaliima .
40002002	Ɓe ?ami : " Toy ɓiŋgel danyaaŋgel tammiiŋgel laataago laamiiɗo Yahuudu'en ? Min ngi'i horre maagel waŋgi , min ngari sujidango ngel . "
40002003	Nde laamiiɗo Hirudus nani ɗum , o hultori masin , ɗum sakli yimɓe Urusaliima boo .
40002004	O mooɓti mawɓe liman'en e moodiɓɓe tawreeta fuu , o ?ami ɓe : " Toy Almasiihu danyete ? "
40002005	Ɓe mbi'i mo : " Haa Baytilaama , nder lesdi Yahudiya . Ngam ndaa ni annaboojo windi :
40002006	An wuro Baytilaama nder lesdi Yahudiya ,
40002007	Nden Hirudus ewni marɓe anndal go bee sirri ngam haa o heɓta haa maɓɓe saa'i horre waŋgi .
40002008	O wi'i ɓe : " Njehe Baytilaama , ɗaɓɓite ɓiŋgel man bee tiinaare . To on tawi ngel , anndineeɗam min boo , ngam mi yaha , mi sujidana ngel . "
40002009	Nde ɓe keɓi tindinoore haa laamiiɗo , ɓe ndilli . Horre nde ɓe ngi'no go ardi ɓe , nde yotti dow nokkuure ɓiŋgel woni , nde dari .
40002010	Nde ɓe ngi'i horre , ɓe ceyi bee seyo maŋgo masin .
40002011	Ɓe nasti suudu , ɓe tawi ɓiŋgel e Mariyama , daada maagel . Ɓe tuggi koppi , ɓe cujidani ngel . Nden ɓe pisti boorooji maɓɓe , ɓe ndokki ngel dokke : kaŋgeeri e tamre urdi e ɗaccere uurnde .
40002012	Ɓaawoɗon Allah anndini ɓe nder koyɗol taa ɓe loro haa Hirudus , ɓe kooti lesdi maɓɓe bee laawol feere .
40002013	Nde marɓe anndal go ndilli , malaa'ikaajo Jawmiraawo waŋgani Yusufu nder koyɗol , o wi'i : " Umma , hoo'u ɓiŋgel e daada maagel , dillu haa Misra , jooɗa ton haa to mi yecci ma , ngam Hirudus tammi tefugo ɓiŋgel haa o halka ngel . "
40002014	Yusufu ummi , hoo'i ɓiŋgel e daada maagel , dilli Misra bee jemma .
40002015	O jooɗi ton haa yotti maayde Hirudus , ngam haa ko Jawmiraawo wi'no bee hunduko annaboojo laato , o wi'i : " Mi ewnoto ɓiŋgel am diga lesdi Misra . "
40002016	Nde Hirudus anndi marɓe anndal go mbaɗaay bana o yiɗi , o tikki masin , o umri ɓe mbara ɓikkoy ngorkoy haa Baytilaama e gure piltuɗe ngo fuu , diga markoy duuɓi ɗiɗi bee koy cikaay duuɓi ɗiɗi , fodde saa'i baŋguki horre o ?ami haa marɓe anndal go .
40002017	Kanjum gooŋɗini ko annabi Yeremiya wi'no :
40002018	" Gookaali mbaɗi haa Rama ,
40002019	Nde Hirudus maayi , malaa'ikaajo Jawmiraawo waŋgani Yusufu nder koyɗol haa Misra ,
40002020	o wi'i mo : " Umma , hoo'u ɓiŋgel bee daada maagel , hootu lesdi Isra'iila , ngam ɗaɓɓanooɓe mbarugo ɓiŋgel maayi . "
40002021	Yusufu ummi , hoosi ɓiŋgel e daada maagel , hooti lesdi Isra'iila .
40002022	Ammaa nde o nani Arkilawus ronti laamu baaba muuɗum Hirudus dow lesdi Yahudiya , o huli jooɗaago lesdi maajum . Allah waŋginani mo bee koyɗol ko o waɗata ,
40002023	ngam maajum o suɓi jooɗaago nder berniwol bi'eteeŋgol Nasaratu . Ɗum laati non ngam gooŋɗingo bolle annabo'en : " O ewneteeɗo Nasaratuujo . "
40003001	Yoo , nder saa'i maajum Yuhanna baɗoowo ngiiwam baptisma waŋgi nder ladde Yahudiya , o fuɗɗi waajaago .
40003002	O wi'i : " Tuube , ngam laamu Allah ɓadake . "
40003003	Yuhanna woni mo Esaaya wolwi dow muuɗum , wi'i :
40003004	Yuhanna ɗon ɓorni limce kuuwraaɗe gaasa geelooɗi , o ɗon taadi taadorgol laral , nyaamdu maako woni baɓɓatti e njumri ladde .
40003005	Yimɓe iwɓe haa Urusaliima e lesdi Yahudiya e lesdi kombi maayo Urdun fuu , ngari haa maako .
40003006	Ɓe mbaŋgini hakkeeji maɓɓe , Yuhanna boo yiiwi ɓe ngiiwam baptisma nder maayo Urdun .
40003007	Nde Yuhanna yi'i Farisa'en e Saduki'en ɗon ngara haa maako ngam ɓe keɓa ngiiwam baptisma , o wi'i ɓe : " Ɓiɓɓe poosokje , moy wi'i on on kisan tikkere Allah warannde ?
40003008	Kuuwe kuuɗe ɗe mbaŋginta on tuubi , on acci kuuɗe mooɗon naane .
40003009	Taa nume nder ɓerɗe mooɗon : Ibrahiima woni kaaka amin . Ngam mi ɗon wi'a on , Allah woodi baawɗe waɗugo kaa'e ɗe'e laato ɓiɓɓe Ibrahiima .
40003010	Fe''irde ɗon taaskani fe''ugo lekki diga ɗaɗi mum , lekki ki rimataa ɓiɓɓe booɗɗe fuu ki fe''e , ki wudine nder yiite .
40003011	Min mi ɗon yiiwa on ngiiwam baptisma bee ndiyam ngam seedaago on tuubi . Ammaa garanɗo ɓaawo am yiiwan on ngiiwam baptisma bee Ruuhu Ceniiɗo e bee yiite . Kaŋko o ɓuri yam baawɗe piw . Mi he'aay sam mi turo , mi itta paɗe maako .
40003012	O woodi jaartirɗum haa juŋŋgo maako ngam o jaarta gawri , o senda ndi bee nyaande . O mooɓtan gawri haa beembal maako , ammaa o wulan nyaande bee yiite nge nyifataa . "
40003013	Yoo , Yeesu ummi lesdi Galili , wari maayo Urdun haa Yuhanna , ngam Yuhanna yiiwa mo ngiiwam baptisma .
40003014	Yuhanna jaɓaay , wi'i mo : " Min maa , mi woodi haaje a yiiwanammi ngiiwam baptisma , nden a wara haa am na ? "
40003015	Ammaa Yeesu jaabi mo : " Yerda ɗum jonta , ngam bana ni kuuwreten ko Allah ɗaɓɓi haa meeɗen . "
40003016	yiiwi mo ngiiwam baptisma . Nde Yeesu wurti ndiyam , asamanji maɓɓiti , o yi'i Ruuhu Allah ɗon jippo bana poola , ɗon wara dow maako .
40003017	Sawtu boo iwi haa asama , wi'i : " Oo woni Ɓiɗɗo am giɗaaɗo , mi ɗon seyoro mo masin . "
40004001	Too , ɓaawoɗon Ruuhu Allah yahri Yeesu haa ladde ngam Iblisa jarribo mo .
40004002	Yeesu nyaamaay sam nyalawmaaje cappanɗe nayi e jemmaaje cappanɗe nayi , o maati weelo .
40004003	Iblisa ɓaditi , wi'i mo : " To a Ɓiɗɗo Allah kam , umru kaa'e ɗe'e laato nyaamdu . "
40004004	Yeesu jaabi : " Deftere wi'i : Neɗɗo yeeɗataa bee nyaamdu tan , ammaa bee wolde nde Allah wolwi fuu . "
40004005	Iblisa yahri mo haa berniwol ceniiŋgol , jo''ini mo dow hoore haykaliiru ,
40004006	wi'i mo : " To a Ɓiɗɗo Allah kam , diw diga ɗo haa lesdi , ngam deftere wi'i :
40004007	Yeesu jaabi mo : " Deftere wi'i boo : Taa jarriba Allah Jawmiraawo maaɗa . "
40004008	Nden Iblisa wa''ini mo dow hooseere townde masin , o sappini mo mooɓgal laamuuji duniyaaru e tedduŋgal maaji fuu ,
40004009	o wi'i mo : " Ɗum fuu mi hokkete to a tuggi koppi , a sujidani yam . "
40004010	Ammaa Yeesu wi'i mo : " Dillu , accam , an Iblisa , ngam deftere wi'i : Sujidan Allah Jawmiraawo maaɗa tan , kaŋko feere maako a huuwanta . "
40004011	Saa'i maajum Iblisa acci Yeesu , nden malaa'ika'en ngari haa maako , kuuwani mo .
40004012	Too , nde Yeesu nani ɓe nastini Yuhanna fursinafe , o ummi , o dilli lesdi Galili .
40004013	O acci jooɗaago haa Nasaratu , o yehi , o jooɗi haa Kafarnahum , wuro wonŋgo dow fomoonde weendu Galili , nder tayre lesdi Jabulon e Neftalim .
40004014	Bee waɗugo non o gooŋɗini bolle annabi Esaaya , bi'ɗo :
40004015	" Lesdi Jabulon e lesdi Neftalim ,
40004016	yimɓe jooɗiiɓe nder nyiɓre ngi'an annoora makka .
40004017	Diga saa'i maajum Yeesu fuɗɗi waajaago . O wi'i : " Tuube , ngam laamu Allah ɓadake . "
40004018	Nde Yeesu ɗon saalo kombi weendu Galili , o yi'i deerɗiraaɓe ɗiɗo , ɓe ngaawooɓe liɗɗi , kamɓe ngoni Simon bi'eteeɗo Piyer , e Andire deerɗiiko , ɓe ɗon naŋga liɗɗi bee jubaawol .
40004019	Yeesu wi'i ɓe : " Tokkeeɗam , mi waɗan on ngaawooɓe yimɓe . "
40004020	Law ɓe acci jubaaji maɓɓe , ɓe tokki mo .
40004021	O yehi yeeso fahin , o yi'i worɓe ɗiɗo nder koombowal , Yakuba e deerɗum Yuhanna , kamɓe e baaba maɓɓe Jebede , ɓe ɗon mbo''itina jubaaji maɓɓe . O ewni ɓe .
40004022	Law ɓe acci koombowal e baaba maɓɓe , ɓe tokki mo .
40004023	Yeesu yilli lesdi Galili fuu , o anndini Yahuudu'en nder suudu waajaago maɓɓe , o waajini kubaruwol belŋgol ngol laamu Allah , o yamɗitini nyawɓe e jiijiiɓe ɗuuɗɓe .
40004024	Kubaru maako saŋkiti nder lesdi Isra'iila fuu . Ɓe ngaddani mo torraaɓe nyawji feere feere , bana ginnaaji e paɗɗe e garsa , o yamɗitini ɓe .
40004025	Jama'aare ɗuunde tokki mo . Ɓe ngari diga lesdi Galili , e lesdi mbi'eteendi Gure-sappo , e Urusaliima e lesdi Yahudiya , e yimɓe lesdi gaɗa maayo Urdun fuu .
40005001	Too , nde Yeesu yi'i jama'aare ɗuunde nde'e , o wa''i towndiire , o jooɗi . Pukara'en maako ngari haa maako ,
40005002	kaŋko o fuɗɗi waajingo ɓe bana ni :
40005003	" Barka laatanto annduɓe ko'e muuɗum'en ɓe talaka'en yeeso Allah , ngam ɓe ngondan bee Allah nder laamu muuɗum .
40005004	" Barka laatanto woyooɓe ngam daliila halleende duniyaaru , ngam Allah de'itinan ɓe .
40005005	" Barka laatanto de'itɓe , ngam Allah hokkan ɓe lesdi bana o wi'no .
40005006	" Barka laatanto ɗaɓɓanɓe huuwugo muuyo Allah bee ɓernde fuu , ngam Allah wallan ɓe huuwugo ko ɓe ɗaɓɓi .
40005007	" Barka laatanto enɗooɓe , ngam Allah enɗan ɓe .
40005008	" Barka laatanto laaɓa-ɓerɗe'en , ngam ɓe ngi'an Allah .
40005009	" Barka laatanto narrinooɓe yimɓe , ngam Allah ewnoto ɓe ɓiɓɓe maako .
40005010	" Barka laatanto toonyaaɓe ngam daliila huuwugo ko Allah yiɗi , ngam ɓe ngondan bee Allah nder laamu muuɗum .
40005011	" Barka laatanto on , to yimɓe kuɗi on , toonyi on , mbaɗi tufle meere dow mooɗon ngam on laati pukara'en am .
40005012	" Ceye masin , ngam Allah warjoto on mbarjaari ɗuundi haa asamanji . Bana non ɓe kuuwino annabo'en aartuɓe on fuu . "
40005013	" Bana manda nafrata haa nyaamdu , bana non on nafrata duniyaaru . Ammaa to lammeeŋga manda ittake , noy ɗam heɓtirta lammeeŋga man fahin ? Manda man nafataa sam , sey wudingo tan , yimɓe njaaɓan ɗam .
40005014	" Onon ngoni annoora ngam duniyaaru , berniwol nyiɓaaŋgol dow towndiire wirnataako sam .
40005015	Ɓe njamnataa pittirla ngam suuɗugo nga les taasawo . Sey ɓe njo''ina nga dow jo''inirɗum pittirla , haa ɗum yaynana wonɓe nder suudu maajum fuu .
40005016	Sey jayŋgol mooɗon yayna bana non yeeso yimɓe fuu , ngam haa ɓe ndaara kuuɗe mooɗon booɗɗe , ɓe teddina Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama . "
40005017	" Taa nume mi wari fistugo tawreeta Muusa malla bolle annabo'en . Mi waraay ngam mi fista ɗum , ammaa ngam mi gooŋɗina ɗum .
40005018	Bee gooŋga mi wi'ata on : No asama e lesdi nduurdi fuu , walaa koo harfeere ɓurdunde famɗugo malla toɓɓere woore haa tawreeta Muusa wudinte , haa to timmoode kuuje fuu yottake .
40005019	Ngam maajum koomoy yawi umroore ɓurdunde famɗugo nder tawreeta , malla o ekkitini woɗɓe waɗugo bana non , o laatoto ɓurduɗo leesugo nder laamu Allah . Ammaa koomoy jogi ɗe , o ekkitini woɗɓe boo jogaago ɗe , kaŋko o laatoto mawɗo nder laamu Allah .
40005020	Mi ɗon wi'a on bee gooŋga , on keɓataa nastugo laamu Allah , sonaa to on ɗon ɗowtano muuyo Allah ko ɓuri moodiɓɓe e Farisa'en . "
40005021	" On nani ko wi'a kaakaaji meeɗen : Taa mbar hoore , koomoy mbari goɗɗo , heɓan kiita .
40005022	Ammaa min mi ɗon wi'a on : Koomoy tikkani deerɗum , o jahreteeɗo yeeso alkaali . Koomoy wi'i deerɗum : A meereejo , o jahreteeɗo yeeso mawɓe kiita lesdi . Koomoy wi'i deerɗum : A majjuɗo , ɗum he'i nastingo mo nder yiite jahannama .
40005023	Ngam maajum to a wari yeeso Allah bee dokkal ma , haa ton a siftori woodi sooynde narral hakkunde maaɗa bee deerɗiraawo ma ,
40005024	nden kam accu dokkal maaɗa ton yeeso Allah , yah law , narru bee deerɗa tawon . Nden a loro , a lii'ano Allah dokkal maaɗa .
40005025	" To goɗɗo wullake ma , on ɗon njahda haa alkaali , yaaw narrugo bee maako law diga on ɗon dow laawol tawon , ngam taa o yahre haa juŋŋgo alkaali , alkaali boo hokke haa juuɗe sooje'en , ɓe nastine fursina .
40005026	Mi ɗon wi'e bee gooŋga : A wurtataako ton sam , sonaa to a yoɓi ko o tokki ma fuu . "
40005027	" On nani ɗum wi'aama : Taa waɗ njeenu .
40005028	Ammaa min mi ɗon wi'a on : Koomoy gorko fuu to laari debbo goɗɗo bee suuno , waɗi njeenu nder ɓernde muuɗum .
40005029	To yiitere ma nyaamre esti ma waɗugo hakke , ɗoof nde , wudin nde daayiiɗum . Ndikka a majjina terde ɓandu ma woore dow ɓandu ma fuu nasta yiite jahannama .
40005030	To juŋŋgo ma nyaamo nastinte hakke , ta''u ngo , wudin ngo daayiiɗum . Ndikka a majjina terde ɓandu ma woore dow ɓandu ma fuu nasta yiite jahannama . "
40005031	" Ɗum wi'aama boo : Koomoy seeri debbo mum , sey hokka mo ɗereewol seedamku o seeri mo .
40005032	Ammaa min mi ɗon wi'a on : Koomoy seeri debbo muuɗum naa ngam o naŋgi mo nder njeenu , nden kam o laatini mo jeenoowo , to o te'i bee gorko feere . Koomoy te'i debbo ceeraaɗo boo , waɗi njeenu . "
40005033	" On nani ko wi'a kaakaaji meeɗen : Taa huna dow fewre , ammaa hebbin hunayeere ma yeeso Jawmiraawo .
40005034	Ammaa min mi ɗon wi'a on : Taa kunore sam , koo bee asama , ngam ɗum leeso laamu Allah ,
40005035	koo bee lesdi , ngam ɗum jaaɓruɗum kosɗe Allah , koo bee Urusaliima boo , ngam ɗum berniwol laamiiɗo mawɗo .
40005036	Taa kunore koo bee ko'e mon boo , ngam on mbaawataa fuɗnugo gaasa mooɗon ndaneeha malla ɓaleeha .
40005037	Sey on mbi'a : Ooho , malla : Aa'a , ngam wolwugo ko ɓuri non , ɗum iwi haa Iblisa . "
40005038	" On nani ɗum wi'aama : Yiitere bee yiitere , nyiindere bee nyiindere .
40005039	Ammaa min mi ɗon wi'a on : Taa mbaate kuuwɗo on halleende . To goɗɗo maari ma haa galaŋgal nyaamal , waylitan mo nanal boo .
40005040	To goɗɗo yiɗi wullaago ma ngam o jaɓta limce maaɗa pamare , accu mo o hoosa ngapaleewol maaɗa boo .
40005041	To goɗɗo dooli ma roondanaago mo dooŋgal baakin kilomeeta gootel , roondana mo ngal kilomeeta ɗiɗi .
40005042	To goɗɗo ?ami ma huunde , hokku mo nde . To goɗɗo ?ami ma nyamaande , taa salana mo . "
40005043	" On nani ɗum wi'aama : Yiɗ keeddiɗɗiraawo ma , a wanya ganyo ma .
40005044	Ammaa min mi ɗon wi'a on : Ngiɗe konne'en mooɗon , tore Allah ngam toonyiiɓe on ,
40005045	ngam haa on laato ɓiɓɓe Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama . O ɗon yaynina naaŋge maako dow halluɓe e wooɗɓe fuu , o ɗon toɓna iyeende ngam huuwooɓe kuugal booɗŋgal , e huuwooɓe halleende fuu .
40005046	Ngam ɗume on ndeenata mbarjaari haa Allah to on ngiɗi yiɗɓe on tan ? Koo jaɓooɓe jomorgol boo ɗon mbaɗa bana non .
40005047	To on ɗon koofna bandiraaɓe mooɗon tan , on kuuwi huunde mawnde na ? Koo heefeerɓe boo ɗon mbaɗa bana non .
40005048	Laate on timmuɓe , bana Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama o timmuɗo . "
40006001	" To on ɗon kuuwa mbooɗeeŋga , taa kuuwe ɗum ngam haa yimɓe ngi'a on . To on mbaɗi non , on keɓataa mbarjaari sam haa Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama .
40006002	" To a ɗon walla talakaajo , taa waɗ ɗum ngam haa yimɓe ndaara , bana naafiki'en mbaɗata nder suudu waajaago Yahuudu'en e dow laabi . Ɓe ɗon mbaɗa non ngam yimɓe teddina ɓe . Mi ɗon wi'a on bee gooŋga : Ɓe keɓi mbarjaari maɓɓe , jinni .
40006003	Ammaa an , to a ɗon walla talakaajo , waɗ ɗum bee sirri , koo soobaajo ma ɓurɗo ɓadaago , taa annda ɗum .
40006004	Huuw mbooɗeeŋga ma nder cuuɗiiɗum , Baabiraawo ma gi'anɗo ko kuuwata nder cuuɗiiɗum , warjoto ma . "
40006005	" To on ɗon mbaɗa do'a , taa laate bana naafiki'en . Kamɓe ɓe ngiɗi daraago nder cuuɗi waajaago Yahuudu'en e haa kawtirɗe laabi , ɓe mbaɗa do'a ngam haa yimɓe ngi'a ɓe . Mi ɗon wi'a on bee gooŋga : Ɓe keɓi mbarjaari maɓɓe , jinni .
40006006	Ammaa to a yiɗi waɗugo do'a , nastu suudu ma , maɓɓu dammugal , a toro Baabiraawo ma gonɗo nder cuuɗiiɗum , Baabiraawo ma gi'anɗo ko kuuwata nder cuuɗiiɗum , warjoto ma .
40006007	" To on ɗon mbaɗa do'a , taa ɗuɗɗine bolle bana sooyɓe nuɗɗinki mbaɗata . Ɓe ɗon tammo Allah jaɓan do'a maɓɓe to ɓe ɗuɗɗini bolle .
40006008	Taa mbaɗe bana maɓɓe , ngam Baabiraawo mooɗon anndi haaje mooɗon diga on ciwa toraago mo .
40006009	To on ɗon mbaɗa do'a , ndaa ni mbi'oton :
40006010	Waŋginan min laamu ma .
40006011	Hokku min nyaamdu deydey haaje amin hande .
40006012	Yaafana min aybeeji amin , bana no minin boo
40006013	Aynu min ngam taa Sayɗaanu esta min ,
40006014	" To on ɗon njaafano waɗɓe on aybe , Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama yaafanto on hakkeeji mooɗon boo .
40006015	Ammaa to on njaafanaaki waɗɓe on aybe , nden kam Baabiraawo mooɗon boo yaafantaako on hakkeeji mooɗon . "
40006016	" To on ɗon cuumo , taa kolle geese mooɗon on wontuɓe bana naafiki'en mbaɗata , ɓe ɗon nyobba geese maɓɓe ngam yimɓe ngi'a ɓe ɗon cuumi . Mi ɗon wi'a on bee gooŋga : Ɓe keɓi mbarjaari maɓɓe , jinni .
40006017	Ammaa an , to a ɗon suumi , sulmu yeeso ma , mo''itin gaasa hoore ma ,
40006018	ngam taa yimɓe anndita a ɗon suumi . Baabiraawo ma gonɗo nder cuuɗiiɗum kaŋko tan anndi . O ɗon yi'a ko kuuwata nder cuuɗiiɗum , o warjoto ma . "
40006019	" Taa mooɓtane ko'e mooɗon kuuje haa duniyaaru , haa gilɗi bee peewol mbonnata ɗum , haa wuyɓe boo ngasata cuuɗi , ngujja ɗum .
40006020	Ammaa mbaɗane ko'e mooɗon ndesaari haa asama , haa ton gilɗi e peewol mbaawataa wonnugo ɗum , wuyɓe boo mbaawataa wujjugo ɗum .
40006021	Ngam haa jawdi maaɗa woni , ton ɓernde maaɗa boo wonata . "
40006022	" Gite laati bana pittirla ɓandu . To gite maaɗa laaɓɗe , ɓandu maaɗa fuu ɗon nder annoora .
40006023	Ammaa to gite maaɗa laaɓaay , ɓandu ma fuu ɗon nder nyiɓre . Ko hokkete annoora , to nyiɓɓi bana non , fakat ɗum nyiɓre ɓaleere kurum . "
40006024	" Walaa mo waawata huuwango jaagorɓe ɗiɗo , ngam o wanyan oo , o yiɗan oya , o teddina oo , o meeriɗina oya . On mbaawataa on kuuwana Allah , on cuklano ceede boo . "
40006025	" Ngam maajum mi ɗon wi'a on : Taa caklane haala nyaamdu malla njaram malla limce . Yoŋki ɓuri nyaamdu saman , ɓandu boo ɓuri limce saman , naa non na ?
40006026	Ndaare colli , ɗi aawataa , ɗi codataa , ɗi mooɓtataa kooɗume nder beembe , ammaa Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama ɗon nyaamna ɗi . On ɓurataa colli saman piw na ?
40006027	Moy caka mooɗon bee baawɗe muuɗum waawi ɓesdugo balɗe muuɗum koo nyalaade woore ?
40006028	" Ngam ɗume on cuklanto haala limce ? Ndaare pindi ladde no ndi fuɗirta . Ndi huuwataa , ndi sannyataa ,
40006029	ammaa mi ɗon wi'a on , koo Suleymaanu bee ɗuuɗal risku muuɗum fuu meeɗaay ɓornaago limce booɗɗe bana pindi .
40006030	Allah ɗon ɓorna haakooji ɗi tawe hande nder ladde , jaŋgo boo ɗi cakkine nder yiite . To non kam , o ɓornataa on ko ɓuri non na , onon famɗa-nuɗɗinki'en ?
40006031	Taa mbi'e : Ɗume min nyaamata ? Malla : Ɗume min njarata ? Malla : Ɗume min ɓornoto ?
40006032	Sooyɓe nuɗɗinki ɗon ɗaɓɓa kuuje ɗe'e fuu . Ammaa Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama anndi on ngoodi haaje kuuje ɗe .
40006033	Aarte suklanaago laamu Allah e muuyo muuɗum , nden kam o humtanan on haaje mooɗon fuu .
40006034	Taa caklane haala jaŋgo , ngam jaŋgo saklanto hoore muuɗum . Nyalaade fuu , torra maare he'i nde . "
40007001	" Taa kiite yimɓe woɗɓe ngam taa Allah hiito on .
40007002	Ngam Allah hiitoto on bana on kiitori woɗɓe , o etanan on bee etirgal ngal on etani woɗɓe bee muuɗum .
40007003	Ngam ɗume a ɗon yi'a kuɗel haa yiitere deerɗa , ammaa a yi'ataa leggal haa yiitere ma ?
40007004	Koni mbi'ata deerɗa : Accu mi ittane kuɗel haa yiitere ma , an boo , leggal ɗon nder yiitere maaɗa ?
40007005	An naafikiijo , aartu ittugo leggal haa yiitere maaɗa , nden kam a yi'an laaɓɗum , haa a itta kuɗel nder yiitere deerɗa .
40007006	Taa ndokke dawaaɗi huunde seniinde , ngam taa ɗi loro dow mooɗon , ɗi mbara on , taa cakkinane gaduuji luuluuje mon , ngam taa ɗi ndamma ɗe bee kosɗe maaji . "
40007007	" Tore , on keɓan . Ɗaɓɓite , on tawan . Cilmine , ɓe maɓɓitanan on .
40007008	Ngam koomoy tori , heɓan . Koomoy ɗaɓɓiti , tawan . Koomoy silmini boo , ɓe maɓɓitanan mo .
40007009	To ɓiŋgel ma torake ma makala , a hokkan ngel hayre na ?
40007010	Malla to ngel torake ma liiŋgu , a hokkan ngel mboodi na ?
40007011	Onon halluɓe maa , on anndi hokkugo ɓiɓɓe mooɗon kuuje booɗɗe . Sakko Baabiraawo mooɗon mo asama , o ɓurataa hokkugo kuuje booɗɗe haa torotooɓe mo na ?
40007012	" Ko on ngiɗi yimɓe kuuwana on , onon boo kuuwane ɓe bana non . Kanjum woni laaɓɗum tawreeta Muusa e defte annabo'en fuu . "
40007013	" Nastire dammugal paaɗŋgal . Ngam dammugal jaasŋgal e laawol koyŋgol ɗon yahra haa halkere , ɗuuɗɓe ɗon tokko ton .
40007014	Ammaa dammugal paaɗŋgal , laawol boo caɗŋgol , ɗum ɗon yahra haa ngeendam , tokkotooɓe ton ɗuuɗaay . "
40007015	" Ndeente e annabo'en fewooɓe , waranɓe haa mooɗon ɓe ɗon nandi bee baali , ammaa nder maɓɓe ɓe caafaali kalluɗi .
40007016	On annditiran ɓe bee kuuɗe maɓɓe . Lekki gi'e rimataa inabooje , giŋgille boo ndimataa ibbe .
40007017	Lekki booɗki ɗon rima ɓiɓɓe booɗɗe , lekki kalluki boo ɗon rima ɓiɓɓe kalluɗe .
40007018	Lekki booɗki rimataa ɓiɓɓe kalluɗe , lekki kalluki boo rimataa ɓiɓɓe booɗɗe .
40007019	Lekki ki rimataa ɓiɓɓe booɗɗe , ɓe pe''an ki , ɓe ngudina ki nder yiite .
40007020	Bana non boo annditirton annabo'en fewooɓe bee kuuɗe maɓɓe . "
40007021	" Annde , naa wi'anɓe yam : Jawmiraawo , Jawmiraawo , nastata laamu Allah , sey huuwanɓe muuyo Baabiraawo am mo asama .
40007022	To nyalaade man wari , ɗuuɗɓe mbi'an : Jawmiraawo , Jawmiraawo , min ngaaji wolde Allah bee innde ma , min ndiiwi ginnaaji bee innde ma , min kuuwi kaayeefiiji ɗuuɗɗi bee innde ma boo .
40007023	Nden mi wi'an ɓe : Mi meeɗaay anndugo on sam , onon huuwooɓe halleende , ndille . "
40007024	" Yoo , koomoy nani bolle ɗe'e , tokki ɗe , nandi bee goɗɗo marɗo hakkiilo , mahɗo suudu mum dow tapaare .
40007025	Iyeende toɓi , maaje ngaddi ndiyam , keni mbaɗi bee sembe dow suudu man , ammaa ndu yibbaay , ngam ndu mahaandu dow tapaare .
40007026	Ammaa koomoy nani bolle ɗe'e , tokkaaki ɗe , nandi bee goɗɗo mo walaa hakkiilo , mahɗo suudu muuɗum dow njaareendi .
40007027	Iyeende toɓi , maaje ngaddi ndiyam , keni mbaɗi bee sembe dow suudu maajum , ndu yibbi yibbere hallunde . "
40007028	Nde Yeesu timmini wolwugo , yimɓe fuu kayɗini anndinki maako ,
40007029	ngam o wolwanaay ɓe bana moodiɓɓe tawreeta mbolwirta , ammaa o wolwani ɓe bee baawɗe .
40008001	Nden Yeesu dirti towndiire go , yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe tokki mo .
40008002	Goɗɗo kuturuujo ɓaditi mo , tuggi koppi yeeso maako , wi'i : " Moodibbo , to a yiɗi , a waawan yamɗitingo yam . "
40008003	Yeesu forti juŋŋgo muuɗum , meemi mo , nden wi'i : " Mi yiɗi , a yamɗita . " Law kuturuujo go yamɗiti .
40008004	Nden Yeesu wi'i mo : " Nan booɗɗum : Taa a wolwana koomoy haala ka sam , ammaa yah haa limanjo ngam o laare . Nden lii'a dokkal bana Muusa umruno , ngam anndingo yimɓe fuu a yamɗiti . "
40008005	Yoo , Yeesu nasti Kafarnahum . Goɗɗo Romaajo , mawɗo sooje'en , ɓaditi , tori mo ballal ,

40008009	Mi woodi mawɓe dow am , mi woodi sooje'en boo ɓe marmi . To mi wi'i oo : Yah , o yahan . To mi wi'i oya boo : War , o waran . To mi wi'i suka am : Waɗ ni , o waɗan . "
40008010	Nde Yeesu nani bolle maako ɗe'e , o yerdi ɗe , o wi'i tokkiiɓe mo : " Bee gooŋga mi wi'ata on : Mi meeɗaay tawugo nuɗɗinki bana ki'i haa koomoy nder Isra'iila sam .

40008012	Ammaa yimɓe ɓe Allah suɓino ngam laamu muuɗum , ɓe wudinteeɓe yaasi nder nyiɓre , ɓe mboyan , ɓe kir?indiran nyi'e ton . "

40008015	Yeesu meemi juŋŋgo maako , yontere acci mo , o ummi , o weerni Yeesu .
40008016	Nde kiikiɗe waɗi , ɓe ngaddi yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe , marɓe ginnaaji . Yeesu riiwi ginnaaji bee wolde mum , yamɗitini nyawɓe fuu .
40008017	O waɗi non ngam haa a gooŋɗina ko annabi Esaaya wi'i : " O efti tampere meeɗen , o roondi nyawji meeɗen . "
40008018	Nde Yeesu yi'i yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe ɗon taari mo , o umri pukara'en maako , ɓe ndilla gaɗa weendu .
40008019	Moodibbo tawreeta ɓaditi mo , wi'i : " Moodibbo , mi tokkete kootoy njahata fuu . "
40008020	Yeesu jaabi mo : " Doldolɗe ngoodi gasɗe , colli boo ngoodi caɓɓe , ammaa Ɓii-neɗɗo walaa haa o waalo ngam siwtaago . "
40008021	Goɗɗo feere nder tokkiiɓe mo wi'i : " Moodibbo , duŋganam mi yaha , mi uwa baaba am tawon . "

40008026	Yeesu jaabi ɓe : " Ngam ɗume kultorɗon , onon famɗa-nuɗɗinki'en ? " Nden o ummi , o telɓani keni e ndiyam , ɗum de'iti .
40008027	Yimɓe fuu kayɗini masin , ɓe mbi'i : " Goɗɗo moy oo , haa keni bee ndiyam fuu ɗon ɗowtani mo ? "
40008028	Nde Yeesu yotti gaɗa weendu nder lesdi Gadarena'en , marɓe nyaw ginnaaji ɗiɗo ngurti genaale , potti bee maako . Ɓe hulniiɓe masin , walaa mo saalotono laawol maajum .
40008029	Ɓe kooli , ɓe mbi'i : " An Ɓiɗɗo Allah , ko ɗaɓɓata haa amin ? A wari torrugo min diga wakkati siwa na ? "
40008030	Woodino sefre gaduuji haa nokkuure maajum , daayiiɗum seɗɗa , ɗi ɗon ndura .

40008032	Nden Yeesu wi'i ɗi : " Njehe . " Ɗi ngurti yimɓe go , ɗi nasti gaduuji , Gaduuji caamni , ndo''i diga dow fomoonde townde nder ndiyam , ɗi kalki ton .
40008033	Waynaaɓe gaduuji ndoggi , ndilli haa wuro , ngecci yimɓe ko waɗi , ko laatani marɓe ginnaaji ɗiɗo boo .
40008034	Yimɓe wuro fuu ngurti ngam fottugo bee Yeesu . Nde ɓe ngi'i mo , ɓe tori mo ɗuuɗɗum o acca lesdi maɓɓe .
40009001	Too , Yeesu nasti koombowal , ta''i weendu , warti wuro muuɗum .
40009002	Ɓe ngaddani mo goɗɗo marɗo nyaw garsa , ɓe ɗon ndoondi mo dow be''itte . Nde Yeesu yi'i nuɗɗinki maɓɓe , o wi'i nyawɗo : " Ɓiŋgel am , tiɗɗin ɓernde ma , hakkeeji maaɗa njaafaama . "
40009003	Moodiɓɓe tawreeta wonɓe ton numi : " Gorko oo ɗon wolwa kalluka dow Allah . "
40009004	Yeesu anndi ko ɓe numi , o wi'i : " Ngam ɗume on numata numooji kalluɗi bana ɗi'i ?
40009005	Ko ɓuri hoyugo ? Wi'ugo mo : Hakkeeji maaɗa njaafaama na , malla wi'ugo mo : Umma , yah ?
