45003011	Walaa marɗo hakkiilo , ɗaɓɓitanɗo Allah .
45003012	Ɓe fuu ɓe celi laawol gooŋga , ɓe mbonni .
45003013	Kondondi maɓɓe nandi bee genaale maɓɓitiiɗe ,
45003014	Kunduɗe maɓɓe keewi naalooje caatuɗe .
45003015	Kosɗe maɓɓe ɗon njaawa rufugo ?i?am yimɓe ,
45003016	bonnonda e halkere waɗan kootoy ɓe njehi fuu .
45003017	Ɓe anndaa laawol jam ,
45003018	ɓe ngalaa kulol Allah boo . "
45003019	En anndi booɗɗum : ko tawreeta wi'ata fuu , ka ɗon wi'a ɗum hokkaaɓe tawreeta , ngam taa goɗɗo heɓa hujja , ngam haa kiita Allah boo wara dow yimɓe duniyaaru fuu .
45003020	Walaa keɓranɗo yerduye Allah bee ɗowtanaago tawreeta . Neɗɗo woodi hakke , kanjum tan tawreeta anndinta mo .
45003021	Yoo , ko tawreeta e annabo'en anndini en diga ɓooyma , jonta ɗum laatake : Allah bee hoore mum waŋgini no yimɓe keɓrata yerduye maako bilaa tawreeta .
45003022	Allah jaɓan yimɓe to ɓe nuɗɗini Yeesu Almasiihu . Koomoy nuɗɗini Almasiihu , heɓan yerduye Allah . Ngam haa Allah yimɓe fuu potan kal :
45003023	Ɓe fuu ɓe mbaɗi aybe , ɓe keɓaay tedduŋgal ngal Allah annini hokkugo ɓe .
45003024	Ammaa Allah enɗi ɓe , hokkan ɓe yerduye mum caahu . Bee Yeesu Almasiihu o rimɗiniri ɓe diga baawɗe hakke .
45003025	Allah waɗi mo alaama culhotiral yeeso duniyaaru fuu . ?i?am maako ndufaaɗam haa leggal gaafaaŋgal ɗon waddana nuɗɗinɓe fuu yerduye Allah . Ɓooyma Allah munyani yimɓe , hiitaaki hakkeeji maɓɓe . Ammaa jonta o ɗon yaafo ɓe . Bana ni o waŋgini gooŋgaaku maako . Fakat , nder jamanuuru men jontaaru o muuyi waŋgingo ɗum . Kaŋko o koolniiɗo , o ɗon yerdo hooliiɓe Yeesu fuu .
45003026	
45003027	Kadi , daliila mawnitaago ɗon luttani en na ? Luttaay sam ! Ngam ɗume ? Ngam Allah limataa kuuɗe , sey nuɗɗinki .
45003028	En anndi fakat , Allah yerdataako goɗɗo ngam daliila kuuɗe tawreeta , sey ngam o nuɗɗini Yeesu Almasiihu .
45003029	Kadi Allah laati ngam Yahuudu'en tan na ? Naa o Allah ummaatooje goɗɗe boo na ? Nonnon , o Allah ummaatooje fuu .
45003030	Allah o gooto , o ɗon yerdo juulnotooɓe e ɓe njuulnataako fuu , to ɓe nuɗɗini Yeesu Almasiihu .
45003031	To mi wi'i bana ni , mi ɗon meeriɗina tawreeta na ? Naa non sam ! Mi ɗon tabitina tawreeta .
45004001	Noy haala Ibrahiima , kaaka asŋgol men ?
45004002	Kadi Allah yerdi mo ngam daliila kuuɗe maako na ? To non kam , o heɓanno daliila mawnitaago yeeso Allah . Ammaa o heɓaay .
45004003	Fakat deftere wi'i : " Ibrahiima nuɗɗini Allah , Allah boo limani mo ɗum gooŋgaaku . "
45004004	Kuuwoowo fuu foti heɓugo ngeenaari mum , ndi limataake caahu sam .
45004005	Ammaa haa Allah ɗum laataaki bana non . To goɗɗo tuugtaaki kuuɗe mum , ammaa nuɗɗini Allah jaɓanɗo marɗo aybe , nden kam Allah limanan mo nuɗɗinki man gooŋgaaku , yerdoto mo .
45004006	Kanjum , Daawuda boo wi'i ɗum , saa'i o wolwi haala seyo goɗɗo mo Allah yerdi ɗum bilaa kuuɗe . O wi'i :
45004007	" Seyo laatani yimɓe ,
45004008	Seyo laatani goɗɗo , to Jawmiraawo limanaay mo aybeeji . "
45004009	Seyo maajum laatanto juulnotooɓe tan na ? Aa'a , ngo laatanto ɓe njuulnataako boo . Mi aarti mi wi'i : " Ibrahiima nuɗɗini Allah , kaŋko boo o limani mo ɗum gooŋgaaku . "
45004010	Ndey ɗum laati ? Hiddeko o juulno na , koo ɓaawo maajum ? Fakat , saa'i man o siwa juulnaago .
45004011	Ibrahiima heɓi juulnol bana lamba tabitinka yerduye Allah . Allah yerdi mo ngam daliila nuɗɗinki maako , diga o siwa juulnaago . Bana ni Ibrahiima laatori baaba nuɗɗinɓe fuu , heɓɓe yerduye Allah , koo ɓe njuulnaaki boo .
45004012	Fakat o baaba juulnotooɓe boo . Ammaa naa juulniiɓe fuu laati ɓiɓɓe Ibrahiima , sey tokkiiɓe nuɗɗinki maako diga o juulnaakino .
45004013	Allah wi'i Ibrahiima o marnan asŋgol maako duniyaaru fuu . Koŋgol man waranaay Ibrahiima ngam o ɗowtani tawreeta , ammaa ngam o heɓi yerduye Allah bee nuɗɗinki .
45004014	To goɗɗo heɓi maral ngal bee ɗowtanaago tawreeta , nden kam nuɗɗinki nafataa , koŋgol Allah boo laatoto meere .
45004015	Walaa ko tawreeta waddanta yimɓe , sey tikkere Allah tan . Ngam to umroore woodaa , luutugo nde boo woodaa .
45004016	Ngam maajum Allah darni koŋgol mum dow nuɗɗinki , haa ɗum laato dokkal mo''ere maako . Koŋgol maako ɗon tabitana asŋgol Ibrahiima fuu , naa marɓe tawreeta tan , ammaa tokkiiɓe nuɗɗinki Ibrahiima boo . Ibrahiima laati baaba meeɗen en fuu ,
45004017	bana ko winda : " Allah wi'i mo : Mi waɗi ma baaba ummaatooje ɗuuɗɗe . " Allah wi'i mo boo : " Asŋgol ma ɗuuɗan bana koode asama . " Ibrahiima nuɗɗini Allah geeɗitinoowo maayɓe , umranɗo ko woodaa ɗum laato . Bee tammunde o nuɗɗiniri Allah , saa'i daliila tammunde woodaa . Bana ni o laatori baaba ummaatooje ɗuuɗɗe .
45004018	
45004019	Saa'i maajum duuɓi Ibrahiima ndillani teemerre . O anndi o waawataa danyugo ɓikkoy . Debbo maako Saratu boo naywi masin , waawataa reedugo . Bee non fuu o sekaay koŋgol Allah , ammaa o teddini mo bee nuɗɗinki cembiɗki .
45004020	
45004021	O nuɗɗini Allah woodi baawɗe huuwugo ko wi'i fuu .
45004022	Ngam maajum " Allah limani mo ɗum gooŋgaaku , yerdi mo . "
45004023	Wolde nde'e windaama , naa ngam Ibrahiima tan , ammaa ngam meeɗen boo .
45004024	To en nuɗɗini Allah , o limanan en ɗum gooŋgaaku . Kaŋko o ummitini Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu diga maayde .
45004025	Allah acci mo o maaya ngam daliila aybeeji men . O ummitini mo boo ngam haa en keɓa yerduye maako .
45005001	Yoo , en keɓi yerduye Allah ngam en nuɗɗini mo . Jonta hoolaare ɗon hakkunde maako bee meeɗen , barka Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
45005002	Kaŋko o heɓani en mo''ere Allah bee laawol nuɗɗinki , en ɗon tabita nder mo''ere man . En keewi seyo boo , ngam en ɗon tammo heɓugo tedduŋgal Allah .
45005003	En ɗon ceyoro koo ɓillaaje men boo , ngam en anndi ɓillaare waddan munyal .
45005004	Munyal sembiɗinan dartaare , dartaare boo tabitinan tammunde .
45005005	Bee tammunde maajum en mbustataake sam , ngam Allah waŋginani en yiide mum , hokki en Ruuhu mum .
45005006	Saa'i en tampuɓeno huuwugo ko fotti , Almasiihu maayi ngam meeɗen , enen tuurtanɓe Allah . O maayi nder saa'iire nde Allah suɓno .
45005007	Caɗɗum goɗɗo jaɓa maayugo mbattudife goɗɗo gooŋgaajo . Teema o jaɓan maayugo mbattudi goɗɗo booɗɗo masin .
45005008	Ammaa Almasiihu maayi mbattudi meeɗen yaake en konne'en Allah no . Bana ni Allah waŋginiri no o yiɗiri en .
45005009	To laatake en keɓi yerduye Allah bee ?i?am Almasiihu ndufaaɗam ngam meeɗen , nden kam en anndi boo Almasiihu hisnan en tikkere Allah warannde .
45005010	Saa'i en konne'en Allah no , o timmini konnaagu man bee maayde Ɓiɗɗo maako . Sakkoma jonta , nde laatiiɗen sooba'en maako , ngeendam Almasiihu kesam hisnan en kiita Allah .
45005011	Naa ɗu'um tan , ammaa en ɗon ceyoro kawtal bee Allah ngam daliila Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men mo laatini en sooba'en Allah .
45005012	Hakke nasti duniyaaru ngam daliila neɗɗo gooto . Bee hakke man , maayde boo nasti . Maayde laati dow yimɓe fuu , ngam ɓe fuu ɓe mbaɗi hakke .
45005013	Hakke ɗon nder duniyaaru diga tawreeta waraayno . Ammaa Allah limaayno hakkeeji , ngam walaano umroore tawon .
45005014	Bee non fuu , diga Aadamu haa warugo Muusa , maayde laati dow yimɓe fuu , koo ɓe mbaɗaay hakke bana Aadamu mo luuti umroore Allah laaɓnde .
45005015	Ammaa dokkal ngal Allah hokkata en bee goɗɗo oo , nandaay bee aybewol Aadamu sam . Fakat , yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe maayi ngam gooto waɗi aybe . Ammaa mo''ere Allah ɓuri mawnugo piw , non boo dokkal ngal o hokkata yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe ngam daliila neɗɗo gooto , waato Yeesu Almasiihu .
45005016	Dokkal Allah ɓuri aybe goɗɗo gooto go sembe . Kiita Allah dow aybe gooto oo aybini yimɓe fuu . Ammaa mo''ere Allah ɗon jaalo aybeeji ɗuuɗɗi , ɗon laɓɓina yimɓe fuu .
45005017	Fakat , maayde fuɗɗi jaalaago ngam gooto waɗi aybe . Ammaa ɓurɗum mawnugo laati bee goɗɗo feere , waato Yeesu Almasiihu . Ngam daliila maako , ɗuuɗeeŋga mo''ere Allah e yerduye mum laatani en , en keɓi laamu e ngeendam .
45005018	Mi wi'i : Allah aybini yimɓe fuu ngam goɗɗo gooto waɗi aybe . Kadiboo Allah laɓɓinan yimɓe fuu , hokkan ɓe ngeendam ngam goɗɗo gooto huuwi ko fotti .
45005019	Ɗuuɗɓe laati marɓe hakke ngam gooto luuti umroore Allah . Kadiboo ɗuuɗɓe keɓan yerduye Allah ngam gooto ɗowtani mo .
45005020	Tawreeta ɓesdaama ngam mawningo aybe . Ammaa to hakke ɓesdake , mo''ere Allah ɓurtan ɓesdaago .
45005021	Baawɗe hakke waŋgiri bee maayde . Ammaa baawɗe mo''ere Allah e gooŋgaaku mum ɗon waŋga bee ngeendam nduumiiɗam ɗam keɓɗen barka Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men .
45006001	Ko mbi'eten jonta ? En tokko waɗugo hakke ngam haa mo''ere Allah ɓesdo na ?
45006002	Kayya , naa non sam ! Hedi hakke kam , en maayɓe . Kadi noy tokkortooɗen jooɗodaago bee hakke ?
45006003	Nde en ngiiwi ngiiwam baptisma , en kawti bee Yeesu Almasiihu . On anndi booɗɗum ɗum kawtal bee maayde maako .
45006004	Nder ngiiwam baptisma en uwdaama bee maako . Ammaa bana kaŋko o ummiti diga maayde bee baawɗe Allah kaayeefiije , bana non enen boo en keɓi yeeɗugo nder ngeendam kesam .
45006005	To en kawti bee maako nder maayde nandunde maayde maako , nden kam en ummititto boo bana maako .
45006006	En anndi fakat , ko laatiiɗen ɓooyma ɗum maaydi bee maako dow leggal gaafaaŋgal , ngam haa neɗɗo men ɓooymaajo halka , waato ko hakke jaali ɗum , taa en tokko ɗowtanaago hakke bana maccuɓe .
45006007	Ngam to goɗɗo maayi , hakke walaa baawɗe dow maako , timmi .
45006008	To en maaydi bee Almasiihu , nden kam en ɗon nuɗɗina en ngeeɗan bee maako boo .
45006009	Fakat en anndi Almasiihu ummiti diga maayde , meetataa maayugo , maayde walaa baawɗe dow maako .
45006010	Nde woore o maayi hedi hakke , jonta o ɗon yeeɗa ngam Allah .
45006011	Bana non onon boo ndaare ko'e mon on maayɓe hedi hakke , ammaa nder kawtal bee Almasiihu on yeeɗɓe ngam Allah .
45006012	Ngam maajum taa acce hakke laamo nder ɓalli mon maayanɗi , taa tokke suunooji maaji boo .
45006013	Taa acce hakke huuwtinira terɗe mon bana balmi halleende . Ammaa ndokke ko'e mon haa juŋŋgo Allah , ngam on ngurti maayde , on nasti ngeendam . Acce Allah huuwtinira terɗe mon bana balmi mbooɗeeŋga .
45006014	Yeeso ɗo , hakke walaa baawɗe dow mooɗon , ngam tawreeta laamantaako on , sey mo''ere Allah .
45006015	Nde mo''ere ɗon laamano en , naa tawreeta kam , en tokko waɗugo hakke na ? Naa non sam !
45006016	On anndaa na ? Mo mbaɗɗon ko'e mon maccuɓe mum , kaŋko ɗowtantooɗon . To on ɗon ɗowtano hakke , nden kam on maayan . To on ɗon ɗowtano Allah , nden kam on keɓan yerduye maako .
45006017	Yettoore laatano Allah ! Naane on maccuɓe hakke , ammaa jonta on ɗon ɗowtano gooŋga bee ɓernde woore . Gooŋga maajum keɓɗon bee anndinol .
45006018	On rimɓe e njeyaaŋgu hakke , on laati jeyaaɓe gooŋgaaku .
45006019	Mi huuwtiniri balndol njeyaaŋgu ngam haa mi faamtina on ko haani . Naane on mbaɗi terɗe mon fuu maccuɓe coɓki e halleende haa on kuuwa kalluɗum . Bana non jonta boo mbaɗe terɗe mon maccuɓe gooŋgaaku haa on kuuwa ko fottanta Allah .
45006020	Yaake on laatino maccuɓe hakke , on laatino rimɓe hedi gooŋgaaku .
45006021	Ɗume keɓnooɗon bee kuuɗe mon ? Fakat on ɗon cemtira ɗum jonta , ngam timmoode kuuɗe man wonno maayde .
45006022	Ammaa jonta on rimɓe e hakke , on laati jeyaaɓe Allah . Ngam maajum on ɗon kuuwa ko fottanta mo , timmoode kuuɗe mon ɗum ngeendam nduumiiɗam .
45006023	Ngam ngeenaari hakke , ɗum maayde . Ammaa Allah ɗon mo''ana en ngeendam nduumiiɗam nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men .
45007001	Deerɗam'en , on fuu on paaman ko mbi'anmi , ngam on anndi tawreeta . Tawreeta mari baawɗe dow goɗɗo yaake o geeto .
45007002	Bana debbo te'aaɗo : Umroore tawreeta haɓɓi mo haa goriiko yaake gorko ɗon bee yoŋki . To gorko maayi , debbo rimɗi e umroore nde'e .
45007003	Ngam maajum , to o wondi bee gorko feere saa'i goriiko geeto , nden kam o jeenoowo . Ammaa to goriiko maayi , umroore maajum walaa dow maako , o waɗaay njeenu to o te'i bee gorko feere .
45007004	Bana non onon boo , deerɗam'en : On maaydi bee Almasiihu . Ngam maajum on maayɓe hedi tawreeta . Jonta goɗɗo feere mari on , oon ummitiiɗo diga maayde . Jonta on mbaawan nafugo Allah bee kuuɗe mon .
45007005	Yaake en ɗonno tokko numooji ko'e men , suunooji njaali ɓalli men , nastini en nder hakke . Tawreeta umminno suunooji man , en kuuwi ko waddani en maayde .
45007006	Ammaa jonta en rimɓe e tawreeta , en maayɓe hedi umroore haɓɓunoonde en . Ngam maajum en tokkataako Allah dow laawol ɓooymawol ngol umrooje bindaaɗe . En ɗon tokko mo dow laawol kesol ngol Ruuhu maako .
45007007	Ko mbi'eten jonta ? Tawreeta ɗum hakke na ? Naa non sam ! Ammaa to tawreeta woodaano , mi anndataano baawɗe hakke . To tawreeta wi'aayno : " Taa suuna " , suuno ɓillataano yam .
45007008	Umroore maajum hokki hakke laawol ummingo suunooji kooɗiye fuu nder am . To walaano umroore , hakke waatanno .
45007009	Naane mi geetono , mi anndaano tawreeta . Nden umroore wari , hakke boo fuɗɗi yeeɗugo .
45007010	Ammaa min mi maayi . Umroore man hokkaama ngam sappingo yam laawol ngeendam , ammaa nde waddani yam maayde .
45007011	Ngam hakke huuwtiniri umroore man ngam haa estammi , mbarammi .
45007012	Fakat , tawreeta iwi haa Allah , umrooje maaka ceniiɗe , pottuɗe , booɗɗe .
45007013	To non kam , huunde woonde waddani yam maayde na ? Naa non sam ! Ammaa hakke huuwtiniri huunde woonde nde'e haa mbarammi , ngam haa hakke waŋga ɗum hakke fakat . Ngam daliila umroore , hakke heɓi waŋgingo halleende mum fuu .
45007014	Walaa seko , tawreeta iwi haa Allah . Ammaa min mi neɗɗo maayanɗo , mi maccuɗo hakke .
45007015	Mi faamataa ko kuuwanmi . Mi huuwataa ko ngiɗmi , ammaa ko mi yiɗaa , kanjum kuuwanmi .
45007016	To mi muuyaay kalluɗum ko kuuwanmi , nden kam mi gooŋɗini tawreeta ka mbooɗka .
45007017	Waato min bee hoore am mi huuwataa ɗum , ammaa hakke ɗon jooɗi nder am , ɗon huuwa ɗum .
45007018	Mi anndi , booɗɗum woodaa nder am . Mi ɗon muuya huuwugo booɗɗum , ammaa mi waawataa .
45007019	Mi huuwataa booɗɗum ko ngiɗmi , sey kalluɗum ko nganymi .
45007020	To ni mi ɗon huuwa ko mi yiɗaa , fakat naa min bee hoore am huuwata ɗum , ammaa hakkewol jooɗiiŋgol nder am huuwata ɗum .
45007021	Ndaa laawol ngol kuuɗe am tokkoto : To mi yiɗi huuwugo booɗɗum , kalluɗum tan laatoto .
45007022	Ɓernde am ɗon seyoro tawreeta Allah , ammaa ɓandu am ɗon tokko umroore feere .
45007023	Umroore maajum ɗon haɓa bee umroore nde hakkiilo am yerdoto . Nde wartiri yam naŋgaaɗo hakke , umroore hakke ɗon jaalo ɓandu am boo .
45007024	Hakkiilo am ɗon yerdo tawreeta Allah , ammaa kuuɗe am ɗon ɗowtano umroore hakke . Kayto , mi jurumɗo ! Walaa ko luttani yam , sey maayde . Moy rimɗintammi e ɓillaare nde'e?  Yettoore laatano Allah ngam barka Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men .
45008001	Ngam maajum , to goɗɗo hawti bee Yeesu Almasiihu , Allah hiitataako mo .
45008002	O ɗon tokko umroore Ruuhu waddanannde mo ngeendam nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu . Umroore maajum rimɗini mo diga umroore hakke waddannde mo maayde .
45008003	Allah bee hoore mum huuwi ko tawreeta waawaay huuwugo ngam en tampuɓe . O neli Ɓiɗɗo maako marɗo ɓandu , maatuɗo esto hakke bana yimɓe fuu . O hiiti hakke nder ɓandu neɗɗo oo . Bana non o jaalori hakke .
45008004	Jonta kam en mbaawan huuwugo gooŋgaaku ngu tawreeta ɗaɓɓata . Ngam en ɗon ɗowtano Ruuhu Allah , naa giɗaaɗi ko'e men .
45008005	To goɗɗo tokkake giɗaaɗi mum , giɗaaɗi maajum njaaloto hakkiilo maako . Ammaa to Ruuhu Allah ɗon jooɗi nder maako , nden kam Ruuhu maajum laamanto hakkiilo maako .
45008006	Tokkiiɗo giɗaaɗi mum maayan , ammaa tokkiiɗo Ruuhu Allah heɓan ngeendam e jam .
45008007	Tokkiiɗo giɗaaɗi mum woni konneejo Allah . O ɗowtantaako umroore Allah , fakat o waawataa ɗowtanaago nde sam .
45008008	Tokkiiɗo giɗaaɗi mum waawataa fottango Allah .
45008009	Ammaa onon kam , giɗaaɗi mon njaalataako on . On ɗon ɗowtano Ruuhu Allah , to fakat Ruuhu maajum ɗon jooɗi nder mooɗon . Mo heɓaay Ruuhu ngu Almasiihu hokkata , laataaki mo maako .
45008010	To Almasiihu ɗon huuwa nder mooɗon , nden kam ɓalli mon maayan ngam daliila hakke , ammaa Ruuhu Allah hokkan on ngeendam , ngam on keɓi yerduye Allah .
45008011	Allah ummitini Yeesu Almasiihu diga maayde . To Ruuhu maako ɗon jooɗi nder mooɗon , nden kam o yeeɗitinan ɓalli mon maayanɗi boo bee Ruuhu maajum .
45008012	Deerɗam'en , ngam maajum walaa ko doolata en tokkaago ɗabiya men , doole man timmi .
45008013	Ngam to on tokkake giɗaaɗi mon , on maayan . Ammaa to on acci Ruuhu Allah mbara giɗaaɗi mon , nden kam on ngeeɗan .
45008014	Ɗowaaɓe Ruuhu Allah fuu , kamɓe laati ɓiɓɓe Allah .
45008015	Walaa haaje on puɗɗita diwnugo yeeso Allah , ngam Ruuhu ngu o hokki on , laatinaay on maccuɓe maako , ammaa ɓiɓɓe maako . Ruuhu maako ɗon jooɗi nder meeɗen . Ngam maajum mbi'eten Allah : " Baaba ! "
45008016	Ruuhu Allah ɗon tabitina seedamku ruuhuuji men : En ɓiɓɓe Allah fakat .
45008017	To ni en ɓiɓɓe maako , nden kam en keɓan boo ko o sigani ɓiɓɓe maako , o hokkan en ko o hokki Almasiihu . Ngam to en njaɓi geɗal torraaji Almasiihu , en keɓan geɗal tedduŋgal maako boo .
45008018	Mi numi haala torraaji men nder jamanuuru jontaaru . Fakat , ɗi potaay foondeego bee tedduŋgal ngal Allah tammi waŋginango en .
45008019	Duniyaaru fuu ɗon yenwa masin haa Allah waŋgina ɓiɓɓe mum bee tedduŋgal .
45008020	Allah yoofi duniyaaru fuu haa ndu majja , naa ngam aybe maaru . Ammaa Allah nastini ndu nder kiita dow aybe yimɓe . Bee non fuu o hokki duniyaaru tammunde
45008021	rimɗugo e njeyaaŋgu halkere , ndu hawta bee ɓiɓɓe maako nder ndimu e tedduŋgal .
45008022	En anndi , haa jonta duniyaaru ɗon uuma , ɗon luuwe bana ɓesnanɗo .
45008023	Naa duniyaaru tan , ammaa enen heɓɓe Ruuhu Allah ngu dokkal mum aartuŋgal , enen boo en ɗon uuma . En ɗon ngenwa wondugo bee Allah bana ɓiɓɓe mum , o rimɗina en e majjere ɓalli men .
45008024	Kisndam men ɗon tabiti , ammaa dow tammunde . Ammaa to en ɗon ngi'a ko tammotooɗen heɓugo , nden kam naa ɗum tammunde gooŋgaare . Moy tammoto hayru ngu o heɓi ?
45008025	Ammaa to en ɗon tammo heɓugo ko en ngi'aay tawon , nden kam en ndeenan ɗum bee munyal .
45008026	Ruuhu Allah ɗon walla en , ngam en tampuɓe . En anndaa koo toraago Allah bana no haani . Ruuhu bee hoore mum ɗon toro Allah ngam meeɗen , naa bee bolle yimɓe .
45008027	Allah linyoowo ɓerɗe ɗon faama ko Ruuhu ɗaɓɓata . Ngam Ruuhu ɗon torano yimɓe Allah bana Allah yiɗi .
45008028	En anndi , to goɗɗo yiɗi Allah , nden kam kooɗume fuu laatoto ngam hayru maako ngu Allah tammini mo fodde anniya muuɗum .
45008029	Diga ɓooyma Allah heerɗini suɓaaɓe mum fuu ngam haa ɓe keɓa ngeendam bana Ɓiɗɗo maako , Almasiihu boo laato afo caka deerɗiraaɓe ɗuuɗɓe .
45008030	Heerɗinaaɓe ɓe'e fuu , Allah ewni ɓe boo . Nden o yerdi ɓe , o nastini ɓe nder tedduŋgal maako boo .
45008031	Jonta kam , ko lutti wi'eego ? To Allah ɗon wondi bee meeɗen , moy waawata honugo en ?
45008032	O jogitaaki koo Ɓiɗɗo maako , ammaa o acci mo o maaya mbattudi meeɗen en fuu . To non kam , o hokkataa en kooɗume fuu bee maako na ?
45008033	Walaa mo foti wullaago suɓaaɓe Allah , ngam Allah bee hoore mum gooŋɗini ɓe .
45008034	Walaa mo foti hiitaago ɓe . Ngam Yeesu Almasiihu maayi mbattudi maɓɓe . Ko ɓuri ɗum boo , o ummiti diga maayde . O ɗon jooɗi haa nyaamo Allah , o ɗon seetto en .
45008035	To non kam , moy waawata sendugo en bee yiide Almasiihu ? Bone na , ɓillaare na , toonyaare na , weelo na , talakaaku na , joote na , malla kaafahi ?
45008036	Bana ko winda :
45008037	Ammaa nder kuuje ɗe'e fuu en keɓan jaalorgal timmuŋgal bee ballal Almasiihu , giɗɗo en .
45008038	Mi anndi fakat , walaa ko sendata en bee yiide maako , koo maayde , koo ngeendam , koo malaa'ika'en , koo baawɗeeji goɗɗi , koo jontaajum , koo garanɗum ,
45008039	koo baawɗe nder asama malla nder jahannama . Yiide Allah laatani en bee Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men . Ngam maajum walaa kooɗume nder duniyaaru fuu heɓata sendugo en bee yiide Allah .
45009001	Yoo , ko mbi'anmi jonta , ɗum gooŋga . Almasiihu mari yam , ngam maajum mi fewataa . Ruuhu Ceniiɗo ɗon laamano numo ɓernde am , kanjum boo ɗum ɗon seedo yam mi fewataa .
45009002	Mi cakliiɗo masin , ɓernde am accataa naawugo ngam daliila bandiraaɓe am , yimɓe lenyol am . To min kam , mi jaɓanno naaloore Allah e seedugo bee Almasiihu ngam daliila maɓɓe .
45009003	
45009004	Kamɓe ɓe asŋgol Isra'iila , suɓaaɓe Allah . Allah laatini ɓe ɓiɓɓe mum , waŋginani ɓe tedduŋgal mum , haɓɓi alkawalji bee maɓɓe , hokki ɓe tawreeta e diina ngooŋɗuka , iinani ɓe hayruuji ɗuuɗɗi .
45009005	Ɓe danygol kaakiraaɓe aartuɓe , koo Almasiihu boo o goɗɗo asŋgol maɓɓe . Yettoore laatano Allah , gonɗo dow kooɗume fuu , haa foroy . Aamiina !
45009006	Mi wi'aay koŋgol Allah laati meere . Ammaa naa Isra'iila'en fuu laati yimɓe Allah suɓaaɓe .
45009007	Naa iwɓe haa Ibrahiima fuu laati ɓiɓɓe Ibrahiima bee gooŋga . Allah wi'i Ibrahiima : " Nder Isiyaaku danygol ma ewna . "
45009008	Waato danyaaɓe ɓandu laataaki ɓiɓɓe Allah , sey danyaaɓe ngam daliila koŋgol Allah limete nder ɓiɓɓe .
45009009	Ndaa ni Allah wi'i : " To saa'iire nde muuymi yottake , mi waran , mi tawan Saratu heɓi ɓiɗɗo gorko . "
45009010	Naa kanjum tan , ammaa ndaarenma ɓiɓɓe Rebekka ɗiɗo boo . Baaba maɓɓe gooto , waato kaaka men Isiyaaku .
45009011	Ammaa cuɓol Allah ɗon dari dow anniya muuɗum tan . Ngam maajum o wi'i Rebekka : " Mawniraawo huuwanan minyiraawo . " Allah wi'i ɗum diga ɓe ciwa danyeego , hiddeko ɓe kuuwa booɗɗum malla kalluɗum . Cuɓol Allah daraaki dow kuuɗe maɓɓe , sey dow muuyo Allah tan .
45009012	
45009013	Bana ko winda : " Yakubu ngiɗmi , Isuwa nganymi . "
45009014	To non kam , ko mbi'eten ? Kadi Allah ɗon huuwa ko fottaay na ? Naa non sam !
45009015	O wi'i Muusa : " Mi enɗan mo enɗanmi , mi hinnoto mo kinnotoomi . "
45009016	Waato haala man fuu darataako dow muuyo neɗɗo malla tiinaare mum , sey dow hinnuye Allah .
45009017	Nder deftere njaŋgeten boo ko Allah wi'i Firawna : " Mi waɗi ma laamiiɗo ngam daliila ngoota tan : Haa mi waŋgina baawɗe am dow maaɗa , mi anndina innde am nder duniyaaru fuu . "
45009018	Waato Allah ɗon huuwa bana o muuyi : O hinnoto oo , o saatinan hoore oya .
45009019	Teema on mbi'atam : " To ɗum laatake bana ni , ngam ɗume Allah aybinta min ? Moy waawi dartaago muuyo maako ? "
45009020	Kayya ! En ɓeye haa ngaabotiren bee Allah ? Kadi tagdi wi'an tagɗo ɗum : " Koni mbaɗɗa mi bana ni ? "
45009021	Mahoowo payanɗe maraay baawɗe dow loope kecce na ? Bee loope goote o waawan waɗugo payanɗe ɗiɗi , woɗnde marnde saman , woɗnde boo walaa saman .
45009022	Bana ni kuugal Allah wa'i . Haa woɗɓe o muuyi waŋgingo ɓernuki maako e baawɗe maako . Ɓe kaandi halkugo , ammaa o munyani ɓe munyal ɗuuɗŋgal .
45009023	Haa woɗɓe boo o muuyi waŋgingo ɗuuɗeeŋga tedduŋgal maako . O enɗi ɓe , o taaskitini ɓe diga ɓooyma ngam haa ɓe keɓa tedduŋgal maako .
45009024	Ɗum enen ! Ngam maajum o ewni en , naa nder Yahuudu'en tan , ammaa nder ummaatooje goɗɗe boo .
45009025	O wi'i bee hunduko annabi Hose'a :
45009026	Haa nokkuure ɓe mbi'ana :
45009027	Annabi Esaaya boo wolwi dow Isra'iila . O wi'i : " Koo to yimɓe Isra'iila ɗuuɗiri bana njaareendi maayo , hisanɓe maɓɓe ɗuuɗataa sam .
45009028	Ngam Jawmiraawo timminan anniya mum dow duniyaaru , o timminan ka law . "
45009029	Bana Esaaya aarti , wi'i :
45009030	Ko mbi'eten jonta ? Yimɓe ummaatooje goɗɗe keɓi yerduye Allah , koo ɓe ɗaɓɓitaay ɗum . Allah yerdi ɓe , ngam ɓe nuɗɗini Almasiihu .
45009031	Isra'iila'en kaɓdi ɗowtanaago tawreeta ngam haa ɓe keɓa yerduye Allah , ammaa ɓe keɓaay .
45009032	Ngam ɗume ? Ngam ɓe kaɓdi fottango Allah bee kuuɗe , naa bee nuɗɗinki . Ngam maajum ɓe pergi dow mo wi'ete " hayre fergoore " ,
45009033	bana ko winda :
45010001	Deerɗam'en , bee ɓernde am fuu ngiɗmi yimɓe lenyol am kisa . Mi accataa toraago Allah ngam maɓɓe .
45010002	Mi ɗon seedo ɓe ɓe mari tiinaare haa ɓe ɗowtano Allah . Ammaa tiinaare maɓɓe daraaki dow anndal gooŋɗuŋgal .
45010003	Ɓe paamaay no Allah yerdorto yimɓe yerduye mum . Ɓe ɗon ɗaɓɓa gooŋgaaku maɓɓe dow laawol kuuɗe maɓɓe . Bana ni ɓe ɗon luutira nufaye Allah .
45010004	Diga Almasiihu wari , jamanu tawreeta timmi . Koomoy nuɗɗini mo , Allah yerdoto ɗum .
45010005	Ndaa ko Muusa windi dow haala gooŋgaaku bee laawol tawreeta : " Koomoy ɗowtani umrooje tawreeta , yeeɗan bee maajum . "
45010006	Ammaa ndaa ko wi'a dow haala gooŋgaaku bee laawol nuɗɗinki : " Taa wi' : Moy eeŋgata haa asama ? " o waato ngam jippingo Almasiihu .
45010007	" Taa wi' boo : Moy dirtoto nder ngaska lugguka masin ? " o waato ngam eeŋgtingo Almasiihu diga joonde maayɓe .
45010008	Ndaa ni wolde man : " Wolde Allah ɓadi ma masin , nder hunduko ma e nder ɓernde ma . " Kanjum woni kubaruwol nuɗɗinki ngol min ngaajinta .
45010009	To a seedake bee hunduko ma : " Yeesu woni Jawmiraawo " , to a nuɗɗini bee ɓernde ma Allah ummitini mo diga maayde , nden kam a hisan .
45010010	Nuɗɗinɗo bee ɓernde heɓan yerduye Allah , ceediiɗo Almasiihu bee hunduko boo hisan .
45010011	Ngam deftere wi'i : " Koomoy nuɗɗini mo , kiita do''ataa mo . "
45010012	Haala ka ngoota ngam yimɓe fuu , walaa ko sendata Yahuudu'en bee ummaatooje goɗɗe . Ngam Allah woni Jawmiraawo maɓɓe ɓe fuu , o ɗon mo''ana seedotooɓe mo fuu .
45010013	Bana ko deftere wi'ata : " Koomoy seedi innde Jawmiraawo , hisan . "
45010014	Ammaa noy ɓe ceedorto mo to ɓe nuɗɗinaay kubaruwol kisndam ? Noy ɓe nuɗɗinirta ngol to ɓe meeɗaay nanugo ngol ? Noy ɓe keɓrata nanugo ngol to gaajoowo ngol woodaa ?
45010015	E noy goɗɗo waajirta to nelaaka ? Bana ko winda : " Ɗume wooɗiri bana kosɗe waajooɓe kubaruwol seyo ? "
45010016	Ammaa naa yimɓe fuu njaɓi kubaruwol ngo'ol . Annabi Esaaya wi'i : " Ya Jawmiraawo , moy nuɗɗini waaju amin ? "
45010017	Bana non nuɗɗinki iwi haa nanugo waaju , waaju boo ɗon iwa haa kubaruwol Almasiihu .
45010018	Too , sey mi ?ama : Isra'iila'en nanaay kubaruwol ngol na ? Fakat ɓe nani ! Deftere ɗon wi'a :
45010019	Sey mi ?amta fahin : Isra'iila'en paamaay na ? Muusa aarti , jaabi :
45010020	Esaaya boo hulaay wi'ugo :
45010021	Ammaa dow Isra'iila o wi'i : " Mi nyalli fortugo juuɗe am haa mi jaɓɓo yimɓe luutooɓe , tuurtooɓe . "
45011001	Ngam maajum ?amanmi : Allah wudini yimɓe mum na ? Naa non sam ! Min bee hoore am mi goɗɗo Isra'iila , mi danygol Ibrahiima , mi goɗɗo lenyol Benyamin .
45011002	Allah wudinaay yimɓe mum ɓe o suɓno diga fuɗɗam . Ciftore haala deftere , nde Eliya woyani Allah ngam daliila Isra'iila'en .
45011003	O wi'i : " Ya Jawmiraawo , ɓe mbari annabo'en ma , ɓe ngibbini kirsirɗe ma . Min feere am lutti , ammaa ɓe ɗon ɗaɓɓa mbarugo yam min boo . "
45011004	Ɗume Allah jaabi mo ? O wi'i : " Mi luttani hoore am worɓe ujine njoweeɗiɗo ɓe cujidanaay Ba'al . "
45011005	Bana non jonta boo : Allah lutti suɓaaɓe seɗɗa ngam daliila hinnuye mum .
45011006	Cuɓol maako darataako dow kuuɗe maɓɓe sam . Ngam to cuɓol Allah darino dow kuuɗe yimɓe , nden kam hinnuye maako naa ɗum hinnuye .
45011007	Kadi noy jonta ? Ko Isra'iila'en ɗaɓɓiti , ɓe keɓaay ɗum . Sey suɓaaɓe Allah nder maɓɓe keɓi ɗum . Ɓurna maɓɓe laati saata-ko'e'en , ɓe nanaay ewnaandu Allah .
45011008	Bana ko winda :
45011009	Daawuda boo wi'i :
45011010	Wumnu gite maɓɓe ngam taa ɓe ngi'a .
45011011	Ngam maajum ?amanmi : Ɗum laatani yimɓe Isra'iila ngam haa ɓe ndo''o na ? Naa non sam ! Kamɓe ɓe mbaɗi aybe . Ngam maajum kisndam warani yimɓe ummaatooje goɗɗe . Allah waɗi ɗum ngam haa o ummina kaajal Isra'iila'en .
45011012	Aybe maɓɓe waddani ummaatooje barkaaji ɗuuɗɗi , asar maɓɓe laati risku ummaatooje . Sakkoma to Isra'iila'en fuu tuubi , nden kam barkaaji ɓesdan ɗuuɗugo masin .
45011013	Onon ɓe laataaki Yahuudu'en , jonta mi ɗon wolwana on : Mi laati nelaaɗo haa ummaatooje goɗɗe , mi ɗon samɗina kuugal am boo .
45011014	Teema mi heɓan ummingo kaajal yimɓe lenyol am , haa mi hisna woɗɓe maɓɓe .
45011015	Saa'i ɓe ngudina , duniyaaru fuu heɓi hoolaare bee Allah . Kadi ɗume laatoto to Allah jaɓi ɓe fahin ? Ɓe laatoto bana ummitinaaɓe diga maayde !
45011016	To goɗɗo lii'anake Allah tamseere aartunde , tamseeje fuu laatoto cenaaɗe . To ɗaɗi lekki laatanake Allah , nden kam lice boo kaŋko jeyi .
45011017	Lice goɗɗe ittaama haa jaytunhi jarne . Onon on nastinaama haa pellel maaje bana lice kese iwɗe jaytunhi laddehi . On kawti bee luttuɓe Isra'iila , on ɗon keɓa sembe diga ɗaɗol jaytunhi jarne .
45011018	Ngam maajum taa njawe lice ittaaɗe go . On ngalaa daliila mawnitaago . Ngam onon on njogataako ɗaɗol , ammaa ɗaɗol ɗon jogi on .
45011019	Teema on mbi'an jonta : " Lice man ittaama ngam haa min nasta pellel maaje . "
45011020	Gooŋga kam , ammaa ɗe ittaama ngam ɗe cali nuɗɗingo . Onon boo on nastinaama ngam on nuɗɗini . Ngam maajum taa mawnite . Ndikka on kula .
45011021	Allah enɗaay Isra'iila'en , koo nde ɓe lice asliije . Kadi on tammi o enɗan on na ?
45011022	Ndaare le mbooɗeeŋga Allah e caatal mum fuu . O ɗon saatana accuɓe mo , ammaa o ɗon woonana on nde on ɗon tabiti nder mbooɗeeŋga maako . To naa non , onon boo on itteteeɓe .
45011023	To Isra'iila'en lortake , nuɗɗini , nden kam Allah nastinan ɓe fahin nder jaytunhi , ngam o mari baawɗe waylugo kiita maako .
45011024	Onon yimɓe ummaatooje on nandi bee lice jaytunhi laddehi . Nde Allah nastini on nder jaytunhi jarne , ɗum luuti ɗabiya fuu . To non kam , ɗum koyɗum haa Allah nastina lice asliije fahin nder jaytunhi ki ɗe iwi haa muuɗum .
45011025	Deerɗam'en , mi yiɗi waŋginango on sirri , ngam taa ndaaron ko'e mon bana on marɓe anndal fuu . Allah acci Isra'iila'en woɗɓe laato saata-ko'e'en . Ammaa ɗum timman to suɓaaɓe Allah nder ummaatooje goɗɗe ngari haa maako bee limgal keewŋgal .
45011026	Nden kam Isra'iila fuu hisan , bana ko winda :
45011027	Kanjum woni alkawal am bee maɓɓe ,
45011028	Kamɓe ɓe laati konne'en Allah , ngam haa onon on keɓa nanugo linjiila . Ammaa Allah suɓi kaakiraaɓe maɓɓe aartuɓe . Ngam maajum ɓe yiɗaaɓe maako .
45011029	To Allah barkiɗini ummaatoore koondeyeere , suɓi nde , nden kam o mimsitittaako .
45011030	Onon on ɗowtanaakino Allah . Bee non fuu on keɓi enɗam maako jonta , ngam Yahuudu'en luuti muuyo maako .
45011031	Bana non kamɓe boo : Jonta ɓe ɗowtantaako Allah ngam o enɗi on . Ammaa ɗum laati ngam haa ɓe keɓa enɗam maako , kamɓe boo .
45011032	Allah haɓɓi yimɓe fuu nder sooynde ɗowtaare , ngam o muuyi enɗugo ɓe fuu .
45011033	Kay ! Jeynitaare Allah ɗuuɗi masin . Faamu maako e anndal maako heɓtataake . Moy foti linyugo kiitaaji maako ? Moy faamata laabi maako ?
45011034	Deftere wi'i :
45011035	Moy meeɗi hokkugo mo huunde ngam haa heɓa mbarjaari ? "
45011036	Allah tagi kuuje fuu . Haa maako ɗe iwi , haa maako ɗe loroto boo . Tedduŋgal laatano mo haa foroy . Aamiina !
45012001	Deerɗam'en , Allah waŋginani en enɗam mum ɗuuɗɗam . Ngam maajum mi ɗon toro on on lii'ano mo ko'e mon haa on kuuwana mo . Kanjum woni dokkal pottananŋgal mo .
45012002	Taa tokke al'aadaaji duniyaaru ndu , ammaa acce Allah wayla ɓerɗe mon , hesɗitina hakkiilooji mon . Nden kam on anndan muuyo Allah , on anndan ko wooɗi , on anndan ko Allah yerdoto , ko laati timmuɗum .
45012003	Allah mo''ani yam , waɗi yam nelaaɗo mum . Ngam maajum umranmi koomoy mooɗon : Taa goɗɗo numana hoore mum maŋgu ɓuranŋgu no foti , ammaa koomoy laara hoore mum deydey geɗal nuɗɗinki ngal Allah hokki mo .
45012004	Ndaare ɓandu neɗɗo : Ndu woodi terɗe ɗuuɗɗe , terde fuu woodi kuugal mum boo , ammaa ɓandu laati wooru .
45012005	Bana non enen boo : En fuu en laati ɓandu wooru nder kawtal bee Almasiihu , en ɗon mballindira bana terɗe feere-feereeje haa ɓandu maajum .
45012006	Allah mo''ani en dokke feere-feereeje , haa en kuuwtinira ɗe deydey nuɗɗinki men . Mo heɓi dokkal waajugo wolde Allah , sey o waaja ko Allah wi'i mo tan .
45012007	Mo heɓi dokkal wallugo tampuɓe , sey o walla ɓe . Mo heɓi dokkal ekkitingo nuɗɗinɓe , sey o ekkitina ɓe .
45012008	Mo heɓi dokkal de'itingo woɗɓe , sey o de'itina ɓe . Mo yiɗi sendugo risku mum bee woɗɓe , sey waɗa ɗum bee caahaaki . Mo heɓi kaliifaaku , sey o huuwa bee tiinaare . Mo woonanta woɗɓe , sey o waɗa ɗum bee seyo .
45012009	Yiide mon laato laaɓnde , nde walaa faasikaare . Nganye halleende koondeye , taa acce huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga .
45012010	Ngiɗindire ngam on deerɗiraaɓe nder nuɗɗingo Almasiihu , koomoy ɓurna deerɗum dow hoore mum .
45012011	Taa laate on mbaateendam'en , acce Ruuhu Allah tiɗɗina on , kuuwane Jawmiraawo bee anniya .
45012012	Ceyore tammunde hayru mon , munyane ɓillaaje , tiine do'aago .
45012013	Mballite nuɗɗinɓe laafuɓe bee jawdi mon , njaɓɓe hoɗɓe bee booɗɗum .
45012014	Tore Allah barkiɗina toonyiiɓe on . Torane ɓe barka , naa naaloore .
45012015	Ceyode bee seyiiɓe , mboyde bee woyanɓe .
45012016	Njooɗode on narruɓe . Taa ɗaɓɓe maŋgu nder jama'aare mon , ndikka on njaɓa kuuɗe leesɗe , jaŋkiniiɗe . Taa ndaare ko'e mon bana on marɓe anndal fuu .
45012017	To goɗɗo huuwi on kalluɗum , taa mbaate mo . Kakkile haa on kuuwa ko wooɗi haa yimɓe fuu .
45012018	Onon kam , tiine no mbaawɗon fuu haa on njooɗodo jam bee koomoy .
45012019	Soobiraaɓe am , to goɗɗo waɗi on aybe , taa mbaate mo , ammaa acce tikkere Allah waɗa ɗum , ngam deftere wi'i : " Min mi waatoto aybe , min mi hiitoto ɓe . Ni Jawmiraawo wi'i . "
45012020	Mbaɗe ko deftere wi'i on : " To konneejo ma weelaama , nyaamnu mo . To o ɗomɗi , yarnu mo . Bana ni cemtinirta mo . "
45012021	Taa accu halleende jaalo ma , ammaa jaalora nde bee mbooɗeeŋga .
45013001	Sey koomoy fuu ɗowtano marɓe laamu . Laamu woodaa , sonaa iwŋgu haa Allah . To woodi marɓe laamu , Allah bee hoore mum halfini ɓe ngu .
45013002	Koomoy tuurtani marɓe laamu , luuti umroore Allah , fooɗani hoore mum kiita .
45013003	Kuuwanɗo booɗɗum hulataa mawɓe , sey kuuwanɗo kalluɗum . To on ngiɗaa hulugo marɗo baawɗe , kuuwe ko fotti , nden kam o maŋgtan on .
45013004	Ngam marɗo laamu ɗon huuwana Allah , haa o walla on huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga . Ammaa to on kuuwi kalluɗum , doole on kula mo . Ngam o woodi baawɗe hiitaago , Allah darni mo ngam haa o timmina tikkere Allah dow huuwanɓe halleende .
45013005	Ngam maajum doole on ɗowtano mo , naa ngam tikkere Allah tan , ammaa ngam numooji ɓerɗe mon ɗon umra on ɗum .
45013006	To marɓe laamu ɗon kuuwa kuugal ngal , ɓe ɗon kuuwana Allah . Ngam maajum njoɓoton jomorgol boo .
45013007	Ndokke marɓe laamu ko haandani ɓe , njoɓe jomorgol , ndokke ko mawɓe lesdi umri on fuu . Teddine ɓe , ngam ɓe poti jaɓugo tedduŋgal .
45013008	To goɗɗo hokki on nyamaande , njoɓe mo nde . Huunde woore tan luttata dow mooɗon foroy bana nyamaande nde on timmintaa yoɓugo ɗum , ɗum umroore yiɗindirgo . Koomoy yiɗi keeddiɗɗum , ɗowtani tawreeta bee gooŋga .
45013009	On anndi umrooje : " Taa waɗ njeenu , taa mbar hoore , taa wujju , taa suuna . " Umrooje ɗe'e e goɗɗe fuu mooɓaama nder umroore woore : " Yiɗ keeddiɗɗiraawo ma bana hoore ma . "
45013010	Koomoy yiɗi keeddiɗɗum , huuwataa mo halleende . Ngam maajum mo yiɗi keeddiɗɗum , ɗon ɗowtano tawreeta fuu .
45013011	Kuuwe ɗum , ngam on anndi saa'i waɗi jonta haa on pina e ɗoyŋgol mon . Wakkati kisndam men ɓadi masin , ɓuri naane nde puɗɗunooɗen nuɗɗingo Jawmiraawo .
45013012	Jemma jeŋgi masin , nyalawma ɓadake . Ngam maajum en acca huuwugo kuuɗe nyiɓre , en naŋga balmi annoora ngam haa en njaalo nyiɓre .
45013013	Sey kuuwen ko fotti ngam en yimɓe nyalawma : walaa pijirle kalluɗe e wuykere , walaa daakaareeku e coɓki , en acca jokkirgol e kaajal boo .
45013014	Acce Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu laamano ngeendam mon fuu . Taa cuklane giɗaaɗi mon , ngam taa ɗi njaalo on .
45014001	Koo to goɗɗo woodi nuɗɗinki tampuki , njaɓe mo . Ammaa taa njokkire bee maako dow haala faamu .
45014002	Teema nuɗɗinki goɗɗo duŋganto mo nyaamugo kooɗume fuu . Ammaa mo nuɗɗinki mum tampi , ɗon nyaama haakooji tan .
45014003	Nyaamanɗo kooɗume fuu , taa yawo nyaamanɗo haakooji tan . Nyaamanɗo haakooji boo , taa fela oya , ngam Allah jaɓi ɓe ɗiɗo fuu .
45014004	Kadi on poti felugo maccuɗo goɗɗo feere na ? Sey jawmiiko tan wi'ata to kuugal maako fotti malla fottaay . Fakat o do''ataako , ngam Jawmiraawo mari baawɗe jogaago mo .
45014005	Goɗɗo ɗon wi'a nyalaade kaja ɓuran goɗɗe maŋgu . Goɗɗo boo ɗon wi'a nyalaaɗe fuu potan kal . Sey koomoy tabita nder faamu mum , tokko ɗum .
45014006	To goɗɗo ɗon ɓurna nyalaade woore dow goɗɗe , o ɗon waɗa ɗum ngam haa o teddina Jawmiraawo . Nyaamanɗo kooɗume fuu ɗon ɗaɓɓa teddingo Jawmiraawo , ɗon yetta Allah ngam nyaamdu . Bana non boo mo sali nyaamugo kuuje goɗɗe , ɗon ɗaɓɓa teddingo Jawmiraawo , ɗon yetta Allah ngam nyaamdu .
45014007	Walaa koo gooto meeɗen yeeɗata ngam hoore mum , walaa mo maayata ngam hoore mum boo .
45014008	To en ɗon ngeeɗa , ngam teddingo Jawmiraawo ngeeɗeten . To en maayi boo , ngam teddingo Jawmiraawo maayeten . Kaŋko o mari en koo nder ngeendam koo nder maayde .
45014009	Ngam Almasiihu maayi , yeeɗiti haa o laato Jawmiraawo maayɓe e yeeɗɓe fuu .
45014010	To non kam , koni pelata deerɗa ? Malla koni njawotooɗa deerɗa ? Enen fuu en daroyto yeeso kiita Allah haa o linya en .
45014011	Ngam deftere wi'i :
45014012	Saa'i maajum koomoy meeɗen jaabanto hoore mum yeeso Allah .
45014013	Too , en acca felindirgo . Ndikka on mbaɗa anniya taa on kuuwa ko nastinta deerɗiraawo goɗɗo nder hakke .
45014014	Mi ɗon tuugofi Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men . Ngam maajum anndumi fakat , walaa kooɗume laati coɓɗum bee hoore muuɗum . Sey to goɗɗo laari ɗum bana coɓɗum , nden kam ɗum laatanto mo coɓɗum .
45014015	To a naawni ɓernde deerɗa bee nyaamdu ma koonduye , nden kam a tokkaaki yiide . Almasiihu maayi ngam deerɗa . Ngam maajum taa nastin mo nder halkere bee nyaamdu ma .
45014016	Taa goɗɗo heɓa hallingo ko on ndaarata bana booɗɗum .
45014017	Laamu Allah kam , naa ɗum haala nyaamdu e njaram , ammaa ɗum haala gooŋgaaku e hoolaare bee Allah , e seyo ngo Ruuhu Ceniiɗo hokkata .
45014018	Koomoy huuwani Almasiihu bana ni , heɓan yerduye haa Allah e yimɓe fuu .
45014019	Ngam maajum sey en tiino haa en njooɗodo jam , en mballindira .
45014020	Taa on mbonna kuugal Allah ngam haala nyaamdu . Nyaamduuji fuu laaɓi , ammaa to goɗɗo seki dow nyaamdu mum , nden kam ɗum soɓnan mo .
45014021	Ndikka taa on nyaama kusel , taa on njara inaboojam , taa on mbaɗa kooɗume ko nastinta deerɗiraawo goɗɗo nder hakke .
45014022	Njoge ko on nuɗɗini nder haala ka'a , hakkunde mooɗon bee Allah . Booɗɗum to faamu goɗɗo tabiti , to numo ɓernde maako felaay mo .
45014023	Ammaa to goɗɗo seki dow nyaamdu mum , Allah hiitoto mo , ngam o daraaki dow nuɗɗinki . Ko goɗɗo waɗataa bee nuɗɗinki , ɗum laatoto aybe .
45015001	Enen sembiɗɓe nder nuɗɗinki , sey en mballa tampuɓe . Taa mbaɗen ko fottanta ko'e men .
45015002	Koomoy meeɗen ɗaɓɓa fottango keeddiɗɗum . Kanjum ɗum booɗɗum ngam haa jama'aare fuu sembiɗa nder nuɗɗinki .
45015003	Fakat , Almasiihu suklanaaki hoore mum . On anndi ko winda dow maako : " Kuudi huɗɓe ma yani dow am . "
45015004	Ko winda nder defte ceniiɗe , ɗum windaama ngam anndinki en , haa en ekkito munyal , ɓerɗe men nde'a . Bana ni tammunde men sembiɗirta .
45015005	Allah , dokkoowo en munyal e de'ere ɓernde , hokku on on njooɗodo hakkiilo wooto haa on tokko misaalu Almasiihu .
45015006	Nden kam on teddinan Allah , Baabiraawo Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , bee ɓernde woore e hunduko wooto .
45015007	Bana Almasiihu jaɓri on , bana non onon boo njaɓindire , ngam haa on teddina Allah .
45015008	Mi wi'i on : Almasiihu laati kuuwanoowo Yahuudu'en haa o waŋginana ɓe gooŋgaaku Allah , o hebbina ko Allah wi'no kaakiraaɓe maɓɓe aartuɓe .
45015009	Sey ummaatooje fuu ngetta Allah ngam enɗam maako , bana ko winda :
45015010	Fahin deftere wi'i :
45015011	Fahin :
45015012	Annabi Esaaya boo wi'i :
45015013	Mi ɗon toro Allah , tabitinɗo tammunde men , haa o hebbina ɓerɗe mon bee seyo e hoolaare fuu dow laawol nuɗɗinki , ngam haa tammunde mon sembiɗa bee baawɗe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo .
45015014	Onon deerɗam'en , mi anndi fakat on ɗon kuuwa ko fotti . On anndi muuyo Allah , on mbaawan waajindirgo boo .
45015015	Ammaa mi windani on haalaaji goɗɗi bee dartaare haa mi siftinora on ko annduɗon . Mi windi bana ni ngam daliila mo''ere nde Allah hokki yam .
45015016	Kaŋko o waɗi yam kuuwanoowo Yeesu Almasiihu haa ummaatooje ɗe laataaki Yahuudu'en . Mi ɗon huuwa kuugal bana ngal limanjo , mi ɗon waajina linjiila Allah , haa ummaatooje ɗe'e laato dokkal pottananŋgal mo , lii'otooŋgal bee Ruuhu Ceniiɗo .
45015017	Ngam daliila kawtal am bee Yeesu Almasiihu mantortoomi kuugal am yeeso Allah .
45015018	Mi walaa dartaare wolwugo haala feere , sey ko Almasiihu laatini bee kuugal am : O waɗi yimɓe nder ummaatooje fuu ɗowtano Allah , o huuwi bee bolle am e kuuɗe am ,
45015019	non boo bee kaayeefiiji mawɗi , e baawɗe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo . Ngam maajum keɓmi waajingo linjiila Almasiihu nder gure ɗuuɗɗe , diga Urusaliima haa yotti lesdi Illiriya .
45015020	Nder kuugal am ɗaɓɓumi foroy waajingo linjiila haa nokkuuje ɗe innde Almasiihu meeɗaay naneego , ngam taa mi maha dow caɓɓawal goɗɗo .
45015021	Bana ko winda :
45015022	Ngam daliila kuugal am nga'al mi heɓaay warugo haa mooɗon tawon .
45015023	Ammaa jonta kuugal am nder lesɗe ɗe'e timmi . Mi ɗon yenwa yi'ugo on diga duuɓi ɗuuɗɗi .
45015024	Mi tammi ɗum heɓoto jonta . Mi yiɗi yaalugo haa mooɗon , saa'i njahanmi Espaniya . On mbaawan wallugo yam yottaago ton , to mi seyorake kawtal bee mooɗon baakin seɗɗa .
45015025	Ammaa jonta mi yahan Urusaliima tawon , haa mi yahrana yimɓe Allah ton walliinde .
45015026	Masiihiŋko'en nder Makedoniya e Akaya mbaɗi anniya mooɓtugo dokkal ngam talaka'en nder jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe haa Urusaliima .
45015027	Ɓe mbaɗi ɗum bee anniya maɓɓe . Ammaa yimɓe Urusaliima poti jaɓugo ɗum boo , ngam ɓe mballiri ummaatooje goɗɗe hayruuji ɗi Ruuhu Allah hokki ɓe . Ngam maajum sey ummaatooje man mballira ɓe jawdi muuɗum'en boo .
45015028	To mi timmini kuugal ngal , waato to mi hokki ɓe dokkal ceede , nden kam mi yaalan haa mooɗon nder jahaaŋgal am haa Espaniya .
45015029	To mi wari haa mooɗon , mi anndi mi wardan bee barka Almasiihu fuu .
45015030	Deerɗam'en , mi ɗon toro on bee innde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , ngam daliila yiide boo nde Ruuhu Allah hokki on , haa on tiino do'anaago yam . Mballeeɗam toraago Allah ,
45015031	haa o hisnammi juuɗe heefeerɓe haa Urusaliima , haa kuugal am ngam yimɓe maako haa Urusaliima boo fottana ɓe .
45015032	Bana ni keɓranmi warugo haa mooɗon bee seyo , to Allah muuyi .
45015033	Allah , dokkoowo en jam , wonda bee mooɗon fuu . Aamiina !
45016001	Yoo , mi ɗon toro on ngam daliila Febe , deerɗiraawo men debbo , balloowo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe haa Keŋkereya .
45016002	Njaɓe mo bee innde Jawmiraawo bana no haandani Masiihiŋko'en . Mballe mo nder haaje maako fuu , ngam kaŋko o walli yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe , o walli yam boo .
45016003	Koofne Piriskilla e Akilas , huuwdooɓe bee am ngam Yeesu Almasiihu ,
45016004	foondiranɓe maayugo ngam hisnugo yoŋki am . Naa min feere am yettata ɓe , ammaa jama'aaje nuɗɗinɓe nder ummaatooje fuu .
45016005	Koofne Masiihiŋko'en mooɓtotooɓe haa saare maɓɓe boo .
45016006	Koofne Mariyama mo huuwani on bee tiinaare ɗuunde .
45016007	Koofne boo Andaronikus e Yuniyas , yimɓe lenyol am , haɓɓanooɓe bee am nder fursina . Ɓe tedduɓe caka waajooɓe linjiila , ɓe aarti yam nuɗɗingo Almasiihu boo .
45016008	Koofne Ampiliyatus , soobaajo am nder kawtal bee Jawmiraawo .
45016009	Koofne Urbanus , kuuwdoowo bee meeɗen ngam Almasiihu . Non boo Istakis , soobaajo am .
45016010	Koofne Apelles , tokkiiɗo Almasiihu bee gooŋgaaku . Koofne yimɓe saare Aristobul .
45016011	Koofne Hirodiyon mo lenyol am . Non boo yimɓe Jawmiraawo nder saare Narkis .
45016012	Koofne Tirifena e Tirifosa , deerɗiraaɓe men rewɓe , huuwanooɓe Jawmiraawo . Non boo Persis , deerɗiraawo debbo , giɗaaɗo men mo huuwani Jawmiraawo bee tiinaare ɗuunde .
45016013	Koofne Rufus , kuuwanoowo Jawmiraawo cuɓaaɗo . Non boo daada maako mo hakkilani yam foroy bana daada am .
45016014	Koofne Asiŋkirit e Felegon e Hermes e Patrobas e Hermas e deerɗiraaɓe wonduɓe bee maɓɓe fuu .
45016015	Koofne Filologus e Yuliya , non boo Neriyus e deerɗum debbo , e Olimpas e yimɓe Jawmiraawo wonduɓe bee maɓɓe fuu .
45016016	Koofnindire bee harlotirgo . Jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en fuu koofni on .
45016017	Deerɗam'en , mi ɗon toro on ɗuuɗɗum : Ndeente e waɗooɓe luural , wonnooɓe nuɗɗinki yimɓe , luutooɓe anndinol ngol njaɓɗon . Ndaaye ɓe .
45016018	Irin maɓɓe kuuwantaa Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men , sey deeɗi maɓɓe tan . Ɓe ɗon majjina sooyɓe anndal bee bolle ne'iiɗe e haalaaji belɗi .
45016019	Kootoy yimɓe anndi on ɗowtaniiɓe Jawmiraawo . Ngam maajum mi ɗon seyoro on . Ko ngiɗmi kam , on laato waawɓe huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga , ammaa on daayiiɓe halleende .
45016020	Allah , dokkoowo en jam , hokkan on jaalorgal timmuŋgal dow Sayɗaanu , neeɓataa . Mo''ere Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu wonda bee mooɗon fuu .
45016021	Timote , kuuwdoowo bee am , hoofni on , non boo Lukiyus e Yason e Sosipater , yimɓe lenyol am .
45016022	Min Tertiyus , binduɗo bataakewol ngo'ol , mi hoofni on ngam daliila kawtal men bee Jawmiraawo .
45016023	Gayus , beero am e beero nuɗɗinɓe haa ɗo fuu , hoofni on . Non boo Erastus , aynoowo ceede wuro , e Kawartus , deerɗiraawo men .
45016025	En ngettu Allah ! Kaŋko o mari baawɗe sembiɗingo on fodde linjiila ka ngaajinanmi . Linjiila ɗon wolwa haala Yeesu Almasiihu , ka ɗon waŋgina gooŋga Allah sirriiha . Gooŋga maajum suuɗino diga ɓooyma ,
45016026	ammaa jonta ka waŋginaama . Defte annabo'en ɗon ceedo ka . Bee umroore Allah duumiiɗo ka anndinaama yimɓe nder ummaatooje fuu , ngam haa ɓe nuɗɗina linjiila , ɓe ɗowtano Allah .
45016027	Allah feere muuɗum mari hikma . Tedduŋgal laatorano mo bee Yeesu Almasiihu haa foroy . Aamiina !
46001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , laatiiɗo nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu bee ewnaandu e muuyo Allah , min bee Sostenes , deerɗiraawo men ,
46001002	yahugo haa jama'aare yimɓe Allah wonɓe haa Korintu . Min ɗon koofna ewnaaɓe Allah fuu ton , laatiiɓe maral maako nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu , e seedotooɓe innde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo maɓɓe e Jawmiraawo amin :
46001003	Allah , Baabiraawo men , e Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men ndokka on mo''ere e jam .
46001004	Tum mi ɗon yetta Allah am ngam daliila mooɗon , ngam o waŋginani on mo''ere maako bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
46001005	Nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu keɓɗon hayruuji e dokke fuu . Wolde Allah fanti haa mooɗon , anndal mon ɗon ɓesdo yeeso yeeso .
46001006	Kubar Yeesu Almasiihu ɗon tabiti nder mooɗon .
46001007	Ngam maajum on keɓi dokke Allah fuu , on cooyataa koo gootal . On ɗon ndeena nyalaade baŋguki Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
46001008	Kaŋko o ɗon walla on ngam on tabita haa timmoode , ngam taa goɗɗo heɓa felugo on nder nyalaade kiita maako .
46001009	Allah bee hoore mum ewni on haa kawtal bee Ɓiɗɗo mum Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men . Allah oo woni koolniiɗo .
46001010	Deerɗam'en , mi ɗon toro on bee innde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu : Njooɗe on narruɓe ! Taa jokkirli laato hakkunde mooɗon , ammaa on narra dow hakkiilo wooto e anniya ngoota .
46001011	Deerɗam'en , mi nani haala jokkirli ummiiɗi caka mooɗon . Woɗɓe haa saare Kolowe , deerɗiraawo men debbo , ngecci yam ɗum .
46001012	Ndaa ko mi wi'ata : Oo ɗon wi'a : " Min mo Pol . " Oya ɗon wi'a : " Min mo Apollos . " Goɗɗo ɗon wi'a : " Min mo Piyer . " Goɗɗo feere boo ɗon wi'a : " Min mo Almasiihu . "
46001013	Kadi Almasiihu sendake geɓe feere feere na ? Kadi Pol oon maayi mbattudifa mooɗon dow leggal gaafaaŋgal na ? Malla on keɓi ngiiwam baptisma bee innde Pol ?
46001014	Mi ɗon yetta Allah ngam mi yiiwaay koo gooto mooɗon ngiiwam baptisma , sey Kirispus e Gayus .
46001015	Bana ni on keɓataa wi'ugo min mi laatini on pukara'en am bee ngiiwam man .
46001016	Asee , taa mi yejjita ! Mi yiiwi boo yimɓe saare Estefanas ngiiwam baptisma . Ammaa mi siftoraay goɗɗo feere .
46001017	Fakat , Almasiihu nelaay yam ngam haa mi yiiwa ngiiwam baptisma , ammaa ngam mi waajina linjiila . To mi ɗon waajina ka , mi jillindirtaa ka bee ko wi'ete anndal lugguŋgal , ngam taa mi meeriɗina maayde Almasiihu dow gaafaaŋgal .
46001018	Kubar maayde Almasiihu dow leggal gaafaaŋgal , halkanɓe ɗon ndaara ɗum bana faataare . Ammaa enen hisnaaɓe en anndi ɗum baawɗe Allah .
46001019	Deftere wi'i :
46001020	Kadi toy marɓe anndal lugguŋgal luttata , malla moodiɓɓe , malla wela-ɗemɗe'en anndugo waabaago ? Anndal duniyaaru ndu , Allah wartiri ɗum faataare .
46001021	Fakat , Allah marɗo anndal fuu hokki yimɓe laawol anndugo mo bee hakkiilo maɓɓe . Ammaa ɓe kuuwtiniraay ngo , ɓe cali anndugo mo . Ngam maajum Allah muuyi hisnugo yimɓe bee ko annduɓe duniyaaru mbi'ata faataare , waato bee kubaruwol maayde dow gaafaaŋgal go . Koomoy jaɓi ngol , hisan .
46001022	Yahuudu'en ɗon ɗaɓɓa kaayeefiiji , Yunaniŋko'en ɗon ɗaɓɓita anndal lugguŋgal .
46001023	Ammaa enen en ɗon ngeyna kubar Almasiihu ɓilaaɗo haa leggal gaafaaŋgal . Haa Yahuudu'en ɗum haala kalluka , haa ummaatooje goɗɗe boo ɗum faataare .
46001024	Ammaa ewnaaɓe Allah , koo ɓe Yahuudu'en koo ɓe ummaatooje goɗɗe , ɓe fuu ɓe paami no baawɗe Allah e hikma mum waŋgiri bee Almasiihu .
46001025	Ko Allah huuwata , ɗum nandi bee faataare , ammaa ɗum ɓuri anndal yimɓe fuu . Ɗum nandi bee tampere boo , ammaa ɗum ɓuri yimɓe fuu sembe .
46001026	Ndaare le ko'e mon , onon deerɗam'en , ewnaaɓe Allah . Haa gite yimɓe kam , marɓe anndal malla baawɗe malla tedduŋgal ɗuuɗaay caka mooɗon .
46001027	Ammaa Allah suɓi humaki'en , haa o semtina marɓe anndal . O suɓi tampuɓe , haa o semtina sembiɗɓe .
46001028	O suɓi leesɓe e yawniiɓe e meere'en nder duniyaaru , ngam haa o meeriɗina tedduɓe duniyaaru .
46001029	Bana ni walaa neɗɗo heɓata juraago yeeso Allah .
46001030	Ammaa onon , Allah ewni on haa kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu . Almasiihu laati anndal men iwŋgal haa Allah . Bee Almasiihu keɓruɗen yerduye Allah , en laati yimɓe Allah senaaɓe , en rimɓe e maayde boo .
46001031	Allah muuyi ɗum laato bana ko winda : " To goɗɗo yiɗi mantaago , sey o mantoro kuugal Allah . "
46002001	Deerɗam'en , saa'i ngarmi waŋginango on gooŋga Allah sirriiha , mi waɗaay ɗum bee bolle mawɗe e haala lugguka .
46002002	Wakkati mi ɗonno wondi bee mooɗon , mi sali anndugo kooɗume , sonaa Yeesu Almasiihu , maayɗo dow leggal gaafaaŋgal .
46002003	Mi wari haa mooɗon mi tampuɗo , diwnanɗo bee kulol ɗuuɗŋgol .
46002004	Anndinol am e waaju am laataaki bee baawal bolle fodde anndal yimɓe , ammaa bee baŋginki Ruuhu Allah e baawɗe mum ,
46002005	ngam taa nuɗɗinki mon daro dow anndal yimɓe , sey dow baawɗe Allah .
46002006	Bee non fuu mi ɗon waŋgina anndal lugguŋgal haa nuɗɗinɓe he'uɓe . Ammaa anndal maajum iwaay haa duniyaaru ndu , malla haa marɓe baawɗe nder jamanuuru ndu , ngam baawɗe maɓɓe ɗon majja .
46002007	Min kam mi waŋginan anndal Allah cuuɗiiŋgal . Diga Allah tagaayno duniyaaru , o annini hokkugo en tedduŋgal maako . Ammaa o suuɗino anniya ka .
46002008	Walaa koo gooto nder laamaniiɓe duniyaaru ndu annduno ka . To naa non , ɓe ɓilataano Jawmiraawo marɗo tedduŋgal Allah haa leggal gaafaaŋgal .
46002009	Ammaa ɗum laati bana ko winda :
46002010	Ammaa enen , Allah anndini en sirri mum bee Ruuhu ngu o hokki en . Ruuhu maajum ɗon wiɗito kooɗume fuu , koo nufayeeji Allah lugguɗi boo .
46002011	Walaa neɗɗo anndi ko goɗɗo numata , sey ruuhu goɗɗo man . Bana non boo walaa annduɗo numooji Allah , sey Ruuhu Allah tan .
46002012	Ammaa enen en keɓaay ruuhu duniyaaru ndu , en keɓi Ruuhu iwŋgu haa Allah . Ngam maajum en anndi ko Allah huuwani en .
46002013	Mi wolwataa haala maajum bee bolle ɗe anndal yimɓe anndini yam . Ammaa mi ɗon wolwa ko Ruuhu Allah anndintammi , haa mi faamtina heɓɓe Ruuhu kuuje Ruuhu man .
46002014	Koomoy tokki hakkiilo mum , ɗon salo ko Ruuhu Allah waŋginta . O ɗon laara ɗum bana faataare . O faamataa ɗum sam , ngam ɗum faamataako , sey bee ballal Ruuhu tan .
46002015	Keɓɗo Ruuhu Allah ɗon faama kooɗume fuu , ammaa kaŋko bee hoore maako , walaa paamanɗo mo .
46002016	Ngam deftere ɗon wi'a : " Moy anndi numooji Jawmiraawo ? Moy laati dawroowo maako ? " Ammaa enen en ngoodi Ruuhu Almasiihu .
46003001	Deerɗam'en , mi waawaay wolwango on bana no mbolwiranmi heɓɓe Ruuhu Allah . Doole mi wolwana on bana tokkiiɓe anndal muuɗum'en , bana ɓikkoy pamaroy nder nuɗɗinki Almasiihu .
46003002	Ngam maajum ndokkumi on kosam , naa nyaamdu sembindu , ngam on ke'aayno ndu . Jonta boo on ke'aay ndu ,
46003003	ngam on ɗon tokko al'aada duniyaaru . On ɗon kaajindira , on ɗon njokkira . To non kam , on tokkaaki al'aada duniyaaru bana yimɓe woɗɓe na ?
46003004	To goɗɗo wi'i : " Min mo Pol " , goɗɗo feere boo : " Min mo Apollos " , naa ɗum al'aada yimɓe na ?
46003005	Kadi moy woni Apollos ? Moy woni Pol ? Min laataaki mawɓe , min huuwanooɓe Allah , wallooɓe on haa on nuɗɗina mo . Allah halfini koomoy amin kuugal mum .
46003006	Min mi aawi , Apollos yarni ko fuɗi , ammaa Allah mawnini ɗum .
46003007	Aawoowo e jarnoowo ɗiɗo fuu laataaki kooɗume , sey Allah mawninoowo tan mari tedduŋgal .
46003008	Walaa ko sendindirta aawoowo bee jarnoowo , ngam Allah warjoto koomoy fodde kuugal mum .
46003009	Minin min hawtiɗɗiraaɓe , huuwanooɓe Allah , onon boo on ngesa maako .
46003010	Min mi huuwtiniri dokkal ngal Allah mo''ani yam , bana mahoowo baawɗo mballinmi caɓɓawal . Woɗɓe ɗon maha dow maagal . Ammaa sey koomoy maɓɓe hakkila no o mahrata .
46003011	Caɓɓawal ɗon tabiti , ɗum Yeesu Almasiihu . Walaa baawanɗo wallingo caɓɓawal feere .
46003012	Woɗɓe ɗon maha dow maagal bee kaŋgeeri malla cardi malla kaa'e marɗe saman , woɗɓe boo bee leɗɗe malla huɗo malla ?ombe .
46003013	Ammaa nyalaade darŋgal kiita waŋginan no kuugal koomoy wa'i , ngam yiite sendindiran ngal .
46003014	To yiite nyaamaay kuugal goɗɗo , nden kam o heɓan mbarjaari maako .
46003015	To yiite nyaami ngal , nden kam o walaa mbarjaari . Kaŋko o hisan , ammaa bee dakkerr , bana caaliiɗo nder yiite .
46003016	Onon on haykaliiru Allah , Ruuhu Allah ɗon jooɗi nder mooɗon . On anndaa ɗum na ?
46003017	To goɗɗo wonni haykaliiru Allah , Allah halkan mo . Ngam haykaliiru Allah seniindu , onon bee ko'e mon on laati haykaliiru man .
46003018	Taa goɗɗo esta hoore mum . To goɗɗo mooɗon numi o marɗo anndal fodde gikku duniyaaru ndu , sey o laato paataaɗo tawon haa o heɓa anndal fakat .
46003019	Ngam ko duniyaaru wi'ata anndal lugguŋgal , ɗum faataare haa Allah . Deftere wi'i : " Allah naŋgan marɓe anndal nder tuuforgol dabareeji maɓɓe . "
46003020	Haa pellel feere boo : " Jawmiraawo anndi numooji marɓe anndal , ɗi meere . "
46003021	Ngam maajum taa goɗɗo mantoro yimɓe . Fakat , kooɗume fuu , onon mari .
46003022	Koo Pol koo Apollos koo Piyer , koo duniyaaru , koo ngeendam koo maayde , koo kuuje jontaaje koo kuuje garanɗe , kooɗume fuu laatani on .
46003023	Ammaa onon , Almasiihu mari on . Almasiihu boo , Allah mari mo .
46004001	Too , ndaare min bana huuwanooɓe Allah , bana wakiili'en , halfinaaɓe sirriiji Allah .
46004002	Sey wakiiliijo laato koolaaɗo , kanjum tan ɗaɓɓete haa maako .
46004003	Mi koolaaɗo na ? Onon on mbaawataa linyugo ɗum . Walaa kiita yimɓe foti linyugo ɗum . Koo min bee hoore am boo mi waawataa ɗum .
46004004	Ɓernde am felaay yam , ammaa bee non fuu gooŋgaaku am tabitaay tawon . Jawmiraawo feere mum woni kiitoowo yam .
46004005	Ngam maajum taa kiite goɗɗo diga saa'i man siwa . Munye haa Jawmiraawo wara . Kaŋko o wurtinan kuuje cuuɗiiɗe nder nyiɓre , o waŋginan numooji yimɓe nyukkiiɗi . Saa'i maajum koomoy heɓan yettoore mum haa Allah bana no fotti .
46004006	Deerɗam'en , ngam daliila mooɗon mbi'mi haala ka'a fuu dow am e dow Apollos . Mi yiɗi on ndaara haa amin ko saawi nder wolde nde'e : " Taa goɗɗo ?aɓɓo keerol umrooje bindaaɗe . " Taa goɗɗo mooɗon mantoro jaŋginoowo oo , yawo oya .
46004007	Moy ɓurnu ma dow woɗɓe ? Ko marɗa fuu , na Allah hokku ma ɗum na ? To ɗum dokkal kam , koni a ɗon juro bee maajum ?
46004008	Ammaa onon on kaari , timmi . On riskuɓe , on keɓi laamu . Minin min keɓaay tawon . Booɗɗum to on laamakeno fakat , nden kam minin boo min keɓanno laamu bee mooɗon .
46004009	Ammaa minin nelaaɓe , mi tammi Allah laatini min ɓaawo'en . Min laati bana hiitaaɓe mbareego haa babal pijirle , bana fijirde laareteende haa duniyaaru fuu , haa malaa'ika'en e yimɓe .
46004010	Minin min faataaɓe ngam daliila Almasiihu , ammaa onon on marɓe anndal nder kawtal bee maako . Minin min tampuɓe , ammaa onon on sembiɗɓe . Minin min yawaaɓe , ammaa onon on teddinaaɓe .
46004011	Haa warugo hande min ɗon bee weelo e ɗomka , min ɓorniiɓe limce kiiɗɗe , min ɓoccaaɓe , min ɗon ngiilo kootoy ngam min ngalaa saare .
46004012	Min ɗon kuuwa bee tiinaare haa min nyaamna ko'e amin . To goɗɗo naali min , min mbarkiɗina mo . To goɗɗo toonyake min , min munyana mo .
46004013	To goɗɗo huɗi min , min njaabo mo bolle booɗɗe . Min laati bana mbuuri duniyaaru fuu , bana nyidduɗum ko yimɓe ngudinta ɗum , haa jonta .
46004014	Mi windanaay on ɗum haa mi semtina on . Mi yiɗi eltugo on , ngam on ɓikkoy am ngiɗaakoy .
46004015	Koo to on keɓi anndinooɓe ujine sappo , ɗowooɓe on haa laawol Almasiihu , on ngoodi baaba gooto tan . Saa'i ngaddanmi on linjiila , min oon laati baaba mon hedi ngeendam mon nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
46004016	Ngam maajum mi ɗon toro on : Laate bana am .
46004017	Mi neli Timote haa mooɗon boo . Kaŋko woni ɓiɗɗo am giɗaaɗo , koolaaɗo nder kawtal bee Jawmiraawo . O siftinoran on umrooje ɗe tokkotoomi bana Masiihiŋkeejo , ɗe anndinanmi kootoy caka nuɗɗinɓe boo .
46004018	Woɗɓe mon mawniti ngam ɓe tammi mi warataa haa mooɗon .
46004019	Ammaa to Jawmiraawo muuyi , mi waran law . Mi yiɗi anndugo mawnitiiɓe ɓe'e , naa bolle maɓɓe , sey baawal maɓɓe .
46004020	Ngam laamu Allah waŋgataa bee bolle , sey bee baawɗe .
46004021	Ɗume ngiɗɗon ? Mi wara haa mooɗon bee ɓoccol na ? Malla bee yiide e ɓernde ɗelemnde ?
46005001	Ndaa mi nani njeenu ɗon haa mooɗon . Irin njeenu man tawataake koo haa heefeerɓe . Goɗɗo ɗon wonda bee debbo baaba mum .
46005002	Bee maajum fuu on ɗon keewi mawnitaare . Kayto ! Ndikka ɓerɗe mon keewa mettamɓeram , on ngurtina gorko oo caka mooɗon .
46005003	To min kam , mi ta''i haala man . Ɓandu am daayi on , ammaa ruuhu am ɗon wondi bee mooɗon . Bee innde Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men kiitoriimi kuuwɗo cemtiniiɗum ɗu'um bana ni'i : To on mooɓtake , ruuhu am boo ɗon wondi bee mooɗon bee baawɗe Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men ,
46005004	
46005005	sey on lii'o gorko oo haa juŋŋgo Sayɗaanu ngam haa ɓandu maako halka , ammaa ruuhu maako hisa nyalaade Jawmiraawo waɗata kiita .
46005006	On ngalaa daliila juraago sam . On anndi geccawol ngo'ol : " Ufnirɗum seɗɗa ufnan kuroori njiiɓaandi fuu . "
46005007	Itte le ufnirɗum kiiɗɗum , waato hakkeeji mon , ngam haa on laato jiiɓaaɗum kesum ɗum ufnaaka . Kanjum laatiiɗon boo , ngam Almasiihu , jawgel Paska meeɗen , hirsaama .
46005008	Ngam maajum en mbaɗa juulde Paska , naa bee ufnirɗum kiiɗɗum ɗum hakkeeji e halleende , ammaa bee tamseere nde ufnaaka , waato tamseere laaɓeeŋga e gooŋga .
46005009	Nder bataakewol am aartuŋgol mi windani on taa on kawta bee waɗooɓe njeenu .
46005010	Fakat , mi numaay dow jeenooɓe caka yimɓe duniyaaru ndu , malla suunaaɓe malla wuyɓe malla tokkiiɓe labbi . To nonnon kam , doole on ngurto duniyaaru .
46005011	Ko ngiɗmi wi'ugo , ndaa ɗum : Taa kawte bee goɗɗo marɗo innde Masiihiŋkeejo ammaa o jeenoowo malla o cuunaaɗo ceede malla o tokkotooɗo labbi malla o baɗoowo tufle malla o guykoowo malla o gujjo . Taa nyaamde bee irin goɗɗo oo .
46005012	Walaa ko yaali yam bee hiitaago yimɓe ɓe laataaki nuɗɗinɓe Yeesu . Allah bee hoore mum hiitoto ɓe . Ammaa on yowanaaɓe hiitaago wonɓe nder mooɓtorde mon . Ngam deftere wi'i : " Ngurtine kalluɗo caka mooɗon . "
46005013	
46006001	To goɗɗo mon woodi wullaandu dow deerɗiraawo feere , o yahri ndu yeeso hiitooɓe ɓe nuɗɗinaay Jawmiraawo . Kanjum ɗum fottaay . Koni o ɗaɓɓataa kiita haa yimɓe Allah ?
46006002	On anndi saa'i waran haa yimɓe Allah kiito duniyaaru fuu . Nde non kam , on mbaawataa hiitaago kuuje pamare na ?
46006003	On ngejjiti na ? Saa'i maajum en kiitoto koo malaa'ika'en boo , sakko haala duniyaaru .
46006004	Ammaa onon , to on ngoodi jokkirli dow kuuje duniyaaru , on ɗon ɗaɓɓa kiita haa yimɓe ɓe ngalaa tedduŋgal nder jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe .
46006005	Mi wi'i ɗum haa on cemta . Kadi walaa marɗo hakkiilo koo gooto caka mooɗon haa o ta''a jokkirgol hakkunde deerɗiraaɓe na ?
46006006	Koni deerɗiraawo yahrata wullaandu dow deerɗum yeeso hiitooɓe ɓe ngalaa nuɗɗinki ?
46006007	Fakat on ɗon ngullotira , kanjum ɗum ɗon aybina on on fuu . Ngam ɗume on munyantaa aybe ? Ngam ɗume on munyantaa jaɓteego ?
46006008	Ammaa onon on ɗon mbaɗa aybe , on ɗon njaɓta . Asee , hakkunde deerɗiraaɓe irin ɗu'um laatoto !
46006009	On anndi halluɓe keɓataa barkaaji laamu Allah . Taa este ko'e mon ! Daakaaje e tokkiiɓe labbi e jeenooɓe e luuɗu'en ,
46006010	non boo wuyɓe e suunaaɓe riba e wuykooɓe e waɗooɓe tufle e jaɓtooɓe , ɓe fuu ɓe ngi'ataa laamu Allah .
46006011	Woɗɓe mooɗon laatino bana non . Ammaa jonta hakkeeji mon lootaama , on laati yimɓe Allah senaaɓe , on keɓi yerduye maako bee innde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu e Ruuhu Allah men .
46006012	Teema woɗɓe mon mbi'an : " Kooɗume fuu daganake yam . " Gooŋga , ammaa naa kuuje fuu nafata on . Min , kuuje fuu ndaganake yam . Ammaa sey mi hakkila ngam taa mi laato maccuɗo kuuje man .
46006013	On ɗon mbi'a boo : " Nyaamdu ɗon ngam reedu , reedu boo ngam nyaamdu . " Gooŋga , ammaa Allah halkan ɗiɗi fuu . Ɓandu neɗɗo laataaki ngam waɗugo njeenu , sey ngam huuwango Jawmiraawo , kaŋko woni Jawmu ɓalli meeɗen boo .
46006014	Allah ummitini Jawmiraawo men diga maayde , bana non o ummitiniran en , enen boo , bee baawɗe maako .
46006015	On anndi ɓalli mon laati terɗe haa ɓandu Almasiihu . Kadi mi hoo'a terde Almasiihu , mi waɗa nde terde jeenoowo na ? Waɗataako !
46006016	Naa ɗakkotirɗo bee jeenoowo laati ɓandu wooru bee maako na ? Kadi on anndaa ɗum na ? Deftere wi'i : " Ɓe ɗiɗo fuu ɓe laatoto ɓandu wooru . "
46006017	Ammaa ɗakkotirɗo bee Jawmiraawo laatoto Ruuhu ngootu bee maako .
46006018	Ndaaye haala njeenu fuu . Hakkeeji goɗɗi fuu ɗi neɗɗo huuwata , ɗi meemataa ɓandu maako . Ammaa baɗanɗo njeenu ɗon waɗa hakke dow ɓandu mum .
46006019	Taa ngejjite : Ɓandu koomoy mooɗon woni haykaliiru Ruuhu Ceniiɗo . Allah hokki on Ruuhu mum njooɗiiŋgu nder mooɗon jonta . Ngam maajum on maraay ko'e mon .
46006020	Allah soodi on bee saman . Ngam maajum teddine mo bee ɓalli mon .
46007001	Yoo , haa mi jaabo ?amɗe ɗe mbinduɗon nder bataakewol mon : To gorko te'aay sam , kanjum ɓuri wooɗugo .
46007002	Ammaa ngam taa on laato daakaaje , ndikka koomoy te'a , debbo boo , koomoy laato te'aaɗo .
46007003	Gorko wonda bee debbo mum bana no haandi , debbo boo humtana gorum haaje .
46007004	Debbo maraay ɓandu mum , ndu laatani goriiko . Non boo gorko maraay ɓandu mum , ndu laatani debbo maako .
46007005	Taa calotire baaldal , sonaa to on narri dow maajum ngam wakkati seɗɗa , haa keɓon de'ere ngam do'aago . Ammaa ɓaawoɗon kawte fahin , ngam taa Sayɗaanu heɓa estugo on ngam sooynde naŋgtaare mon .
46007006	Mi wi'aay ɗum bana umroore , ammaa bana duŋgaye .
46007007	Min kam mi ɓuri yiɗugo yimɓe fuu njooɗo bana am . Ammaa Allah hokki koomoy dokkal mum , oo bana ni , oya bana non .
46007008	Mi ɗon wi'a worɓe ɓe meeɗaay ɓaŋgugo e rewɓe ɓe meeɗaay ɓaŋgeego e rewɓe yurumɓe : Ndikka on njooɗo bana am .
46007009	Ammaa to on mbaawaay naŋgtaago , sey on te'a . Ndikka te'ugo dow suuno ɓilla on .
46007010	Ammaa te'ɓe e te'aaɓe , mi ɗon hokka ɓe umroore , nde iwaay haa am , ammaa haa Jawmiraawo : Taa debbo sendira bee gorum .
46007011	Ammaa to a sendiri bee maako , sey o jooɗo bilaa gorko , malla o narra bee goriiko fahin . Gorko boo , taa seera debbo mum .
46007012	Ammaa luttuɓe , mi ɗon wi'a ɓe , min , naa Jawmiraawo : To gorko Masiihiŋkeejo woodi debbo mo nuɗɗinaay , debbo boo yerdake jooɗodaago bee maako , nden kam taa o seera mo .
46007013	Nonnon boo Masiihiŋkeejo debbo mo gorum nuɗɗinaay . To gorko yerdake jooɗodaago bee maako , taa debbo sendira bee maako .
46007014	Debbo nuɗɗinɗo ɗon sena gorum mo nuɗɗinaay . Non boo gorko nuɗɗinɗo ɗon sena debbo mum mo nuɗɗinaay . To naa non , ɓikkoy mon boo koy coɓkoy , ammaa jonta koy cenaakoy .
46007015	Ammaa to cooyɗo nuɗɗinki yiɗi sendirgo bee nuɗɗinɗo , njoofe mo . Nden kam Masiihiŋkeejo gorko malla debbo rimɗi e teegal mum . Allah ewni on haa on njooɗo bee de'ere .
46007016	An debbo , a waawan hisnugo gorko ma na ? Malla an gorko , a waawan hisnugo debbo ma na ? Fakat on anndaa .
46007017	Sey koomoy tokko jooɗaago bana Allah heerori mo . O jooɗo bana no o wa'i nde Allah ewno mo . Bana ni umranmi nder jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en fuu .
46007018	To goɗɗo laatake juulniiɗo saa'i Allah ewno mo , taa o ɗaɓɓita ittugo batte juulnolfe . To goɗɗo juulnaaki saa'i Allah ewno mo , taa o juulno .
46007019	Ngam juulnol e sooynde juulnol ɗiɗi fuu nafataa kooɗume , sey ɗowtanaago umrooje Allah tan nafata goɗɗo .
46007020	Sey koomoy jooɗo bana no o wa'i nde Allah ewno mo .
46007021	To a maccuɗo saa'i Allah ewno ma , taa saklana ɗum . Ammaa to a heɓi baawɗe rimɗugo , naftora ɗum .
46007022	Maccuɗo mo Allah ewni ɗum , laati dimo ngam Jawmiraawo mari mo . Bana non boo dimo mo Jawmiraawo ewni ɗum , laati maccuɗo Jawmiraawo .
46007023	Jawmiraawo sootti on bee saman . Ngam maajum taa ngartire ko'e mon maccuɓe yimɓe .
46007024	Deerɗam'en , sey koomoy mooɗon jooɗo yeeso Allah bana no o wa'i nde Allah ewno mo .
46007025	Too , dow yimɓe ɓe meeɗaay ɓaŋgugo , mi walaa umroore Jawmiraawo . Ammaa mi wi'an ko numanmi . Jawmiraawo mo''ani yam , hokki yam faamu , laatini yam koolniiɗo .
46007026	Ndaa ko mi numi : To goɗɗo meeɗaay ɓaŋgugo , ɗum ɓuran wooɗugo ngam daliila ɓillaaje jontaaje .
46007027	To a woodi debbo , taa ɗaɓɓu seerugo mo . To a walaa debbo , taa ɗaɓɓu te'ugo .
46007028	Ammaa to a te'i , a waɗaay aybe . Paanyo boo , to te'aama , waɗaay aybe . Ammaa mi yiɗi hisnugo on cakle laatantooɗe te'ɓe e te'aaɓe .
46007029	Deerɗam'en , ndaa ko ngiɗmi anndingo on : Wakkati rammiti . Diga jonta , marɓe rewɓe laato bana ɓe ngalaa .
46007030	Woyanɓe , taa mettamɓeram jaalo ɓe . Seyotooɓe , taa seyo jaalo ɓe . Soodanɓe kuuje ndaara ɗe bana ɓe maraay ɗe .
46007031	Naftortooɓe duniyaaru boo , taa cuklano ndu bee ɓerɗe muuɗum'en fuu . Ngam duniyaaru bana ndu wa'i jonta ni , ndu jinnan .
46007032	Mi yiɗi on laato rimɓe e saklere fuu . Mo te'aay ɗon suklano kuugal Jawmiraawo , haa fottana Jawmiraawo .
46007033	Ammaa te'ɗo ɗon suklano kuuje duniyaaru , haa fottana debbo mum .
46007034	Bana ni ɓernde maako sendake ɗiɗi . Non boo debbo jurumɗo malla ceeraaɗo malla paanyo mo meeɗaay te'eego . O ɗon suklano kuugal Jawmiraawo , haa o laato cenaaɗo bee ɓandu e ruuhu fuu . Ammaa te'aaɗo ɗon suklano kuuje duniyaaru , haa fottana gorum .
46007035	Mi ɗon wi'a ɗum ngam mi yiɗi wallugo on . Mi ɗaɓɓataa haɗugo on . Mi yiɗi on kuuwa ko fotti , on kuuwana Jawmiraawo bee ɓernde woore .
46007036	Teema goɗɗo narran bee muuyaaɗo mum taa ɓe ɓaŋga . Nden o numti accugo mo non fottaay , ngam o heewti , suuno hoo'ugo mo boo ɗon ɓesdo . To non kam , sey ɓe ɓaŋga , naa ɗum aybe .
46007037	Ammaa to gikku maako tabiti , walaa ko dooli mo , suuno boo ɓillaay mo , nden kam o jogito anniya maako , taa o ɓaŋga muuyaaɗo maako .
46007038	Ɓaŋɗo muuyaaɗo mum huuwi booɗɗum , ammaa mo ɓaŋgaay mo huuwi ko ɓuri wooɗugo .
46007039	Debbo te'aaɗo laati kaɓɓaaɗo yaake goriiko ɗon bee yoŋki . Ammaa to gorko maayi , debbo rimɗi . To o yiɗi , o jaɓan te'eego , ammaa sey o teera bee gorko Masiihiŋkeejo .
46007040	Ammaa seyo maako ɓuran mawnugo to o jooɗake bilaa gorko . Kanjum woni numo am . Ammaa mi tammi min boo mi woodi Ruuhu Allah .
46008001	Too , en linya haala kusel iwŋgel e dabbaaji kirsaaɗi ngam labbi . On ɗon mbi'a : " En fuu en mari anndal . " Gooŋga kam , ammaa anndal bana nga'al laatinan goɗɗo mawnitiiɗo . Yiide tan sembiɗinta jama'aare Masiihiŋko'en .
46008002	To goɗɗo tammake o mari anndal , nden kam o heɓaay anndal gooŋgawal tawon .
46008003	Ammaa to goɗɗo yiɗi Allah , nden kam Allah anndi mo .
46008004	Goɗɗo nyaaman kusel kirsaaŋgel ngam labbi na ? En anndi lawru naa ɗum huunde gooŋga nder duniyaaru , walaa ɗowanteeɗo feere , sey Allah gooto .
46008005	Woodi ko yimɓe mbi'ata ɗowanteeɓe haa asama e dow lesdi , fakat ɓe ɗon teddina ɗowanteeɓe e jawmiraaɓe ɗuuɗɓe .
46008006	Bee non fuu , enen en ngoodi Allah gooto tan , Baabiraawo tagɗo kuuje fuu , haa maako lorotooɗen . Non boo Jawmiraawo gooto tan , Yeesu Almasiihu . Bee maako kuuje fuu tagra , bee maako keɓruɗen ngeendam kesam boo .
46008007	Ammaa naa yimɓe fuu anndi ɗum . Woɗɓe mboowi haala labbi . To ɓe nyaami kusel go , ɓe ndaaran ngel bana kirsaaŋgel ngam labbi fakat . Ngam daliila numooji ɓerɗe maɓɓe tampuɗi , ɓe kulan soɓnugo ko'e maɓɓe bee nyaamugo ngel .
46008008	Fakat , nyaamdu mo''intaa en haa Allah . To en nyaamaay kuuje goɗɗe , tedduŋgal men ustataako . To en nyaami ɗe , tedduŋgal men ɓesdataako .
46008009	Ammaa kakkile , ngam taa ndimu mooɗon nastina tampuɓe nder hakke .
46008010	Teema a mari ko an a wi'ata anndal , a nasti suudu lawru . Goɗɗo tampuɗo yi'i ma ton saa'i a ɗon nyaama . Ɗum sembiɗinan mo haa o nyaama kaŋko boo , o luuta numo ɓernde maako .
46008011	Tampuɗo oo , deerɗiraawo ma mo Almasiihu maayi ngam muuɗum , halkan ngam daliila anndal ma .
46008012	To non on mbaɗi hakke dow deerɗiraaɓe mon , on naawni numooji ɓerɗe maɓɓe tampuɗe , nden kam on mbaɗi hakke dow Almasiihu .
46008013	Ngam maajum , to nyaamdu waawi nastingo deerɗam nder hakke , mi meetataa nyaamugo kusel sam . Ngam mi yiɗaa deerɗam majja .
46009001	Naa mi dimo na ? Naa mi nelaaɗo na ? Naa mi gi'ɗo Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men na ? Onon boo , naa on nafuda kuugal am ngam Jawmiraawo na ?
46009002	Koo to woɗɓe njaɓaay yam bana nelaaɗo , haa mooɗon kam mi nelaaɗo fakat . On laati Masiihiŋko'en , kanjum woni seedamku no mi nelaaɗo .
46009003	Woɗɓe ɗon pelammi . Ndaa ko mi jaaboto ɓe :
46009004	Woodi ko haɗi yam jaɓugo nyaamdu e njaram ngam kuugal am na ?
46009005	Woodi ko haɗi yam yahdugo bee debbo Masiihiŋkeejo nder jahaale am bana nelaaɓe woɗɓe e deerɗiraaɓe Jawmiraawo e Piyer mbaɗata na ?
46009006	Sey min e Barnabas tan kuuwata ngam nguure amin na ?
46009007	Soojeejo moy nyaamnata hoore mum ? Moy juboto inabooje , o nyaamataa ɓiɓɓe maaje ? Moy durata tokkere dabbaaji , o yarataa kosam maaje ?
46009008	Kanjum naa ɗum ɗabiya yimɓe tan , ɗum umroore Allah boo .
46009009	Ndaa ko winda nder tawreeta Muusa : " Taa waɗan ngaari corɓoori sabakaare . " Kadi Allah ɗon suklano ngaari na ?
46009010	O wi'aay ɗum ngam daliila amin na ? Fakat ɗum windaama ngam daliila amin . Sey aawoowo gawri e codoowo ndi kuuwa dow tammunde heɓugo geɗal maɓɓe haa maari .
46009011	Min aawi barkaaji Ruuhu nder mooɗon . Kadi to min codi hayruuji duniyaaru haa mooɗon , ɗum huunde mawnde na ?
46009012	To walaa ko haɗata woɗɓe jaɓugo ɗum haa mooɗon , minin min ɓurataa ɓe na ?
46009013	On anndi booɗɗum , huuwooɓe kuuɗe ceniiɗe keɓan nguure muuɗum'en nder haykaliiru , lii'otooɓe kirseteeɗi dow hirsirde boo keɓan geɗal muuɗum'en haa kirseteeɗi man .
46009014	Bana non boo waajooɓe linjiila . Jawmiraawo umri ɓe nguura dow kuugal waaju maɓɓe .
46009015	Ammaa min mi meeɗaay naftoraago baawɗe ɗe'e . Mi windaay ɗum boo ngam haa mi ɗaɓɓa baawɗe man jonta . Ndikka mi maaya ! Walaa mo sottinta juro ngo haa am .
46009016	To mi ɗon waajina linjiila , mi fotaay mantaago . Doole mi waajina ka . Bone ɗon dow am to mi waɗaay ɗum .
46009017	To mi huuwi kuugal am bee muuyo ɓernde am , mi tammoto heɓugo mbarjaari . Ammaa jonta mi ɗon huuwa ngal dow umroore , bana wakiilaaku ngu Allah halfini yam .
46009018	Ɗume mbarjaari am kadi ? Ndaa ndi : Mi ɗon waajina linjiila caahu , mi ɗaɓɓaay ko marmi baawɗe heɓugo .
46009019	Mi dimo , walaa neɗɗo mari yam . Ammaa mi waɗi hoore am maccuɗo yimɓe fuu ngam haa mi heɓana Almasiihu ɗuuɗɓe maɓɓe .
46009020	To mi ɗon huuwa caka Yahuudu'en , mi laatoto bana Yahuuduujo , haa mi heɓa Yahuudu'en . Min bee hoore am mi laataaki jowaaɗo tawreeta . Ammaa to mi ɗon wondi bee ɗowtantooɓe tawreeta , min boo mi ɗowtanto ka , haa mi heɓa ɓe .
46009021	Bana non boo to mi ɗon wondi bee yimɓe ɓe anndaa tawreeta , mi laatoto bana maɓɓe . Mi wi'aay mi ɗowtantaako umroore Allah , ngam fakat mi ɗon tokko umroore Almasiihu .
46009022	To mi ɗon wondi bee nuɗɗinɓe tampuɓe , mi laatanto ɓe bana min boo mi tampuɗo , haa mi heɓa ɓe . Waato mi laatanto kooɓeye fuu bana ɓe mba'i , haa mi hisna woɗɓe maɓɓe koonoy fuu .
46009023	Ɗum fuu mi ɗon huuwa ɗum ngam linjiila , haa mi heɓa geɗal barkaaji maaka .
46009024	On anndi ɗuuɗɓe ndoggan nder daɗadaɗa , ammaa gooto maɓɓe tan heɓan saman jaalorgal . Ngam maajum ndogge bee sembe haa keɓon saman oo .
46009025	Giɗɗo daɗugo fuu eltan hoore mum bee caatal , ngam haa o heɓa meetaleewol haakooji ɗaylanɗi . Ammaa enen en ɗon tammo heɓugo meetaleewol ngol jinnataa .
46009026	Ngam maajum mi ɗon tiito timmitirde daɗadaɗa . Mi laati bana lukkoowo mo lukkataa meere nder hendu .
46009027	Mi ɗon elta ɓandu am bee caatal haa mi ɗowtina ndu . Ngam min ewniiɗo woɗɓe haa daɗadaɗa mi yiɗaa wurtineego bana mo he'aay .
46010001	Onon deerɗam'en , mi yiɗi on ciftora ko heɓi kaakaaji men yahdunooɓe bee Muusa . Ɓe fuu ɓe tokki laawol maɓɓe les ɗowdi ruulde . Ɓe fuu ɓe eeri maayo Maaliya jam .
46010002	Nder ruulde e nder maayo ɓe ngiiwaama ngiiwam baptisma bana tokkiiɓe Muusa .
46010003	Ɓe fuu ɓe nyaami nyaamdu wooru iwndu haa asama .
46010004	Ɓe fuu ɓe njari njaram ngootam ɗam Allah hokki ɓe . Ɓe njari haa tapaare Ruuhu nde yahdi bee maɓɓe , tapaare maajum ɗum Almasiihu .
46010005	Bee non fuu , Allah yerdaaki ɓurna maɓɓe , maayni ɓe nder ladde .
46010006	Kuuje ɗe'e laati ngam reentingo en , ngam taa en tokko suunooji kalluɗi bana ɓeya tokkori .
46010007	Taa cujidane labbi bana woɗɓe maɓɓe . Deftere wi'i dow maɓɓe : " Yimɓe njooɗi , ɗon nyaama , ɗon njara . Nden ɓe ummi haa ɓe pija . "
46010008	Taa mbaɗe njeenu bana woɗɓe maɓɓe , ujine noogas e tato maayi nder nyalaade woore .
46010009	Taa poonde munyal Jawmiraawo bana woɗɓe maɓɓe , kamɓe ɓe maayi ngam boɗɗe ngati ɓe .
46010010	Taa ngurŋgurte dow Jawmiraawo bana woɗɓe maɓɓe , malaa'ikaajo maayde halki ɓe .
46010011	Kuuje ɗe'e fuu laatani ɓe ngam faamtingo woɗɓe . Ɗe mbindaama ngam reentingo en , enen yeeɗɓe haa timmoode jamanuuji .
46010012	Ngam maajum ndeente . Mo tammi o ɗon dari , sey o hakkila ngam taa o do''o .
46010013	Jarribooje keɓɗe on , ɗon keɓa yimɓe fuu . Ammaa Allah o koolniiɗo , o accataa on njarribe ko ɓuri sembe mon . To o jarribake on , o hokkan on sembe munyango ɗum boo haa on kisa .
46010014	Ngam maajum , soobiraaɓe am , ndaaye cujidanki labbi .
46010015	Mi ɗon wolwana on bana marɓe hakkiilo , nume ko mbi'anmi .
46010016	Ciftore jardugel kiirtaari ngel ngetteten Allah ngam muuɗum . Na ngel hawtan en bee ?i?am Almasiihu na ? Ciftore tamseere nde cendeten . Na nde hawtan en bee ɓandu Almasiihu na ?
46010017	Woodi tamseere woore tan . Ngam maajum , koo en ɗuuɗɓe , en laati ɓandu wooru , ngam en fuu en kawti nyaamugo tamseere woore .
46010018	Ndaare no yimɓe Isra'iila mbaɗata : Nyaamanɓe kusel kirsaaɗi ngoodi kawtal bee hirsirde senaande ngam Allah .
46010019	Ko saawi nder bolle am ? Kusel kirsaaŋgel ngam lawru ɗum huunde gooŋga na ? Malla lawru ɗum huunde gooŋga na ? Naa non sam !
46010020	Ammaa ko sujidanooɓe labbi kirsata , ɓe lii'antaako ɗum Allah , sey ginnaaji .
46010021	On mbaawataa yardugo jardugel Jawmiraawo , nden on njarda jardugel ginnaaji boo . On mbaawataa nyaamugo haa teebur Jawmiraawo , nden on nyaama haa teebur ginnaaji boo .
46010022	Malla en ngiɗi tikkingo Jawmiraawo na ? Kadi en ɓuri mo sembe na ?
46010023	Woɗɓe mon ɗon mbi'a : " Kooɗume fuu dagake . " Gooŋga , ammaa naa kuuje fuu mbooɗi . Kooɗume fuu dagake , ammaa naa kuuje fuu nafata nuɗɗinki mon .
46010024	Taa ɗaɓɓite ko nafata ko'e mon , sey ko nafata yimɓe woɗɓe .
46010025	Kusel coorreteeŋgel haa luumo , nyaame ngel . Walaa haaje on ?ama haa toy ngel iwi ngam daliila numooji ɓerɗe mon .
46010026	Ngam deftere wi'i : " Jawmiraawo mari lesdi e ko hebbini ndi fuu . "
46010027	To goɗɗo mo nuɗɗinaay ewnake on ngam nyaamdu haa saare mum , to on njaɓi ewnaandu maako , nden kam nyaame ko o jo''inanta on fuu . Walaa haaje on ?ama haa toy kusel iwi ngam daliila numooji ɓerɗe mon .
46010028	Ammaa to goɗɗo wi'i on : " Kusel ngel iwi haa kirsaaŋga cenaaŋga " , nden kam taa nyaame ngel , ngam daliila anndinɗo on ɗum , ngam daliila numo ɓernde boo .
46010029	Mi wi'aay numooji ɓerɗe mooɗon , ammaa numo maako .
46010030	To mi yetti Allah ngam nyaamdu am , koni goɗɗo hallintammi ngam daliila nyaamdu ndu njaɓmi bee yettoore ?
46010031	Ngam maajum mbi'anmi : To on ɗon nyaama malla on ɗon njara malla on ɗon kuuwa kooɗume , mbaɗe ɗum ngam teddinki Allah .
46010032	Taa cakle koomoy , koo Yahuudu'en , koo Yunaniŋko'en , koo jama'aare yimɓe Allah .
46010033	Kuuwe bana min mi huuwata . Mi ɗon tiino haa mi yerdina koomoy bee kooɗume fuu . Mi ɗaɓɓitittaa ko nafatammi , sey ko nafata yimɓe fuu ngam haa ɓe kisa .
46011001	Tokkeeɗam , bana min mi tokkori Almasiihu .
46011002	Mi ɗon mana on ngam on ɗon ciftorammi foroy , on ɗon tokko ko anndinmi on boo .
46011003	Ammaa woodi ko ngiɗmi faamtingo on : Almasiihu woni mawɗo gorko fuu , gorko woni mawɗo debbo mum , Allah boo woni mawɗo Almasiihu .
46011004	Ngam maajum to gorko ɗon waɗa do'a malla ɗon waaja nder mooɓtorde , o ɗon suddi hoore maako , nden kam o meeriɗini Almasiihu .
46011005	Ammaa to debbo ɗon waɗa do'a malla ɗon waaja nder mooɓtorde , suddaay hoore mum , nden kam o meeriɗini goriiko . O laati bana laɓɗo hoore mum .
46011006	To debbo suddaay hoore mum bee sallabi , koni o laɓaay hoore maako ? Ammaa ta''ugo gaasa malla laɓugo hoore debbo ɗum cemtuɗum . Ngam maajum sey o sudda hoore maako .
46011007	Ammaa gorko , taa sudda hoore mum , ngam jaati maako nandi bee Allah , o ɗon waŋgina tedduŋgal Allah . Ammaa debbo ɗon waŋgina tedduŋgal gorum .
46011008	Gorko iwaay haa debbo , ammaa debbo iwi haa gorko .
46011009	Allah tagaay gorko ngam debbo boo , ammaa o tagi debbo ngam gorko .
46011010	Ngam maajum debbo sudda hoore mum bee sallabi bana alaama baawɗe gorum , ngam daliila malaa'ika'en boofi .
46011011	Ammaa haa Jawmiraawo kam , gorko sendiraay bee debbo , debbo boo sendiraay bee gorko .
46011012	Ngam bana debbo iwi haa gorko , bana non gorko danya e debbo . Ammaa ɓe ɗiɗo fuu ɓe iwi haa Allah , tagɗo kuuje fuu .
46011013	Nume bee ko'e mon : To debbo ɗon toro Allah nder mooɓtorde , suddaay hoore mum boo , ɗum fottan na ?
46011014	Koo ɗabiya boo ɗon anndina on , to gorko yoofti gaasa hoore mum , ɗum cemtuɗum .
46011015	Ammaa to debbo yoofti gaasa hoore mum , ɗum daraja maako . O heɓi gaasa maako njuutka bana suddaare .
46011016	To goɗɗo yiɗi waabotirgo bee am dow haala ka'a , nden kam mi wi'an mo : Koo min , koo jama'aaje yimɓe Allah , min ngalaa al'aada feere .
46011017	Too , woodi haala feere boo . Ngam daliila maaka mi manataa on . To on ɗon mooɓto , ɗum laatataako ngam hayru mon , ammaa ngam sarru mon .
46011018	Aran , mi nani on cendaama geɓe feere feere nder jama'aare mon . Goɗɗum haala maajum mi tammi ɗum gooŋga .
46011019	Doole biɗu'aakuuji laato hakkunde mooɗon , ngam haa hoolaaɓe mbaŋga .
46011020	To on ɗon mooɓto , on nyaamataa kiirtaari Jawmiraawo bee gooŋga .
46011021	Ngam koomoy mooɗon ɗon yaawana nyaamugo nyaamdu mum . Bana ni woɗɓe luttan bee weelo , woɗɓe boo nguykan .
46011022	Asee , on mbaawataa nyaamugo e yarugo diga saare na ? Malla on njawi jama'aare yimɓe Allah na ? On ngiɗi semtingo talaka'en na ? Ko ngiɗɗon mi wi'a on ? Mi mana on na ? Fakat , mi manataa on .
46011023	Jawmiraawo bee hoore mum umri ko anndinmi on : Nder jemmaare nde Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men , hokkano haa juuɗe konne'en mum , o hoo'i tamseere ,
46011024	o yetti Allah ngam maare , o yewi nde , o wi'i : " Ɗum ɓandu am yewaandu ngam mooɗon . Kuuwe ɗum ngam haa on ciftorammi . "
46011025	Ɓaawo nyaamugo maɓɓe , o hoo'i jardugel boo , o wi'i : " Jardugel ngel woni alkawal kesal ngal Allah tabitinta bee ?i?am am . Koondey njaroton nder maagel fuu , mbaɗe ɗum ngam haa on ciftorammi . "
46011026	To on ɗon nyaama tamseere nde'e , on ɗon njara nder jardugel ngel boo , on ɗon ngaajina kubar maayde Jawmiraawo , haa nyalaade o wari .
46011027	To goɗɗo nyaami tamseere Jawmiraawo , yari nder jardugel maako , ammaa hakkilanaay hoore mum , nden kam o waɗi aybe dow ɓandu Jawmiraawo e ?i?am mum .
46011028	Ngam maajum sey koomoy linya hoore mum , hiddeko o nyaama tamseere , o yara nder jardugel boo .
46011029	Ngam to o sendindiraay ɓandu Jawmiraawo bee nyaamdu meere , o fooɗanan hoore maako kiita bee nyaamugo maako e yarugo maako .
46011030	Ngam daliila maajum ɗuuɗɓe nder mooɗon nyawi , tampi , ɗuuɗɓe boo maayi .
46011031	To en kakkilani ko'e men , Allah hiitataako en .
46011032	Ammaa to o ɓocci en , ɗum laatoto ngam o elta en , ngam taa o do''a en kiita hawtaade bee duniyaaru fuu .
46011033	Ngam maajum , deerɗam'en , to on ɗon mooɓto ngam nyaamugo kiirtaari Jawmiraawo , munye haa to on kawti on fuu .
