46011034	To goɗɗo nani weelo , sey o aarta o nyaama diga saare . Nden kam mooɓtaago mon fooɗantaa on kiita Allah . Haalaaji luttuɗi , mi ta''an ɗi to mi wari .
46012001	Too , en linya haala dokke ɗe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo hokkata . Deerɗam'en , mi yiɗi on paama ɗum laaɓɗum .
46012002	Yaake on nuɗɗinaayno Jawmiraawo , al'aada mon ɗonno yerɓa on haa labbi muukaaji .
46012003	Ngam maajum ngiɗmi on paamta ɗu'um : To Ruuhu Allah naŋgi goɗɗo , goɗɗo oo waawataa wi'ugo : " Yeesu naalaaɗo ! " Bana non boo , goɗɗo wi'ataa : " Yeesu woni Jawmiraawo " , sonaa Ruuhu Allah ɗon nder maako .
46012004	Woodi dokke feere-feereeje , ammaa Ruuhu ngootu ɗon hokka ɗe fuu .
46012005	Woodi kuuɗe feere-feereeje , ammaa Jawmiraawo gooto umri huuwugo ɗe fuu .
46012006	Woodi boo baawɗe huuwugo feere-feereeje , ammaa Allah gooto ɗon hokka koomoy baawal mum .
46012007	Dokkal Ruuhu Allah ɗon waŋga nder koomoy meeɗen haa ngal nafa jama'aare fuu .
46012008	Goɗɗo , Ruuhu ɗon hokka mo dokkal wolwugo bee hikma , goɗɗo boo ɗon heɓa dokkal wolwugo bee anndal .
46012009	Ruuhu maajum ɗon hokka goɗɗo nuɗɗinki cembiɗki , goɗɗo feere boo baawal yamɗitingo .
46012010	Ngu ɗon hokka oo baawal huuwugo kaayeefiiji , oya boo dokkal waɗugo annabaaku . Goɗɗo feere ɗon heɓa dokkal sendindirgo Ruuhu Allah bee ruuhuuji goɗɗi . Oo ɗon heɓa dokkal wolwugo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka , oya boo dokkal fassitirgo ɗe .
46012011	Ammaa Ruuhu ngootu go huuwata ɗum fuu , ngu ɗon yeɗa koomoy baawal mum bana ngu muuyi .
46012012	Almasiihu laati bana ɓandu wooru marndu terɗe ɗuuɗɗe . Fakat , ɓandu maajum wooru , koo ndu woodi terɗe feere-feereeje boo .
46012013	En fuu , Yahuudu'en e iwɓe haa ummaatooje goɗɗe , maccuɓe e rimɓe , en keɓi ngiiwam baptisma bee Ruuhu ngootu go , ngam haa en kawta nder ɓandu wooru , en fuu en laati yarnaaɓe Ruuhu maajum boo .
46012014	Ɓandu kam laataaki tergal gootal , ammaa terɗe ɗuuɗɗe .
46012015	Teema kosŋgal wi'an : " Mi laataaki juŋŋgo , ngam maajum mi hawtaay bee ɓandu . " Bee non fuu , ngal terde ɓandu fakat .
46012016	Malla nofru wi'an : " Naa mi yiitere , ngam maajum mi hawtaay bee ɓandu . " Fakat , ɗum haɗataa nofru laataago terde ɓandu .
46012017	To ɓandu fuu laatake yiitere , noy ndu narrata ? To ndu laatake nofru tan , noy ndu luuɓnirta ?
46012018	Fakat , Allah hawti terɗe kooɗeye nder ɓandu wooru bana o muuyi .
46012019	To ɓandu fuu laatake terde woore tan , nden kam naa ɗum ɓandu .
46012020	Ammaa jonta , woodi terɗe ɗuuɗɗe haa ɓandu wooru .
46012021	Yiitere fotaay wi'ugo juŋŋgo : " Mi walaa haaje ma . " Hoore boo fotaay wi'ugo kosɗe : " Mi walaa haaje mon . "
46012022	Naa non sam ! Ammaa terɗe ɓandu ɗe ndaareten bana tampuɗe , kanje ɗe ɓuran nafugo .
46012023	Terɗe ɗe pottanaay en , en ɓuran hakkilango ɗe . Terɗe ɗe cemtirten , en cuuɗan ɗe bee hakkiilo .
46012024	Terɗe ɓuranɗe fottango en , ngalaa haaje suuɗeego . Allah hawti ɓandu fuu , hokki terɗe leesɗe tedduŋgal ɓuranŋgal .
46012025	Ngam o yiɗaa luural laato nder ɓandu , ammaa terɗe fuu njiŋgindira bee hakkiilo wooto .
46012026	To terde woore naawi , terɗe fuu naawan bee maagal . To woore teddinaama , ɗe fuu ɗe ceyodo bee maare boo .
46012027	On fuu on ɓandu Almasiihu , koomoy mooɗon laati terde haa maaru .
46012028	Allah hokki koomoy joonde mum nder jama'aare : aran nelaaɓe , ɗiɗawre waajooɓe kubaruuji Allah , tataɓre boo jaŋginooɓe . Nden huuwooɓe kaayeefiiji , e waawɓe yamɗitingo e wallooɓe e ɗowooɓe e wolwooɓe bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka .
46012029	Naa ɓe fuu ɓe nelaaɓe malla waajooɓe malla jaŋginooɓe . Naa ɓe fuu ɓe huuwooɓe kaayeefiiji
46012030	malla waawɓe yamɗitingo malla wolwooɓe bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka malla fassitirooɓe ɗe .
46012031	Tefe dokke ɓuranɗe mawnugo .
46013001	To mi anndi wolwugo ɗemɗe yimɓe e malaa'ika'en fuu , ammaa mi walaa yiide , nden kam mi nandan bee njamndi iidoori malla bee koŋsiire hooloore .
46013002	To mi heɓi dokkal waajugo kubaruuji Allah , malla to mi anndi sirriiji Allah fuu , to mi woodi nuɗɗinki haa mi sottina kooseeje boo , ammaa mi walaa yiide , nden kam mi huunde meere .
46013003	Koo to mi sendani talaka'en jawdi am fuu , to mi jaɓi wuleego ngam daliila nuɗɗinki am boo , ammaa mi walaa yiide , nden kam ɗum nafataa yam sam .
46013004	Marɗo yiide munyanan woɗɓe , woonanan ɓe . O haajataa , o jurataako , o mawnitittaako .
46013005	Marɗo yiide huuwataa cemtuɗum , o suklantaako hoore maako , o tikkataa law , o limataa aybeeji goɗɗo .
46013006	O seyortaako kuuɗe kalluɗe , ammaa o seyorto gooŋga .
46013007	Marɗo yiide munyanan kooɗume fuu . Nuɗɗinki maako e tammunde maako e munyal maako tampataa sam .
46013008	Yiide ɗon duumo haa foroy . Bolle annabaaku njinnan , wolwugo bee ɗemɗe Ruuhu timman , anndal boo majjan .
46013009	Ngam anndal men e waaju men waŋgintaa gooŋga fuu , sey geɓe pamare .
46013010	Ammaa geɓe man majjan to gooŋga fuu waŋgi .
46013011	Yaake mi ɓiŋgelno , mi wolwi bana ɓiŋgel , mi numi bana ɓiŋgel , mi hiisti bana ɓiŋgel boo . Jonta laatiimi gorko , ngam maajum accumi laawol ɓiŋgel .
46013012	Jonta en ɗon ngi'a bana foto nder daarorgal , en ngi'ataa ɗum laaɓɗum . Ammaa saa'i waran haa en ngi'a Allah gite bee gite . Jonta mi anndi mo dow dow , ammaa saa'i maajum mi anndan mo laaɓɗum bana kaŋko o anndiri yam .
46013013	Jonta kam , kuuje tati ɗon tabiti : nuɗɗinki e tammunde e yiide . Ammaa yiide ɓuri kooɗume fuu mawnugo .
46014001	Tiine haa keɓon yiide . Ɗaɓɓite dokke Ruuhu boo , sakkoma baawal waajugo kubaruuji Allah .
46014002	Bolwanɗo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka , wolwantaa yimɓe , sey Allah , ngam walaa paamanɗo mo . Bee baawɗe Ruuhu Allah o ɗon wolwa bolle sirriije .
46014003	Ammaa gaajanɗo kubaruuji Allah ɗon wolwana yimɓe haa o walla ɓe , o sembiɗina ɓe , o de'itina ɓe .
46014004	To goɗɗo wolwi bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka , o nafan hoore maako tan . Ammaa gaajanɗo kubaruuji Allah ɗon nafa jama'aare fuu .
46014005	Mi yiɗi on fuu on keɓa wolwugo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka , ammaa mi ɓuran yiɗugo on keɓa waajugo kubaruuji Allah . Kanjum ɗum ɓuran nafugo jama'aare dow wolwugo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka . Ngam wolwugo bee ɗemɗe man nafataa jama'aare sonaa goɗɗo fassitiri ɗe ngam haa o sembiɗina nuɗɗinki jama'aare fuu .
46014006	Deerɗam'en , ko ɗum nafata on to mi wari haa mooɗon , mi wolwi bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka ? Fakat , ɗum nafataa on , sonaa to mi waŋginani on gooŋgaaji Allah , malla to mi waddani on anndal , malla to mi waaji on kubaruuji Allah , malla to mi anndini on .
46014007	Ciftore kuuje gimi bana algaytaaru malla moolooru . To puufoowo ndu malla piyoowo ndu waɗaay ɗum laaɓɗum , noy goɗɗo heɓtirta gimol maako ?
46014008	Malla to puufoowo luwal konu fuufaay laaɓɗum , moy taaskanto haɓre ?
46014009	Bana non haa mooɗon boo : To on mbolwi bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka , noy goɗɗo faamrata ko mbi'ɗon ? Nden kam on mbolwi meere .
46014010	Woodi ɗemɗe ɗuuɗɗe feere-feereeje nder duniyaaru , ummaatoore koondeye woodi ɗemŋgal mum .
46014011	Ammaa to mi anndaa ɗemŋgal ngal goɗɗo wolwani yam , nden kam goɗɗo oo laatani yam jananno , min boo mi jananno haa maako .
46014012	Onon on ɗon camɗina dokke Ruuhu masin . Tiine heɓugo dokke nafooje ngam mawninki jama'aare .
46014013	Ngam maajum , to goɗɗo waawi wolwugo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka , sey o toro Allah haa o heɓa baawal fassitirgo ɗe boo .
46014014	To mi ɗon waɗa do'a bee ɗemŋgal janannal , ruuhu am ɗon do'o , ammaa hakkiilo am huuwataa .
46014015	To non kam , ko mbaɗanmi ? Mi waɗan do'a bee ruuhu am , ammaa mi waɗan do'a bee hakkiilo am boo . Mi yiman maŋgtoore bee ruuhu am , ammaa mi yiman nde bee hakkiilo am boo .
46014016	Ammaa to a ɗon maŋgta Allah bee ɗemŋgal ruuhu , noy goɗɗo nder mooɓtorde mo anndaa ɗemŋgal man wi'rata " Aamiina " haa do'a ma ? Ngam o faamataa sam ko mbi'ata .
46014017	Koo to do'a ma wooɗi masin , ɗum nafataa mo sam .
46014018	Mi ɗon yetta Allah ngam mi ɓuri on fuu wolwugo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka .
46014019	Ammaa nder mooɓtorde mi ɓuran yiɗugo mi wolwa bolle jowi paameteeɗe haa mi anndina woɗɓe , dow bolle ujine sappo bee ɗemŋgal janannal .
46014020	Deerɗam'en , taa nume bana ɓikkoy . Nder kuuɗe mon laate on ngalaa halleende bana ɓikkoy . Ammaa nder numooji mon laate on mawɓe .
46014021	Ndaa ko winda nder deftere Allah :
46014022	Ngam maajum wolwugo bee ɗemɗe man laati alaama , naa ngam nuɗɗinɓe , ammaa ngam sooyɓe nuɗɗinki . Ammaa waaju kubaruuji Allah laataaki alaama ngam sooyɓe nuɗɗinki , sey ngam nuɗɗinɓe .
46014023	To jama'aare mon fuu mooɓtake , koomoy mooɗon fuɗɗi wolwugo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka . Nden humaki'en malla heefeerɓe ngari , nasti . Ɓe ndaarataa on bana yinnaaɓe na ?
46014024	Ammaa to koomoy ɗon waaja kubaruuji Allah , cooyɗo nuɗɗinki malla humakiijo boo nasti , nden kam bolle ɗe o nanata fuu paamtinan mo aybeeji maako . Bolle ɗe'e fuu kiitoto mo ,
46014025	numooji ɓernde maako cuuɗiiɗi mbaŋgan . O sujidanan Allah , o seedoto : " Fakat , Allah ɗon wondi bee mooɗon . "
46014026	Deerɗam'en , to non kam , noy mbaɗoton ? To on ɗon mooɓti , oo woodi yimre , oya woodi anndinol , goɗɗo woodi wahayu , goɗɗo feere wolwan bee ɗemŋgal ngal anndaaka , goɗɗo feere fahin fassitiran ngal . Sey ɗum fuu ɗum nafa ngam mawninki jama'aare .
46014027	To ɗemɗe jananne kam , acce yimɓe ɗiɗo mbolwa , taa ɓura tato , ɓe mbolwa bee tokkindirki boo . Sey goɗɗo fassitira ko wi'ete .
46014028	Ammaa to passitiroowo woodaa , sey bolwanɗo bee ɗemɗe go jeeɗo nder mooɓtorde , o wolwana hoore maako e Allah .
46014029	Heɓɓe wahayu Allah ɗiɗo malla tato mbolwa , luttuɓe fuu linya ko ɓe mbi'ata .
46014030	Teema goɗɗo heɓan wahayu saa'i goɗɗo feere ɗon wolwa tawon . Nden kam arano acca .
46014031	On fuu on mbaawan waajugo kubaruuji Allah , gooto gooto bee tokkindirki , ngam haa jama'aare fuu faama , nuɗɗinki koomoy sembiɗa .
46014032	Waajooɓe kubaruuji Allah ɗon naŋgta ruuhuuji muuɗum'en .
46014033	Allah yiɗaa en njooɗodo bee fitina , sey bee jam .
46014034	bana non nder mooɓtorde mooɗon boo : Sey rewɓe njeeɗo . Ɓe nduŋganaaka wolwugo . Sey ɓe laato ɗowtiiɓe bana no tawreeta umri .
46014035	To ɓe ngiɗi faamtugo huunde , sey ɓe ?ama worɓe maɓɓe haa saare . Ngam to debbo wolwi nder mooɓtorde , ɗum cemtuɗum .
46014036	Malla haa mooɗon wolde Allah iwi ? Malla haa mooɗon tan nde wari ?
46014037	To goɗɗo numi o keɓɗo wahayuuji malla o keɓɗo Ruuhu Allah , nden kam o faaman ko mbindanmi on ɗum umrooje Jawmiraawo .
46014038	Ammaa to o jaɓaay ɗum , Allah boo jaɓataa mo .
46014039	Ngam maajum , deerɗam'en , tiine waajugo kubaruuji Allah , ammaa taa kaɗe wolwugo bee ɗemɗe ɗe anndaaka .
46014040	Sey kooɗume fuu laato bee laawol booɗŋgol , bana no haandi .
46015001	Deerɗam'en , sey mi siftinora on linjiila ka ngaajumi on . On njaɓi ka , nuɗɗinki mon ɗon dari dow maaka .
46015002	Bee maaka kisoton , to on njogitake ka bana ngaajirmi on ka . To naa non , on nuɗɗini meere .
46015003	Mi anndini on kubaruwol ngol njaɓmi bee hoore am . Ndaa ko aartumi wi'ugo on : Almasiihu maayi ngam daliila hakkeeji men bana no winda nder defte .
46015004	Ɓe uwi mo . Nyande tataɓre Allah ummitini mo diga maayde , bana no winda nder defte .
46015005	O waŋgani Piyer , nden o waŋgani pukara'en sappo e ɗiɗo fuu .
46015006	Ɓaawo maajum o waŋgani deerɗiraaɓe ko ɓuri teemeɗɗe njowo . Ɓurna maɓɓe ɗon lutti haa jonta , ammaa woɗɓe maɓɓe maayi .
46015007	Ɓaawo maajum o waŋgani Yakuba , nden o waŋgani nelaaɓe fuu .
46015008	Haa ragare , ɓaawo maɓɓe fuu , o waŋgani yam , min boo , koo mi laati bana ɓiŋgel danyaaŋgel ngel hebbidinaay lebbi mum .
46015009	Mi ɓurɗo leesugo caka nelaaɓe , ngam mi toonyi jama'aare yimɓe Allah . Mi he'aay wi'eego nelaaɗo .
46015010	Ammaa ngam mo''ere Allah laatiimi nelaaɗo , mo''ere maako dow am laataaki meere boo . Mi huuwi ko ɓuri nelaaɓe fuu , waato naa min huuwi ɗum , ammaa mo''ere Allah nder am .
46015011	Koo min , koo kamɓe , minin nelaaɓe fuu min ɗon ngaajina linjiila bana mbi'mi on , bana non nuɗɗinirɗon boo .
46015012	Ndaa ni waaju amin : Allah ummitini Almasiihu diga maayde . Noy woɗɓe mon mbi'rata maayɓe ummitittaako ?
46015013	To ummitineeki maayɓe woodaa , nden kam Almasiihu boo ummitaaki .
46015014	To Almasiihu ummitaaki , nden kam waaju amin laati meere , nuɗɗinki mon boo meere .
46015015	Ko tulli ɗum , min pewani Allah , ngam min ceedi mo o ummitini Almasiihu diga maayde . Asee , o ummitinaay mo , to fakat maayɓe ummitittaako kam .
46015016	Ngam to maayɓe ummitittaako , nden kam Almasiihu boo ummitaaki .
46015017	Ammaa to Almasiihu ummitaaki , nuɗɗinki mon nafataa , on majjuɓe nder hakkeeji mon haa jonta ,
46015018	nuɗɗinɓe Almasiihu maayɓe boo kalki .
46015019	To en tammake heɓugo hayru haa Almasiihu nder ngeendam jontaajam tan , nden kam en ɓuran yimɓe fuu yurmugo .
46015020	Ammaa fakat , Almasiihu ummiti diga maayde , ngam maajum maayɓe fuu ummititto .
46015021	Bana no maayde nastiri duniyaaru ngam daliila neɗɗo , bana non ummitineeki maayɓe boo wardan bee neɗɗo .
46015022	Yimɓe fuu maayan ngam daliila kawtal muuɗum'en bee Aadamu . Ɓe fuu ɓe ummititto boo ngam daliila kawtal maɓɓe bee Almasiihu ,
46015023	ammaa koomoy dow tokkindirki mum : Almasiihu woni aartuɗo . To o waroyi , Masiihiŋko'en ummititto .
46015024	Nden timmoode waran . Almasiihu halkan marɓe laamu e baawɗe , e ruuhuuji konneeji Allah fuu , nden o hokka laamu haa juŋŋgo Allah Baabiraawo .
46015025	Ngam doole Almasiihu laamo sey to Allah wallini konne'en maako fuu les kosɗe maako .
46015026	Konneejo ragareejo kalketeeɗo , ɗum waade .
46015027	Ngam deftere wi'i : " Allah wallini kooɗume fuu les kosɗe maako . " To wi'aama : " Kooɗume fuu " , fakat Allah ballinanɗo mo ɗum limaaka :
46015028	To Ɓiɗɗo Allah laatake Jawmiraawo dow kooɗume fuu , nden kam o sappanan Allah , baɗɗo mo Jawmiraawo dow kooɗume fuu , haa Allah laato kooɗume fuu nder koomoy .
46015029	Numte haala feere boo : Woodi woɗɓe nder jama'aare mon , jaɓanɓe ngiiwam baptisma ngam maayɓe . To gooŋga , maayɓe ummitittaako , ɗume ngiiwam man nafata kadi ?
46015030	Koo minin boo , ngam ɗume min njaɓata naawneego malla mbareego tum ?
46015031	Deerɗam'en , fakat bana mi mantorto on yeeso Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , nyalɗe fuu mi ɗon nder joote maayde .
46015032	Haa Efesus mbaɗmi haɓre saatunde bana bee dabbaaji kalluɗi . To mi walaa tammunde ummitineego , ɗume ɗum nafatammi ? To maayɓe ummitittaako , ndikka en tokko koŋgol ngo'ol : " Nyaamen , njaren , ngam jaŋgo en maayan . "
46015033	Taa este ko'e mon ! " Gondal bee kalluɗo wonnan gikku mbooɗŋgu . "
46015034	Laate on hakkilɓe , fottananɓe Allah , taa mbaɗe hakke . Ammaa woɗɓe mon anndaa Allah . Mi wi'i ɗum ngam haa on cemta .
46015035	Teema goɗɗo ?aman : " Noy maayɓe ummitorto ? Ɓandu nduye ɓe marata ? "
46015036	Kayya ! A walaa hakkiilo na ? To a aawi aawdi , doole ndi maaya tawon ngam haa fuɗŋgo maari yeeɗa .
46015037	Ko aawa boo , naa ɗum fuɗŋgo maŋgo bee haakooji mum , ammaa ɗum gawel meere , bana gawel gawri malla kooŋgele .
46015038	Ammaa Allah ɗon hokka gawel fuu irin ɓandu maagel bana o muuyi . Aawdi koondiye heɓan ɓandu muuɗum .
46015039	Ɓalli kuuje marɗe yoŋki naa ɗi gooti . Ɓalli yimɓe cendiri bee ɓalli dabbaaji , ɓalli colli cendiri bee ɓalli liɗɗi .
46015040	Woodi boo ɓalli asama e ɓalli lesdi . Ɓalli lesdi mari ngarol , ammaa ɓalli asama boo mari ngarol feere .
46015041	Naaŋge woodi ngarol mum , lewru woodi ngarol feere , koode boo ngoodi ngarol feere . Koo ngarol koode boo laataaki gootol , jayŋgol horre nde'e sendiri bee jayŋgol horre ndeya .
46015042	Bana non ummitineeki maayɓe laatorto . Ko uwa , ɗum nyolan . Ko ummititto , ɗum halkataa sam .
46015043	Ko uwa , ɗum tampuɗum , nyidduɗum . Ko ummititto , ɗum cembiɗɗum , booɗɗum masin .
46015044	Ko uwa , ɗum ɓandu ndu kusel . Ko ummititto , ɗum ɓandu ndu ruuhu . To woodi ɓandu ndu kusel , woodi ɓandu ndu ruuhu boo .
46015045	Ngam deftere wi'i : " Aadamu , neɗɗo arano laati yoŋki geeti . " Ammaa Aadamu ragareejo , waato Almasiihu , laati Ruuhu ndokkoowu ngeendam .
46015046	Naa mo Ruuhu aartata , ammaa mo ɓandu , ɓaawoɗon mo Ruuhu .
46015047	Aadamu arano tagraama bee mbulwuldi lesdi . Aadamu ɗiɗaɓo iwi haa asama .
46015048	Yimɓe lesdi nandi bee Aadamu iwɗo haa mbulwuldi . Yimɓe asama nandan bee iwɗo haa asama .
46015049	Jonta en nandi bee mbulwuldiijo . Ammaa saa'i waran nde nandeten bee iwɗo haa asama .
46015050	Deerɗam'en , ko ngiɗmi faamtingo on , ndaa ɗum : Marɓe kusel e ?i?am nastataa laamu Allah . Ɓandu maayanndu heɓataa duumaago .
46015051	Sey mi waŋginana on sirri : Naa en fuu en maayan , ammaa en fuu en ngayloto .
46015052	Ɗum waɗan law , bana ma''annde yiitere , saa'i hoolo luwal anndinta garki kiitoowo duniyaaru . Haa puufki luwal man , maayɓe ummititto bee ngeendam nduumiiɗam . Enen yeeɗɓe saa'i maajum , en keɓan ɓalli kesi .
46015053	Ɓalli men kalkanɗi ɓornoto ɓandu duumiindu ndu halkataa .
46015054	To ɗum laatake bana non , nden kam wolde annabaaku gooŋɗan :
46015055	An waade , toy jaalorgal ma ?
46015056	Baawɗe waade iwi haa hakke , baawɗe hakke boo iwi haa tawreeta .
46015057	Ammaa yettoore laatano Allah , dokkanɗo en jaalorgal bee Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
46015058	Ngam maajum , onon deerɗam'en yiɗaaɓe , laate on tabitɓe ɓe ndimbataako . Cuklane kuugal Jawmiraawo foroy , ngam on anndi tiinaare mon nder kawtal bee Jawmiraawo laatataako meere .
46016001	Too , sey mi ɓesda bolle seɗɗa dow walliinde ceede ngam yimɓe Allah haa Urusaliima . Bana no mbi'rumi jama'aaje nuɗɗinɓe nder Galaatiya , kuuwe onon boo bana non .
46016002	Nyande Alat fuu sey koomoy mooɗon resa ceede seɗɗa baakin no o waawi . Cige ɗum booɗɗum haa mi wara . Nden kam walaa haaje mi fuɗɗa mooɓtugo ɗum .
46016003	To mi wari , mi nelan suɓaaɓe mon bee bataakeeji haa Urusaliima , haa ɓe njahra dokkal mon ton .
46016004	To dokkal mon he'i haa mi yahra ngal bee hoore am , nden kam ɓe njahdan bee am .
46016005	Mi tammi tokkaago nder Makedoniya ngam haa mi yaala jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en ton . Ɓaawo maajum ngaranmi haa mooɗon .
46016006	Teema mi faɓɓan haa mooɗon , to heɓoto mi waɗan dabbunde haa mooɗon boo . Nden on mballammi nder haaje jahaaŋgal am haa nokkuure nde ngiɗmi yahugo .
46016007	To mi wari laarugo on , mi yiɗaa dillugo law . Mi yiɗi faɓɓugo haa mooɗon , to Jawmiraawo duŋgake .
46016008	Ammaa mi jooɗoto haa Efesus haa juulde Pentekosta .
46016009	Ngam mi heɓi baawɗe huuwugo kuugal maŋgal nafoowal haa ɗo , koo nde konne'en ɗuuɗani yam boo .
46016010	To Timote wari haa mooɗon , njaɓɓe mo booɗɗum haa o jooɗo caka mooɗon bilaa kulol . Ngam kaŋko boo o ɗon huuwana Jawmiraawo bana am .
46016011	Taa goɗɗo yawo mo . Mballe mo haa o timmina jahaaŋgal maako bee jam , ngam haa o warta haa am . Min e deerɗiraaɓe haa ɗo min ɗon ndeena garki maako .
46016012	Ammaa Apollos , deerɗiraawo men kam , mi tiɗɗini mo ɗuuɗɗum o yaha haa mooɗon bee deerɗiraaɓe woɗɓe . Ammaa o sali yahugo jonta . Yeeso seɗɗa , to o heɓi laawol , o yahan .
46016013	Ayne , tabite nder nuɗɗinki . Tiɗɗine ɓerɗe mon , laate on sembiɗɓe .
46016014	Ko kuuwoton fuu , kuuwe ɗum bee yiide .
46016015	Deerɗam'en , on anndi Estefanas e saare mum . Kamɓe ɓe nuɗɗinɓe aartuɓe nder Akaya , ɓe ɗon tiini huuwango yimɓe Allah .
46016016	Mi ɗon toro on on ɗowtano irin maɓɓe , kamɓe e huuwdooɓe bee maɓɓe , tiiniiɓe fuu .
46016017	Mi ɗon seyoro garki Estefanas e Fortunatus e Aka'ikus . Kamɓe ɓe ndokki yam ko on mbaawaay ngam on daayiiɓe .
46016018	Ɓe nde'itini ɓernde am , bana ɓe nde'itini nde mooɗon . Camɗine irin maɓɓe .
46016019	Jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en nder lesdi Asiya fuu koofni on . Akilas e Piriskilla e nuɗɗinɓe mooɓtotooɓe nder saare maɓɓe fuu koofni on bee innde Jawmiraawo .
46016020	Deerɗiraaɓe wonɓe haa ɗo fuu koofni on .
46016021	Ndaa ko mbindumi bee juŋŋgo am : Min Pol mi hoofni on .
46016022	To goɗɗo yiɗaa Jawmiraawo bee ɓernde woore , naaloore dow maako ! " Maranata " - war , ya Jawmiraawo amin !
46016023	Mo''ere Jawmiraawo men Yeesu wondu bee mooɗon .
46016024	Yiide am ɗon tabitani on nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
47001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu bee muuyo Allah , min bee Timote , deerɗiraawo men , yahugo haa jama'aare yimɓe Allah wonɓe haa Korintu , e Masiihiŋko'en nder lesdi Akaya fuu :
47001002	Allah , Baabiraawo men , e Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men ndokka on mo''ere e jam .
47001003	Yettoore laatano Allah , Baabiraawo Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , ngam o baabiraawo enɗoowo , o Allah de'itinoowo min foroy .
47001004	Koo to ɓillaaje ɗuuɗani min , kaŋko o ɗon sembiɗina min tum . Ngam maajum min mbaawan sembiɗingo yaranɓe boneeji feere-feereeji . Min ndokkan ɓe de'itinki ki min keɓi haa Allah .
47001005	Bana no geɗal boneeji ɗuuɗirani min , bana non boo de'itinki ɗuuɗani min haa maako .
47001006	To min ɗon njara bone , ɗum laatoto haa onon on nde'ita , on kisa . To Allah de'itini min , ɗum laatoto haa onon on cembiɗa , on munyana irin boneeji ɗi min njarata .
47001007	To min ɗon ciftora on , hoolaare amin ɗon tabiti , ngam min anndi on ɗon kawta bee amin nder boneeji , bana non nder de'itinki boo .
47001008	Deerɗiraaɓe , min ngiɗi anndingo on ɓillaaje keɓɗe min nder lesdi Asiya . Ɗe teddani min masin haa ɓuri sembe amin . Min itti koo tammunde ngeendam boo .
47001009	Min maati nder ɓerɗe amin bana min do''aaɓe kiita mbareego . Ɗum laati ngam taa min koolo ko'e amin , ammaa min koolo Allah , ummitinoowo maayɓe .
47001010	Kaŋko o hisni min ɓillaaje maayde fuu , min ɗon koolo mo o hisnan min koo yeeso ɗo boo .
47001011	Onon on ɗon mballa min bee do'aaji mon . Ɗuuɗɓe ɗon ndo'ano min , Allah boo jaɓanan ɓe , woonanan min , ngam haa ɗuuɗɓe ngetta mo ngam amin .
47001012	Numooji ɓerɗe amin ɗon ceedo min joonde amin nder duniyaaru , sakkoma caka mooɗon , laati bee gooŋgaaku e laaɓeeŋga ɗum Allah hokki min . Kanjum min mantorto . Min tokkaaki faamu yimɓe , sey mo''ere Allah .
47001013	Walaa ko saawi nder bataakeeji amin , sonaa ko on njaŋgata , ko on paamata boo . Min ɗon tammi , yeeso ɗo on paamtan
47001014	ko paamoton jonta dow dow . To Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men waroyi , on mbaawan mantoraago min bana minin min mantorto on .
47001015	Ngam daliila anndugo ɗum mi waɗno anniya yaalugo haa mooɗon nder jahaaŋgal am haa Makedoniya . Mi muuyno yahrango on mo''ere Allah ɗiɗawre . Saa'i lortaago am e Makedoniya mi yaaltanno on fahin , haa on mballammi nder haaje jahaaŋgal am yahugo Yahudiya .
47001016	
47001017	Nde mi waɗa anniya ka'a , mi numaayno bee hakkiilo am na ? Malla mi waɗi ɗum bana anniya yimɓe tan na ? Kadi mi wi'i " ooho " , ammaa mi numi " aa'a " na ?
47001018	Fakat bana Allah o koolniiɗo , ko mbi'mi on laataaki ooho bee aa'a ɗiɗi fuu .
47001019	Yeesu Almasiihu , Ɓiɗɗo Allah mo min anndini on , min e Silas e Timote , kaŋko o laataaki ooho bee aa'a , sey ooho tan .
47001020	Fakat , kaŋko woni ooho dow koŋguɗi Allah fuu . Ngam daliila maako mbi'eten " aamiina " boo ngam teddinki Allah .
47001021	Allah bee hoore mum tabitini en , minin bee mooɗon , nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu . O suɓi en ,
47001022	o waɗani en lamba maral maako . O hokki en Ruuhu maako nder ɓerɗe men bana jiŋginafa hayruuji ɗi o sigani en .
47001023	Allah woni ceedoowo yam , o hiito yam to mi fewi ! Mi waraay haa Korintu tawon ngam haa mi hoynana on .
47001024	Min ɗaɓɓataa laamanaago nuɗɗinki mon , ngam on ɗon tabiti nder maaki . Ammaa min ngiɗi wallugo on haa keɓon seyo .
47002001	Ngam maajum mi waɗi anniya taa mi wara haa mooɗon ngam sunugo on .
47002002	Ngam to on cunake , moy seynatammi ?
47002003	Kanjum mi windani on ɗum . To mi wari haa mooɗon , mi yiɗaa on cunammi , ngam haani mi seyoro on . Mi anndi fakat , to min mi heɓi seyo , nden kam on fuu on ceyoto .
47002004	Bataakewol naane mi winduno ngol bee gonɗi ɗuuɗɗi e cakle ɗuuɗɗe , ɓernde am naawino masin . Ammaa mi windaay haa mi suna on . Mi ɗaɓɓititi waŋginango on no mi yiɗiri on masin .
47002005	To goɗɗo nder mooɗon laatake daliila suno , naa min o suni , ammaa on fuu . Malla ndikka mi wi'a o suni woɗɓe mooɗon , ngam taa mi saalo gooŋga .
47002006	Ɓurna mooɗon hiiti mo , ɗum he'i kadi .
47002007	Jonta kam , sey on njaafo mo , on nde'itina mo , ngam taa ɓernde maako ta''a , o itta tammunde fuu .
47002008	Ngam maajum mi ɗon toro on : Kolle mo yiide mon .
47002009	Mi windani on ngam haa mi linya gooŋgaaku mon , mi heɓta to on ɗon tokko anndinol am foroy .
47002010	To on njaafake goɗɗo oo , nden kam min boo mi yaafoto mo . To mi woodi haaje yaafaago kooɗume , fakat kaŋko boo mi yaafoto mo ngam daliila mooɗon yeeso Almasiihu ,
47002011	ngam taa Sayɗaanu jaalo en . Ngam en anndi dabareeji maako booɗɗum .
47002012	Mi yotti Torowas haa mi waajina linjiila Almasiihu ton . Jawmiraawo hoynani yam kuugal am boo .
47002013	Ammaa mi walaano de'ere , ngam mi tawaay soobaajo am Titus ton . Ngam maajum mi jaɓɓotiri bee maɓɓe , mi dilli Makedoniya .
47002014	Yettoore laatano Allah , ngam barka Almasiihu o ɗon yahra min foroy nder jahaaŋgal jaaliiɗo . Bana ni o huuwtinirta min haa min anndina kubar maako kootoy , anndal maajum ɗon heewa lesdi bana uureeŋgol belŋgol .
47002015	Min laati bana urle belɗe ɗe Almasiihu lii'ani Allah . Uureeŋgol maajum ɗon yotto hisanɓe e majjanɓe fuu .
47002016	Haa majjanɓe ɗum uureeŋgol maayde haa ɓe maaya . Haa hisanɓe ɗum uureeŋgol ngeendam haa ɓe ngeeɗa . Moy he'i huuwugo kuugal ngal ?
47002017	Ɗuuɗɓe ɗon ndaara wolde Allah bana huunde filu . Minin min laataaki bana maɓɓe , ngam Allah neli min . Min ɗon mbolwa bee ɓernde laaɓnde yeeso Allah , bana huuwanooɓe Almasiihu .
47003001	Asee ! Min ɗon puɗɗita maŋgtugo ko'e amin na ? Malla min ngoodi haaje bana yimɓe woɗɓe haa min njahrana on bataakeeji anndinirɗi min na , malla min njaɓa irin maaji haa mooɗon na ?
47003002	Onon bee ko'e mon on laati bataakewol anndinirgol min , bindaaŋgol nder ɓerɗe amin . Koomoy to yiɗi , jaŋgan ngol , anndan ngol .
47003003	Fakat , onon on bataakewol Almasiihu , minin min mbindi ngol . Ngol windaaka bee dawa , ammaa bee Ruuhu Allah geeto . Ngol windaaka dow alluhaaje kaa'e , ammaa nder ɓerɗe yimɓe .
47003004	Min ɗon mbi'a ɗum ngam min ɗon kooli Allah ngam daliila Almasiihu .
47003005	Minin bee ko'e amin min ke'aay huuwugo kuugal ngal sam . Baawal amin fuu iwi haa Allah .
47003006	Kaŋko o waawni min anndingo alkawal maako kesal kootoy . Ngal daraaki dow umrooje bindaaɗe , ammaa dow Ruuhu maako . Umrooje bindaaɗe ɗon njahra haa maayde , ammaa Ruuhu ɗon yahra haa ngeendam .
47003007	Umrooje man mbindaama bee karfeeje dow alluhaaje kaa'e . Saa'i maajum tedduŋgal Allah waŋgi . Yeeso Muusa yayni boo , haa yimɓe Isra'iila mbaawaay munyugo jayŋgol man , koo ngol jinnanŋgol . To kuugal umrooje gadduŋgal maayde mari tedduŋgal bana nga'al ,
47003008	nden kam kuugal Ruuhu jahranŋgal haa ngeendam maran tedduŋgal ɓurŋgal mawnugo piw .
47003009	Kuugal gaddanŋgal yimɓe do''eeki kiita maa mari tedduŋgal , sakko kuugal gaddananŋgal ɓe yerduye Allah .
47003010	Fakat , tedduŋgal ɓooymawal fotataa bee tedduŋgal kesal sam , ngal laati bana meere .
47003011	Koo caaliiɗum maa waŋgini tedduŋgal Allah , sakko duumotooɗum haa foroy .
47003012	Ngam daliila tammunde tabinde nde'e min ɗon mbolwa bee dartaare .
47003013	Min mbaɗataa bana Muusa mo wirni yeeso muuɗum bee suddaare , ngam taa yimɓe Isra'iila ngi'a no jayŋgol maago jinnirta .
47003014	Ammaa hakkiilooji maɓɓe mbaawataa faamugo boo . To ɓe ɗon njaŋga bolle alkawal ɓooymawal , suddaare maajum ɗon waali dow maaje haa warugo hande . Nde ittataake , sey to goɗɗo jaɓi Almasiihu .
47003015	Koo jonta boo , koondeye ɓe njaŋgata tawreeta Muusa , suddaare maajum ɗon waali dow hakkiilooji maɓɓe .
47003016	Ammaa ko laatani Muusa , ɗum laatanto ɓe boo , bana ko winda : " To goɗɗo lortake haa Jawmiraawo , suddaare sottan . "
47003017	Mo wi'ete Jawmiraawo haa ɗo , ɗum Ruuhu . Ammaa haa Ruuhu Jawmiraawo woni , ton ndimu woni .
47003018	Enen fuu en ɗon ndaara tedduŋgal bee geese cudditaaɗe , en ɗon mbaŋgina ngal bana daarorgal . Bana ni en ngaylorto haa en nanda bee Jawmiraawo , haa tedduŋgal maako ɓesdano en yeeso yeeso . Kanjum woni kuugal Ruuhu Jawmiraawo nder meeɗen .
47004001	Allah enɗi min , halfini min kuugal nga'al . Ngam maajum min ittataa tammunde sam .
47004002	Min cali kuuɗe cuuɗiiɗe , cemtiniiɗe fuu , min kuuwataa bee dabareeji , min ngaylataa wolde Allah boo . Ammaa min ɗon anndina gooŋga maako laaɓka . Koomoy linyoowo ɓernde mum yeeso Allah , gooŋɗinan min .
47004003	Linjiila ka min ngaajinta , fakat ka suuɗaaki . Ka suuɗoto majjanɓe tan .
47004004	Kamɓe ɓe nuɗɗinaay ka , ngam Sayɗaanu , ɗowanteeɗo duniyaaru ndu wumni hakkiilooji maɓɓe , ngam taa ɓe ngi'a jayŋgol linjiila . Jayŋgol man ɗon waŋgina tedduŋgal Almasiihu . Nder Almasiihu boo , Allah bee hoore mum waŋgata .
47004005	Min ngaajintaa haala ko'e amin , sey haala Yeesu Almasiihu , kaŋko woni Jawmiraawo . Minin kam min huuwanooɓe on ngam daliila Yeesu .
47004006	Ɓooyma Allah wi'i : " Sey annoora yayna nder nyiɓre . " Allah oo acci annoora mum yayna nder ɓerɗe amin boo , ngam haa min annda tedduŋgal Allah ngal waŋgata bana jayŋgol dow yeeso Almasiihu .
47004007	Anndal ngal min keɓi , nandi bee ndesaari . Ammaa minin min nandi bee payanɗe loope , ngam haa koomoy yi'a no baawɗe mawɗe ɗe'e iwi haa Allah , naa haa min .
47004008	Min ɓilliiɓe koonoy , ammaa min timminaaka . Min sakliiɓe nde ɗuuɗɗum , ammaa min ittataa tammunde .
47004009	Konne'en ɗuuɗɓe ɗon toonyo min , ammaa Allah accataa min . Ɓe ɗon ndo''a min haa lesdi , ammaa min kalkaay .
47004010	Foroy min ɗon maata maayde Almasiihu nder ɓalli amin , ngam haa ngeendam maako boo waŋga nder maaji .
47004011	Nder ngeendam amin fuu min ɓadiiɓe maayde ngam daliila Yeesu , haa ngeendam maako boo waŋga nder ɓalli amin maayanɗi .
47004012	Bana wi'ugo : Maayde Yeesu ɗon huuwa nder amin , ammaa ngeendam maako ɗon huuwa nder mooɗon .
47004013	Deftere wi'i : " Mi nuɗɗini Jawmiraawo , ngam maajum mbolwumi . " Nuɗɗinki man iwi haa Ruuhu Allah , minin boo min keɓi ki . Min ɗon nuɗɗini Jawmiraawo , ngam maajum min accataa waajingo linjiila .
47004014	Allah ummitini Jawmiraawo men Yeesu diga maayde . Min anndi o ummitinan min , minin boo , bee Yeesu , o darnan min bee mooɗon yeeso maako .
47004015	Ɗum fuu ɗum laatoto ngam mooɗon , haa mo''ere Allah yotto yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe , limgal maɓɓe ɓesdo yeeso yeeso . Bana ni limgal yettooɓe Allah , teddinooɓe mo ɓesdorto .
47004016	Ngam daliila maajum min ittataa tammunde sam . Fakat , ngeendam ɓalli amin ɗon halka , ammaa ngeendam ɗam Allah hokki min , ɗon hesɗita nyalɗe fuu .
47004017	Fakat , min ɗon nder ɓillaare , ammaa nde hoynde , nde duurataa . Nde waddanan min tedduŋgal duumiiŋgal , maŋgal masin .
47004018	Min tiitataako kuuje gi'eteeɗe , ammaa kuuje ɗe ngi'ataake . Ngam kuuje gi'eteeɗe nduurataa , ammaa kuuje ɗe ngi'ataake , kanje nduumoto .
47005001	Min anndi , to suudu amin jontaaru , waato ɓandu lesdiiru yibbinaama , suudu feere ɗon ngam amin haa asama . Allah bee hoore mum waɗi ndu , ndu duumoto haa foroy .
47005002	Yaake min ɗon njooɗi haa duniyaaru , min ɗon uuma . Min ɗon ngenwa ɓorneego suudu maajum iwndu haa asama .
47005003	Sey min keɓa ɓandu hesru , ngam taa min mbaŋga yeeso Allah min tembuɓe .
47005004	Yaake min ɗon ngeeɗa nder ɓandu lesdiiru , min ɗon uuma , min ɗon ɓillo . Min ngiɗaa ɓortaago ɓandu amin maayanndu , min ngiɗi ɓornaago ɓandu duumiindu dow maaru , ngam haa ngeendam moɗa maayanɗum .
47005005	Koo jonta boo Allah ɗon huuwa nder amin ngam haa ɗum laato bana ni . O hokki min Ruuhu maako bana jiŋgina hayruuji garanɗi .
47005006	Ngam maajum min ɗon tiɗɗina ɓerɗe amin foroy . Min anndi , yaake min ɗon nder ɓandu ndu'u , min daayiiɓe bee Jawmiraawo .
47005007	Min mbaawataa yi'ugo mo tawon , kawtal amin bee maako laati nder nuɗɗinki tan .
47005008	Ammaa min hooliiɓe . Min ɓuri yiɗugo haa min egga e ɓandu ndu'u , min njooɗodo bee Jawmiraawo .
47005009	Ammaa dow maajum fuu min ngiɗi fottango mo , koo min jooɗiiɓe haa ɗo koo min jooɗodiiɓe bee maako .
47005010	Doole en fuu en mbaŋgoya yeeso leeso kiita Almasiihu . Saa'i maajum koomoy meeɗen heɓan mbarjaari deydey kuuɗe mum haa duniyaaru , koo booɗɗe koo kalluɗe .
47005011	Min ngiɗi faamtingo yimɓe ko Jawmiraawo muuyi . Ammaa nyande feere Jawmiraawo ?aman min dow kuugal amin fuu , doole min jaabo mo . Kaŋko o anndi min booɗɗum . Ammaa min tammi onon boo on anndi min nder numooji ɓerɗe mon .
47005012	Min ngiɗaa maŋgtugo ko'e amin yeeso mooɗon fahin . Ammaa min ngiɗi on paama on ngoodi daliila mantoraago min , haa on cukka kunduɗe yimɓe woɗɓe , jurortooɓe kuuje gi'eteeɗe , naa gikku laaɓŋgu .
47005013	To on ndaari min saa'i feere bana min yinnaaɓe , nden kam ɗum haala hakkunde amin bee Allah . Ammaa to min mari hakkiilo , nden kam min mari ngo ngam mooɗon .
47005014	Almasiihu waŋginani en yiide mum . Yiide maajum woni daliila kuuɗe amin fuu . En anndi fakat , to gooto maayi mbattudi yimɓe fuu ,
47005015	nden kam ɓe fuu ɓe laati bana maayɓe . O maayi ngam maɓɓe , ngam maajum ɓe maraay ngeendam maɓɓe , ammaa ɓe ngeeɗan ngam maako , kaŋko maayɗo ngam maɓɓe , ummitinaaɗo nder maayɓe ngam maɓɓe boo .
47005016	Ngam maajum , yeeso ɗo min ndaarataa koo gooto fodde gikku yimɓe . Koo Almasiihu boo , to min meeɗi laarugo mo bana non , yeeso ɗo min meetataa .
47005017	Koomoy hawti bee Almasiihu , laati neɗɗo keso . Ko o laatino ɓooyma , saalake , kooɗume fuu laati kesum .
47005018	Allah huuwi ɗum , o umri min min ngaajina kubaruwol ngo'ol . Naane en laatino konne'en maako , ammaa bee Almasiihu o waɗi sulhu bee meeɗen .
47005019	Ko Almasiihu huuwi , ɗum laati bana kuugal Allah on . O laatini konne'en maako sooba'en maako , o limantaa ɓe aybeeji maɓɓe . O halfini min yeynugo kubar kuugal maako kootoy .
47005020	Ngam maajum min wakiili'en Almasiihu . Allah ɗon wolwana on bee kunduɗe amin . Ngam daliila Almasiihu min ɗon toro on : Njaɓe soobaaku ngu Allah waɗata bee mooɗon .
47005021	Almasiihu waɗaay hakke sam . Ammaa Allah yowi hakkeeji meeɗen fuu dow maako , ngam haa keɓen yerduye Allah nder kawtal bee Almasiihu .
47006001	Minin min huuwdooɓe bee Allah . Ngam maajum min ɗon toro on : On keɓi mo''ere Allah , kakkile ngam taa nde majjira on .
47006002	Ngam o wi'i :
47006003	Min ngiɗaa goɗɗo heɓa felugo kuugal amin . Ngam maajum min ɗon kakkila , taa min kaɗa nuɗɗinki goɗɗo koonoy .
47006004	Ammaa nder kooɗume fuu min ɗon mbaŋgina min huuwanooɓe Allah . Bee munyal ɗuuɗŋgal min ɗon eftira caɗeele e torraaji e ɓillaaje .
47006005	Yimɓe ɓocci min , nastini min nder cuuɗi fursina . Ɓe ummini fitina dow amin . Min comi bee kuuɗe , nde ɗuuɗɗum min keɓaay ɗaanaago , min keɓaay nyaamugo .
47006006	Min ɗon mbaŋgina min huuwanooɓe Allah bee laaɓeeŋga amin e anndal amin , bee munyal e mbooɗeeŋga , bee ballal Ruuhu Ceniiɗo , bee yiide nde walaa naafikaare ,
47006007	bee waaju gooŋga , bee baawɗe Allah . Balmi amin ngam fiyugo konne'en e aynugo ko'e amin , ɗum gooŋgaaku .
47006008	Yimɓe ɗon teddina min , ɓe ɗon njawna min boo . Ɓe ɗon mbolwa booɗɗum dow amin , ɓe ɗon mbolwa kalluɗum boo . Woɗɓe ɗon ndaara min bana fewooɓe , koo min ɗon mbolwa gooŋga .
47006009	Ɓe ɗon mbi'a ɓe anndaa min , ammaa fakat koomoy anndi min . Ɓe ɗon ndaara min bana maayɓe , ammaa ndaa , min ɗon ngeeɗi . Ɓe ɗon ɓocca min , ammaa ɓe mbaraay min tawon .
47006010	Ɓe ɗon cuna min , ammaa min ɗon ceyi foroy . Min nandi bee talaka'en , ammaa min ɗon ndiskina ɗuuɗɓe . Min laati bana min ngalaa kooɗume , ammaa fakat min ɗon mari kooɗume fuu .
47006011	Onon Korintu'en , min mbolwani on bee dartaare . Min maɓɓitani on ɓerɗe amin jaasɗum .
47006012	Min maɓɓanaay on ɗe , ammaa onon on maɓɓani min ɓerɗe mooɗon .
47006013	Mi ɗon wolwana on bana ɓikkoy am . Kuuwane min bana min kuuwranta on , maɓɓite ɓerɗe mon jaasɗum .
47006014	Taa laate huuwdooɓe bee yimɓe ɓe nuɗɗinaay Jawmiraawo , kawtal maajum fottaay . Noy gooŋgaaku hawtirta bee halleende , malla annoora bee nyiɓre ?
47006015	Almasiihu e Sayɗaanu mbaawataa narrugo . To non kam , noy nuɗɗinɗo narrata bee mo nuɗɗinaay ?
47006016	Ɗume hawtata haykaliiru Allah bee labbi ? Fakat enen en haykaliiru Allah geeto , ngam Allah wi'i :
47006017	Ngam maajum o wi'i boo :
47006018	mi laatoto baaba mon ,
47007001	Soobiraaɓe am , bolle Allah ɗe'e fuu laatani en . Ngam maajum en laɓɓinu ko'e men , en ittu ko soɓnata ɓandu malla ruuhu . Sey en laato senaaɓe timmuɓe , en hulɓe Allah .
47007002	Maɓɓitane min ɓerɗe mon . Min mbaɗaay koo gooto mon aybefe , min mbonnaay koo gooto mon , min koocaay maral goɗɗo bee ?oyre .
47007003	Mi wi'aay ɗum haa mi hiito on . Mi aarti wi'ugo , ɓerɗe amin maɓɓitani on ngam haa en ngonda koo nder maayde koo nder ngeendam .
47007004	Mi ɗon hooli on laaɓɗum , mi ɗon mantoro on ɗuuɗɗum . Nder ɓillaaje amin fuu mi ɗon heewi de'ere e seyo .
47007005	Koo wakkati min njotti Makedoniya boo , min keɓaay siwtaago sam . Saklere laatani min kootoy , jokkirli bee yimɓe woɗɓe , kulol boo nder ɓerɗe amin .
47007006	Ammaa Allah , de'itinoowo sakliiɓe , de'itini min bee garki Titus .
47007007	Naa garki maako tan de'itini min , ammaa o yecci min boo no on nde'itiniri mo . O yecci min on ɗon ngenwa yi'ugo yam , on ɗon mimsito ko waɗi , on ɗon tiino wallugo yam boo . Kanjum ɗum seyni yam masin .
47007008	Bataakewol am suni on , ammaa mi mimsitaaki windugo ngol . Aran , nde ngi'mi no ngol suniri on , mi ɓadakeno mimsitaago .
47007009	Ammaa jonta kam mi ɗon seyo . Fakat mi seyoraaki sunugo on , ammaa suno mon tuubni on . Allah huuwtiniri suno mon ngam hayru , ngam maajum min mbaɗaay on sarru .
47007010	Ngam suno ngo Allah huuwtinirta ɗum , laatinan tuubu , tuubu boo waddan kisndam . Nder suno bana ngo'o , mimsitaare woodaa . Ammaa suno fodde gikku duniyaaru yahran haa maayde .
47007011	Ndaare ko Allah laatini bee suno mon : On ɗon tiino masin , on ɗon ɗaɓɓa laɓɓingo ko'e mon e aybe . Hakkiilooji mon ummi , kulol mon ɗuuɗi , on ɗon ngenwammi , on ɗon tiino hiitaago halleende . Bee maajum fuu on mbaŋgini ko'e mon on laaɓɓe nder haala ka'a .
47007012	Mi windaay bataakewol go ngam daliila baɗɗo aybe malla ngam baɗaaɗo aybe . Ammaa mi windi ngol haa on paama , haa on mbaŋgina yeeso Allah boo no on tiinorto ngam amin .
47007013	Kanjum mbaɗɗon , ngam maajum min nde'iti .
47007014	Mi mantorino on yeeso maako , onon boo on cemtinaay yam . Foroy min mbolwani on gooŋga . Bana non boo ko min mantori on yeeso Titus , ɗum laati gooŋga .
47007015	Yiide maako haa mooɗon ɗon ɓesdo , koondeye o siftorta no on njaɓɓori mo bee kulol e diwŋgol , no on ɗowtorani umrooje am fuu .
47007016	Walaa ko haɗatammi hoolaago on , kanjum mi seyorto .
47008001	Deerɗiraaɓe , min ngiɗi anndingo on ko mo''ere Allah huuwi nder jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en haa lesdi Makedoniya .
47008002	Nuɗɗinki maɓɓe foondaama bee ɓillaaje ɗuuɗɗe , ammaa ɓe ngoodi seyo maŋgo masin . Ngam maajum , koo ɓe talaka'en boo , ɓe mooɓti dokke ɗuuɗɗe .
47008003	Mi ɗon seedano ɓe ɓe ndokki ko ɓe mbaawi , fakat ko ɓuri baawɗe maɓɓe , ɓe ndokki bee muuyo maɓɓe boo .
47008004	Ɓe tori min ɗuuɗɗum haa ɓe keɓa duŋgaye hawtugo bee woɗɓe nder walliinde ngam yimɓe Allah haa lesdi Yahudiya .
47008005	Ɓe kuuwi ko ɓuri tammunde amin . Ɓe aarti ɓe ndokki ko'e maɓɓe haa Jawmiraawo , nden bee muuyo Allah haa amin boo .
47008006	Ngam maajum min tiɗɗini Titus haa o suklano kuugal ngal caka mooɗon . Kaŋko o fuɗɗi ngal , jonta o walla on timmingo ngal bee caahaaki .
47008007	Onon on feesiiɓe nder kooɗume fuu , on ngoodi nuɗɗinki e baawal wolde e anndal e tiinaare e yiide hedi amin . Min ngiɗi on laato feesiiɓe nder kuugal nga'al boo .
47008008	Mi wi'aay on ɗum bana umroore . Ammaa bee kubar tiinaare woɗɓe ngiɗmi foondugo laaɓeeŋga yiide mon .
47008009	On anndi mo''ere nde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu waɗani on . Koo o diskuɗo , o wartiri hoore maako o talakaajo ngam daliila mooɗon , haa o riskina on bee talakaaku maako .
47008010	Mi yecci on ko mi numata . Mi tammi ɗum nafan on to on timmini ko puɗɗuɗon . Diga rowani on mbaɗi anniya , on puɗɗi kuugal man boo .
47008011	Jonta kam , timmine ngal . On tiini waɗugo anniya , bana non boo tiine timmingo ɗum . Ndokke fodde baawɗe mon .
47008012	To on tiinake hokkugo , Allah jaɓan dokkal mon . O ɗon ?ama ko on mari , naa ko on maraay .
47008013	Mi wi'aay on laato talaka'en ngam haa woɗɓe poofta . Ammaa mi yiɗi fotingo on bee maɓɓe .
47008014	Jonta ɗum fottan onon on mballa ɓe nder haaje maɓɓe . Yeeso ɗo , to onon on ɓillake , kamɓe ɓe mballa on . Bana ni potuki laatorto ,
47008015	bana ko winda :
47008016	Min ɗon ngetta Allah baɗɗo tiinaare amin nde'e nder ɓernde Titus boo ngam haa o walla on .
47008017	Titus jaɓi tornde amin . Naa kanjum tan , ammaa ngam daliila tiinaare maako o waɗi anniya yahugo haa mooɗon .
47008018	Hawtaade bee maako min neli deerɗiraawo mo nuɗɗinɓe fuu teddinta ngam waaju linjiila .
47008019	Jama'aaje haa ɗo cuɓi mo ngam haa o ɗofta min saa'i min njahrata dokkal go haa Yahudiya . Min ɗon kuuwa ɗum haa min teddina Jawmiraawo , min mbaŋgina anniya amin boo .
47008020	Min ɗon kakkila no min njogorto dokkal maŋgal nga'al , ngam taa goɗɗo heɓa felugo min .
47008021	Min ngiɗi huuwugo ko fotti , naa yeeso Jawmiraawo tan , ammaa yeeso yimɓe boo .
47008022	Min nelan deerɗiraawo goɗɗo bee maɓɓe . Min poondi tiinaare maako nde ɗuuɗɗum , min tawi o tiiniiɗo foroy . Jonta boo o ɓesdi tiinaago , ngam o ɗon hooli on ɗuuɗɗum .
47008023	Titus woni kawtiɗɗiraawo am , kuuwdoowo bee am ngam hayru mooɗon . Deerɗiraaɓe yahdanɓe bee maako , kamɓe ngoni nelaaɓe jama'aaje , ɓe teddinooɓe Almasiihu .
47008024	Kolle ɓe yiide mon . Nden kam nuɗɗinɓe fuu anndan fakat min mantoraaki on meere .
47009001	Walaa haaje mi windana on dow walliinde ngam yimɓe Allah haa lesdi Yahudiya .
47009002	Mi anndi on muuyi wallugo ɓe . Mi mantori on haa Makedoniya'en boo , mi wi'i : " Deerɗiraaɓe nder Akaya ɗon mooɓta dokkal man diga rowani . " Tiinaare mon findini ɗuuɗɓe maɓɓe .
47009003	Jonta nelanmi deerɗiraaɓe go ngam taa manoore amin dow mooɗon laato meere . Mi yiɗi walliinde mon taasko fakat bana mbi'mi .
47009004	Ngam to Makedoniya'en ngardi bee am , tawi on mooɓtaay dokkal man , doole min cemtira hoolaare amin , sakkoma onon on cemtan !
47009005	Ngam maajum mi laari ɗum bana doole mi toro deerɗiraaɓe go aarta min yahugo haa mooɗon , ɓe mooɓta dokkal ngal mbi'ɗon diga naane , ngal taasko hiddeko min ngara , ngal waŋga ngal caahu fakat , naa ngal jomorgol .
47009006	Ciftore ɗu'um : Aawɗo peetum , peetum sodata , aawɗo ɗuuɗɗum boo , ɗuuɗɗum sodata .
47009007	Koomoy hokka deydey anniya ɓernde mum , naa bee mimsitaare malla bee doole . Ngam Allah ɗon yiɗi dokkanɗo bee seyo .
47009008	Allah waawan ɗuɗɗinango on mo''e fuu , naa deydey haaje mon tan , ammaa haa on mboonana woɗɓe boo bee caahaaki .
47009009	Bana ko winda :
47009010	Allah dokkanɗo aawoowo aawdi e nyaamdu , hokkan on aawdi deydey haaje mon , fuɗnan ndi , haa caahu mon waɗa nafuda ɗuuɗka .
47009011	O riskinan on haa on laato saahiiɓe foroy , haa ɗuuɗɓe ngetta Allah ngam dokke mon ɗe min njahranta ɓe .
47009012	Fakat , dokkal mon wallan yimɓe Allah nder haaje muuɗum'en . Ammaa ko ɓuri ɗum , ngal ɗuɗɗinan gettooje haa Allah .
47009013	To dokkal maajum waŋgini gooŋgaaku mon , nden kam ɓe teddinan Allah , ngam on ɗowtani seedamku linjiila Almasiihu , on cendi hayruuji mon boo bee maɓɓe e bee yimɓe fuu .
47009014	To ɓe ngi'i no mo''ere Allah ɗuuɗirani on , ɓe ndo'anto on , ɓe ngenwan on masin .
47009015	Dow maajum fuu , ngetten Allah ngam dokkal muuɗum , ngal tindintaake .
47010001	Too , min Pol mi yiɗi wolwango on haala hoore am jonta . Woɗɓe ɗon mbi'a mi leesɗo saa'i mi ɗon wondi bee mooɗon , ammaa mi cembiɗɗo dow mooɗon saa'i mi daayiiɗo . Mi ɗon toro on bee yaŋkinaare Almasiihu e mbooɗeeŋga muuɗum :
47010002	Taa ndooleeɗam hollugo on sembe am to mi wari haa mooɗon . Kamɓe ɓe mbi'i min ɗon kuuwa fodde gikku duniyaaru . Mi anndi mi he'i hollugo ɓe sembe am .
47010003	Fakat , minin min yimɓe , ammaa min kaɓataa bana yimɓe .
47010004	Nder haɓre amin min kuuwtinirtaa balmi duniyaaru , sey balmi Allah cembiɗɗi . Bee maaji min ɗon ngibbina mahi . Min ɗon ndo''a numooji fewre ,
47010005	min ɗon ngibbina mawnitaare fuu nde luuti anndal Allah . Min ɗon ngartira numooji fuu naŋgaaɗi , haa ɗi ɗowtano Almasiihu .
47010006	Min taaskiiɓe hiitaago geddal fuu , to on laatake on timmuɓe nder ɗowtaare .
47010007	Ndaare le ko waŋgani gite mon . To goɗɗo limi hoore mum nder yimɓe Almasiihu , sey o numta kadi , ngam minin boo min yimɓe Almasiihu .
47010008	Walaa daliila mi semta , koo to mi ɗuɗɗini mantoraago baawɗe ɗe Jawmiraawo hokki min . Ammaa min keɓi baawɗe man haa min mbo''ina on , naa ngam min mbonna on .
47010009	Mi yiɗaa on numa mi ɗon ɗaɓɓita hulnugo on bee bataakeeji am .
47010010	Ngam woɗɓe ɗon mbi'a : " Bataakeeji Pol tedduɗi , cembiɗɗi . Ammaa to o ɗon wondi bee meeɗen , o tampuɗo , bolle maako boo meereeje . "
47010011	Koomoy numi bana ni , ndaa ko mi wi'ata mo : Bana no bataakeeji amin mba'i saa'i min daayiiɓe , bana non kuuɗe amin boo mba'i saa'i min ngondan bee mooɗon .
47010012	Fakat , min potaay nandingo ko'e amin bee maŋgtanɓe ko'e muuɗum'en . Kamɓe ɓe ɗon poondira ko'e maɓɓe bee poondirɗum maɓɓe , ɓe ɗon nandinira ko'e maɓɓe bee ko'e maɓɓe boo . Kayto , ɓe faataaɓe !
47010013	Minin kam min mantataako bana ni , min caalataako keerol ngol Allah waɗani min . O yottini min bee linjiila Almasiihu haa mooɗon . Kanjum woni keerol juro amin .
47010014	To min mantorake ɗum , min caalaaki keerol , ngam fakat min njotti haa mooɗon bee linjiila Almasiihu .
47010015	Min njurataako meere bee kuugal yimɓe woɗɓe . Ammaa min ɗon tammi , to nuɗɗinki mon ɓesdake , maŋgu amin boo ɓesdoto caka mooɗon . Bee non fuu min caalaaki keerol ngol Allah waɗani min .
47010016	Teema yeeso ɗo min keɓan waajingo linjiila nder lesɗe gaɗa mooɗon . Walaa haaje min njuroro kuugal ngal goɗɗo feere aarti huuwugo nder ngesa muuɗum .
47010017	Deftere wi'i : " To goɗɗo yiɗi mantaago , sey o mantoro kuugal Jawmiraawo . "
47010018	Goɗɗo laatoto gerdaaɗo to Jawmiraawo maŋgti mo , naa to o maŋgti hoore maako .
47011001	Ko ngiɗmi kam , haa on munyanammi , koo to mi laatake paataaɗo seɗɗa . Useni munyaneeɗam mi maŋgta hoore am jonta .
47011002	Mi ɗon haaja on bee kaajal bana ngal Allah . On laati bana paanyo debbo mo kaɓɓanmi gorko gooto tan , waato Almasiihu . Mi yiɗi mi yahrana mo paanyo man o laaɓɗo .
47011003	On anndi no mboodi estiri Hawwa bee ?oyre mum . Mi ɗon hula hakkiilooji mooɗon , taa mbonno bana non , haa on acca yiɗugo Almasiihu bee laaɓeeŋga e ɓernde woore .
47011004	Ngam to goɗɗo wari haa mooɗon , waaji on Yeesu feere mo min ngaajaay , on munyanan mo bee koyɗum . On njaɓan ruuhu feere ngu on njaɓaayno haa amin , on njaɓan linjiila feere boo ka on nanaayno haa amin .
47011005	Mi anndi fakat mi tullaay nelaaɓe mon hayniiɓe sam .
47011006	Teema mi laataaki wela-ɗemŋgaljo , ammaa mi marɗo anndal , mi waŋginani on ngal koondey e koonoy .
47011007	Nde ngaajumi on linjiila , mi ɗaɓɓaay ngeenaari haa mooɗon , mi leesni hoore am ngam haa on ɓaŋgo . Kadi bee maajum mbaɗmi on aybe na ?
47011008	Yaake mi ɗonno huuwa haa mooɗon , mi jaɓi ngeenaari haa jama'aaje goɗɗe , fakat mi ɓilli ɗe ngam daliila mooɗon .
47011009	Yaake mi ɗonno wondi bee mooɗon , nde mi ɓilliiɗo , mi teddanaay koo gooto mon . Ngam deerɗiraaɓe warɓe diga Makedoniya kumtani yam haaje am fuu . Mi yiɗaano teddango on nder kooɗume . Koo yeeso ɗo boo mi yiɗaa .
47011010	Bee gooŋga Almasiihu ngonka nder am mbi'anmi on : Walaa koo gooto nder Akaya fuu jaɓtatammi juro am ngo'o .
47011011	Ngam ɗume mbi'mi ɗum ? Ngam mi yiɗaa on na ? Aa'a , Allah anndi mi yiɗi on !
47011012	Ko kuuwanmi jonta , mi tokkoto huuwugo ɗum . Kanjum ngam taa nelaaɓe hayniiɓe go keɓa daliila juraago , taa ɓe mbi'a ɓe ɗon kuuwa kal kal bee am .
47011013	Kamɓe ɓe laataaki nelaaɓe bee gooŋga , ɓe fewooɓe , waɗooɓe rikisi , ɓe mbaɗi ko'e maɓɓe bana ɓe nelaaɓe Almasiihu .
47011014	Kanjum ɗum walaa kaayeefi , ngam Sayɗaanu boo ɗon waɗa hoore mum bana o malaa'ikaajo annoora .
47011015	Ngam maajum naa ɗum kayniiɗum to wallooɓe mo ɗon mbaɗa ko'e muuɗum'en bana ɓe huuwanooɓe gooŋga . Ammaa haa timmoode ɓe keɓan kiita deydey kuuɗe maɓɓe .
47011016	Sey mi wi'a ɗum fahin : Taa goɗɗo laarammi bana mi paataaɗo . Ammaa to on ngiɗi laarugo yam bana non , nden kam njaɓeeɗam bana mi paataaɗo , haa min boo mi juro seɗɗa .
47011017	Fakat , ko mbolwanmi jonta , ɗum fottanaay Jawmiraawo . To mi jaɓi juraago , mi wolwan bana mi walaa hakkiilo .
47011018	Ammaa ndaa , ɗuuɗɓe ɗon njuroro ɓural muuɗum'en haa duniyaaru . Ngam maajum min boo mi fuɗɗan juraago .
47011019	Onon kam on hakkilɓe , ngam maajum on ɗon munyana faataaɓe bee seyo .
47011020	On ɗon munyana koomoy toonyi on , nyaami on , naŋgi on bee tuuforgol , yawi on , maari on .
47011021	Mi ɗon semta wi'ugo ɗum : Nder kuuɗe bana ɗe'e min tampuɓe .
47011022	Ɓe Ibraniŋko'en na ? Min boo nonnon . Ɓe Isra'iila'en na ? Min boo nonnon . Ɓe asŋgol Ibrahiima na ? Min boo nonnon .
47011023	Ɓe huuwanooɓe Almasiihu na ? Sey mi wolwa bana mi ginnaaɗo : Mi ɓuri ɓe nder kuugal maajum . Mi ɓuri ɓe tiinaago . Mi ɓuri ɓe nastineego nder cuuɗi fursina . Mi ɓuri ɓe ɓocceego . Mi ɓuri ɓe nastugo joote maayde .
47011024	Nde jowi Yahuudu'en ɓocci yam ɓocci cappanɗe tati e joweenayi .
47011025	Nde tati Roma'en paɗɗi yam bee cabbi . Nde woore yimɓe piɗi yam bee kaa'e . Nde tati koombowal yooli bee am , nde woore mi jooɗi jemmaare e nyalawmaare nder ndiyam .
47011026	Mi waɗi jahaale ɗuuɗɗe . Mi yari bone nder maaje . Fasooɓe purkiti yam . Yimɓe lenyol am e heefeerɓe toonyi yam . Mi yari bone nder gure , nder laɗɗe , nder mbeela , caka deerɗiraaɓe fewooɓe boo .
47011027	Mi munyani torra e ɓillaare . Nde ɗuuɗɗum mi heɓaay ɗaanaago , nde ɗuuɗɗum nanmi weelo e ɗomka . Nde ɗuuɗɗum mi heɓaay nyaamdu sam , jaaŋgol torri yam , mi walaa limce boo .
47011028	Taa mi limta kuuje goɗɗe , ammaa woodi ko ɓuri ɓillugo yam nyalɗe fuu , ɗum suklanaago jama'aaje fuu .
47011029	To goɗɗo maati tampere , min boo mi maatan nde . To goɗɗo do''ake , waɗi aybe , ɓernde am naawan masin .
47011030	To doole mi juro , nden kam mi jurorto tampere am .
47011031	Allah , Baabiraawo Jawmiraawo men Yeesu anndi mi fewataa . Yettoore laatano mo haa foroy !
47011032	Saa'i mi ɗonno haa Damas , kaliifaajo laamiiɗo Aretas jo''ini aynooɓe haa dammuɗe berniwol haa ɓe naŋgammi .
47011033	Ammaa deerɗiraaɓe ndirtini yam nder silaawo haa wurdere mahol taariiŋgol berniwol . Bana ni kisrumi juuɗe kaliifaajo .
47012001	Doole mi juro , koo to ɗum nafaay goɗɗo sam . Sey mi wolwa haala kaayeefiiji ɗi Jawmiraawo yi'ni yam , e wahayuuji ɗi o hokki yam .
47012002	Mi anndi goɗɗo Masiihiŋkeejo . Waɗi duuɓi sappo e nayi jonta , kaŋko o eeŋgtinaama haa asamawu tataɓu . Koo ɗum laati bee ɓandu , koo Jawmiraawo yi'ni mo ɗum , mi anndaa , sey Allah tan anndi ɗum .
47012003	Mi anndi fakat , goɗɗo oo eeŋgtinaama haa aljanna . Koo ɗum laati bee ɓandu , koo Jawmiraawo yi'ni mo ɗum , mi anndaa , sey Allah tan anndi ɗum .
47012004	Ton haa aljanna o nani bolle sirriije ɗe neɗɗo fotaay wolwugo .
47012005	Goɗɗo oo njurortoomi , ammaa mi jurortaako hoore am , sonaa tampere am .
47012006	Koo to mi yiɗi juraago , naa mi paataaɗo , ngam mi wi'an gooŋga . Ammaa mi yiɗaa juraago , ngam taa goɗɗo ɓurnammi dow ko o yi'i haa am malla ko o nani haa am .
47012007	Mi yi'i kaayeefiiji ɗi tindintaake . Ammaa ngam taa mi mawnito bee maaji , Allah hokki yam ko naawatammi bana gi'al , ɗum bana nelaaɗo Sayɗaanu mo faɗɗatammi ngam taa mi mawnito .
47012008	Nde tati toriimi Jawmiraawo haa o ittanammi ɗum .
47012009	Ammaa o jaabi yam : " Mo''ere am he'an haaje ma fuu . Yaake a tampuɗo , baawɗe am ɓuran huuwugo nder maaɗa . " Jonta munyananmi tampe am bee seyo , mi ɗon juroro ɗe boo , ngam haa baawɗe Almasiihu ngonda bee am .
47012010	Ngam maajum ceyortoomi tampe am , mi seyoto to yimɓe kuɗi yam , toonyi yam , to cakle e ɓillaaje keɓi yam ngam daliila Almasiihu . Ngam yaake mi tampuɗo , yaake maajum mi cembiɗɗo .
47012011	Fakat , mi wolwi bana mi paataaɗo , ammaa on ndooli yam wolwugo bana non . Ngam onon on ceedanaaki yam bana no haandi . Koo to mi laataaki kooɗume , mi tullaay nelaaɓe mon hayniiɓe sam .
47012012	Kuuɗe anndinooje nelaaɗo fuu laati caka mooɗon , mi holli on munyal timmuŋgal , mi huuwi kaayeefiiji e kuuɗe baawɗe .
47012013	Woodi ko mi huuwani jama'aaje goɗɗe , mi huuwanaay on ɗum na ? Mi ɗaɓɓaay on kumtanammi haaje am . Njaafaneeɗam aybewol ngo'ol !
47012014	Jonta taaskiimi warugo haa mooɗon tataɓre . To mi wari , mi teddantaa on . Onon ɗaɓɓanmi , naa ceede mon . Fakat , ɓikkoy nyaamnataa saarooji , ammaa saarooji nyaamnan ɓikkoy .
47012015	To min kam , bee seyo ndokkanmi ko marmi fuu , koo hoore am boo , ngam haa mi walla on . Kadi on pamɗitinan yiɗugo yam ngam mi ɓuri yiɗugo on na ?
47012016	Walaa ngaaba , mi teddanaay on . Ammaa teema goɗɗo wi'an mi ?oyri on , mi naŋgi on bee dabare .
47012017	Woodi nelaaɓe am mi neli ngam jaɓtugo kuuje mon na ?
47012018	Mi nelno Titus e deerɗiraawo goɗɗo haa mooɗon . Kadi Titus jaɓti on na ? Na minin ɗiɗo min ɗon kuuwa bee anniya ngoota , min ɗon tokko laawol gootol na ?
47012019	Teema on ɗon numa diga ɓooyma , min ngiɗi laɓɓingo ko'e amin yeeso mooɗon . Naa non sam ! Min ɗon mbolwa yeeso Allah bana yimɓe Almasiihu . Deerɗiraaɓe yiɗaaɓe , min ɗon mbi'a ɗum fuu ngam haa min mawnina on nder nuɗɗinki .
47012020	Mi ɗon hula , saa'i ngaranmi haa mooɗon mi tawataa on bana no ngiɗmi , onon boo on tawataa yam bana no ngiɗɗon . Mi ɗon hula mi tawan jokkirli e kaajal e ɓernuki e ciɗotiral e bolle kalluɗe e tufle e mawnitaare e fitinaaji .
47012021	To mi wari haa mooɗon kadiboo , mi yiɗaa Allah am leestinammi , haa mi woya dow ɗuuɗɓe waɗnooɓe hakke , ngam ɓe tuubaay , ɓe accaay waɗugo coɓɗum e njeenu e daakaareeku .
47013001	Mi ɗon wara haa mooɗon tataɓre . Deftere wi'i : " Sey wullaandu fuu daro dow seedamku seedooɓe ɗiɗo malla tato . "
47013002	Waɗɓe hakke caka mooɗon e luttuɓe fuu mbi'anmi fahin ko mbi'noomi yaake mi ɗonno wondi bee mooɗon ɗiɗawre . To mi wari fahin , mi hiitoto ɓe fakat .
47013003	On keɓan seedamku ngu ɗaɓɓititton , on paaman Almasiihu ɗon wolwa bee hunduko am . Kaŋko naa o tampuɗo haa mooɗon , ammaa o waŋginan baawɗe maako nder mooɗon .
47013004	Saa'i o maayi haa leggal gaafaaŋgal , saa'i maajum o tampuɗo . Ammaa jonta o geeto bee baawɗe Allah . Ngam daliila kawtal amin bee Almasiihu minin boo min tampuɓe . Ammaa on ngi'an min yeeɗɓe bee maako ngam daliila baawɗe Allah .
47013005	Linye ko'e mon kadi . On ɗon tabiti nder nuɗɗinki na ? Sey on keɓta ɗum bee ko'e mon . On anndi Yeesu Almasiihu ɗon wondi bee mooɗon na ? To naa non , on ndo''ake .
47013006	Ammaa mi ɗon hooli on anndan minin min ndo''aaki .
47013007	Min ɗon toro Allah ngam taa on kuuwa kalluɗum . Min ɗaɓɓataa tabitingo gooŋga amin , ammaa min ngiɗi on kuuwa ko fotti , koo to minin min laatake bana min do''iiɓe .
47013008	Min mbaawataa honugo gooŋga , sey huuwango ka .
47013009	Min ɗon ceyo to minin min tampuɓe , ammaa onon on sembiɗɓe . Ngam maajum min ɗon toro Allah boo haa on laato timmuɓe .
47013010	Mi ɗon windana on kuuje ɗe'e fuu saa'i mi daayiiɗo tawon . Ngam to mi wari , mi yiɗaa saatango on bee baawɗe ɗe Jawmiraawo hokki yam . Mi heɓaay baawɗe man haa mi yibbina on , sey ngam mi tabitina on .
47013011	Too , deerɗiraaɓe , njooɗe jam . Tiine haa on laato timmuɓe , njaɓe bolle am haa ɓerɗe mon . Njooɗode bee narral e hoolaare . Nden kam Allah , dokkoowo en yiide e jam , wondan bee mooɗon .
47013012	Koofnindire bee harlotirgo . Yimɓe Allah fuu koofni on .
47013013	
47013014	Mo''ere Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , e yiide Allah , e kawtal Ruuhu Ceniiɗo wondu bee mooɗon fuu .
48001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , nelaaɗo . Mi laataaki nelaaɗo bee muuyo yimɓe malla dow hunduko neɗɗo , ammaa bee umroore Yeesu Almasiihu e Allah Baabiraawo , ummitinɗo Yeesu nder maayɓe .
48001002	Deerɗiraaɓe wonduɓe bee am fuu kawti bee am haa min nelda koofli amin haa jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en nder lesdi Galaatiya .
48001003	Allah , Baabiraawo men , e Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men ndokka on mo''ere e jam .
48001004	Almasiihu hokki hoore mum ngam daliila hakkeeji men , ngam haa o hisna en jamanuuru hallundu ndu'u . Bana ni o huuwri muuyo Allah , Baabiraawo men .
48001005	Tedduŋgal laatano Allah haa abada abadin . Aamiina !
48001006	Mi ɗon hayɗina on . Bee linjiila Allah ewnori on haa on ngeeɗa bee mo''ere Almasiihu . Ammaa law on acci mo , on ngayliti haa linjiila feere .
48001007	Fakat , linjiila feere woodaa . Ammaa woodi yimɓe woɗɓe , saklinɓe on . Ɓe ɗon ɗaɓɓa waylugo linjiila Almasiihu .
48001008	Ammaa to goɗɗo , koo min , koo malaa'ikaajo iwɗo haa asama boo waaji on linjiila feere , luutka ka min ngaaji on , nden kam naaloore Allah ukkano mo !
48001009	Mi meeɗi wi'ugo on ɗum , sey mi wi'a ɗum fahin : To goɗɗo waaji on linjiila feere , luutka ka njaɓɗon , nden kam naaloore Allah ukkano mo !
48001010	Kadi mi yiɗi yerdingo yimɓe na ? Woodaa ! Mi ɗon ɗaɓɓa yerduye Allah . Malla mi ɗon ɗaɓɓa fottango yimɓe ? Nden kam naa mi maccuɗo Almasiihu .
48001011	Onon deerɗam'en , sey mi faamtina on : Linjiila ka ngaajinmi , iwaay haa numooji yimɓe .
48001012	Mi jaɓaay ka haa neɗɗo , walaa neɗɗo anndini yam ka . Ammaa Yeesu Almasiihu waŋgani yam , anndini yam ka .
48001013	On meeɗi nanugo no tokkoriimi diina Yahuudu'en ɓooyma . Mi ɗonno toonyo jama'aaje yimɓe Allah bilaa enɗam , haa mi halka ɗe .
48001014	Mi ɗonno ɗowtano farillaaji tawreeta e umrooje kaakaaji am bee tiinaare ko ɓuri ngorgiraaɓe am fuu .
48001015	Ammaa Allah enɗi yam , suɓi yam diga mi siwa danyeego . O ewni yam haa mi huuwana mo . Nde ɗum fottani mo ,
48001016	o waŋginani yam Ɓiɗɗo maako , haa mi waajina kubar maako nder ummaatooje . Saa'i maajum mi sarwotiraay bee neɗɗo ,
48001017	mi yahaay Urusaliima boo haa mi yiida bee nelaaɓe aartuɓe yam , ammaa mi yaawɗi yahugo lesdi Arabiya , diga ton mi lorti haa Damasfa .
48001018	Mi munyi duuɓi tati , nden mi yehi Urusaliima haa mi yiida bee Piyer . Mi jooɗodi bee maako asaweeje ɗiɗi .
48001019	Mi yi'aay nelaaɓe ton , sey Yakuba , deerɗu Jawmiraawo .
48001020	Ko mbindanmi on ɗum gooŋga , Allah anndi mi fewataa .
48001021	Ɓaawo maajum mi yehi lesdi Siriya e lesdi Silikiya .
48001022	Yaake man , jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en nder Yahudiya anndaano yam .
48001023	Ammaa ɓe nani ko woɗɓe mbi'i : " Toonyiiɗo en naane , jonta o ɗon waajina nuɗɗinki ki o ɗaɓɓuno halkugo . "
48001024	Ɓe teddini Allah ngam daliila am .
48002001	Ɓaawo duuɓi sappo e nayi njahmi Urusaliima fahin . Barnabas yahdi bee am , mi hoo'i boo Titus bee am .
48002002	Mi yehi ton ngam daliila wahayu ngu Allah hokki yam . Mi hawti bee mawɓe jama'aare , mi yecci ɓe linjiila bana no ngaajiranmi ka nder ummaatooje . Ngam mi yiɗaa kuugal am laato meere , koo aartuŋgal koo jontawal .
48002003	Soobaajo am Titus o Yunaniŋkeejo , ammaa ɓe ndoolaay mo juulnaago .
48002004	Woodino deerɗiraaɓe naafiki'en , nastuɓe jama'aare bee dabare . Kamɓe ɓe ɗaɓɓi linyugo ndimu amin nder kawtal bee Almasiihu , ɓe ɗaɓɓi wartirgo min maccuɓe tawreeta boo .
48002005	Ammaa min ɗowtanaaki ɓe koo tis , ngam haa gooŋga linjiila tabitana on .
48002006	Wi'eteeɓe mawɓe go - fakat , ko ɓe laatino ɓooyma , walaa ko yaali yam , ngam Allah sendindirtaa yimɓe . Wi'eteeɓe mawɓe go njowanaay yam kooɗume .
48002007	Ɓe paami Allah halfini yam waaju linjiila nder ummaatooje saadooni'en , bana no o halfiniri Piyer waaju linjiila caka Yahuudu'en .
48002008	Allah tabitini Piyer o nelaaɗo caka Yahuudu'en , bana non boo o tabitini yam mi nelaaɗo haa ummaatooje goɗɗe .
48002009	Yakuba e Piyer e Yuhanna , laareteeɓe bana daŋraŋge nder jama'aare , annditi mo''ere nde Allah hokki yam bee kuugal ngal . Ngam maajum ɓe ndokki min , min e Barnabas , juŋŋgo narral , ngam haa minin min kuuwa nder ummaatooje goɗɗe , kamɓe boo caka Yahuudu'en .
48002010	Ammaa ɓe tori min min ciftora talaka'en nder jama'aare Urusaliima . Kanjum min tiini huuwugo ɗum .
48002011	Nde Piyer wari haa Antakiya , mi feli mo gite yimɓe , ngam o waɗno aybe .
48002012	Aran o nyaamdunooɗo bee deerɗiraaɓe ɓe njuulnaaki . Nden yimɓe Yakuba woɗɓe ngari , ɓe samɗinooɓe juulnol masin . Piyer huli ɓe . Ngam maajum o seedi bee deerɗiraaɓe go , o acci nyaamdugo bee maɓɓe .
48002013	Deerɗiraaɓe Yahuudu'en woɗɓe haa Antakiya mbaɗi naafikaare bana Piyer , koo Barnabas boo fuɗɗi hulugo , tokki naafikaare man .
48002014	Nde ngi'mi ɓe ɗon cela gooŋga linjiila , mi wi'i Piyer yeeso yimɓe fuu : " An a Yahuuduujo , ammaa haa ɗo a jooɗi bana a goɗɗo ummaatooje . Jonta boo a yiɗi doolugo yimɓe ummaatooje haa ɓe laato bana Yahuudu'en na ? "
48002015	Fakat , enen en danyaaɓe nder Yahuudu'en , naa en yimɓe ummaatooje ɓe anndaa tawreeta .
48002016	Ammaa en anndi walaa mo heɓata yerduye Allah bee ɗowtanaago tawreeta , sey bee nuɗɗingo Yeesu Almasiihu . Enen boo en nuɗɗini Yeesu Almasiihu , en ɗon ɗaɓɓita yerduye Allah bee nuɗɗinki man , naa bee ɗowtanaago tawreeta . Ngam bee kuuɗe tawreeta walaa koo gooto heɓata yerduye Allah .
48002017	Nonnon , koo minin Yahuudu'en boo min ɗon kooli Almasiihu ngam haa min keɓa yerduye Allah . Waato minin min marɓe hakke kal kal bee yimɓe ummaatooje . To non kam , Almasiihu ɗon sembiɗina hakke na ? Naa non sam !
48002018	Ammaa to goɗɗo meeriɗini tawreeta , wi'i ka hisnataa , ɓaawoɗon boo tabitini ka fahin , nden kam o waŋgini hoore maako o luutɗo tawreeta .
48002019	Min kam mi maayɗo hedi tawreeta , kaŋka kan mbari yam . Jonta mi ɗon yeeɗa ngam Allah . Mi maaydi bee Almasiihu dow leggal gaafaaŋgal .
48002020	Naa min yeeɗata jonta , ammaa Almasiihu ɗon yeeɗa nder am . Yaake mi ɗon yeeɗa nder duniyaaru ndu , mi ɗon yeeɗa bee nuɗɗingo Ɓiɗɗo Allah mo yiɗi yam , hokki yoŋki mum ngam am .
48002021	Min mi meeriɗintaa mo''ere Allah . Ngam to goɗɗo heɓi yerduye Allah bee ɗowtanaago tawreeta , nden kam Almasiihu maayi meere .
48003001	Onon Galaatiya'en faataaɓe ! Moy hiili on ? Na mi waŋginani gite mon Yeesu Almasiihu , maayɗo dow gaafaaŋgal na ?
48003002	Njaabeeɗam ?amol gootol tan : Allah hokki on Ruuhu mum ngam on ɗowtani tawreeta na , malla ngam on nani linjiila , on nuɗɗini Almasiihu ?
48003003	Koni on paamataa ? Ko Ruuhu fuɗɗi nder mooɗon , on ngiɗi timminirgo ɗum bee sembe mooɗon na ?
48003004	Ko laatani on , ɗum fuu ɗum meere na ? Fakat , kuuje mawɗe bana ɗe'e laatataako meere !
48003005	Allah hokki on Ruuhu mum , ɗon huuwa kaayeefiiji caka mooɗon boo . O ɗon waɗa ɗum ngam on ɗowtani tawreeta na ? Malla ngam on nani linjiila , on nuɗɗini Almasiihu ?
48003006	Numte le haala Ibrahiima . Deftere wi'i : " Ibrahiima nuɗɗini Allah , kanjum Allah limani mo ɗum gooŋgaaku . "
48003007	Bee maajum paamoton ɗu'um : Nuɗɗinɓe Allah , kamɓe ngoni ɓiɓɓe Ibrahiima bee gooŋga .
48003008	Deftere wi'i diga ɓooyma no yimɓe ummaatooje keɓrata yerduye Allah bee nuɗɗinki . Bana ni deftere anndiniri Ibrahiima linjiila diga ɓooyma boo , nde wi'i : " Bee maaɗa ummaatooje fuu keɓan barka . "
48003009	Ibrahiima nuɗɗini Allah , nuɗɗinɓe Allah bana Ibrahiima keɓan barka Allah bana Ibrahiima boo .
48003010	Ammaa tuugtooɓe kuuɗe tawreeta , naaloore ɗon dow maɓɓe . Ngam deftere wi'i : " Naaloore Allah dow koomoy mo ɗowtanaaki foroy umrooje bindaaɗe nder deftere tawreeta nde'e fuu . "
48003011	Ammaa bee non fuu , walaa mo heɓata yerduye Allah dow laawol tawreeta , ngam deftere wi'i boo : " Nuɗɗinɗo Allah heɓan yerduye maako , yeeɗan . "
48003012	Tawreeta kam darataako dow nuɗɗinki sam , ammaa " kuuwanɗo umrooje ɗe'e yeeɗan bee maaje . "
48003013	Almasiihu rimɗini en e naaloore nde tawreeta waddani en , ngam kaŋko o laati naalaaɗo mbattudife meeɗen . Deftere wi'i : " Koomoy ɓilaaɗo haa leggal , o naalaaɗo . "
48003014	Yeesu Almasiihu huuwi ɗum ngam haa barka Allah dow Ibrahiima warana ummaatooje fuu . Koomoy nuɗɗini Almasiihu , heɓan Ruuhu ngu Allah wi'i o hokkan ɗum .
48003015	Deerɗam'en , sey mi faamtina on bee balndol al'aada yimɓe : To goɗɗo waɗi alkawal , tabitini ngal , nden kam walaa potanɗo meeriɗingo ngal malla ɓesdugo goɗɗum haa maagal .
48003016	Yoo , Allah waɗani Ibrahiima alkawal , ngam maako e danygol maako . Deftere wi'aay " danygolji ma " , bana ɗi ɗuuɗɗi , ammaa " danygol ma " , bana ngol neɗɗo gooto , waato Almasiihu .
48003017	Ndaa ko ngiɗmi wi'ugo : Allah waɗani Ibrahiima alkawal , tabitini ngal . Duuɓi teemeɗɗe nayi e cappanɗe tati ( 430 ) ɓaawo maajum , tawreeta wari . Ka waawataa meeriɗingo alkawal man .
48003018	Allah wi'i Ibrahiima o hokkan mo maral . To dokkal maajum darake dow tawreeta , nden kam ngal darataako dow koŋgol alkawal . Ammaa Allah mo''ani ɗum Ibrahiima bee koŋgol alkawal .
48003019	Nde non kam , ɗume tawreeta nafata ? Ka ɓesdaama ngam haa ka waŋgina kuuɗe luutanɗe muuyo Allah , sey to danygol Ibrahiima go wari , waato mo koŋgol alkawal wolwi e muuɗum . Tawreeta hokkaama bee malaa'ika'en , goɗɗo hakkundeejo boo waddi ka .
48003020	Ammaa to ɗum goɗɗo gooto , walaa haaje hakkundeejo wara . Allah boo o gooto !
48003021	To non kam , tawreeta ɗon luuta koŋgol alkawal Allah na ? Naa non sam ! Ngam to tawreeta laatakeno fakat ngam haa ka waddana yimɓe ngeendam , nden kam goɗɗo heɓanno yerduye Allah dow laawol tawreeta .
48003022	Ammaa deftere wi'i hakke ɗon laamano yimɓe fuu , ngam haa dokkal fodde koŋgol Allah laatano ɓe dow laawol nuɗɗinki . Koomoy nuɗɗini Yeesu Almasiihu , heɓan ngal .
48003023	Ammaa diga jamanu nuɗɗinki siwa , tawreeta ɗonno jogiti en bana nder suudu fursina , haa nuɗɗinki man waŋgi .
48003024	Bana non tawreeta laatino eltoowo en haa Almasiihu wari , ngam haa en keɓa yerduye Allah bee nuɗɗinki .
48003025	Jonta jamanu nuɗɗinki waɗi , ngam maajum en ndimɗi e juŋŋgo eltoowo .
48003026	Ngam daliila nuɗɗinki on fuu on laati ɓiɓɓe Allah nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
48003027	Saa'i on keɓi ngiiwam baptisma bee innde Almasiihu , on kawti bee maako , o laati bana limce ɗe ɓorniiɗon .
48003028	Ngam maajum walaa ko sendirta Yahuuduujo bee mo laataaki Yahuuduujo , malla maccuɗo bee dimo , malla gorko bee debbo . Onon fuu on laati neɗɗo gooto nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
48003029	Ammaa to on laatake yimɓe Almasiihu , nden kam on asŋgol Ibrahiima boo , on keɓan ko Allah wi'no Ibrahiima .
48004001	Ndaa ko ngiɗmi wi'ugo : Yaake ɓiɗɗo donanɗo maral baaba o derkeejo tawon , walaa ko sendirta mo bee maccuɗo , koo o marɗo kuuje fuu .
48004002	Woɗɓe ɗon kakkilana mo , kaŋko e maral maako , haa warugo nyalaade nde baaba maako ta''ino .
48004003	Bana non enen boo , yaake en ciwa heewtugo , en maccuɓe ruuhuuji laamaniiɗi duniyaaru .
48004004	Ammaa nde wakkati Allah waɗi , o neli Ɓiɗɗo maako . Kaŋko o danyaama e debbo , o leestani tawreeta ,
48004005	ngam haa o rimɗina jeyaaɓe tawreeta fuu , o laatina en ɓiɓɓe Allah .
48004006	Onon on laati ɓiɓɓe Allah fakat . Ngam maajum o hokki on Ruuhu Ɓiɗɗo maako nder ɓerɗe mon , ngu ɗon ewno : " Abba ! " waato : " Baaba am ! "
48004007	Nonnon , njeyaaŋgu mon timmi , on ɓiɓɓe . To on ɓiɓɓe , nden kam on keɓan boo ko Allah sigani ɓiɓɓe mum .
48004008	Ɓooyma on anndaano Allah , on maccuɓeno ɗowanteeɓe ɓe laataaki ɗowanteeɓe bee gooŋga .
48004009	Ammaa jonta on anndi Allah , ndikka mi wi'a : Allah anndi on . Koni lorotooɗon haa ruuhuuji tampuɗi jurumɗi go ? Kadi on ngiɗi on laato maccuɓe maaji fahin na ?
48004010	On ɗon kakkilana nyalɗe goɗɗe e lebbi goɗɗi e duuɓi goɗɗi .
48004011	Mi huli , taa kuugal am fuu laato meere caka mooɗon .
48004012	Deerɗam'en , mi ɗon toro on : Laate bana am . Min boo mi laati bana mooɗon . On mbaɗaay yam aybe sam .
48004013	On ɗon ciftora no aartirmi waajugo on linjiila . Saa'i maajum mi nyawɗo .
48004014	Nyaw am foondi munyal mon masin . Ammaa on njawaaki yam , on calaaki yam sam . On njaɓi yam bana malaa'ikaajo Allah , bana on njaɓranno Yeesu Almasiihu .
48004015	Saa'i maajum on keewi seyo . Toy ngo jonta ? Mi ɗon seedano on , to on mbaawino , on ɗoofanno gite mon , on ndokkammi .
48004016	Kadi mi laati konneejo mon ngam mi ɗon yecca on gooŋga na ?
48004017	Yimɓe woɗɓe ɗon cuklano on masin , ammaa naa ngam hayru mon . Ɓe ɗon ɗaɓɓa sendugo on bee am , ngam haa on tokko ɓe bee tiinaare .
48004018	Booɗɗum to on nanani goɗɗo ngam hayru , ammaa sey on nanana mo foroy , naa saa'i ngondanmi bee mooɗon tan .
48004019	Onon ɓikkoy am , mi ɗon yara bone ngam daliila mooɗon fahin , bana luuwe debbo ɓesnanɗo , ngam haa jaati Almasiihu waŋga nder mooɗon .
48004020	Mi yiɗi wondugo bee mooɗon jonta , haa mi wolwana on hunduko bee hunduko . Mi cakliiɗo masin , mi anndaa ko mbaɗananmi on .
48004021	Onon kam on ngiɗi leestango tawreeta . Mi ɗon ?ama on : On nanaay ko tawreeta wi'ata na ?
48004022	Deftere wi'i : Ibrahiima woodi ɓiɓɓe ɗiɗo , oo ɓii Hajara , culaaɗo , oya boo ɓii Saratu , dimo .
48004023	Ɓii culaaɗo danyaama bee baawɗe ɓandu , ammaa ɓii dimo danyaama ngam daliila koŋgol Allah .
48004024	Ndaa ko saawi nder haala maajum : Rewɓe ɗiɗo ɓe'e , ɓe alkawalji Allah ɗiɗi . Alkawal gootal , waato Hajara , iwi haa hooseere Sina , ɗon danya maccuɓe .
48004025	Hajara , ɗum hooseere Sina nder lesdi Arabiya . O fotan bee Urusaliima , berniwol jontawol , jooɗiiŋgol bee ɓikkoy mum nder njeyaaŋgu .
48004026	Ammaa Urusaliima ngol asama , ngol dimol . Kaŋgol woni daada meeɗen .
48004027	Ngam deftere wi'i :
48004028	Deerɗam'en , onon on nandi bee Isiyaaku , on laati ɓiɓɓe Allah ngam daliila koŋgol alkawal .
48004029	Ammaa ɓooyma danyaaɗo bee laawol yimɓe toonyi danyaaɗo fodde Ruuhu Allah . Bana non hande boo ɗum wa'i .
48004030	Ammaa ɗume deftere wi'ata ? " Riiw culaaɗo bee ɓiyum fuu , ngam ɓii culaaɗo ronataa , sey ɓii dimo . "
48004031	Deerɗam'en , enen en laataaki ɓiɓɓe culaaɗo , ammaa en ɓiɓɓe dimo .
48005001	Almasiihu rimɗini en haa en njooɗo en rimɓe . Ngam maajum tabite nder ndimu , taa acce goɗɗo wartira on maccuɓe fahin .
48005002	Naneeɗam ! Min Pol ko mbi'anmi on : To on njaɓi juulnaago , nden kam Almasiihu nafataa on sam .
48005003	Koomoy jaɓi juulnaago , mi ɗon seedo mo fahin , o haɓɓi hoore maako haa o ɗowtano tawreeta fuu .
48005004	To on ɗaɓɓiti yerduye Allah dow laawol tawreeta , nden kam on ceedi bee Almasiihu , on ngurtoto mo''ere Allah boo .
48005005	Minin min ɗon tammi heɓugo yerduye Allah . Kanjum min nuɗɗinta , min ɗon ndeena ɗum bee baawɗe Ruuhu Allah .
48005006	To goɗɗo hawti bee Almasiihu , juulnol malla sooynde juulnol fuu walaa saman , sey nuɗɗinki ki huuwrata bee yiide tan .
48005007	On puɗɗi laawol mon booɗɗum . Moy haɗi on tokkaago gooŋga ?
48005008	Ɓe ngiɗi estugo on , ammaa esto maajum iwaay haa Allah ewniiɗo on .
48005009	Taa ngejjite : " Ufnirɗum seɗɗa ufnan kuroori njiiɓaandi fuu . "
48005010	Ammaa ngam daliila Jawmiraawo mi ɗon hooli on , mi anndi on numataa bee hakkiilo feere . Estuɗo on o kiiteteeɗo , koo ɗum moye .
48005011	Deerɗam'en , to mi ɗon waajina nafuda juulnol haa jonta bana ko ɓe pewantammi , ngam ɗume ɓe toonyoto yam ? To fakat mi waajino bana non , nden kam haala gaafaaŋgal Almasiihu ɓillataano ɓe .
48005012	Fitinɓe on ɓe'e , tiiniiɓe juulnugo , ndikka ɓe ta''a les maɓɓe fuu .
48005013	Deerɗam'en , Allah ewni on haa on laato rimɓe . Ammaa taa kuuwtinire ndimu mon bana hujja suunooji mon . Mballindire bee yiide .
48005014	Tawreeta fuu hawti nder umroore woore : " Yiɗ keeddiɗɗiraawo ma bana hoore ma . "
48005015	Ammaa to on ɗon ngatindira , on ɗon nyaamindira bana dabbaaji kalluɗi , kakkile ngam taa on moɗindira .
48005016	Ndaa ko ngiɗmi wi'ugo : Acce Ruuhu Allah laamano on , taa tokke suunooji ko'e mon .
48005017	Suunooji neɗɗo ɗon luuta Ruuhu Allah , Ruuhu Allah boo ɗon hona suunooji neɗɗo . Ngam daliila haɓre man on mbaawataa huuwugo booɗɗum ko ngiɗɗon .
48005018	Ammaa to Ruuhu Allah ɗon ɗowa on , nden kam tawreeta walaa baawɗe dow mooɗon .
48005019	Ko suuno neɗɗo laatinta , ɗum baŋguɗum : njeenu e kuuɗe coɓɗe , cemtiniiɗe ,
48005020	e cujidanki labbi e hiilaaji e nganyŋgu e haɓre e kaajal e tikkere e jokkirli e luural e biɗu'aakuuji ,
48005021	e nganyaandi e wuykere e pijirle kalluɗe e kuuɗe goɗɗe irin ɗe'e . Ko mbi'mi on diga ɓooyma , sey mi wi'a ɗum fahin : Huuwanɓe irin kuuɗe ɗe'e keɓataa joonde nder laamu Allah .
48005022	Ammaa Ruuhu Allah ɗon mawnina nafuda feere , waato yiide e seyo e hoolaare e munyal e enɗam e mbooɗeeŋga e gooŋgaaku
48005023	e yaŋkinaare e naŋgtaare . Walaa umroore haɗata kuuje ɗe'e .
48005024	Koomoy laati goɗɗo Yeesu Almasiihu , tiggi hoore mum bee giɗaaɗi e suunooji fuu haa gaafaaŋgal .
48005025	Ruuhu Allah hokki en ngeendam , sey en ɗowtano Ruuhu maajum bee yoŋkiiji men fuu .
48005026	Mawnitaare e tikkere e kaajal , taa ɗum meeta laataago caka mooɗon .
48006001	Deerɗam'en , to on tawi goɗɗo baɗɗo aybewol kooŋgole , onon marɓe Ruuhu Allah , lortine mo dow laawol booɗŋgol . Ammaa kolle mo enɗam . Kakkile ngam taa on ndo''o bee ko'e mon .
48006002	Mballindire roondaago dooŋgle mon , bana ni on ɗowtoranto umroore Almasiihu .
48006003	To goɗɗo laari hoore mum bana o mawɗo , ammaa o laataaki non , nden kam o majjini hoore maako .
48006004	Sey koomoy linya kuugal mum . To ngal fotti , o heɓan mantoraago ko o huuwi bee hoore maako . Walaa haaje o foondira ɗum bee kuugal goɗɗo .
48006005	Ngam doole koomoy fuu efta dooŋgal kuuɗe mum , jaabano hoore mum .
48006006	Jaŋginaaɗo kubar nuɗɗinki senda ko o mari bee jaŋginoowo mo .
48006007	Taa este ko'e mon ! Allah accataa goɗɗo fijira mo . Ko neɗɗo aawi fuu , kanjum sodata .
48006008	To goɗɗo aawi dow ngesa suunooji mum , codol ngesa maajum laatoto maayde tan . Ammaa to o aawi dow ngesa Ruuhu , Ruuhu fuɗnanan mo ngeendam nduumiiɗam .
48006009	Taa comen huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga , ngam to en tampaay , en keɓan codol booɗŋgol nder wakkati maajum .
48006010	Ngam maajum , yaake en ngoodi wakkati , sey en kuuwana yimɓe fuu booɗɗum , sakkoma hawtiɗɗiraaɓe men nder nuɗɗinki .
48006011	Ndaare no karfeeje mawniri ɗe mbindanmi on jonta bee juŋŋgo am .
48006012	Ɗaɓɓanɓe yerduye yimɓe bee kuuɗe ɓandu , kamɓe ɓillata on bee haala juulnol . Ammaa ɓe ɗon mbaɗa ɗum fuu ngam taa Yahuudu'en toonyo ɓe ngam daliila gaafaaŋgal Almasiihu .
48006013	Koo ɓe juulniiɓe , ɓe ɗowtantaako tawreeta . Ɓe ngiɗi on njaɓa juulnol ngam haa ɓe njuroro ɗum .
48006014	Min kam mi jurortaako kooɗume , sonaa gaafaaŋgal Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu . Ngam daliila maayde maako haa gaafaaŋgal , duniyaaru laatani yam maayndu , min boo mi maayɗo hedi duniyaaru .
48006015	Ngam maajum juulnol malla sooynde juulnol fuu walaa saman . To goɗɗo laatake neɗɗo keso , kanjum tan mari saman .
48006016	Tokkotooɓe laawol ngo'ol fuu , Allah hokku ɓe jam e mo''ere , kamɓe e ummaatoore Isra'iila gooŋgaare , yimɓe Allah fuu .
48006017	Yeeso ɗo , taa goɗɗo fitinammi . Min mi maccuɗo Yeesu , ɓattajje haa ɓandu am ɗon mbaŋgina ɗum .
48006018	Onon deerɗam'en , mo''ere Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu wondu bee mooɗon . Aamiina !
49001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu bee muuyo Allah , yahugo haa yimɓe Allah wonɓe haa Efesus , hoolaaɓe nder kawtal muuɗum'en bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
49001002	Allah , Baabiraawo men , e Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men ndokka on mo''ere e jam .
49001003	Yettoore laatano Allah , Baabiraawo Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu . Ngam o hokki en barkaaji maako kooɗiye gonɗi nder asama , en keɓi ɗi fuu bee Almasiihu .
49001004	Diga o tagaayno duniyaaru , o suɓi en haa en laato yimɓe maako nder kawtal bee Almasiihu , en ndaro yeeso maako en senaaɓe ɓe ngalaa aybefa . O yiɗi en ,
49001005	ngam maajum o waɗi anniya jaɓugo en bana ɓiɓɓe maako bee kuugal Almasiihu . Kanjum woni muuyo maako , bana ni ɗum fottani mo .
49001006	En maŋgta mo''ere maako kaayeefiire nde o hokki en bee Ɓiɗɗo maako giɗaaɗo .
49001007	Ngam daliila ?i?am Almasiihu ndufaaɗam keɓɗen ndimu e yaafuye hakkeeji men . Bana ni Allah waŋginani en maŋgu mbooɗeeŋga muuɗum .
49001008	O woonani en ɗuuɗɗum masin , o hokki en faamu e hakkiilo fuu .
49001009	O anndini en anniya maako sirriiha ka o waɗno diga ɓooyma bee muuyo maako ,
49001010	haa o laatina ɗum nder saa'iire fottannde bee Almasiihu . O waɗi anniya mooɓtugo kuuje gonɗe nder asama e dow lesdi fuu , o waɗa Almasiihu laato hoore maaje .
49001011	Nder kawtal bee Almasiihu keɓɗen geɗal men haa kisndam . Allah , kuuwanɗo kooɗume fuu fodde muuyo mum e nufaye mum , suɓno en diga ɓooyma haa en keɓa ɗum .
49001012	Ngam maajum , sey maŋgten tedduŋgal maako , naa minin aartuɓe reenugo Almasiihu tan ,
49001013	ammaa onon boo , onon nanɓe wolde gooŋga , kubar kisndam mon . Nde nuɗɗinɗon , Allah hokki on Ruuhu mum Ceniiŋgu ngu o wi'no o hokkan . Bana ni o waɗani on lamba maral maako .
49001014	Ruuhu maajum woni ceedoowo hayruuji fuu ɗi Allah tammani en . En keɓan ɗi to kisndam men timmidi . En maŋgta tedduŋgal maako !
49001015	Too , mi nani haala nuɗɗinki mon dow Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men , non boo haala yiide mon haa yimɓe Allah fuu .
49001016	Ngam maajum mi accataa yettugo Allah ngam daliila mooɗon . Mi ɗon siftora on foroy nder do'aaji am .
49001017	Mi ɗon toro Allah , Baabiraawo Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , Allah marɗo tedduŋgal , haa o hokka on Ruuhu maako , ngu faamtina on , ngu waŋginana on Allah haa anndon mo .
49001018	Allah maɓɓita hakkiilooji mon bee jayŋgol mum , haa on ngi'a timmitirde laawol nde o ewni on haa on njotto ton , on paama maŋgu maral kaayeefiwal ngal o sigani yimɓe maako .
49001019	On paama boo baawɗe maako ɓurɗe mawnugo , kuuwooje nder meeɗen , enen nuɗɗinɓe . Baawɗe ɗe'e , Allah huuwtiniri ɗe bee sembe muuɗum fuu ,
49001020	nde o ummitini Almasiihu nder maayɓe , nde o jo''ini mo haa nyaamo maako haa asamanji .
49001021	Haa ton Almasiihu ɗon laamano mawɓe asama , e marɓe laamu e baawɗe , e jawmiraaɓe e inɗe tedduɗe ewneteeɗe kooɗeye , naa nder jamanuuru ndu'u tan , ammaa nder waranndu boo .
49001022	Allah wallini kooɗume fuu les kosɗe maako , waɗi mo Jawmiraawo dow kooɗume fuu , laatini mo hooreejo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe .
49001023	Kayre woni ɓandu Almasiihu . Nder maare Almasiihu ɗon waŋga bee laaɓɗum , kaŋko kebbinanɗo kooɗume fuu kootoy .
49002001	Naane kam on maayɓeno , ngam on ɗowtanaaki Allah , on mbaɗi aybeeji .
49002002	On tokki laawol kalluŋgol ngol duniyaaru ndu , on ɗowtani laamiiɗo ruuhuuji gonɗi nder hawa hakkunde asama bee lesdi . Koo jonta boo ruuhu man ɗon laamano yimɓe luutooɓe Allah .
49002003	Fakat , en fuu en laatino bana maɓɓe , en tokkino suunooji men . En mbaɗino ko ɓalli men e hakkiilooji men ɗaɓɓi fuu . Bana no en mba'ino bee ɗabiya , tikkere Allah ɗonno dow meeɗen bana dow yimɓe woɗɓe fuu .
49002004	Ammaa enɗam Allah ɗuuɗi , yiide maako boo mawni masin .
49002005	Koo en maayɓeno ngam en luuti mo , kaŋko o yeeɗini en hawtaade bee Almasiihu . Taa ngejjite : On kisi ngam daliila mo''ere maako tan .
49002006	Allah ummitini en bee Almasiihu , jo''idini en bee maako haa asamanji .
49002007	Bana ni o waŋginirta no mo''ere maako ɓurdi kooɗume fuu mawnugo . Jamanuuji garanɗi fuu ngi'an mbooɗeeŋga maako nga o huuwani en bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
49002008	Fakat , kisndam mon ɗon dari dow mo''ere maako tan . Naa ɗum kuugal mooɗon , ɗum dokkal Allah ngal njaɓɗon bee nuɗɗinki .
49002009	Kisndam mon iwaay haa kuuɗe mon , ngam taa goɗɗo heɓa juraago .
49002010	Enen bee ko'e men en kuugal Allah . Kaŋko o tagri en bee Almasiihu haa en kuuwa kuuɗe booɗɗe . Kanje boo , Allah aarti taaskitini ɗe ngam haa en kuuwa ɗe .
49002011	Numte ko laatinooɗon naane . Onon on yimɓe ummaatooje . Yahuudu'en ɗon mbi'a ɓe ɓe saadooni'en , ɓe ɗon mbi'a ko'e maɓɓe boo ɓe juulniiɓe . Ammaa juulnol maɓɓe ɗon waɗe haa ɓandu bee juuɗe yimɓe .
49002012	Saa'i maajum on ceedi bee Almasiihu , on jananɓe , on ngalaa kawtal bee Isra'iila , on daayiiɓe alkawalji ɗi Allah haɓɓuno bee ummaatoore mum suɓaande . On njooɗino nder duniyaaru , on ngalaa tammunde hayru , on ngalaa Allah .
49002013	On daayinooɓe Allah , ammaa nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu on ɓadiiɓe jonta ngam ?i?am Almasiihu ndufaaɗam .
49002014	Kaŋko o waɗani en sulhu , o laatini Yahuudu'en e yimɓe woɗɓe fuu ummaatoore woore . Bee maayde maako o yibbiniri mahol cenduŋgol caka meeɗen , o timmini konnaagu caka meeɗen .
49002015	O sottini tawreeta bee umrooje mum e farillaaji mum , ngam haa o hawta asli yimɓe ɗiɗi , o laatina ɓe ummaatoore hesre nder kawtal bee maako , o waɗana ɓe sulhu .
49002016	Bee maayde maako dow leggal gaafaaŋgal o itti konnaagu , bee gaafaaŋgal man o hawti asli ɗiɗi nder ɓandu wooru , o sulhindira ɓe bee Allah .
49002017	Nonnon ɗum laatori . Almasiihu wari , waaji yimɓe fuu kubar sulhu , onon yimɓe ummaatooje daayinooɓe Allah , e Yahuudu'en ɓadinooɓe mo fuu .
49002018	Ngam daliila Almasiihu en fuu en keɓi ɓaditaago Allah Baabiraawo bee ballal Ruuhu ngootu .
49002019	Jonta kam , onon yimɓe ummaatooje go , naa on jananɓe malla hoɗɓe , ammaa on hawtiɗɗiraaɓe ummaatoore Allah , on yimɓe saare Allah boo .
49002020	Onon boo on laati kaa'e ɗe suudu nyiɓaandu ndu caɓɓawal mum laati nelaaɓe e annabo'en . Yeesu Almasiihu bee hoore mum laati hayre ɓurnde tedduŋgal .
49002021	Kaŋko o ɗon jogi nyiɓol fuu haa ngol mawna , ngol laato haykaliiru Jawmiraawo seniindu .
