49002022	Nder kawtal bee maako onon boo on kaa'e nastinaaɗe nder mahugo suudu ndu Ruuhu Allah jooɗoto haa muuɗum .
49003001	Ngam maajum min Pol , kaɓɓaaɗo ngam daliila Yeesu Almasiihu , ngam hayru mooɗon boo , onon yimɓe ummaatooje , mi ɗon toro Allah .
49003002	On meeɗi nanugo fakat no Allah yowani yam kuugal waŋgingo mo''ere mum ngam mooɗon .
49003003	O waŋginani yam anniya maako sirriiha , bana ko aartumi windango on bee bolle seɗɗa .
49003004	To on njaŋgi ko mbindumi , on anndan no mi faamri sirri Almasiihu .
49003005	Ɓooyma yimɓe anndaano sirri maajum , ammaa jonta Allah waŋgini ɗum bee Ruuhu mum haa senaaɓe mum nelaaɓe e annabo'en .
49003006	Ndaa sirri oo : Nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu , yimɓe ummaatooje keɓan geɗal barkaaji Allah kal kal bee Yahuudu'en , ɓe laatoto terɗe haa ɓandu Almasiihu , ɓe keɓan hayruuji boo ɗi Allah wi'no hokkan Isra'iila .
49003007	Allah mo''ani yam , waɗi yam kuuwanoowo linjiila man . Bana ni o waŋginiri baawɗe maako haa am .
49003008	Fakat , min mi tullidiɗɗo Masiihiŋko'en fuu . Ammaa Allah enɗi yam , halfini yam waajugo ummaatooje , haa mi anndina ɓe jeynitaare Almasiihu ɗuunde nde heɓtataake sam ,
49003009	haa mi holla ɓe no Allah timminirta nufaye mum . Allah , tagɗo kuuje fuu waɗno nufayeere man diga jamanuuji ciwa , ammaa o suuɗino nde .
49003010	Jonta o waŋginiran nde bee jama'aare Masiihiŋko'en , ngam haa marɓe laamu e baawɗe nder asamanji ngi'a faamuuji Allah feere feere fuu .
49003011	Allah huuwi ɗum fodde anniya ka o waɗino diga ɓooyma , o timminira ka bee Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men .
49003012	En ɗon nuɗɗini Jawmiraawo oo , ngam maajum keɓɗen dartaare e hoolaare haa en ndaro yeeso Allah .
49003013	Ngam maajum mi ɗon toro on boo , taa on itta tammunde ngam daliila boneeji am . Mi ɗon yara ɗi ngam mooɗon , ɗi laatanto on tedduŋgal .
49003014	Ngam maajum mi ɗon sujidana Allah . Kaŋko woni Baabiraawo bee gooŋga .
49003015	Ko wi'ete baaba fuu haa asama e dow lesdi , heɓi innde mum haa maako .
49003016	Mi ɗon toro Allah , marɗo tedduŋgal maŋgal , haa o sembiɗina ɓerɗe mon bee baawɗe Ruuhu maako ,
49003017	haa Almasiihu jooɗo nder ɓerɗe mon , mo njaɓɗon bee nuɗɗinki . Mi ɗon toro Allah haa on mbaɗa ɗaɗi nder yiide , on tabita nder maare ,
49003018	ngam haa on keɓa faamugo , onon e yimɓe Allah fuu , no nufaye maako yaajiri , juutiri , towri , luggiri fuu ,
49003019	haa anndon yiide Almasiihu boo , koo to nde ɓuri faamu neɗɗo . Allah hebbina on bee kebbinki muuɗum fuu .
49003020	Allah waawan huuwugo ko ɓuri do'aaji men e numooji men , ngam o ɗon huuwa nder meeɗen bee baawɗe maako mawɗe .
49003021	Tedduŋgal laatano mo nder jama'aare Masiihiŋko'en , non boo bee kuugal Yeesu Almasiihu , haa gide fuu , haa abada abadin . Aamiina !
49004001	Ngam maajum , min kaɓɓaaɗo ngam daliila Jawmiraawo , mi ɗon toro on : Kuuwe ko fotti , bana ewnaaɓe Allah kuuwrata .
49004002	Taa mawnite dow woɗɓe , njooɗe bee mbooɗeeŋga e munyal , munyindire bee yiide .
49004003	Tiine jooɗodaago hakkiilo wooto bana Ruuhu Allah hawriti on , hoolaare hawta on fuu bana ɓoggol .
49004004	Onon fuu on keɓi Ruuhu ngootu , on laati ɓandu wooru . Tammunde woore laatani on bee ewnaandu Allah .
49004005	Woodi Jawmiraawo gooto e nuɗɗinki gooti e ngiiwam baptisma ngootam .
49004006	Woodi Allah gooto tan , kaŋko woni Baabiraawo yimɓe fuu , o ɗon laamano ɓe fuu , o ɗon huuwra bee maɓɓe fuu , o ɗon huuwa nder maɓɓe boo .
49004007	Koomoy meeɗen heɓi geɗal mo''ere , deydey ko Almasiihu hokki mo .
49004008	Ngam deftere wi'i :
49004009	Ko saawi nder bolle ɗe'e ? O eeŋgi , ɗum bana wi'ugo : O aarti o jippi haa nokkuuje lesdi ɓurɗe leesugo .
49004010	Jippiiɗo oo , kaŋko woni eeŋgtuɗo haa dow asamanji ngam haa o hebbina tageefooji fuu .
49004011	Kaŋko woni dokkuɗo dokke boo : O waɗi woɗɓe nelaaɓe , woɗɓe annabo'en , woɗɓe waajooɓe , woɗɓe boo ardiiɓe e jaŋginooɓe jama'aare .
49004012	O waɗi ɗum fuu haa ɓe taaskitina yimɓe Allah ngam kuugal muuɗum , haa ɓe mawnina ɓandu Almasiihu boo .
49004013	Bana ni en fuu en kawritan bee nuɗɗinki gooti e anndal Ɓiɗɗo Allah gootal , en laato timmuɓe nder kawtal bee Almasiihu , en njotto darnde maako timmunde .
49004014	Ɓaawoɗon en laatataako ɓikkoy , anndinol goɗɗo dimbataa en bana ?uuge e hendu ndimbirta koombowal . To nuɗɗinki goɗɗo heewtaay tawon , nden kam waɗooɓe rikisi keɓan estugo mo bee hiilaaji e dabareeji .
49004015	Ammaa enen en ngaajindira gooŋga , en ngiɗindira , ngam haa en mawna nder kooɗume fuu , en njotto darnde Almasiihu , laatiiɗo hoore meeɗen .
49004016	Ngam daliila maako terɗe ɓandu fuu ɗon mooɓi , ɓandu fuu ɗon hawti bee jokke mum kooɗeye . Terɗe ɓandu ɗon mballindira , kooɗeye bee kuugal muuɗum'en . Bana ni ɓandu ɗon ɓesdo , ɗon mawna bee yiide .
49004017	Ndaa ko mbi'anmi on bee innde Jawmiraawo , mi ɗon tiɗɗina on taa on meeta tokkaago al'aadaaji yimɓe ummaatooje . Kamɓe , numooji maɓɓe ɗon majjina ɓe .
49004018	Hakkiilooji maɓɓe nyiɓɓi , ko'e maɓɓe caati , ɓe anndaa Allah . Ngam maajum ɓe cendi bee ngeendam ɗam Allah hokkata .
49004019	Ɓe ngalaa naŋgtaare , ɓe njoofi ko'e maɓɓe haa kuuɗe cemtiniiɗe e coɓɗe kooɗeye , ɓe tokki suunooji maɓɓe fuu .
49004020	Onon kam on ekkitaaki irin kuuɗe ɗe'e bee ekkitinol Almasiihu .
49004021	On nani kubar maako fakat , on njaɓi mo , on anndinaaɓe gooŋga ka waŋgi nder maako .
49004022	Ngam maajum sey on ceeda bee neɗɗo mon ɓooymaajo , waato bee kuuɗe mon ɓooymaaje . Ko laatiiɗon ɓooyma , suunooji pewooji ɗon kalka ɗum .
49004023	Acce ɓerɗe mon e hakkiilooji mon kesɗita foroy .
49004024	Sey on ɓorno neɗɗo keso mo Allah tagi dow jaati mum , haa on kuuwa pottuɗum , ceniiɗum fodde gooŋga Allah .
49004025	Ngam maajum acce fewugo . Mbolwindire gooŋga , ngam en fuu en kawti bana terɗe haa ɓandu Almasiihu .
49004026	To on tikki , taa mbaɗe hakke . Taa on nyalla bee tikkere ,
49004027	ngam taa on ndokka Iblisa laawol naŋgugo on .
49004028	Laatinooɗo gujjo , taa meeta wujjugo . Sey o huuwa kuugal gooŋga bee juuɗe maako , haa o wuura , o heɓa wallugo laafuɓe boo .
49004029	Taa mbolwe bolle bonnooje , sey nafooje tan , haa on mawnina nuɗɗinki woɗɓe , on mo''ana nananɓe on .
49004030	Taa mettine Ruuhu Ceniiŋgu , ngam bee maagu Allah waɗani on lamba maral muuɗum , haa o rimɗina on nder nyalaade warannde .
49004031	Ngam maajum cottine metteeŋga e ɓernuki e tikkere fuu diga nder ɓerɗe mon . Taa telɓindire , taa kuɗindire , itte nganyaandi fuu caka mooɗon .
49004032	Ammaa maslindire , mboonindire , njaafotire bana Allah yaaforani on ngam daliila Almasiihu .
49005001	Onon on ɓiɓɓe Allah yiɗaaɓe . Ngam maajum kuuwe bana maako .
49005002	Sey on kuuwa bee yiide . Ciftore no Almasiihu yiɗiri en haa o hokki yoŋki maako ngam meeɗen . O lii'ani ki Allah bana kirsaaɗum , bana dokkal ngal Allah yerdi ɗum .
49005003	On laati yimɓe Allah . Ngam maajum njeenu e coɓki e suuno e irin maaji fuu fottaay caka mooɗon , koo wolwugo haala man .
49005004	Bana non boo bolle cemtiniiɗe e meereeje e tunwuɗe pottaay . Ndikka on ngetta Allah bee ɗemɗe mon .
49005005	On anndi , walaa jeenoowo malla coɓɗo malla cuunaaɗo ( fakat , suuno e sujidango labbi ɗum gootum ) , walaa koo gooto maɓɓe heɓata joonde nder laamu Almasiihu bee Allah .
49005006	Taa acce goɗɗo esta on bee haalaaji meereeji . Ngam daliila kuuje ɗe'e fuu tikkere Allah ukkanto kooɓeye ɓe ɗowtantaako mo .
49005007	Taa kawte bee irin maɓɓe sam .
49005008	Onon boo on ɗonno nder nyiɓre , ammaa jonta on ɗon ngondi bee annoora ngam kawtal mon bee Jawmiraawo . Ngam maajum kuuwe boo bana yimɓe annoora .
49005009	Mbooɗeeŋga e gooŋgaaku e gooŋga fuu haa annoora iwata .
49005010	Tiine heɓtugo ko fottanta Jawmiraawo .
49005011	Taa kawte bee huuwooɓe kuuɗe meereeje ɗe nyiɓre , ammaa mbaŋgine kuuɗe man .
49005012	Fakat , kuuɗe ɗe'e ɗe ɓe kuuwata bee sirri , koo wolwugo ɗe woni cemtuɗum .
49005013	Ammaa ɗe fuu ɗe mbaŋgan laaɓɗum to annoora waŋgini ɗe .
49005014	Ngam to huunde waŋgi , nde laatoto annoora . Ngam maajum ngimeten :
49005015	Ngam maajum linye laabi mon booɗɗum , naa bana faataaɓe , ammaa bana marɓe hakkiilo .
49005016	Naftore wakkati , ngam nyalaaɗe jontaaje ɗe kalluɗe .
49005017	Kadi , taa laate faataaɓe , ammaa paame ko Jawmiraawo ɗaɓɓata haa mooɗon .
49005018	Taa keewe nguykinoojam , ɗam ittan naŋgtaare . Ndikka on keewa Ruuhu Allah .
49005019	Ceynindire bee gime jabuura e maŋgtooje e gime ɗe Ruuhu hokkata on . Ngimane Jawmiraawo , maŋgte mo bee ɓerɗe mon fuu .
49005020	Ngette Allah Baabiraawo koondey ngam kooɗume bee innde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
49005021	Koomoy mooɗon leestana woɗɓe ngam daliila ɗowtaare mon haa Almasiihu .
49005022	Onon rewɓe , leestane worɓe mon . Bana ni mbaŋgirton on leestani Jawmiraawo .
49005023	Ngam gorko laati hoore debbo mum , bana Almasiihu laatori hoore jama'aare Masiihiŋko'en . Almasiihu woni kisnoowo jama'aare laatiinde ɓandu muuɗum .
49005024	Bana jama'aare ɗon leestana Almasiihu , bana non rewɓe boo leestirana worɓe muuɗum'en nder kooɗume fuu .
49005025	Onon worɓe , ngiɗe rewɓe mon bana Almasiihu yiɗiri jama'aare . O hokki hoore maako ngam maare ,
49005026	haa o sena nde . O laɓɓini nde bee ngiiwam e wolde maako ,
49005027	haa o darna nde yeeso maako bana ɓaŋgeteeɗo booɗɗo , laaɓɗo mo walaa batte malla nyodi malla aybe feere .
49005028	Bana non boo worɓe , sey ɓe ngiɗa rewɓe maɓɓe bana ɓalli maɓɓe . Gorko giɗɗo debbo mum , yiɗi hoore mum .
49005029	Fakat , walaa mo wanyata ɓandu mum , ammaa o nyaamnan ndu , o aynan ndu . Bana ni Almasiihu huuwanta jama'aare boo ,
49005030	ngam enen en terɗe ɓandu maako .
49005031	Deftere wi'i : " Gorko accan baaba mum e daada mum , ɗakkotiran bee debbo mum , kamɓe ɗiɗo ɓe laatoto ɓandu wooru . "
49005032	Aayaare nde'e ɗon waŋgina sirri mawɗo . Haa am kam , nde ɗon wolwa haala Almasiihu bee jama'aare mum .
49005033	Ammaa nde ɗon wolwa haala mooɗon boo : Sey koomoy mooɗon yiɗa debbo mum bana hoore mum , debbo boo teddina gorum .
49006001	Onon ɓikkoy , ɗowtane saarooji mon ngam daliila kawtal mon bee Jawmiraawo . Kanjum ɗum pottuɗum .
49006002	" Teddin baaba ma e daada ma " , kanjum woni umroore arandeere ɓesdannde koŋgol hayru :
49006003	" Nden kam a heɓan hayru , balɗe ma njuutan haa duniyaaru . "
49006004	Onon baabiraaɓe , taa mettine ɓerɗe ɓikkoy mon , ammaa ne'e koy , elte koy nder laawol Jawmiraawo .
49006005	Onon jeyaaɓe , ɗowtane jawmiraaɓe mon haa duniyaaru bee kulol e diwŋgol e ɓernde woore , bana on ɗowtoranto Almasiihu .
49006006	Ɗowtane ɓe , naa gite maɓɓe tan haa on ngerdina ɓe , ammaa kuuwe muuyo Allah bee anniya mon , bana jeyaaɓe Almasiihu .
49006007	Kuuwe kuugal mon bee tiinaare bana huuwanooɓe Jawmiraawo , naa yimɓe .
49006008	On anndi , kuuɗe booɗɗe ɗe goɗɗo huuwata fuu , koo o maccuɗo koo o dimo , Jawmiraawo warjoto ɗe .
49006009	Onon jawmiraaɓe , njogore jeyaaɓe mon bana no fotti . Acce furkitaago ɓe . On anndi Jawmiraawo ɗon haa asama , kaŋko o mari on fuu , onon bee maɓɓe . Yeeso maako yimɓe fuu poti kal .
49006010	Yeeso ɗo , cembiɗe nder kawtal mon bee Jawmiraawo . Acce baawɗe maako mawɗe cembiɗina on .
49006011	Koo'e balmi Allah fuu ngam haa on keɓa dartanaago dabareeji Iblisa .
49006012	Ngam en kaɓataa bee yimɓe , ammaa bee ruuhuuji kalluɗi gonɗi hakkunde asama bee lesdi , marɗi laamu e baawɗe nder jamanuuru nyiɓɓundu ndu'u .
49006013	Ngam maajum njoge balmi Allah , haa on keɓa dartanaago konneejo to nyalaade hallunde wari . To on njaalake kooɗume fuu , nden kam on tabitan .
49006014	Taaske kadi , taade gooŋga bana taadorgol , ɓorne gooŋgaaku bana sulke .
49006015	Taaskitaare waajingo kubar sulhu laato paɗe haa kosɗe mon .
49006016	Koondey fuu njoge nuɗɗinki bana wawarde mon . Bee maaki nyifoton kuri Sayɗaanu giiteleeji fuu .
49006017	Kufne kisndam bana hufneere njamndi , naŋge wolde Allah boo bana kaafahi ki Ruuhu Allah hokkata on .
49006018	Mbaɗe ɗum fuu bee do'a . Tore Allah ngam haa o walla on . Tore mo foroy bana Ruuhu maako ekkitinirta on . Ayne , taa acce do'anaago yimɓe Allah fuu .
49006019	Tore mo ngam am boo , haa o hokkammi wolwugo bolle pottuɗe , haa mi waŋgina sirri linjiila bee dartaare .
49006020	Koo mi kaɓɓaaɗo nder fursinafe jonta , mi nelaaɗo kuuwanoowo linjiila . Ndo'aneeɗam haa mi waajina ka bee dartaare bana no umraami .
49006021	Tikikus , deerɗiraawo men giɗaaɗo , kuuwanoowo Jawmiraawo koolaaɗo yeccan on no njooɗoriimi , ko mbaɗanmi boo .
49006022	Kanjum mi neli mo haa mooɗon , o anndina on no minin fuu min ngorri , haa o de'itina ɓerɗe mon .
49006023	Allah Baabiraawo e Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo , ndokka deerɗiraaɓe fuu jam e yiide iwnde haa nuɗɗinki .
49006024	Mo''ere Allah laatano yiɗɓe Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu bee yiide nde wonnataako .
50001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol e Timote , maccuɓe Yeesu Almasiihu , yahugo haa yimɓe Allah , nuɗɗinɓe Yeesu Almasiihu wonɓe haa Filippi fuu , bee ardiiɓe e wallooɓe jama'aare :
50001002	Allah , Baabiraawo men , e Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men ndokka on mo''ere e jam .
50001003	Koondeye mi siftori on , mi ɗon yetta Allah am ngam mooɗon ,
50001004	mi ɗon do'ano on bee seyo nder do'aaji am fuu .
50001005	Ngam on njaɓi linjiila , on mballi yam anndingo ka diga nyande aartunde haa warugo hande .
50001006	Mi anndi fakat , Allah puɗɗuɗo kuugal booɗŋgal nder mooɗon timminan ngal boo haa nyalaade Yeesu Almasiihu waroyta .
50001007	To mi ɗon numana on bana ni , ɗum pottuɗum , ngam mi ɗon jogi on nder ɓernde am . On fuu on laati hawtiɗɗiraaɓe kuugal ngal Allah mo''ani yam , koo jonta boo , saa'i mi kaɓɓaaɗo nder fursinafa haa mi seedano linjiila , mi tabitina ka yeeso kiita .
50001008	Mi ɗon yenwa on fuu bee yiide iwnde haa ɓernde Yeesu Almasiihu , Allah anndi mi ɗon wolwa gooŋga .
50001009	Mi ɗon toro Allah haa yiide mon ɓesdo yeeso yeeso bee faamu e anndal kooŋgale ,
50001010	haa on cuɓa ko ɓuri fottugo . Bana ni on laatorto laaɓɓe , on ngalaa aybe nder nyalaade Almasiihu waɗata kiita ,
50001011	on huuwanɓe kuuɗe pottuɗe ɗuuɗɗe ɗe Almasiihu huuwrata bee mooɗon ngam teddinki Allah e maŋgtoore mum .
50001012	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , mi yiɗi on paama booɗɗum . Naawɗum ko heɓi yam , walli linjiila yahugo yeeso yeeso .
50001013	Aynooɓe laamorde e wonɓe haa ɗo fuu anndi jonta mi kaɓɓaaɗo ngam mi kuuwanoowo Almasiihu .
50001014	Kaɓɓorli am cembiɗini ɓerɗe deerɗiraaɓe ɗuuɗɓe , haa ɓe ɓesdi hoolaago Jawmiraawo , ɓe ɗon ɓesda waajingo wolde Allah bilaa kulol boo .
50001015	Gooŋga kam , woɗɓe ɗon ngaajina kubar Almasiihu ngam daliila kaajal dow am , malla ngam ɓe ngiɗi gaabotiral . Ammaa woɗɓe ɗon ngaajina kubar maako bee anniya mbooɗka .
50001016	Ɓe ɗon mbaɗa ɗum ngam ɓe ngiɗi Almasiihu , ngam ɓe anndi Allah halfini yam seedanaago linjiila .
50001017	Ammaa ɓeya ɗon ngaajina kubar Almasiihu bee numooji kaajuɗi , naa bee ɓerɗe laaɓɗe . Ɓe ɗon ɗaɓɓa ɗuɗɗingo ɓillaaje am nder fursina .
50001018	Kanjum ɗum daamataa yam . To ɓe ɗon ngaajina kubar Almasiihu koonoy , koo bee faasikaare koo bee ɓerɗe gooŋɗuɗe , min kam mi seyorto ɗum . Koo yeeso ɗo boo mi seyoto ,
50001019	ngam mi anndi timmoode ɓillaaje am fuu ɗum kisndam am , barka do'aaji mon e ballal Ruuhu Yeesu Almasiihu .
50001020	Tammunde am ɗon tabiti , mi ɗon hooli Allah semtintaa yam dow kuugal am sam . Ammaa bana foroy , non jonta boo hoolaare am timmidi , mi anndi mi teddinan Almasiihu , koo bee ngeendam am koo bee maayde am boo .
50001021	Min kam , Almasiihu woni ngeendam am , maayugo boo ɗum riba .
50001022	Ammaa to mi tokkake yeeɗugo , ɗum nafan haa mi ɓesda huuwango Almasiihu . Ngam maajum mi anndaa ko cuɓanmi .
50001023	Hakkiilo am sendake ɗiɗi : Mi ɓuri yiɗugo mi dilla , mi wonda bee Almasiihu , kanjum ɗum ɓurantam wooɗugo piw .
50001024	Ammaa ngam daliila mooɗon kam , ndikka mi jooɗo tawon .
50001025	Ngam maajum anndumi fakat mi jooɗoto , mi wonda bee mooɗon fuu , mi walla on ɓesdaago , haa nuɗɗinki mon heewa seyo .
50001026	To mi wartani on , on keɓan mantoraago kawtal mon bee Yeesu Almasiihu ngam daliila am .
50001027	Ammaa sey joonde mon fottida bee linjiila Almasiihu . Koo mi heɓan warugo haa mooɗon , mi yi'a on , koo mi heɓataa boo , sey mi nana kubar mon , on ɗon tabiti dow hakkiilo wooto , on ɗon kaɓda ngam nuɗɗinki linjiila bee ɓernde woore .
50001028	Taa acce konne'en kulna on koo seɗɗa . Bee maajum Allah hollirta ɓe kamɓe ɓe halkuɓe , ammaa onon on jaaliiɓe .
50001029	Allah waɗani on mo''ere ngam haa on teddina Almasiihu , naa bee nuɗɗingo mo tan , ammaa bee munyango bone ngam maako boo .
50001030	On ɗon kawta bee am nder haɓre . Naane on ngi'i haɓre am nde'e , jonta boo on ɗon nana haala maare .
50002001	To goɗɗo tiɗɗini on bee innde Almasiihu , to o wolwani on bee yiide , on njaɓan ɗum na ? On ɗon camɗina kawtal ngal Ruuhu Allah hawriti en na ? On ɗon ngiɗindira na ? On ɗon enɗindira na ?
50002002	To nonnon , nden kam timmidine seyo am : Njooɗode hakkiilo wooto e yiide woore e ɓernde woore e anniya ngoota .
50002003	Taa kuuwe kooɗume bee numooji kaajuɗi malla ngam mantoraago ko'e mon meere . Taa koomoy mawnito dow woɗɓe , ammaa o laara ɓe bana ɓuranɓe mo .
50002004	Taa goɗɗo ɗaɓɓa ko nafata hoore mum , ammaa ko nafata deerɗum'en .
50002005	Kuuwindire foroy fodde numooji iwɗi haa Yeesu Almasiihu :
50002006	Kaŋko o woodino darnde Allah ,
50002007	Ammaa o leestini hoore maako ,
50002008	Fakat o leestini hoore maako ,
50002009	Ngam maajum Allah ɓaŋgti mo dow kooɗume fuu ,
50002010	To innde Yeesu ewnaama ,
50002011	Ɗe fuu ɗe teddinan Allah , ɗe ceedoto :
50002012	Soobiraaɓe am , saa'i mi ɗonno wondi bee mooɗon , on ɗowtani yam foroy . Sakkoma jonta nde mi daayiiɗo , ɗowtaneeɗam boo . Kuuwe kisndam mon bee kulol e diwŋgol .
50002013	Ngam Allah bee hoore mum ɗon findina muuyo mon , o ɗon hokka on baawɗe huuwugo ɗum boo , ngam o waɗi anniya hisnugo on .
50002014	Nder kuuɗe mon fuu taa ngurngurte dow Allah , taa ceke yiide maako ,
50002015	ngam haa on laato laaɓɓe ɓe ngalaa aybe , on ɓiɓɓe Allah timmuɓe caka yimɓe duniyaaru wonniiɓe , halluɓe . Sey on njayna caka maɓɓe bana koode asama .
50002016	Njoge kubar ngeendam , haa mi heɓa mantoraago on nder nyalaade Almasiihu , ngam kuugal am e torra am fuu laataaki meere .
50002017	Onon on ɗon lii'ano Allah nuɗɗinki mon e ɗowtaare mon bana dokkal . Teema ?i?am am laatoto dokkal dufeteeŋgal dow dokkal mooɗon . To non kam , mi seyoto , mi hawtanan seyo mooɗon .
50002018	Bana non ceye onon boo , ceyode bee am .
50002019	Mi ɗon hooli Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men , mi heɓan nelugo Timote haa mooɗon yeeso seɗɗa , ngam haa o de'itinammi bee kubar mooɗon .
50002020	Mi walaa goɗɗo mo hakkiilo mum nandi bee ngo maako , cuklaniiɗo on bana maako boo .
50002021	Luttuɓe fuu ɗon cuklano ko'e muuɗum'en , naa kuugal ngam Yeesu Almasiihu .
50002022	Onon on anndi o koolaaɗo . Bana ɓiɗɗo wallirta baaba mum , non o huuwdi bee am ngam linjiila .
50002023	Mi tammi nelugo mo haa mooɗon law , to mi yi'i ko laatanto yam .
50002024	Mi ɗon hooli Jawmiraawo boo , yeeso seɗɗa min bee hoore am mi waran haa mooɗon .
50002025	Mi laari bana pottuɗum mi lornana on deerɗiraawo men Epafroditus , kuuwdoowo bee am , balloowo yam haɓugo . On nelno mo haa am , haa o wallammi nder haaje am .
50002026	Ammaa o ɗon yenwa on masin , hakkiilo maako ummi ngam on nani o nyawɗono .
50002027	Fakat o nyawino haa o ɓadi maayugo . Ammaa Allah enɗi mo , naa Epafroditus tan , ammaa min boo , ngam taa mettamɓeram ɗuuɗanammi .
50002028	Ngam maajum mi yaawɗi lornugo mo haa mooɗon , haa on ceyo fahin bee yi'ugo mo , min boo saklere am usto .
50002029	Njaɓɓe mo bee seyo bana goɗɗo Jawmiraawo . Teddine irin maako ,
50002030	ngam o ɓadino maayugo ngam kuugal Almasiihu . O suklanaaki yoŋki maako , ngam haa o hebbina ko luttuno haa ballal mooɗon ngam am .
50003001	Deerɗam'en , ko lutti wi'eego : Ceyore kawtal mon bee Jawmiraawo . Windango on haala ka'a fahin saklataa yam , ammaa ɗum tabitinan anndal mon .
50003002	Ndeente e waajooɓe halluɓe , dawaaɗi'en ɓe'e , ɗaɓɓooɓe ta''ugo laral ɓandu .
50003003	Mi ɗon wi'a bana ni ngam enen en mari juulnol gooŋɗuŋgol , naa kamɓe , enen huuwanooɓe Allah bee ballal Ruuhu maako . En ɗon mantoro kawtal men bee Yeesu Almasiihu , ammaa en tuugtataako ko yimɓe mbi'ata ɓural muuɗum'en .
50003004	Koyɗum haa am mi tuugto irin ɓural maajum . To goɗɗo tammake woodi daliila tuugtaago ngal , min mi ɓuran mo .
50003005	Nyande joweetataɓre am njuulnaami . Mi danyaama nder Isra'iila , lenyol Benyamin , mi Ibraniŋkeejo asliijo . To hakkilango tawreeta kam , mi Farisaajo .
50003006	Nder maajum mi tiinino masin haa mi toonyino jama'aare Masiihiŋko'en . To woodi gooŋgaaku dow laawol tawreeta , nden kam mi laaɓɗo .
50003007	Kuuje ɗe'e fuu , ɓooyma mi limino ɗe bana riba . Ammaa jonta mi ɗon lima ɗe bana asar , ngam daliila Almasiihu .
50003008	Naa kuuje ɗe'e tan , ammaa mi ɗon lima kooɗume fuu bana asar , ngam mi heɓi ko ɓuri ɗum fuu saman : Mi anndi Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo am . Ngam daliila maako ngudinmi kooɗume . Mi ɗon laara ɗum bana mbuuri meere , ngam haa mi heɓa Almasiihu .
50003009	Sey kawtal bee maako tan ɗaɓɓanmi . Mi meetataa ɗaɓɓugo gooŋgaaku am bee ɗowtanaago tawreeta . Ammaa mi ɗon ɗaɓɓa yerduye Allah bee nuɗɗingo Almasiihu . Ngam to mi ɗon nuɗɗini Almasiihu , nden kam Allah yerdoto yam .
50003010	Walaa ko ngiɗmi , sey anndugo Almasiihu e baawɗe ummitineeki mum . Mi yiɗi hawtugo bee maako nder torraaji maako e maayde maako ,
50003011	ngam haa mi heɓa min boo mi yotto ummitineeki maayɓe .
50003012	Mi wi'aay mi heɓi ɗum fuu malla mi yottake keerol daɗadaɗa . Ammaa mi ɗon dogga bee sembe ngam haa mi naŋga keɓal jaalorgal , ngam Almasiihu aarti , naŋgi yam .
50003013	Fakat , deerɗam'en , mi laaraay hoore am bana mi yottake . Ndaa ko mbaɗanmi : Mi ɗon yejjita ko accumi ɓaawo , mi ɗon tiito yeeso .
50003014	Mi ɗon haɓda yottaago keerol daɗadaɗa , haa mi heɓa keɓal daɗki , waato ngeendam haa asama . Ngam ngeendam maajum Allah ewnori yam bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
50003015	Sey en numa bana non to en limi ko'e men nder timmuɓe . To woodi goɗɗum ko paamroton bee laawol feere , Allah waŋginanan on ɗum .
50003016	Bee non fuu , sey en tokko laawol ngol tokkiiɗen haa jonta .
50003017	Kuuwe bana am , onon deerɗam'en , ndaare tokkiiɓe misaalu ɗum keɓɗon haa amin .
50003018	Ko mbi'mi on nde ɗuuɗɗum , jonta mbi'anmi ɗum bee gonɗi : Woodi ɗuuɗɓe huuwanɓe bana konne'en kubar maayde Almasiihu dow leggal gaafaaŋgal .
50003019	Ragare maɓɓe ɗum halkere . Suunooji maɓɓe laati ɗowanteeɗo maɓɓe . Ko ɓe mbi'ata tedduŋgal maɓɓe , ɗum yawnaare maɓɓe . Ɓe ɗon cuklano kuuje duniyaaru tan .
50003020	Ammaa enen kam , saare meeɗen haa asama woni . En ɗon ndeeni garoyki Kisnoowo en , Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , iwanɗo haa ton .
50003021	Kaŋko o waylan ɓalli men tampuɗi leesɗi , haa ɗi laato bana ɓandu maako marndu tedduŋgal . Ngam o baawɗo doolugo kuuje fuu haa ɗe ɗowtano mo .
50004001	Onon deerɗam'en yiɗaaɓe , ngam maajum tabite bana ni nder kawtal mon bee Jawmiraawo . Mi ɗon yenwa on masin , onon on daliila seyo am e daraja am .
50004002	Mi ɗon toro Ewodi e Sintike haa ɓe narra bana deerɗiraaɓe rewɓe , nuɗɗinɓe Jawmiraawo .
50004003	An boo , soobaajo am koolaaɗo , mi ɗon toro ma a walla rewɓe ɓe'e , ngam ɓe tiini huuwdugo bee am ngam linjiila , kamɓe e Kelemes e luttuɓe huuwdooɓe bee am . Inɗe maɓɓe fuu mbindaama nder deftere ngeendam .
50004004	Ceye foroy ngam daliila kawtal mon bee Jawmiraawo . Mi wi'an ɗum fahin : Ceye !
50004005	Mbooɗeeŋga mon waŋgana yimɓe fuu . Jawmiraawo ɓadi warugo .
50004006	Taa caklane kooɗume , ammaa anndine Allah haaje mon fuu bee do'a e tornde , bee yettoore boo .
50004007	Salaaman Allah ɓurka faamu neɗɗo fuu , aynan ɓerɗe mon e numooji mon nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
50004008	Deerɗam'en , ndaa ko lutti wi'eego : Kakkilane ko wooɗi , ko he'i mantoore , waato ko gooŋɗi , ko fotti , ko laaɓi , ko he'i yiɗeego e teddineego .
50004009	Kuuwe ko anndinmi on , ko ekkitinmi on bee bolle am e kuuɗe am . Allah boo , dokkoowo en jam , wondan bee mooɗon .
50004010	Kawtal men bee Jawmiraawo laatani yam daliila seyo maŋgo jonta , ngam on keɓi baawɗe wallugo yam fahin . Koo naane maa , on ɗonno ciftorammi , ammaa on keɓaay hollugo ɗum .
50004011	Mi wi'aay ɗum ngam daliila haaje . Ngam mi ekkiti heynitaago bee ko keɓmi ,
50004012	koo ɗum seɗɗa koo ɗum ɗuuɗɗum masin . Mi ekkiti heynitaago koondey e kootoy , mi anndi weelo e haarannde , ɗuuɗeeŋga e sooynde .
50004013	Mi munyanan kooɗume fuu , ngam Almasiihu hokkatam sembe .
50004014	Ammaa on kuuwi booɗɗum bee wallugo yam jonta nder ɓillaare am .
50004015	Onon Filippi'en on anndi booɗɗum , saa'i min puɗɗi waajingo linjiila , nde ngurtiimi Makedoniya , walaa jama'aare hawti bee am dow haala hokkugo e jaɓugo , sey onon tan .
50004016	Saa'i mi ɗonno haa Tessaloniiki , on neldi yam walliinde , naa nde woore tan .
50004017	Taa nume mi ɗon ɗaɓɓa ceede mon . Mi yiɗi risku mooɗon ɓesdo , waato nuɗɗinki mon waɗa nafuda .
50004018	Yoo , mi heɓi dokkal ngal nelduɗon bee juŋŋgo Epafroditus . Ɗum ɓuri haaje am piw . Ɗum laati bana dokkal urdi mbelndi . Allah seyorto ngal , yerdoto ngal .
50004019	Allah am humtanan on haajeeji mon fuu bee tedduŋgal muuɗum maŋgal , ɗum laatanto on bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
50004020	Tedduŋgal laatano Allah , Baabiraawo men haa abada abadin . Aamiina !
50004021	Koofne yimɓe Allah fuu bee innde Yeesu Almasiihu . Deerɗiraaɓe wonduɓe bee am koofni on .
50004022	Masiihiŋko'en wonɓe haa ɗo fuu koofni on , sakkoma deerɗiraaɓe huuwanooɓe laamiiɗo Roma .
50004023	Mo''ere Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu wondu bee mooɗon fuu .
51001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu bee muuyo Allah , min bee Timote , deerɗiraawo men ,
51001002	yahugo haa yimɓe Allah wonɓe haa Kolossi , deerɗiraaɓe amin tokkiiɓe Almasiihu bee gooŋga :
51001003	Min ɗon ndo'ano on tum . Nder do'a amin , min ɗon ngetta Allah , mo Baabiraawo Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo meeɗen .
51001004	Kadi min nani no on nuɗɗiniri Yeesu Almasiihu , min nani boo no on ngiɗiri nuɗɗinɓe Allah fuu .
51001005	Nde kubar linjiila yotti on , on nani haala tammunde maaka . Non nuɗɗinki mon e yiide mon fuu ndari dow tammunde mon . Tammunde nde , Allah on ɗon ayna nde haa asama .
51001006	Yimɓe ɗon ngaaja linjiila man haa duniyaaru fuu , ka ɗon waddana yimɓe barka . Non ɗum laati haa mooɗon diga nyande on aarti nanugo kubar mo''ere Allah , diga on puɗɗi anndugo linjiila ka bee gooŋga .
51001007	On nani ka haa Epafras , kuuwdiɗɗiraawo amin giɗaaɗo , kuuwanoowo Almasiihu haa mooɗon .
51001008	Kaŋko yecci min haala yiide nde Ruuhu Allah hokki on .
51001009	Ngam maajum min accaay toraago Allah ngam mooɗon diga min nani kubar mon . Min ɗon toro Allah , o anndina on muuyo maako fuu , o hokka on hakkiilo e faamu bee Ruuhu maako .
51001010	Nden kam on mbaawan huuwugo bana Jawmiraawo yiɗi , ko fottanta mo . Joonde mon nafan bee kuuɗe booɗɗe feere feere , on ɓesdoto anndugo Allah boo .
51001011	Allah sembiɗina on bee sembe mum e baawɗe mum mawɗe haa on mbaawa munyugo kooɗume fuu .
51001012	Kadi sey on ngetta Baabiraawo bee seyo ngam kaŋko o yottini on jaɓugo geɗal kuuje booɗɗe fuu ɗe o sigani yimɓe maako nder laamu annoora .
51001013	Ngam o wurtini en baawɗe nyiɓre , o nastini en jam nder laamu Ɓiɗɗo maako giɗaaɗo .
51001014	Bee Ɓiɗɗo oo en keɓi ndimu , hakkeeji boo njaafaama .
51001015	Almasiihu ɗon waŋginana en Allah mo yi'ataake , ngam o nanduɗo bee maako . Kaŋko o afo , ɓurduɗo tagle Allah fuu .
51001016	Bee maako Allah tagri kuuje fuu haa asama e dow lesdi , naa ko yi'ete tan , ammaa ko yi'ataake boo , waato baawɗeeji e laamuuji e mawɓe asama fuu . Allah tagri kuuje fuu bee Almasiihu , o tagi ɗe ngam maako boo .
51001017	Almasiihu aarti ɗe fuu , ngam daliila maako ɗe fuu ɗe laati .
51001018	Kaŋko laati hooreejo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe mo , laatiiɓe ɓandu maako . O fuɗɗoode ngeendam kesam boo , ngam Allah aarti ummitingo mo diga maayde , laatini mo arano nder kooɗume fuu .
51001019	Ngam Allah waɗi anniya , hebbini mo bee baawɗe muuɗum fuu ,
51001020	narrini tageefooji fuu bee muuɗum . Ɓiɗɗo maako huuwi narral man , rufi ?i?am mum , maayi dow leggal gaafaaŋgal . Bana ni Allah timminiri konnaagu bee duniyaaru , narrini tageefooji fuu bee muuɗum , koo ɗi lesdi , koo ɗi asama .
51001021	Naane kam on konne'en Allah ngam daliila kuuɗe mon kalluɗe e numooji mon kalluɗi , on daayiiɓe Allah .
51001022	Ammaa jonta , o soobri bee mooɗon ngam Ɓiɗɗo maako laati neɗɗo , maayi . Ngam maajum on laati yimɓe maako laaɓɓe ɓe ngalaa aybe .
51001023	Ammaa sey on tokko nuɗɗingo , on tabita . Taa on acca kooɗume sottina on diga tammunde nde keɓɗon saa'i on nani linjiila .
51001024	Jonta mi ɗon seyoro boneeji am ngam mooɗon . On anndi Almasiihu yari bone . Ɓandu maako , waato jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe mo , doole ndu yara bone boo . Ko mi torroto ngam mooɗon , kanjum woni geɗal am haa boneeji ɗi'i .
51001025	Allah waɗi yam mi maccuɗo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe . O umri yam mi anndina on kubar maako fuu ngam nafugo on .
51001026	Diga fuɗɗam duniyaaru , Allah suuɗi sirri muuɗum haa koomoy . Ammaa jonta o ɗon waŋgina ɗum haa yimɓe maako .
51001027	Ngam o waɗi anniya waŋgingo tedduŋgal sirri maajum maŋgal ngal o taaskitinani yimɓe ummaatooje fuu . Sirri maajum ɗum Almasiihu gonɗo nder mooɗon , kaŋko oon hokki on tammunde heɓugo geɗal haa tedduŋgal maako .
51001028	Ngam maajum min ɗon ngaajina yimɓe fuu haala Almasiihu oo . Min ɗon maatina ɓe , min ɗon anndina ɓe anndal fuu ngal Allah hokki min , ngam haa min ndarna ɓe yeeso Allah , koomoy maɓɓe laato timmuɗo nder kawtal bee Almasiihu .
51001029	Ngam daliila maajum mi ɗon haɓda masin , mi ɗon torro , baawɗe Almasiihu cembiɗɗe ɗe o hokki yam , kanje kuuwata nder am .
51002001	Mi yiɗi anndingo on no kuugal am saɗiri . Mi ɗon huuwa ɗum ngam mooɗon e ngam yimɓe Lawdikiya . Mi ɗon huuwa ɗum boo ngam yimɓe ɓe meeɗaay yi'ugo yam tawon .
51002002	Mi yiɗi ɓe ndaro bee sembe , ɓe kawta nder yiide , ɓe keewa anndal gooŋga fuu , ɓe paama sirri Allah , kanjum woni Almasiihu .
51002003	Ko neɗɗo waawi anndugo dow Allah , o tawan ɗum fuu haa Almasiihu .
51002004	Mi ɗon wi'a ɗum ngam taa goɗɗo esta on bee dabareeji e ?oye .
51002005	Koo nde mi daayiiɗo on bee ɓandu am boo , mi ɗon wondi bee mooɗon nder numooji am . Mi ɗon seyoro nanugo no on nuɗɗiniri Almasiihu , no on tabitiri haa maako .
51002006	On njaɓi Yeesu Almasiihu , o laati Jawmiraawo mooɗon . Kadi sey on ɗakkotira bee maako boo .
51002007	Tabite nder maako bana no lekki darorto nder lesdi bee ɗaɗi maaki . Ndarne yoŋkiiji mooɗon dow maako , cembiɗine nuɗɗinki mon , njogite ko on ekkiti , ngette Allah tum .
51002008	Kakkile ngam taa goɗɗo esta on bee haala anndal lugguŋgal , malla bee ekkitinol meere iwŋgol haa numooji yimɓe tan . Ko ɓe mbi'ata , ɗum anndinol dow baawɗeeji hawa , naa dow Almasiihu .
51002009	Nder Almasiihu en ɗon ngi'a Allah e no o wa'i fuu .
51002010	To on kawti bee Almasiihu , on ngoodi kawtal bee Allah boo . Almasiihu ɓuri baawɗeeji e ruuhuuji fuu maŋgu .
51002011	Nder kawtal bee maako on keɓi irin juulnolfa . Ammaa naa juulnol ɓandu , mi ɗon wolwa haala juulnol ngol Almasiihu waɗata . Juulnol maajum , ɗum bana ittugo hakkeeji marɗi baawɗe dow ɓalli mooɗon .
51002012	Ngam nde on keɓi ngiiwam baptisma , on laati uwdaaɓe bee Almasiihu . Hawtaade bee maako on laati ummitinaaɓe ngam ngeendam kesam boo , ngam on nuɗɗini baawɗe Allah ummitinɗo Almasiihu diga maayde .
51002013	Naane , Allah ɗonno laara on bana maayɓe ngam daliila hakkeeji mooɗon , ngam Almasiihu waɗanaayno on juulnol go boo . Ammaa jonta Allah yeeɗitini on hawtaade bee Almasiihu . O yaafi hakkeeji meeɗen fuu .
51002014	O seeki ɗereewol nyamaande meeɗen ɗuunde , ɓilluŋgol en bee umrooje muuɗum . O meeriɗiniri ngol bee tiggugo ngol haa gaafaaŋgal .
51002015	Bana non o ɓortiri baawɗeeji e ruuhuuji fuu . O semtini ɗi yeeso yimɓe fuu , saa'i o yahri ɗi , ɗi kaɓɓaaɗi nder jama'aare maako .
51002016	Taa goɗɗo daama on bee umrooje dow nyaamdu e njaram , koo dow nyalɗe ceniiɗe , koo dow juulde hakkunde lebbi , koo dow nyande siwtorde .
51002017	Ɗum fuu ɗum misaalu ngam kuuje tammiiɗe warugo tan , ammaa gooŋga kuuje man woni haa Almasiihu .
51002018	Woodi woɗɓe , sujidanooɓe malaa'ika'en , wolwanɓe haala kaayeefiiji ɗi ɓe ngi'i , koomoy ɗon laara ɓe bana ɓe yaŋkiniiɓe . Taa acce ɓe mbaɗa on rikisi bee haala maɓɓe meere , ɓe mawnitiiɓe bee numooji yimɓe .
51002019	Ɓe acci ɗakkotirgo bee Almasiihu , mo laati hoore ɓandu muuɗum , kayru woni jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe mo . Ngam daliila hoore man , ɓandu fuu hawti bee jokke e ɗaɗi , ɗon mawna bana Allah muuyi .
51002020	On maaydi bee Almasiihu , ngam maajum walaa ko yaali on bee baawɗeeji e ruuhuuji gonɗi nder hawa . Koni on tokkoto huuwugo bana yimɓe duniya ? Koni on ɗowtanto dookaaji bana ɗi'i :
51002021	" Taa meem ɗum " , " Taa metta ɗuma " , " Taa meem ɗu'um boo " .
51002022	Ɗum fuu ɗum umrooje meere e anndinol yimɓe . Allah waɗi kuuje ɗe ngam yimɓe kuuwtinira ɗe .
51002023	Fakat to goɗɗo ɗon laara umrooje ɗe bana marɗe saman , o jaɓi ɗe , nden kam o doolan hoore maako sujidango baawɗeeji go , o huuwa kuuɗe yaŋkinaare , o elta ɓandu maako bee caatal boo . Ammaa kuuɗe ɗe fuu nafataa ngam jaalaago suunooji ɓandu sam .
51003001	On ummiti bee Almasiihu , on keɓi ngeendam kesam . Ngam maajum tiitine numooji mon dow kuuje asama , haa Almasiihu jooɗi haa nyaamo Allah .
51003002	Tokke numtugo kuuje gonɗe ton , naa kuuje duniyaaru .
51003003	Ngam on maayi , ngeendam mooɗon ɗon suuɗi bee Almasiihu haa Allah .
51003004	Fakat , Almasiihu woni daliila ngeendam mooɗon . To o waŋgi , onon boo on mbaŋgan bee maako , koomoy yi'an tedduŋgal ngal o hokki on .
51003005	Sey on mbara suunooji luttuɗi nder mooɗon , bana daakaareeku e huuwugo karamɗum e waɗugo njeenu e ɗaɓɓugo kuuje kalluɗe e suuno ( ngam suuno e sujidango labbi , ɗum gootum ) .
51003006	Ngam daliila suunooji ɗi'i , ɓernuki Allah waran dow sooyɓe ɗowtaare fuu .
51003007	Naane onon boo on tokki irin suunooji ɗi .
51003008	Ammaa jonta , sey on ngudina ɗi fuu : ɓernuki e tikkere e numooji kalluɗi . Taa kuudi malla bolle kalluɗe ngurto kunduɗe mon .
51003009	Taa pewpewtire , ngam on ngudini gikku mon naane bee al'aadaaji mum ,
51003010	on keɓi gikku kesu , koomoy mooɗon laati neɗɗo keso . Allah mo tagi neɗɗo keso oo , ɗon tokko hesɗitingo mo haa o nanda bee Allah , haa on fuu on annda mo bee laaɓɗum .
51003011	Ngam maajum , walaa ko sendata Yahuudu'en bee ummaatooje goɗɗe , juulniiɓe bee ɓe njuulnaaki , bilki'en bee tullidiɗɓe , malla maccuɓe bee rimɓe . Sey Almasiihu feere muuɗum lutti , kooɗume fuu hawti nder maako .
51003012	On laati yimɓe Allah ngam o yiɗi on , o suɓi on . Ngam maajum sey on laato enɗooɓe , wooɗɓe , yaŋkiniiɓe , ne'iiɓe , munyɓe .
51003013	Mballindire . To goɗɗo mon woodi daliila wullaago deerɗum , ndikka ɓe njaafotira . Njaafotire bana no Jawmiraawo yaafori on .
51003014	Dow ɗum fuu , ɓesde yiide , ngam kayre tabitinta kawtal mooɗon .
51003015	Hoolaare nde Almasiihu hokki on , acce nde heewa ɓerɗe mon . Allah hawti on bana ɓandu wooru ngam on njooɗodo bee hoolaare man . Ngette mo .
51003016	Acce kubar Almasiihu hebbina ɓerɗe mon . Ngaajindire , mballindire bee anndal e hakkiilo fuu . Ngimane Allah bee yettoore nder ɓerɗe mon . Ngimane mo jabuuraaje e maŋgtooje e gime ɗe Ruuhu maako hokkata on .
51003017	Ko kuuwoton , ko mbolwoton fuu laato bee innde Jawmiraawo Yeesu . Ngam daliila maako , ngeendam mooɗon fuu laato yettoore haa Allah Baabiraawo .
51003018	Onon rewɓe , ɗowtane worɓe mon , kanjum fottani Jawmiraawo .
51003019	Onon worɓe , ngiɗe rewɓe mon , taa caatane ɓe .
51003020	Onon ɓikkoy , ɗowtane saarooji mon , ngam ɗum fottanan Jawmiraawo .
51003021	Onon saarooji , taa elte ɓikkoy mon bee caatal , ngam taa ɓerɗe maɓɓe caklo .
51003022	Onon jeyaaɓe , ɗowtane jawmiraaɓe mon nder kuuɗe fuu . Taa kuuwane ɓe dow gite maɓɓe tan , ngam yerdingo ɓe , ammaa ɗowtane ɓe bee ɓernde gooŋgaare ngam on hulɓe Jawmiraawo .
51003023	Kuuwe kooɗume fuu bee anniya ɓernde , ngam on huuwanooɓe Jawmiraawo , naa yimɓe .
51003024	Taa ngejjite , Jawmiraawo oon warjanto on , on keɓan ko o nufani yimɓe maako . Ngam Jawmiraawo mo on kuuwanta ɗum , kaŋko woni Almasiihu .
51003025	Mo waɗi aybe , koo o moye , Allah hiitoto mo ngam aybe maako , ngam Allah sendindirtaa yimɓe .
51004001	Onon jawmiraaɓe , njoge maccuɓe mon bee gooŋgaaku bana no haani . Taa ngejjite , onon boo on ngoodi Jawmiraawo haa asama .
51004002	Tiine waɗugo do'a , taa come yettugo Allah .
51004003	To on ɗon toro , toraneeɗam min boo , ngam haa Allah hoynanammi waajugo habaru maako , haa mi waŋgina sirri Almasiihu . Ngam daliila sirri man mi ɗon haa fursina .
51004004	Tore Allah o wallammi waajugo bee laaɓɗum , bana ko haani .
51004005	Kakkilane joonde mon caka yimɓe ɓe nuɗɗinaay . Koondey on keɓi waŋgingo nuɗɗinki mon , mbaɗe ɗum .
51004006	Sey bolle mon laato belɗe , nafooje . Annde no on njaaborto koomoy .
51004007	Too , Tikikus yeccan on kubar am fuu . Mi yiɗi mo masin ngam o ɗon huuwana Jawmiraawo hawtaade bee am , o koolaaɗo nder kuuɗe maako boo .
51004008	Mi ɗon nela mo haa mooɗon ngam o seyna on bee kubar njamu am , o sembiɗina on .
51004009	O yahdan bee Onesimus , deerɗiraawo men giɗaaɗo , koolaaɗo , mo lesdi mon . Ɓe ngeccan on ko waɗi haa ɗo fuu .
51004010	Aristarkus , gonduɗo bee am nder fursina hoofni on . Non boo Markus , bandiraawo Barnabas . ( Mi wi'no on , to o yottake haa mon , njaɓɓe mo booɗɗum . )
51004011	Yeesu coometeeɗo Yustus hoofni on . Nder Yahuudu'en nuɗɗinɓe , sey yimɓe tato ɓe'e kuuwdata kuugal laamu Allah bee am . Ɓe mballi yam ɗuuɗɗum .
51004012	Epafras hoofni on . Kaŋko boo mo mooɗon , o kuuwanoowo Yeesu Almasiihu . O accaay toraago Allah ngam mooɗon . O ɗon toro mo o tabitina on , haa on laato he'uɓe , taaskiiɓe ngam huuwugo muuyo Allah fuu .
51004013	Min bee hoore am mi anndi no o huuwranta on bee sembe , no o huuwranta yimɓe Lawdikiya e yimɓe Hiyerapolis boo .
51004014	Luka , dokta men giɗaaɗo , hoofni on . Non Demas boo .
51004015	Koofne deerɗiraaɓe wonɓe haa Lawdikiya . Koofne Nimfa e nuɗɗinɓe mooɓtotooɓe haa saare maako .
51004016	To on timmini jaŋgugo bataakewol ngol , sey on ndokka ngol nuɗɗinɓe haa Lawdikiya , kamɓe boo njaŋga ngol . Njaŋge boo bataakewol ngol jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe haa Lawdikiya neldata on .
51004017	Ngecce Arkippus o tiino huuwugo kuugal Jawmiraawo ngal o halfina .
51004018	Ndaa ko mbindumi bee juŋŋgo am : Mi hoofni on . Taa ngejjite mi kaɓɓaaɗo bee callallu !
52001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol e Silas e Timote , yahugo jama'aare Masiihiŋko'en wonɓe haa Tessaloniiki , yimɓe Allah Baabiraawo e Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu :
52001002	Koondeye min toroto Allah , min ɗon ciftora on , min ɗon ngetta Allah , Baabiraawo men , ngam daliila mooɗon fuu . Min ɗon ciftora tum no on kuuwrata bee nuɗɗinki , no on tiinorto bee yiide , no on tabitiri nder ngenka mon haa Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu waroya .
52001003	
52001004	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , min anndi Allah yiɗi on , suɓi on haa on laato yimɓe muuɗum .
52001005	Saa'i min ngaaji on linjiila , ɗum laataaki bolle tan . Ammaa Allah waŋgini baawɗe mum bee maaka . Ruuhu maako ceniiŋgu walli min , hokki min anndal gooŋga tabitŋgal . On anndi no min kuuwri caka mooɗon ngam hayru mon .
52001006	On tokki min , on tokki Jawmiraawo boo . Koo on ɓilliiɓe masin , on njaɓi kubar maako bee seyo ngo Ruuhu Allah hokkata ɗum .
52001007	Bana ni on laatori misaalu haa tiinaare ngam nuɗɗinɓe nder lesɗe Makedoniya e Akaya fuu .
52001008	Haa mooɗon kubar Jawmiraawo iwi , yehi gaɗa keeri lesɗe ɗe'e . Kootoy fuu yimɓe nani no nuɗɗinirɗon Allah , walaa haaje minin min mbolwa haala man .
52001009	Kamɓe ɓe ɗon ngecca min no on njaɓri min , no on acciri labbi haa on ɗowtano Allah geeto , gooŋgaajo .
52001010	Jonta on ɗon ndeena garoyki Ɓiɗɗo maako diga asama , Yeesu mo Allah ummitini diga maayde , kisnanɗo en tikkere Allah warannde .
52002001	Deerɗiraaɓe , onon bee ko'e mon on anndi garki amin haa mooɗon laataaki meere .
52002002	Hiddeko min ngara haa mooɗon , ɓe toonyi min haa Filippi , ɓe kuɗi min , onon on anndi ɗum . Ammaa Allah men sembiɗini ɓerɗe amin haa min anndina on linjiila maako , koo nder haɓre ɗuunde boo .
52002003	Waaju amin daraaki dow numooji pewe malla dow anniyaaji kalluɗi , min ɗaɓɓaay ?oyrugo yimɓe boo .
52002004	Ammaa Allah linyi min , yerdi min , halfini min waaju linjiila , bana non min mbolwirta boo . Min ɗaɓɓaay fottango yimɓe , sey Allah , linyoowo ɓerɗe amin .
52002005	On anndi min meeɗaay wolwango on bee welugo hunduko , walaa suuno saawi nder bolle amin , Allah woni ceedoowo amin !
52002006	Min ɗaɓɓaay tedduŋgal haa yimɓe , koo haa mooɗon koo haa woɗɓe .
52002007	Fakat , min mbaawanno hollugo on maŋgu amin , ngam min nelaaɓe Almasiihu . Ammaa min mboonani on bana daada kakkilananɗo ɓiyum'en .
52002008	Min ngiɗi on masin haa min ndokkanno on koo yoŋkiiji amin , naa linjiila Allah tan . Bana ni yiide amin ɗuuɗiri haa mooɗon .
52002009	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , on ɗon ciftora torra amin e bone amin . Saa'i min ngaaji on linjiila , min kuuwi ngam nguure amin jemma bee naaŋge fuu , ngam taa min teddana koo gooto mooɗon .
52002010	Onon nuɗɗinɓe on seedooɓe amin , Allah boo ceedoowo amin , min njooɗori caka mooɗon min laaɓɓe , huuwɓe ko fotti , min ngalaa feloore .
52002011	Min kuuwani koomoy mooɗon bana baaba huuwranta ɓiyum'en .
52002012	Min ngaaji on , min nde'itini on , min tiɗɗini on on kuuwa ko fottanta Allah ewniiɗo on wondugo bee muuɗum nder laamu mum e tedduŋgal mum .
52002013	Min accataa yettugo Allah , ngam saa'i min ngaaji on kubaruwol maako , on njaɓaay ngol bana wolde yimɓe , ammaa bana wolde Allah . Fakat ɗum wolde Allah huuwoore nder mooɗon , onon nuɗɗinɓe .
52002014	Ko laatani jama'aaje yimɓe Allah nder Yahudiya , waato Masiihiŋko'en wonɓe ton fuu , ɗum laatani on boo , onon deerɗiraaɓe . On munyani torraaji bana ɗi maɓɓe . On njari bone haa yimɓe lenyol mon , bana ɓeya boo njari bone haa Yahuudu'en .
52002015	Yahuudu'en ɓe'e mbari Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men , e annabo'en , ɓe ɗon toonyo min boo . Ɓe pottantaa Allah , ɓe ɗon kona yimɓe fuu .
52002016	Ɓe ɗon tiino haɗugo min anndingo yimɓe ummaatooje goɗɗe kubar kisndam maɓɓe . Bana ni ɓe kebbinirta muudoore hakkeeji maɓɓe haa rufa . Ammaa tikkere Allah ukkani ɓe bee caatal mum fuu .
52002017	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , neeɓi min ceedi bee mooɗon , waato bee gite , naa bee ɓernde . Min ngenwi on masin . Ngam maajum min tiini ɗuuɗɗum haa min keɓa yi'ugo on fahin .
52002018	Min mbaɗi anniya lortaago haa mooɗon . Min Pol mi waɗi anniya man naa nde woore tan . Ammaa Sayɗaanu haɗi min .
52002019	Fakat , onon on laati daliila hoolaare amin e seyo amin , onon feere mon . On meetaleewol jaalorgal amin boo ngol min mantorto , to Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men waroyi .
52002020	Fakat , onon on tedduŋgal amin e seyo amin .
52003001	Too , haa ragare ɗum salori min . Ngam maajum min tabitini min njooɗo haa Ateena feere amin ,
52003002	min nela deerɗiraawo men Timote haa mooɗon . Kaŋko woni kuuwdiɗɗiraawo Allah , kuuwdoowo bee amin ngam waaju linjiila Almasiihu . Min neli mo haa o sembiɗina on , o tabitina nuɗɗinki mon ,
52003003	ngam taa goɗɗo mooɗon koo gooto loro ɓaawo ngam daliila torraaji keɓanɗi en . On anndi kanji ngoni geɗal men bee muuyo Allah .
52003004	Yaake min ɗonno ngondi bee mooɗon , min mbi'i on torraaji ukkanto en . Nonnon ɗum laatori , onon on anndi .
52003005	Ngam maajum mi waawaay mi tokko munyugo , mi neli Timote haa mooɗon , o annda no nuɗɗinki mon wa'i . Mi de'itaay , mi ɗonno numa teema jarriboowo heɓi do''ugo on , meeriɗini kuugal amin fuu .
52003006	Ammaa jonta Timote warti , seyni min bee kubar nuɗɗinki mon e yiide mon . O yecci min on ɗon ciftora min foroy bee yiide , on ɗon ngenwa yi'ugo min bana minin boo min ngenwirta on .
52003007	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , on ɗon tabiti nder nuɗɗinki . Kanjum ɗum tiɗɗini ɓerɗe amin nder torra amin e saklere amin fuu .
52003008	Jonta yoŋkiiji amin ngeeɗiti , ngam min anndi on ɗon tabiti nder kawtal mon bee Jawmiraawo .
52003009	Kadi yettoore fuu nde min ngettirta Allah ngam mooɗon , he'i na ? Min ɗon ngetta mo ngam daliila seyo maŋgo ngo ceynuɗon min yeeso maako .
52003010	Jemma bee naaŋge min ɗon toro mo o hoynana min yi'ugo on gite bee gite , haa min kebbitina ko relli haa nuɗɗinki mon .
52003011	Allah , Baabiraawo men , e Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu koynana min yahugo haa mooɗon .
52003012	Jawmiraawo mawnina yiide mon , ɗuɗɗina nde hakkunde mooɗon , non boo hedi yimɓe fuu , haa nde laato bana yiide nde min ngiɗi on .
52003013	O tabitina ɓerɗe mon haa on ndaro yeeso Allah , Baabiraawo men , on senaaɓe ɓe ngalaa feloore , to Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men wardi bee malaa'ika'en mum fuu . Aamiina .
52004001	Ko lutti wi'ugo on , onon deerɗiraaɓe , ndaa ɗum : On ekkiti haa amin no Masiihiŋko'en njooɗorto haa pottana Allah . Bana non mbaɗoton boo . Jonta min ɗon toro on , min ɗon tiɗɗina on bee innde Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men , on ɓesdo yeeso yeeso .
52004002	On anndi umrooje ɗe min ndokki on bee baawɗe maako .
52004003	Ngam Allah muuyi on laato laaɓɓe , on ndaayo haala njeenu fuu .
52004004	Koomoy gorko haa mooɗon ekkito wondugo bee debbo mum bee naŋgtaare e neɗɗaaku ,
52004005	naa bee suuno bana yimɓe ɓe anndaa Allah .
52004006	Taa goɗɗo waɗa deerɗum aybefa , taa o waɗa mo rikisi nder filu . Min mbi'i on ɗum diga ɓooyma , min ndeentini on : Jawmiraawo hiitoto huuwanɓe irin kuuje ɗe'e .
52004007	Ngam Allah ewnaaki en haa en laato soɓɓe , ammaa en laato senaaɓe .
52004008	Ngam maajum , to goɗɗo salake umrooje ɗe'e , naa neɗɗo o sali , ammaa Allah , dokkuɗo on Ruuhu mum ceniiŋgu .
52004009	Walaa haaje min mbindana on haala yiide hakkunde deerɗiraaɓe . Ngam Allah bee hoore mum anndini on yiɗindirgo .
52004010	Bana non kuuwroton boo hedi deerɗiraaɓe fuu nder lesdi Makedoniya . Ammaa min ɗon toro on on ɓesdo yeeso yeeso .
52004011	Tiine jooɗaago jam , cuklane kuuɗe mon , kuuwe ngam nguure mon boo , bana no min mbi'i on diga ɓooyma .
52004012	Nden kam joonde mon fottan caka yimɓe ɓe nuɗɗinaay , on teddantaa koomoy .
52004013	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , min ngiɗi on paama haala maayɓe , ngam taa on laato suniiɓe bana yimɓe ɓe ngalaa tammunde .
52004014	En ɗon nuɗɗini Yeesu maayi , ummiti . Bana non boo maayɓe nuɗɗinnooɓe Yeesu , Allah wartiran ɓe hawtaade bee Yeesu .
52004015	Ko min mbi'ata on jonta , ɗum wolde iwnde haa Jawmiraawo : Enen luttuɓe bee yoŋki haa nyalaade garoyki Jawmiraawo , en aartataa maayɓe sam .
52004016	To Allah umri bee sawtu , to ardiiɗo malaa'ika'en hooli , luwal Allah boo fuufaama , nden kam Jawmiraawo mo asama jippoto . Maayɓe nuɗɗinnooɓe Almasiihu aartan ummitaago .
52004017	Ɓaawo maɓɓe enen luttuɓe bee yoŋki saa'i maajum en mooɓteteeɓe bee maɓɓe nder duule , ngam haa en potta bee Jawmiraawo nder hawa . Bana ni ngondirten bee Jawmiraawo haa foroy .
52004018	Kadi , nde'itindire bee bolle ɗe'e .
52005001	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , walaa haaje min mbindana on haala saa'iiji e wakkatiiji kuuje ɗe'e fuu laatoto .
52005002	Ngam onon bee ko'e mon on anndi booɗɗum , nyalaade Jawmiraawo waran dow yimɓe bana gujjo garanɗo jemma .
52005003	To ɓe mbi'i : " Jam kooɗume , walaa torra " , nden kam halkere ukkanto ɓe bana luuwe ngaranta ɓesnanɗo , ɓe ndaɗataa sam .
52005004	Ammaa onon deerɗiraaɓe on njooɗaaki nder nyiɓre , haa nyalaade maajum wara dow mooɗon bana gujjo .
52005005	On fuu on yimɓe annoora , on yimɓe nyalawma . En laataaki yimɓe jemma malla nyiɓre .
52005006	Ngam maajum taa en ɗaano bana woɗɓe , ammaa en ayna , taa en nguyka .
52005007	Ɗaaniiɓe kam , bee jemma ɓe ɗaanoto . Wuykuɓe boo , bee jemma ɓe nguykata .
52005008	Ammaa enen en yimɓe nyalawma . Ngam maajum taa nguyken . Sey en ɓorno nuɗɗinki e yiide bana sulke , en kufna tammunde kisndam bana hufneere njamndi .
52005009	Ngam Allah jo''inaay en haa maaten tikkere muuɗum , ammaa en kisra bee Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
52005010	Kaŋko o maayi mbattudi meeɗen ngam haa en ngeeɗa bee maako , koo to en luttuɓe bee yoŋki koo to en maayɓe saa'i o waroyta .
52005011	Ngam maajum ngaajindire , mballindire bana no mbaɗoton jonta .
52005012	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , min ɗon toro on : Teddine suklaniiɓe on , suɓaaɓe Jawmiraawo haa ɓe ardo on , ɓe anndina on boo .
52005013	Teddine ɓe , ngiɗe ɓe ngam daliila kuugal maɓɓe caka mooɗon . Njooɗode on narruɓe .
52005014	Deerɗiraaɓe , min ɗon toro on boo on pela mbaateendam'en , on tiɗɗina tampa-ɓerɗe'en , on mballa tampuɓe , on munyana yimɓe fuu .
52005015	Kakkile ngam taa goɗɗo lornana keeddiɗɗum halleende bee halleende . Ammaa foroy tiine huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga hakkunde mooɗon , non boo haa yimɓe fuu .
52005016	Ceye foroy .
52005017	Taa acce waɗugo do'a .
52005018	Ngette Allah ngam kooɗume fuu . Kanjum woni ko Allah ɗaɓɓata haa mooɗon , onon hawtuɓe bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
52005019	Taa kaɗe kuugal Ruuhu Allah .
52005020	Taa njawe annabaakuuji .
52005021	Linye kuuje fuu , njogite ko wooɗi .
52005022	Ammaa ndaaye halleende koondeyeere .
52005023	Allah , dokkoowo en jam , timmitina senugo on , ayna on on laaɓɓe bee ruuhu e yoŋki e ɓandu fuu haa nyalaade garoyki Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
52005024	Allah , ewniiɗo on huuwanan on ɗum , ngam o koolniiɗo .
52005025	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , ndo'ane min .
52005026	Koofne deerɗiraaɓe fuu bee harlotirgo .
52005027	Mi ɗon toro on ɗuuɗɗum bee innde Jawmiraawo , ngam haa on njaŋgana deerɗiraaɓe fuu bataakewol ngol .
52005028	Mo''ere Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu wondu bee mooɗon .
53001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol e Silas e Timote , yahugo haa jama'aare Masiihiŋko'en wonɓe haa Tessaloniiki , ɓe yimɓe Allah , Baabiraawo men , e Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu :
53001002	Allah Baabiraawo , e Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo men ndokka on mo''ere e jam .
53001003	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , ɓerɗe amin keewi yettoore , sey min ngetta Allah foroy ngam daliila mooɗon . Kanjum ɗum fotti , ngam nuɗɗinki mon ɗon mawna masin , yiide hakkunde mooɗon boo ɗon ɓesdo yeeso yeeso .
53001004	Ngam maajum min ɗon mantoro on nder jama'aaje yimɓe Allah fuu . Min ɗon ngecca ɓe no on njogori nuɗɗinki mon , on munyananɓe toonyaare e boneeji fuu .
53001005	Kanjum woni seedamku no Allah hiitorto bee gooŋga . On ɗon njara bone ngam laamu Allah , bee maajum o laatinan on fotanɓe nastugo ngu .
53001006	Ngam Allah huuwan ko fotti , o hiitoto ɓillooɓe on , o ukkanan ɓe ɓillaare .
53001007	Ammaa onon ɓilliiɓe jonta , o siwtinan on bee amin . Kanjum ɗum laatoto saa'i Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men mo asama , waŋgata haa duniyaaru , kaŋko e malaa'ika'en maako , seedooɓe baawɗe maako .
53001008	O waran bee yiite huɓɓanŋge ngam haa o hiito heefeerɓe ɓe teddinaay Allah , e kooɓeye ɓe ɗowtanaaki linjiila Jawmiraawo men Yeesu .
53001009	Kamɓe ɓe hiitorteeɓe halkere duumiinde , ɓe sendeteeɓe bee Jawmiraawo e tedduŋgal baawɗe mum .
53001010	Ɗum laatoto nyalaade go , to o wari ngam haa yimɓe maako teddina mo , nuɗɗinɓe mo fuu kayɗina mo . Onon boo on ngondan bee maɓɓe , ngam on nuɗɗini seedamku amin .
53001011	Ngam maajum min ɗon ndo'ano on foroy . Min ɗon toro Allah men fotina on heɓugo ngeendam ɗam o ewni on haa muuɗum . Kaŋko bee baawɗe maako hebbina anniyaaji mon haa kuuwon mbooɗeeŋga , o timmitina kuugal nuɗɗinki mon .
53001012	Bana ni teddinirton innde Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men , kaŋko boo o hokkan on tedduŋgal . Ɗum fuu ɗum laatoto bee mo''ere Allah men e Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
53002001	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , on ɗon ndeena Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu wara , en mooɓto haa maako . Ammaa min ɗon toro on :
53002002	Taa hakkiilooji mon ummo law , taa on kula to goɗɗo wi'i on nyalaade Jawmiraawo wari . Teema goɗɗo waɗan annabaaku bana non , malla o waaja on ɗum , malla o wi'a minin min mbindi ɗum nder bataakewol .
53002003	Taa acce goɗɗo esta on koonoy , ngam nyalaade maajum warataa , sonaa yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe aarta , tuurtana Allah , neɗɗo kalluɗo boo waŋga , mo hoddiranaama halkere .
53002004	Kaŋko o dartanto kooɗume ko yimɓe cujidanta , ko ɓe mbi'ata ɗowanteeɗo . O ɓurnan hoore maako dow kooɗume fuu , o jooɗoto nder haykaliiru Allah , o wi'an kaŋko woni Allah .
53002005	On ciftoraay na ? Mi wi'i on ɗum fuu saa'i mi ɗonno wondi bee mooɗon .
53002006	On anndi ko haɗata ɗum laataago jonta . Ammaa to saa'iire fottannde waɗi , neɗɗo kalluɗo go waŋgan .
53002007	Baawɗe tuurtol sirriije ɗon kuuwa koo jonta boo . Ammaa kuuje go laatataako , sonaa to kaɗanɗo ɗe sotti , nden kam ɗe laatoto .
53002008	Ɓaawo maajum kalluɗo go waŋgan . Ammaa Yeesu , Jawmiraawo men mbaran mo bee poofɗe hunduko mum , halkan mo bee baŋguki mum saa'i o waroyta .
53002009	Kalluɗo oo waran bee baawɗe Sayɗaanu , huuwan kuuɗe mawɗe e kaayeefiiji pewooji .
53002010	O estan majjuɓe fuu bee hiilaaji maako kalluɗi . Ɓe majjan ngam ɓe cali yiɗugo gooŋga ka hisnanno ɓe .
53002011	Ngam maajum Allah nelanan ɓe baawɗe esto haa ɓe nuɗɗina fewre .
53002012	Kooɓeye ɓe nuɗɗinaay gooŋga , ɓe ceyori junuuba , ɓe hiiteteeɓe .
53002013	Ammaa sey min ngetta Allah foroy ngam daliila mooɗon , onon deerɗiraaɓe . Jawmiraawo yiɗi on , Allah suɓi on haa on aarta hisneego . On kisan ngam Ruuhu Allah ɗon huuwa nder mooɗon , ngam on nuɗɗini gooŋga boo .
53002014	Min ngaaji on linjiila . Bee maaka Allah ewni on haa on keɓa geɗal mon haa tedduŋgal Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
53002015	Ngam maajum , onon deerɗiraaɓe , tabite , njogite ko min anndini on bee bolle amin e bataakewol amin .
53002016	Allah , Baabiraawo men yiɗi en , hokki en tammunde tabinde , tiɗɗini ɓerɗe men haa foroy bee mo''ere mum . Kaŋko e Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu
53002017	nde'itina ɓerɗe mon , ndokka on sembe huuwugo e wolwugo ko wooɗi .
53003001	Ko lutti wi'eego , onon deerɗiraaɓe , ndaa ɗum : Ndo'ane min ngam haa kubaruwol Jawmiraawo saŋkito law , yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe teddina ngol bana ko laati haa mooɗon .
53003002	Tore Allah boo haa o hisna min dabareeji yimɓe wonniiɓe , halluɓe . Ngam naa yimɓe fuu nuɗɗinta linjiila .
53003003	Ammaa Jawmiraawo koolniiɗo . Kaŋko o sembiɗinan on , o aynan on ngam taa Sayɗaanu heɓa do''ugo on .
53003004	Ngam daliila Jawmiraawo min ɗon kooli on boo , min anndi on ɗon kuuwa ko min umri on , koo yeeso boo on kuuwan ɗum .
53003005	Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu ɗowa ɓerɗe mon ngam haa on tokko yiide Allah e munyal maako .
53003006	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , min ɗon umra on bee innde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , on ndaayo deerɗiraaɓe laatiiɓe mbaateendam'en ɓe ɗowtanaaki umrooje ɗe min ndokki on .
53003007	On anndi booɗɗum no min njooɗori caka mooɗon . Tokke min , ngam min laataaki mbaateendam'en ,
53003008	min nyaamaay nyaamdu goɗɗo meere , sonaa to min njoɓi . Min torri , min comi , min kuuwi jemma bee naaŋge fuu , ngam taa min teddana koomoy mooɗon .
53003009	Fakat , min ke'anno ɗaɓɓugo nguure haa mooɗon . Ammaa min mbaɗi ko'e amin misaalu haa tiinaare , haa on tokko min .
53003010	Yaake min ɗonno ngondi bee mooɗon , min mbi'i on : To goɗɗo salake huuwugo , taa o nyaama boo .
53003011	Kanjum ngam min nani woɗɓe mooɗon laati mbaateendam'en . Ɓe kuuwataa sam , ammaa ɓe ɗon nasta haala ka yaalaay ɓe .
53003012	Irin maɓɓe , min ɗon pela ɓe , min ɗon umra ɓe bee innde Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu , sey ɓe nde'a , ɓe kuuwa ngam ɓe nyaamna ko'e maɓɓe .
53003013	Onon deerɗiraaɓe fuu , taa come huuwugo ko wooɗi .
53003014	To goɗɗo ɗowtanaaki umrooje amin nder bataakewol ngo'ol , maande mo , taa kawte bee maako , haa o semta .
53003015	Ammaa taa ndaare mo bana konneejo , sey pele mo bana deerɗiraawo .
53003016	Jawmiraawo , marɗo jam hokku on jam koondey bee koonoy . Jawmiraawo wondu bee mooɗon fuu .
53003017	Ndaa , koofŋgol mbindumi bee juŋŋgo am : Pol - ni bindol am , kanjum woni seedamku bataakeeji am fuu .
53003018	Mo''ere Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu wondu bee mooɗon fuu .
54001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu bee umroore Allah , Kisnoowo en , e Yeesu Almasiihu , daliila tammunde men .
54001002	Mi ɗon windana Timote , laatiiɗo ɓiɗɗo am gooŋgaajo ngam mi nastini mo nuɗɗinki :
54001003	Saa'i mi ɗonno yaha Makedoniya , mi tori ma a jooɗo haa Efesus . Yimɓe woɗɓe ton ɗon anndina haalaaji feere . Umru ɓe ɓe acca ɗum .
54001004	Sey ɓe acca suklanaago kiccaaji sirriiji e defte asli comnanɗe meere . Ngam haala maajum umminan gaabotiral tan , ka nafataa kebbinki nufayeere Allah nde annduɗen bee nuɗɗinki .
54001005	Nafuda umroore nde'e woni yiide iwnde haa ɓernde laaɓnde e numo ɓernde laaɓŋgo e nuɗɗinki ki walaa naafikaare .
54001006	Woɗɓe celi laawol booɗŋgol , ɗon tokko haala meere .
54001007	Ɓe ɗon ndaara ko'e maɓɓe bana ɓe jaŋginooɓe umrooje Allah , ammaa ɓe paamataa ko ɓe mbolwata , ɓe anndaa kuuje ɗe ɓe tabitinta bee sembe .
54001008	Enen kam en anndi tawreeta wooɗi , to goɗɗo ɗon huuwtinira ka bana no haandi ,
54001009	to o yejjitaay ɗu'um : Umrooje mbaɗaaka ngam huuwanɓe ko fotti , sey ngam halluɓe e luutooɓe . Ɗe laati ngam yawiiɓe Allah e marɓe hakke , ngam soɓɓe e faasiki'en , ngam mbarooɓe baaba malla daada , ngam mbarooɓe ko'e fuu ,
54001010	ngam jeenooɓe e luuɗu'enfa , ngam soorrooɓe maccuɓe , ngam fewooɓe e hunortooɓe fewre e huuwooɓe kooɗume ko luuti anndinol gooŋgawol .
54001011	Anndinol ngol iwi haa linjiila ka kalfinaami , kubaruwol baŋginanŋgol tedduŋgal Allah , marɗo barka fuu .
54001012	Mi ɗon yetta Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu mo hokki yam sembe huuwugo kuugal am . Mi ɗon yetta mo ngam o laari yam bana koolaaɗo , o nastini yam kuugal maako .
54001013	Ɓooyma kam , mi wolwuno kalluka dow maako , mi toonyino yimɓe maako , mi torruno ɓe bee caatal . Ammaa Allah enɗi yam , ngam mi walaano nuɗɗinki , mi anndaano ko kuuwmi .
54001014	Jawmiraawo men mo''ani yam ɗuuɗɗum masin , hokki yam nuɗɗinki e yiide iwnde haa kawtal men bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
54001015	Ndaa wolde hoolniinde nde wooɗi haa koomoy jaɓa nde bilaa seko : Yeesu Almasiihu wari nder duniyaaru ngam haa o hisna marɓe hakke . Min woni ɓurduɗo maɓɓe ,
54001016	ammaa ngam daliila maajum Allah enɗi yam , ngam haa Yeesu Almasiihu waŋgina munyal mum ɗuuɗŋgal bee am , min ɓurduɗo nder marɓe hakke mi laato aartuɗo nuɗɗinanɓe mo , heɓanɓe ngeendam nduumiiɗam .
54001017	Allah woni laamiiɗo duumiiɗo , o maayataa , o yi'ataake , kaŋko feere maako woni Allah . Maŋgu e tedduŋgal laatano mo haa abada abadin . Aamiina !
54001018	An Timote , ɓiŋgel am , mi halfini ma anndinol ngol . Siftor ko annabo'en mbolwi dow maaɗa naane . Bolle maɓɓe laato balmi ma nder haɓre woonde nde kaɓata .
54001019	Joga nuɗɗinki ma e numo ɓernde ma laaɓŋgo . Woɗɓe nananaay numooji ɓerɗe muuɗum'en , ngam maajum nuɗɗinki maɓɓe majji .
54001020	Himeneyus e Aleksandire ɗon nder maɓɓe . Mi hokki ɓe haa juŋŋgo Sayɗaanu haa ɓe ekkito ɓe acca wolwugo kalluka .
54002001	Ndaa ko aartanmi anndingo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe : Mbaɗe do'aaji e torndeeji e gettooje ngam yimɓe fuu .
54002002	Ndo'ane laamiiɓe e marɓe baawɗe kooɓeye , ngam haa en njooɗo bee jam e de'ere , bee kulol Allah e neɗɗaaku fuu .
54002003	Kanjum ɗum wooɗi , ɗum fottanan Allah , Kisnoowo en .
54002004	O yiɗi yimɓe fuu kisa , keɓa anndal gooŋga .
54002005	Ngam Allah o gooto , woodi neɗɗo hakkundeejo men bee Allah boo gooto , kaŋko woni Yeesu Almasiihu .
54002006	O hokki hoore maako ngam haa o rimɗina yimɓe fuu . Bana ni o gooŋɗiniri anniya Allah nder saa'iire nde Allah ta''ino ɗum .
54002007	Ngam maajum Allah waɗi yam mi nelaaɗo , mi jaŋginoowo ummaatooje , haa mi yeyna kubar maako bee nuɗɗinki e gooŋgaaku . Mi wi'i gooŋga , mi fewaay !
54002008	Yoo , mi yiɗi worɓe mbaɗa do'a kootoy nder mooɓtorde , ɓe mbeeɗa juuɗe maɓɓe hedi Allah , bee ɓernde laaɓnde , bilaa tikkere malla jokkirgol .
54002009	Rewɓe boo , mi yiɗi ɓe ɓorno limce pottanɗe ɓorneego , ɓe ne'iiɓe , semtooɓe . Taa ɓe pawno bee moorɗi caɗɗi malla kaŋgeeri malla luuluuje malla limce ɗuuɗa-samanje ,
54002010	ammaa bee kuuɗe booɗɗe , bana ko fottanta rewɓe wi'eteeɓe hulɓe Allah .
54002011	Sey rewɓe keɗito anndinol bee jeende e ɗowtaare .
54002012	Mi duŋgataako ɓe ngaaja malla ɓe laamano worɓe .
54002013	Ngam Aadamu aarti Hawwa tageego .
54002014	Aadamu tokkaaki esto , ammaa debbo tokki ngo , luuti umroore Allah .
54002015	Rewɓe kisan bee danyugo ɓikkoy , ammaa sey ɓe tabita nder nuɗɗinki e yiide e senaare , ɓe laato semtooɓe boo .
54003001	Ndaa wolde hoolniinde : To goɗɗo yiɗi o laato ardiiɗo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe , o ɗaɓɓi kuugal booɗŋgal .
54003002	Sey ardiiɗo laato goɗɗo mo walaa feloore , marɗo debbo gooto , naŋgtiiɗo , kakkilɗo , ne'iiɗo , beernoowo hoɗɓe , baawɗo ekkitingo .
54003003	Taa o laato guykoowo malla ?aggiiɗo , ammaa o munyɗo , naa o jokkiroowo malla cuunaaɗo ceede .
54003004	Sey o laamano saare maako booɗɗum , o elta ɓikkoy maako haa koy ɗowtano mo , koy teddina mo .
54003005	Ngam to goɗɗo waawaay laamanaago saare mum , noy o aynirta mooɓtorde yimɓe Allah ?
54003006	To goɗɗo keso nder nuɗɗinki , taa mbaɗe mo ardiiɗo . Ngam to o keso , teema o mawnititto . Nden kam Iblisa heɓan wullaago mo , Allah boo hiitoto mo .
54003007	Sey o mara innde woonde koo haa yimɓe ɓe nuɗɗinaay boo , ngam taa ɓe keɓa huɗugo mo dow aybeeji maako ɓooymaaji . To naa non , o yanan nder tuuforgol Iblisa .
54003008	Wallooɓe jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe , kamɓe boo ɓe laato wooɗa-gikku'en , taa ɓe laato naafiki'en malla yarooɓe inaboojam ɗuuɗɗam malla suunaaɓe riba kalluka .
54003009	Sey ɓe kakkilana gooŋga nuɗɗinki ka Allah waŋgini ɗum , ɓe njogo ka bee numo ɓernde laaɓŋgo .
54003010	Kamɓe boo , sey jama'aare aarta , linya ɓe . To ɓe ngalaa feloore , nden kam ɓe nasta kuugal .
54003011	Rewɓe maɓɓe boo laato wooɗa-gikku'en , taa ɓe laato waɗooɓe tufle , ammaa ɓe naŋgtiiɓe , hoolaaɓe nder kooɗume fuu .
54003012	Balloowo fuu laato marɗo debbo gooto , sey o laamano ɓikkoy maako e saare maako booɗɗum .
54003013	To ɓe kuuwi kuugal maɓɓe booɗɗum , ɓe keɓanan ko'e maɓɓe darnde woonde , non boo dartaare ɗuunde ngam ɓe ɗon nuɗɗini Yeesu Almasiihu .
54003014	Yoo , mi windani ma ɗum fuu . Mi ɗon tammi warugo haa maaɗa yeeso seɗɗa .
54003015	Ammaa to mi faasiti , bataakewol ngol anndinan ma no kuuwrata nder saare Allah , waato nder jama'aare yimɓe Allah geeto . Kayre woni daŋraŋgal gooŋga e caɓɓawal muuɗum .
54003016	Fakat , sirri diina men mawɗo :
54004001	Ruuhu Allah wi'i laaɓɗum , nder nyalɗe ragareeje yimɓe woɗɓe accan nuɗɗinki , ɗowtanto ruuhuuji pewooji e anndinol ginnaaji .
54004002	Ɓe tokkoto esto naafiki'en e fewooɓe . Ɓerɗe fewooɓe ɓe'e mbaati , bana njamndi ngulndi jaw tufi ɗe .
54004003	Ɓe ɗon kaɗa te'ugo e nyaamugo kuuje feere feere . Ammaa Allah tagi kuuje ɗe , ngam haa nuɗɗinɓe Almasiihu , annduɓe gooŋga nyaama ɗe bee yettugo Allah .
54004004	Ko Allah tagi fuu ɗum booɗɗum , walaa karamɗum , to en njaɓi ɗum bee yettoore .
54004005	Ngam wolde Allah e do'a ɗon cena ɗum .
54004006	To a anndini deerɗiraaɓe kuuje ɗe'e , nden kam a kuuwanoowo Almasiihu booɗɗo , nyaamnoowo yoŋki mum bee kubar nuɗɗinki e anndinol booɗŋgol ngol tokkiɗa bee tiinaare .
54004007	Ammaa kiccaaji meereeji bana ɗi rewɓe nayeeɓe , sey a salo ɗi . Eltu hoore ma haa kulol Allah .
54004008	Ɗowtingo ɓandu ɗon nafa seɗɗa , ammaa kulol Allah ɗon nafa kooɗume fuu , ngam ngol waddanan en ngeendam jonta e nder wakkatiiji garanɗi .
54004009	Kanjum woni wolde hoolniinde nde haani koomoy jaɓa nde bilaa seko .
54004010	Ngam maajum en ɗon kuuwa , en ɗon kaɓda , ngam en ɗon tammi heɓugo kisndam haa Allah geeto . Kaŋko woni Kisnoowo yimɓe fuu , sakkoma nuɗɗinɓe Almasiihu .
54004011	Umru nuɗɗinɓe kuuje ɗe , anndin ɓe ɗe .
54004012	Taa goɗɗo yawo ma ngam a ndottidaay tawon . Laatana nuɗɗinɓe fuu misaalu haa bolle e kuuɗe e yiide e nuɗɗinki e laaɓeeŋga .
54004013	Suklana jaŋgango ɓe defte ceniiɗe , waaju ɓe , ekkitin ɓe , haa to mi wari .
54004014	Taa yeeba dokkal Ruuhu Allah ngal keɓɗa nde annabo'en mooɓtorde ewni ma haa kuugal , ndotti'en boo mballini juuɗe muuɗum'en dow hoore maaɗa .
54004015	Suklana kuuɗe ɗe bee tiinaare , ngam haa koomoy fuu yi'a no ɓesdortooɗa yeeso yeeso .
54004016	Hakkilan hoore ma , hakkilan anndinol ma boo . To a tokkake huuwugo ɗum , a hisnan hoore ma e nananɓe ma fuu .
54005001	Taa telɓan goɗɗo ndottiijo . To woodi daliila felugo mo , wolwan mo bana o baaba ma . Suka'en , sey a fela ɓe bana deerɗa'en ,
54005002	rewɓe nayeeɓe bana daadiraaɓe , rewɓe woɗɓe boo bana deerɗa'en rewɓe , bee ɓernde laaɓnde .
54005003	Teddin rewɓe yurumɓe , wallu ɓe to ɓe keɓataa walliinde haa yimɓe saare maɓɓe .
54005004	Ammaa to debbo jurumɗo woodi ɓiɓɓe e taaniraaɓe , sey kamɓe ɓe ekkito huuwugo kuuɗe diina haa yimɓe saare maɓɓe , ɓe mbarjo daada maɓɓe malla maama maɓɓe , ngam kanjum ɗum fottanan Allah .
54005005	Debbo jurumɗo mo walaa cuklaniiɗo ɗum , ɗon tammi heɓugo hayru haa Allah , ɗon toro mo ballal jemma bee naaŋge fuu .
54005006	Ammaa debbo jurumɗo ɗaɓɓanɗo welwelo , laati bana maayɗo , koo o ɗon bee yoŋki tawon .
54005007	Yeccu ɗum rewɓe yurumɓe fuu , ngam taa goɗɗo heɓa felugo ɓe .
54005008	Ammaa to goɗɗo suklanaaki bandum'en , sakkoma wonduɓe bee muuɗum nder saare , nden kam o yeddi nuɗɗinki , o tulli mo nuɗɗinaay .
54005009	Taa windu innde debbo jurumɗo haa ɗereewol rewɓe yurumɓe , sonaa to duuɓi maako njottake cappanɗe joweego , o te'anooɗo nde woore tan .
54005010	Sey o laato anndaaɗo ngam kuuɗe maako booɗɗe , waato o mawnini ɓiiyiiko'en booɗɗum , o weerni hoɗɓe , o looti kosɗe Masiihiŋko'en , o walli ɓilliiɓe , o huuwi kuuɗe booɗɗe kooɗeye .
54005011	Ammaa sala windugo inɗe rewɓe yurumɓe luttuɓe . Ngam to suuno waɗi ɓe , ɓe accan Almasiihu , ɓe ɗaɓɓan te'eego .
54005012	Bana non ɓe laatorto aybuɓe , ngam ɓe pistan anniya ka ɓe mbaɗno bee nuɗɗinki .
54005013	Dow maajum fuu ɓe mboowran bee sooynde kuugal , ɓe ngiiloto diga suudu haa suudu nder wuro fuu . Ko tulli ɗum boo , ɓe mbaɗan tufle , ɓe nastan haala ka yaalaay ɓe , ɓe mbolwan ko fottaay .
54005014	Ngam maajum ngiɗmi rewɓe ɓe'e te'e fahin , ɓe ndanya ɓikkoy , ɓe cuklano ci'e maɓɓe , ngam taa konne'en men keɓa hallingo en .
54005015	Fakat , rewɓe yurumɓe woɗɓe celi laawol gooŋga , ɓe ɗon tokko Sayɗaanu .
54005016	To debbo nuɗɗinɗo woodi rewɓe yurumɓe haa saare mum , sey o walla ɓe ngam taa ɓe teddana jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe . Jama'aare kam walaa rewɓe yurumɓe ɓe ngalaa suklaniiɓe ɗum .
54005017	Ndotti'en ardiiɓe , huuwooɓe kuugal man booɗɗum , ke'i heɓugo ngeenaari cowi ɗiɗi , sakkoma tiiniiɓe bee waaju e anndinki .
54005018	Ngam deftere wi'i : " Taa waɗan ngaari corɓoori sabakaare . " Non boo : " Kuuwoowo he'i heɓugo ngeenaari mum . "
54005019	Taa jaɓ wullaandu dow dawroowo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe , sonaa to seedooɓe ɗiɗo malla tato tabitini ndu .
54005020	Waɗɓe aybe fuu , sey a fela ɓe yeeso jama'aare , ngam haa luttuɓe kula .
54005021	Mi ɗon toro ma yeeso Allah e Yeesu Almasiihu e malaa'ika'en suɓaaɓe , a ɗowtano wasuyeeji ɗi'i , taa a sendindira yimɓe , taa a ɓurna koomoy nder kuuɗe ma fuu .
54005022	Taa yaaw wallingo juuɗe ma dow hoore goɗɗo haa a halfina mo kuugal nder jama'aare . Taa hawtu bee hakkeeji yimɓe woɗɓe , aynu hoore ma a laaɓɗo .
54005023	Taa yar ndiyam tan , ndikka a yara inaboojam seɗɗa haa a hoynana reedu ma , ngam nyawji ma tokkindirɗi boo .
54005024	Hakkeeji yimɓe woɗɓe mbaŋgi hiddeko kiita waɗa , haa woɗɓe ɗi mbaŋgan ɓaawoɗon .
54005025	Bana non boo kuuɗe booɗɗe mbaŋgirta . Koo to ɗe ɗon cuuɗi jonta , ɗe mbaŋgan fakat .
54006001	Koomoy laati jeyaaɗo goɗɗo mo nuɗɗinaay , laara jawmum bana ke'iiɗo teddinki fuu , ngam taa goɗɗo hallina innde Allah e anndinol men .
54006002	Koomoy laati jeyaaɗo goɗɗo Masiihiŋkeejo , taa yawo mo ngam o deerɗiraawo . Sey o huuwana mo bee tiinaare ɓurnde , ngam jawmiiko boo nuɗɗinɗo , giɗaaɗo , tiinotooɗo woonugo .
54006003	To goɗɗo waddi anndinol feere , to o tokkaaki bolle gooŋgaaje ɗe Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu e anndinol diina men ,
54006004	nden kam o mawnitiiɗo meere mo anndaa kooɗume . O ginnaaɗo , cuunaaɗo gaabotiral e jokkirgol dow bolle . Ndaa ko iwata haa maajum : Kaajal e jokkirgol e bolle mettuɗe e gikke kalluɗe
54006005	e haɓre nde walaa keerol . Hakkiilo yimɓe ɓe'e majji , gooŋga boo majjiri ɓe . Ɓe tammi diina ɗum laawol riskugo .
54006006	Fakat , diina ɗum riba makka , to goɗɗo naŋgti suuno mum .
54006007	En nasti duniyaaru en tembuɓe , en ngurtoto ndu boo en tembuɓe .
54006008	Ngam maajum , to en ngoodi nyaamdu e limce , ɗum he'an en .
54006009	Ammaa ɗaɓɓanɓe riskugo , estooji ngaranan ɓe . Ɓe nastan tuuforgol suunooji paataaɗi , kalluɗi , do''anɗi yimɓe nder majjere e halkere .
54006010	Ngam suuno ceede woni ɗaɗol halleende fuu . Woɗɓe cuunaama ɗe masin , haa ɓe celi laawol nuɗɗinki , ɓe ngaddani ko'e maɓɓe torraaji naawɗi .
54006011	Ammaa an , goɗɗo Allah , doggu kuuje ɗe'e . Ɗaɓɓu gooŋgaaku e kulol Allah e nuɗɗinki e yiide e munyal e de'ere ɓernde .
54006012	Sey a haɓa haɓre nuɗɗinki woonde haa keɓa ngeendam nduumiiɗam . Allah ewni ma haa ngeendam man saa'i mbaɗɗa seedamku nuɗɗinki ma mbooɗŋgu yeeso seedooɓe ɗuuɗɓe .
54006013	Yeeso Allah , geeɗinoowo kuuje fuu , e Yeesu Almasiihu , baɗɗo seedamku mbooɗŋgu yeeso Pontiyu Pilaatu , umran ma mi :
54006014	Huuw wakiilaaku ma bee laaɓɗum , bilaa feloore , haa nyalaade Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu waŋgata .
54006015	Baŋguki maajum laatoto nder saa'iire fottannde bee muuyo Allah , marɗo barka fuu , Baawɗo feere muuɗum , laamiiɗo laamlaamɓe , Jawmiraawo jawmiraaɓe .
54006016	Kaŋko feere maako woni duumiiɗo , o ɗon jooɗi nder annoora ka ɓadataake , walaa neɗɗo meeɗi yi'ugo mo , waawataa yi'ugo mo boo . Tedduŋgal e baawɗe duumiiɗe laatano mo . Aamiina !
54006017	Umru riskuɓe bee kuuje duniyaaru ndu , taa ɓe mawnito . Taa ɓe koolo risku ngu tabitittaa , ammaa ɓe koolo Allah , dokkanɗo en kooɗume fuu bee caahaaki haa en ceyoro ɗum .
54006018	Yeccu ɓe ɓe kuuwa mbooɗeeŋga , kuuɗe booɗɗe laato riski maɓɓe , ɓe laato saahiiɓe , ɓe mballa woɗɓe bee jawdi maɓɓe .
54006019	Bana ni ɓe cigoranto ko'e maɓɓe ndesaari mboondi , tabindi ngam nyalɗe garanɗe , haa ɓe keɓa ngeendam gooŋga fakat .
54006020	An Timote , hakkilan anndinol ngol kalfinaɗa . Daaya haalaaji meereeji e gaabi paataaɗi , ɗum ko woɗɓe mbi'ata anndal lugguŋgal .
54006021	Ɓe ɗon mana ngal yeeso yimɓe , ammaa ɓe celi laawol nuɗɗinki .
55001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu bee muuyo Allah , ngam anndinki ngeendam ngonɗam nder kawtal bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
55001002	Mi ɗon windana Timote , ɓiɗɗo am giɗaaɗo :
55001003	Mi ɗon yetta Allah mo kuuwananmi bee numo ɓernde laaɓŋgo , bana kaakaaji am fuu . Mi ɗon siftore nder do'aaji am jemma bee naaŋge fuu , mi ɗon yetta mo foroy .
55001004	Mi ɗon siftora gonɗi ma , mi ɗon yenwa yi'ugo ma , ngam haa ɓernde am heewa seyo .
55001005	Mi ɗon siftora nuɗɗinki ma ki walaa naafikaare . Nuɗɗinki man , maama ma debbo , bi'eteeɗo Lo'is e daadafa ma Ewnike aarti ma marugo ki . Mi anndi fakat ki ɗon jooɗi nder maaɗa boo .
55001006	Ngam maajum mi ɗon siftinore : Hakkilan dokkal Allah ngal keɓɗa nde mballinmi juuɗe am dow hoore maaɗa .
55001007	Allah hokki en Ruuhu mum , ngu hebbintaa en bee kulol , ammaa bee sembe e yiide e naŋgtaare .
55001008	Taa semtu seedanaago Jawmiraawo men malla seedanaago yam , min kaɓɓaaɗo ngam daliila maako . Ammaa munyan geɗal ma haa torraaji ngam linjiila , deydey baawɗe ɗe Allah hokkete .
55001009	Kaŋko o hisni en , o ewni en haa en laato yimɓe maako , naa ngam kuuɗe men booɗɗe , ammaa ngam muuyo maako e mo''ere maako . O mo''ani en bee Yeesu Almasiihu diga jamanuuji ciwa sam .
55001010	Ammaa jonta ɗum waŋgi bee garki Yeesu Almasiihu , Kisnoowo en . Kaŋko o timmini baawɗe waade , o waŋgini ngeendam e duumaare . Kanjum , linjiila ɗon anndina en ɗum .
55001011	Allah waɗi yam mi nelaaɗo , mi jaŋginoowo haa mi yeyna ka .
55001012	Ngam maajum mi ɗon yara boneeji ɗi boo . Ammaa ɗi kulnataa yam , ngam mi anndi mo nuɗɗinmi . Mi ɗon hooli mo o baawɗo aynugo ko o halfini yam , haa to nyalaade kiita wari .
55001013	Joga bolle ɗe nanɗa haa am , tokka ɗe bana misaalu haa anndinol , a tabita nder nuɗɗinki e yiide , ko laatani en nder kawtal men bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
55001014	Anndinol booɗŋgol ngol kalfinaɗa , joga ngol bee ballal Ruuhu Ceniiɗo njooɗiiŋgu nder meeɗen .
55001015	A anndi , wonɓe nder lesdi Asiya fuu acci yam , koo Figelus e Hermogenes boo .
55001016	Jawmiraawo hinno saare Onesiforus , ngam kaŋko o seyni yam nde ɗuuɗɗum . O semtiraay yam , koo mi kaɓɓaaɗo nder fursina .
55001017	Nde o yotti Roma , o fuɗɗi tefugo yam bee tiinaare ɗuunde , haa o heɓti yam .
55001018	Jawmiraawo walla mo , hokka mo hinnuye Allah nder nyalaade kiita . Haa Efesus o huuwani yam kuuɗe ɗuuɗɗe , an a anndi ɗum booɗɗum .
55002001	An ɓiŋgel am , sey a sembiɗa bee mo''ere nde keɓɗen nder kawtal men bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
55002002	A nani ko ngaajinmi yeeso seedooɓe ɗuuɗɓe . Halfin ɗum yimɓe hoolaaɓe , waawɓe anndingo woɗɓe .
55002003	Munyan geɗal ma haa torraaji bana soojeejo Yeesu Almasiihu gooŋgaajo .
55002004	Walaa soojeejo suklanto haala nguure mum , ngam o yiɗi mawɗo maako yerdo mo .
55002005	Non boo baɗoowo gala haa pijirle . To o ɗowtanaaki umrooje gala , o heɓataa keɓal jaalorgal .
55002006	Demoowo boo ɗon torro ɗuuɗɗum . Ngam maajum haandi o aarta yimɓe nyaamugo ɓiɓɓe ngesa maako .
55002007	Numtu ko saawi nder bolle am , Jawmiraawo faamtinan ma kooɗume fuu .
55002008	Siftor Yeesu Almasiihu , ummitiiɗo diga maayde , Kisnoowo mo asŋgol Daawuda , fodde linjiila ka ngaajinanmi .
55002009	Ngam linjiila maajum mi ɗon yara bone , mi kaɓɓaaɗo bee callallu boo bana baɗɗo kalluɗum . Ammaa wolde Allah haɓɓaaka .
55002010	Mi ɗon munyana ɗum fuu ngam daliila suɓaaɓe Allah , ngam haa kamɓe boo ɓe keɓa kisndam e tedduŋgal duumiiŋgal haa Yeesu Almasiihu .
55002011	Ndaa wolde hoolniinde :
55002012	To en ɗon munyana bone , en laamoto bee maako boo .
55002013	To en laataaki hoolaaɓe , kaŋko o tabitan o koolniiɗo ,
55002014	Siftinor ɗum nuɗɗinɓe , reentin ɓe yeeso Allah , ngam taa ɓe njokkira dow bolle . Jokkirli man nafataa kooɗume , ammaa ɗi mbonnan nanooɓe .
55002015	Tiina haa a waŋga yeeso Allah a koolaaɗo , a kuuwoowo mo semtintaake dow kuugal mum , a anndinoowo kubar gooŋga bana no fotti .
55002016	Seedu bee haalaaji meereeji cemtiniiɗi , ngam waɗooɓe ɗi ɗon ɓesdo daayaago Allah .
55002017	Anndinol maɓɓe nandi bee huuduure layannde . Himeneyus e Filetus ɗon nder maɓɓe .
55002018	Kamɓe ɓe acci gooŋga , ɓe ɗon mbonna nuɗɗinki woɗɓe bee wi'ugo ummitineeki men waɗi , timmi .
55002019	Ammaa Allah wallini caɓɓawal , ngal ɗon tabiti . Ndaa ko winda dow maagal : " Jawmiraawo anndi yimɓe muuɗum . " Non boo : " Koomoy ceediiɗo innde Jawmiraawo , sey acca huuwugo kalluɗum . "
55002020	Woodi taasaaje e payanɗe feere-feereeje nder saare mawnde . Goɗɗe ɗe cardi malla kaŋgeeri , goɗɗe boo ɗe leɗɗe malla loope . Ɗe'e laati ngam kuuje marɗe saman , ɗeya ngam kuuje meereeje malla gudinteeɗe .
55002021	To goɗɗo laɓɓini hoore mum e kuuje kalluɗe ɗe mbi'mi , nden kam jawmu saare huuwtiniran mo ngam kuuje marɗe saman , ngam o cenaaɗo , nafoowo jawmum ngam kuuɗe booɗɗe fuu .
55002022	An , reenta e suunooji sukaaku , ɗaɓɓu gooŋgaaku e nuɗɗinki e yiide e jam , an e seedotooɓe Jawmiraawo bee ɓerɗe laaɓɗe .
55002023	Ammaa sala ?amɗe iwɗe haa faataare e humakaare , ɗe umminan jokkirli tan .
55002024	Kuuwanoowo Jawmiraawo , taa jokkira , ammaa o laato ɗelemɗo haa koomoy fuu , o ekkitinoowo booɗɗo , munyɗo .
55002025	Sey o elta luutooɓe bee mbooɗeeŋga . Teema Allah wallan ɓe ɓe tuuba haa ɓe paama gooŋga .
55002026	Nden kam ɓe keɓtan hakkiilo maɓɓe , ɓe ndaɗa tuuforgol Iblisa . Ngam kaŋko o naŋgi ɓe , o waɗi ɓe tokkiiɓe muuyo maako .
55003001	Anndu , nder nyalɗe ragareeje kam , wakkatiiji caɗɗi laatoto .
55003002	Fakat , yimɓe laatoto yiɗɓe ko'e muuɗum'en , suunaaɓe ceede , jurotooɓe meere , mawnitittooɓe . Ɓe kuɗan woɗɓe , ɓe ɗowtantaako saarooji maɓɓe . Ɓe ngettataa koomoy , ɓe teddintaa ceniiɗum sam ,
55003003	ɓe ngalaa yiide , ɓe ngalaa enɗam , ɓe waɗooɓe tufle , ɓe ngalaa naŋgtaare , ɓe saatuɓe , ɓe nganyan mbooɗeeŋga .
55003004	Ɓe jambotooɓe , ɓe numataa kuuɗe maɓɓe , ammaa ɓe keewan mawnitaare . Ɓe ɓuran yiɗugo welwelo dow Allah .
55003005	Gite yimɓe kam ɓe tokkoto diina men , ammaa ɓe ngeddan baawɗe maaka . Daaya irin maɓɓe !
55003006	Woɗɓe maɓɓe ɗon nasta cuuɗi yimɓe boo , haa ɓe laatina rewɓe humaki'en tokkiiɓe ɓe . Rewɓe ɓe'e ɓe siftoranɓe hakkeeji maɓɓe ɗuuɗɗi , ɓe dasaaɓe suunooji kooɗiye .
55003007	Rewɓe ɓe'e ɗon ekkito tum , ammaa ɓe njottataako anndal gooŋga .
55003008	Bana no Yannes e Yamberes ndartani Muusa , bana non yimɓe ɓe'e ndartanto gooŋga . Hakkiilooji maɓɓe mbonni , nder nuɗɗinki boo ɓe meere'en .
55003009	Ammaa ɓe keɓataa yahugo yeeso yeeso , ngam faataare maɓɓe waŋganan koomoy , bana faataare Yannes e Yamberes boo .
55003010	Ammaa an a tokki anndinol am e gikku am e anniyaaji am , non boo nuɗɗinki am e munyal am e yiide am , e dartaare am
55003011	e boneeji am e torraaji am . A anndi ko heɓi yam haa Antakiya e Ikoniya e Listira , boneeji caatuɗi ɗi njarmi . Ammaa nder maaji fuu Jawmiraawo hisni yam .
55003012	Koomoy hawti bee Yeesu Almasiihu , yiɗi jooɗaago bee kulol Allah , fakat o toonyeteeɗo .
55003013	Ammaa halluɓe e rikisi'en tullitan yeeso yeeso , ɓe estan woɗɓe , ɓe esteteeɓe bee ko'e maɓɓe boo .
55003014	Ammaa an kam , sey a tabita nder gooŋgaaji ɗi ekkitiɗa , ɗi nuɗɗinɗa bee sembe . A anndi ekkitinɓe ma ,
55003015	a anndi defte ceniiɗe boo diga a derkeno . Kanje ɗe mbaawan faamtingo ma laawol kisndam ɗam keɓeten to en nuɗɗini Yeesu Almasiihu .
55003016	Ko winda nder defte man fuu , ɗum laati bee wahayu Allah . Ɗum wallan anndingo gooŋga , e waŋgingo boofi , e wo''itingo aybeeji , e ekkitingo ko fottani Allah ,
55003017	ngam haa koomoy tokki Allah laato timmuɗo , taaskaniiɗo kuuɗe booɗɗe kooɗeye .
55004001	Mi ɗon toro ma yeeso Allah e Yeesu Almasiihu mo hiitoto maayɓe e yeeɗɓe fuu . O waran fakat , ngam haa o darna laamu maako . Ngam maajum umran ma mi :
55004002	Anndin yimɓe kubar Allah bee dartaare , koo ɗum fottanan ɓe , koo ɗum fottantaa ɓe . Waŋgin aybeeji maɓɓe , fel ɓe , tiɗɗin ɓe , faamtin ɓe bee munyal fuu .
55004003	Ngam nder nyalɗe garanɗe ɓe caloto nanugo anndinol laaɓŋgol . Ammaa ɓe cuɓanan ko'e maɓɓe jaŋginooɓe deydey suunooji maɓɓe , haa ɓe nana ko welata noppi maɓɓe .
55004004	Ɓe accan nanugo gooŋga , ɓe ngaylititto haa ɓe kakkilana kiccaaji sirriiji .
55004005	Ammaa an kam , laata a de'a-hakkiiloojo nder kooɗume fuu . Munyan torraaji ma . Huuw kuugal gaajoowo linjiila , timmitin wakiilaaku ma .
55004006	Min kam , ?i?am am ɓadi laataago dokkal dufeteeŋgal , saa'i waɗi mi eggita .
55004007	Mi haɓi haɓre woonde , mi timmitini daɗadaɗa , mi jogiti nuɗɗinki .
55004008	Jonta keɓal daɗki ɗon reenammi : Jawmiraawo , kiitoowo gooŋgaajo seedoto gooŋgaaku am nder nyalaade kiita maako , naa gooŋgaaku am tan , ammaa ngu yenwanɓe baŋguki maako fuu .
55004009	Yaawɗa warugo haa am , taa neeɓ .
55004010	Demas acci yam , ngam o yiɗi jamanuuru jontaaru , o dilli Tessaloniiki . Kereskes yehi Galaatiya , Titus boo yehi Dalmaatiya .
55004011	Luka feere mum ɗon wondi bee am . Hoo'u Markus , wardu bee maako , ngam kaŋko o nafatam masin nder kuugal Jawmiraawo .
55004012	Mi neli Tikikus haa Efesus .
55004013	To a ɗon wara , waddanam mojaare am nde accumi haa juŋŋgo Karpus haa Torowas , waddu boo defte ɗe accumi ton , sakkoma defte kuuwraaɗe bee lare .
55004014	Aleksandire kilaajo waɗi yam halleende ɗuunde . Jawmiraawo hiitoto mo deydey kuuɗe maako .
55004015	Reenta e maako , an boo , ngam o dartani bolle amin bee caatal .
55004016	Nyande arande nde ndariimi yeeso kiita ngam haa mi jaabano hoore am , walaa mo walli yam . Ɓe fuu ɓe acci yam . Taa Jawmiraawo limana ɓe ɗum aybe !
55004017	Ammaa Jawmiraawo wondi bee am , sembiɗini yam , ngam haa mi timmitina kuugal waaju am , yimɓe iwɓe haa lesɗe fuu nana ngu . Kaŋko o hisni yam hunduko mbarooga .
55004018	Fakat , Jawmiraawo hisnatam halleende fuu , yottintam jam nder laamu maako ngu asama . Tedduŋgal laatano mo haa abada abadin . Aamiina !
55004019	Hoofnu Piriskilla e Akilas , hoofnu saare Onesiforus boo .
55004020	Erastus ɗon haa Korintu . Torofimus , mi acci mo haa Miletus , ngam o nyawɗo .
55004021	Yaawɗa warugo hiddeko dabbunde waɗa .
55004022	Jawmiraawo wondu bee maaɗa , mo''ere Allah wondu bee mooɗon fuu .
56001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , maccuɗo Allah , nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu . Mi kalfinaaɗo nastingo suɓaaɓe Allah nuɗɗinki e anndal gooŋga bana diina men anndinirta ka .
56001002	Diina men ɗon dari dow tammunde heɓugo ngeendam nduumiiɗam . Diga jamanuuji ɓooymaaji Allah mo fewataa wi'no hokkan en ngeendam maajum .
56001003	Nder saa'iire ta''aande boo o waŋgini wolde maako bee waaju kubar maako . Allah , Kisnoowo en halfini yam waaju ngu bee umroore .
56001004	Mi ɗon windana Titus , ɓiɗɗo am giɗaaɗo nder nuɗɗinki men gooti :
56001005	Mi acci ma haa Kereta , ngam haa a mo''ina ko lutti huuwugo . Sey a darna dawrooɓe jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe nder gure fuu . Siftor ko mi wi'i ma :
56001006	Dawroowo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe laato mo walaa feloore , marɗo debbo gooto , ɓiɓɓe maako boo ɓe nuɗɗinɓe , taa goɗɗo heɓa felugo ɓe ngam ɓe ngalaa neɗɗaaku , ɓe luutooɓe .
