56001007	Sey ardiiɗo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe laato mo walaa feloore , ngam o wakiiliijo Allah . Taa o laato mawnitiiɗo malla tikkoowo malla guykoowo malla ?aggiiɗo malla cuunaaɗo ceede ,
56001008	ammaa o beernoowo hoɗɓe , giɗɗo mbooɗeeŋga , kakkilɗo , gooŋgaajo , laaɓa-ɓerndeejo , naŋgtiiɗo .
56001009	Sey o hakkilana kubaruwol koolniiŋgol deydey anndinol ngol o jaɓi . Bana ni o laatorto baawɗo tiɗɗingo jama'aare bee anndinol laaɓŋgol , o fela waabotooɓe boo .
56001010	Ngam woodi yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe , ɓurna maɓɓe nder Yahuudu'en nuɗɗinɓe , ɓe tuurtooɓe , estooɓe woɗɓe bee haala meere .
56001011	Walaa ko mo''inta ɓe , sey sukkugo kunduɗe maɓɓe , ngam ɓe ɗon mbonna kawtal yimɓe nder ci'efa bee ekkitingo ko haanaay . Ɓe ɗon mbaɗa ɗum ngam haa ɓe keɓa riba kalluka .
56001012	Goɗɗo lesdi maɓɓe wolwi bana annaboojo , o wi'i : " Kereta'en ɗon pewa foroy . Ɓe dabbaaji kalluɗi , mbaateendam'en , suklantooɓe deeɗi muuɗum'en tan . "
56001013	O wi'i gooŋga dey ! Ngam maajum fel ɓe bee caatal , haa hakkiilooji maɓɓe njamɗita bee nuɗɗinki .
56001014	Sey ɓe acca suklanaago kiccaaji Yahuudu'en sirriiji , taa ɓe tokko farillaaji yimɓe tuurtanɓe gooŋga .
56001015	Haa laaɓa-ɓerɗe'en , kooɗume fuu laaɓi . Ammaa haa soɓɓe e sooyɓe nuɗɗinki , walaa ko laaɓi , ngam hakkiilooji maɓɓe e numooji ɓerɗe maɓɓe coɓi .
56001016	Ɓe ɗon mbi'a ɓe anndi Allah , ammaa kuuɗe maɓɓe ɗon luuta ɗum . Ɓe nyidduɓe , tuurtooɓe , ɓe mbaawaay huuwugo kuugal booɗŋgal kooŋgale .
56002001	Ammaa an , ko mbolwata fuu , sey ɗum tokko anndinol gooŋgawol .
56002002	Yeccu worɓe nayeeɓe ɓe laato de'a-hakkiilo'en , ne'iiɓe , naŋgtiiɓe , waŋginɓe nuɗɗinki e yiide e munyal .
56002003	Bana non boo rewɓe nayeeɓe laato senaaɓe nder kuuɗe muuɗum'en , taa ɓe laato waɗooɓe tufle malla horɓe nguykinoojam , ammaa ɓe anndinooɓe ko wooɗi .
56002004	Sey ɓe ekkitina derke'en rewɓe yiɗugo worɓe muuɗum'en e ɓikkoy muuɗum'en ,
56002005	haa ɓe laato hakkilɓe , naŋgtiiɓe , daada'en ci'efa wooɗɓe , ɗowtantooɓe worɓe muuɗum'en , ngam taa goɗɗo hallina kubar Allah .
56002006	Tiɗɗin suka'en boo haa ɓe laato hakkilɓe .
56002007	An bee hoore ma laatana ɓe misaalu haa kuuɗe booɗɗe nder kooɗume fuu . Anndinol ma fuu daro dow gooŋga e de'ere hakkiilo .
56002008	Bolle ma laato laaɓɗe , ɗe ngeddataake . Bana ni cemtinirta konne'en men , ngam ɓe keɓataa wolwugo kalluɗum kooɗume dow meeɗen .
56002009	Jeyaaɓe boo , sey ɓe ɗowtano jawmiraaɓe maɓɓe , ɓe ngerdina ɓe bee kooɗume fuu . Taa ɓe laato waabooɓe ,
56002010	taa ɓe ngujja jawmiraaɓe maɓɓe kooɗume , ammaa ɓe hoolaaɓe timmuɓe foroy . Kuuɗe maɓɓe fuu mawnina saman anndinol ngol Allah , Kisnoowo en hokki en .
56002011	Ngam Allah waŋgini mo''ere mum , haa yimɓe fuu kisa .
56002012	Mo''ere maajum ɗon tiɗɗina en accugo halleende e suunooji duniyaaru fuu , haa en njooɗo bee hakkiilo e gooŋgaaku e kulol Allah nder duniyaaru ndu .
56002013	En ɗon tammi heɓugo hayru nduumiiŋgu , ngam en ɗon ndeena nyalaade nde tedduŋgal Allah men mawɗo e ngal Yeesu Almasiihu , Kisnoowo en waŋgata .
56002014	Kaŋko o hokki yoŋki maako ngam meeɗen . Bana ni o rimɗini en e halleende fuu , o laɓɓini en haa en laato yimɓe maako , maral maako , tiinotooɓe huuwugo kuuɗe booɗɗe .
56002015	Kanjum , anndin ɗum nanooɓe ma , tiɗɗin ɓe , fel ɓe bee baawɗe ma fuu . Taa accu koo gooto maɓɓe yawna baawɗe ma .
56003001	Siftinor nuɗɗinɓe ɓe leestana laamiiɓe e marɓe baawɗe , ɓe ɗowtano ɓe , ɓe taaskano kuugal booɗŋgal kooŋgale .
56003002	Taa ɓe mbolwa kalluka dow koomoy , taa ɓe njokkira boo , ammaa ɓe laato munyɓe , ɓe kolla yimɓe fuu mbooɗeeŋga .
56003003	Ngam ɓooyma enen boo en ngalaano faamu , en laatino luutɓe , majjuɓe . En laatino maccuɓe suunooji e giɗaaɗi kooɗiye . En ɗonno njooɗi bee nganyaandi e kaajindirki , woɗɓe nganyi en , enen boo en nganyi ɓe .
56003004	Ammaa Allah , Kisnoowo en waŋginani en mbooɗeeŋga mum e yiide mum .
56003005	O hisni en , naa ngam en kuuwi ko fottani mo , ammaa ngam o enɗi en . Nde keɓɗen ngiiwam baptisma , Ruuhu Ceniiɗo danyi en fahin , laatini en yimɓe hesɓe .
56003006	Ruuhu maajum , Allah waanji ngu ɗuuɗɗum dow meeɗen bee Yeesu Almasiihu , Kisnoowo en .
56003007	Ngam daliila mo''ere Almasiihu keɓɗen yerduye Allah , en keɓan ngeendam nduumiiɗam boo ɗam ndeeneten .
56003008	Kanjum woni wolde hoolniinde .
56003009	Ammaa daaya ?amɗe iwɗe haa faataare , daaya haala defte asli e jokkirli e gaabotiral dow tawreeta . Ɗum fuu ɗum nafataa , ɗum meereejum meere .
56003010	Goɗɗo biɗu'aakuujo , fel mo nde woore , nde ɗiɗi boo . To o nanaay ma , accu mo .
56003011	A anndi irin maako wonnake fuu , ɗon waɗa hakke . Bana ni o hiitorto hoore maako .
56003012	To mi neli Artemas malla Tikikus haa maaɗa , yaawɗa warugo haa am haa Nikopolis , ngam mi waɗi anniya dabbugo ton .
56003013	Wallu Jenas , alkaaliijo , e Apollos , tiina humtango ɓe haaje maɓɓe fuu ngam jahaaŋgal maɓɓe .
56003014	Yimɓe meeɗen , kamɓe boo sey ɓe ekkito huuwugo kuuɗe booɗɗe , ɓe mballa woɗɓe to haaje wallugo waɗi . To naa non , nuɗɗinki maɓɓe nafataa .
56003015	Wonduɓe bee am fuu koofni ma . Hoofnu soobiraaɓe amin nuɗɗinɓe ton .
57001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Pol , kaɓɓaaɗo ngam daliila Yeesu Almasiihu , min e Timote , yahugo haa Filemon , soobaajo amin , kuuwdoowo bee amin .
57001002	Min neldi ngol boo haa Afiya , deerɗiraawo meeɗen debbo , e Arkippus , kuuwdiɗɗiraawo men , e nuɗɗinɓe mooɓtotooɓe nder saare ma .
57001003	Allah Baabiraawo men e Yeesu Almasiihu Jawmiraawo men ndokka on mo''ere e jam .
57001004	Deerɗam Filemon , koondey mi toroto Allah , mi ɗon siftore , mi ɗon yetta mo ,
57001005	ngam mi nani no a yiɗiri yimɓe Allah fuu , no a nuɗɗiniri Yeesu Almasiihu boo .
57001006	Mi ɗon toro Allah , haa kawtal meeɗen nder nuɗɗinki walla en faamugo barka ka keɓɗen bee Almasiihu .
57001007	Deerɗam giɗaaɗo , yiide ma seyni yam masin , ngam a seyni yimɓe Allah fuu .
57001008	Ngam maajum , mi huuwtinirtaa baawɗe ɗe Almasiihu hokki yam . Mi waawanno umrugo ko haani jonta ,
57001009	ammaa ngam daliila yiide mi ɗon toro ma bee toraago . Min Pol , ndottiijo , jonta boo mi kaɓɓaaɗo ngam Yeesu Almasiihu ,
57001010	mi ɗon toro ma ngam Onesimus , mo laati ɓiŋgel am haa ɗo nder fursinafa , ngam min mi nastini mo nuɗɗinki .
57001011	Naane o nafaay ma , ammaa jonta o nafete , o nafatam boo .
57001012	Jonta mi ɗon lorna mo haa maaɗa , hakkiilo am e yiide am fuu ɗon yahda bee maako .
57001013	Mi ɓuranno yiɗugo o jooɗodo bee am haa o wallammi bana a wallanno yam yaake mi ɗon haa fursina ngam linjiila .
57001014	Ammaa mi yiɗaano ta''ugo haala man sonaa to a yerdake , ngam taa a huuwa mbooɗeeŋga bee doole , sey bee yiide .
57001015	Teema Onesimus seedi bee ma baakin seɗɗa ngam haa o wonda bee ma haa foroy ,
57001016	naa bana maccuɗo , ammaa ko ɓuri maccuɗo piw , bana deerɗiraawo giɗaaɗo nder nuɗɗinki . Min mi yiɗi mo masin , ammaa mi tammi an a ɓuratam yiɗugo mo piw , naa bana neɗɗo tan , ammaa bana tokkiiɗo Jawmiraawo boo .
57001017	To a laari yam bana soobaajo ma fakat , nden kam jaɓɓa mo bana no a jaɓɓorto yam , min .
57001018	To o huuwino ma kalluɗum , to a tokkake mo nyamaande koondeye , min a ?amata .
57001019	Ndaa , mi windi bee juŋŋgo am : Min Pol , mi yoɓete . ( Ngam annditingo ma : Min woni kisnuɗo yoŋki ma . )
57001020	Useni , deerɗam , waɗanam ɗum ngam yiide Jawmiraawo . Seynu ɓernde am bana ko fotti caka deerɗiraaɓe !
57001021	Mi anndi fakat a waɗan ko mi ?ami ma . Wakkati mi ɗon winda ɗum , mi anndi a waɗan ko ɓuri ɗum boo .
57001022	Taaskitanam weerde , ngam mi tammi Allah jaɓan do'a mooɗon , o lornatam haa mooɗon .
57001023	Epafras hoofni on . Min ɗon ngondi nder fursina ngam daliila Yeesu Almasiihu .
57001024	Huuwdooɓe bee am boo koofni on , waato Markus e Aristarkus e Demas e Luka .
57001025	Mo''ere Jawmiraawo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu wondu bee mooɗon fuu .
58001001	Ɓooyma , bee kunduɗe annabo'en , Allah wolwani kaakaaji meeɗen nde ɗuuɗɗum bee laabi feere feere .
58001002	Ammaa nder balɗe ragareeje ɗe'e , Allah wolwani en bee hunduko Ɓiɗɗo muuɗum . Bee maako Allah tagri duniyaaru e asama , o suɓi mo boo ngam o marna mo kuuje fuu haa foroy .
58001003	Ɓiɗɗo Allah ɗon waŋgina annoora tedduŋgal Allah , o nandi bee Allah , o ɗon jogi duniyaaru bee wolde maako sembinde . Ɓaawo o laɓɓini yimɓe diga hakkeeji muuɗum'en , o jooɗi haa asama haa nyaamo Allah , marɗo baawɗe fuu .
58001004	Ɓiɗɗo laati o ɓurduɗo malaa'ika'en tedduŋgal , bana no innde nde Allah hokki mo ɓuri nde maɓɓe .
58001005	Ngam Allah meeɗaay wi'ugo koomoy malaa'ikaajo :
58001006	Ammaa nde Allah ɓadi nelugo Ɓiɗɗo muuɗum afo haa duniyaaru , o wi'i :
58001007	Ndaa ko Allah wi'i dow malaa'ika'en :
58001008	Ammaa dow Ɓiɗɗo o wi'i :
58001009	A yiɗi gooŋga , a wanyi fewre .
58001010	Kadiboo o wi'i :
58001011	kanji ɗi timman , ammaa an a tabitan .
58001012	a taggan ɗi bana ngapaleewol ,
58001013	Allah meeɗaay wi'ugo koomoy malaa'ikaajo :
58001014	Ɓeye ngoni malaa'ika'en ? Ɓe ruuhuuji , ɓe ɗon kuuwana Allah . Allah ɗon nela ɓe ngam haa ɓe mballa heɓanɓe kisndam .
58002001	Ngam maajum sey en ɓesda hakkilango gooŋgaaji ɗi en nani , ngam taa en cela laawol .
58002002	Kubaruwol ngol malaa'ika'en ngaddi ɓooyma , ngol gooŋɗi , goɗɗo mo ɗowtanaaki ngol , heɓan kiita deydey aybefa muuɗum .
58002003	Kadi noy noy en kisrata to en ɗon ngeebi kisndam mawɗam ɗa'am ? Jawmiraawo bee hoore muuɗum aarti waŋgingo kisndam man , nananɓe mo tabitinani en ɗam .
58002004	Allah boo sembiɗini seedamku maɓɓe bee hollugo en baawɗe maako e kaayeefiiji feere feere . Fahin o sendani yimɓe maako dokke Ruuhu Ceniiŋgu fodde muuyo maako .
58002005	Ngam Allah hokkaay malaa'ika'en laamu dow duniyaaru ndu en mbolwata dow muuɗum , waato duniyaaru waranndu .
58002006	Ammaa aayaaje feere mbi'i :
58002007	Wakkati seɗɗa a leesni mo les malaa'ika'en ,
58002008	a wallinani mo kooɗume fuu . "
58002009	Ammaa en ngi'i no Allah leesniri Yeesu les malaa'ika'en wakkati seɗɗa ngam haa Yeesu maaya ngam yimɓe fuu , kanjum woni mo''ere Allah haa meeɗen . Jonta Yeesu heɓi tedduŋgal e hormu ngam boneeji ɗi o yari nder maayde maako .
58002010	Allah woni Jawmiraawo kuuje fuu , tonaa ngam maako , walaa ko daroto . Ngam maajum ɗum fottani mo o laatina Yeesu timmidiɗɗo bee yarugo bone ngam o yahra ɓiɓɓe ɗuuɗɓe haa tedduŋgal maako . Ngam Yeesu on yahrata ɓe haa kisndam .
58002011	Mo yahrata yimɓe haa Allah , e ɓe o yahrata man fuu , ɓe ngoodi Baabiraawo gooto . Ngam maajum o semtaay ewnaago ɓe deerɗiraaɓe maako .
58002012	Bana o wi'i :
58002013	Kadiboo o wi'i :
58002014	Ɓiɓɓe man ngoodi ɓandu e ?i?am , ngam maajum Yeesu bee hoore muuɗum laati bana maɓɓe , o hoo'i ɓandu bana ndu maɓɓe . O waɗi ɗum ngam haa , bee maayde maako , o halka marɗo baawɗe dow maayde , waato Iblisa .
58002015	Bana ni o rimɗiniri laatiiɓe maccuɓe balɗe maɓɓe fuu ngam ɓe kuli maayde .
58002016	Ɗum laaɓɗum , naa malaa'ika'en o wallata , ammaa bana deftere wi'i :
58002017	Ngam maajum doole o laato nanduɗo bee deerɗiiko'en nder kuuje fuu , ngam haa o laato hooreejo liman'en maɓɓe koolaaɗo , enɗuɗo nder kuugal muuɗum yeeso Allah , haa yimɓe keɓa yaafuye hakkeeji muuɗum'en .
58002018	Jonta o waawan wallugo estaaɓe , ngam kaŋko bee hoore maako o estaama , o yari bone .
58003001	Onon deerɗam'en , nastanɓe laamu Allah bee ewnaandu muuɗum , ndaare Yeesu mo Allah neli haa o laato hooreejo liman'en dow nuɗɗinki ki en ceedoto .
58003002	Ngam o koolaaɗo haa Allah , cuɓɗo mo ngam kuugal ngal , bana Muusa boo o koolaaɗo nder kuugal muuɗum nder saare Allah fuu .
58003003	Mahoowo suudu ɓuri suudu man tedduŋgal . Bana non Yeesu ɓurdata Muusa tedduŋgal .
58003004	Saare fuu woodi darnuɗo ɗum , ammaa Allah woni darnuɗo kuuje fuu .
58003005	Muusa woni koolaaɗo nder saare Allah fuu . O suka Allah , o wolwi haala kuuje ɗe Allah tammi waŋgingo nder jamanuuji garanɗi .
58003006	Ammaa Almasiihu o Ɓiɗɗo koolaaɗo , o mawɗo nder saare Allah . Enen en laati saare maako , to en njoofaay cuusal meeɗen e hoolaare meeɗen , to en njogake tammunde meeɗen haa timmoode .
58003007	Ruuhu Allah wi'i :
58003008	taa cattine ko'e mon bana kaakaaji mon tuurtanno yam
58003009	Ton kaakaaji mon njarribi yam , poondi munyal am ,
58003010	Ngam maajum mi ɓernani ɓe , mi wi'i :
58003011	Ngam daliila ɓernuki am mi huni :
58003012	Deerɗam'en , kakkile taa ɓernde koomoy mooɗon halla , sooya nuɗɗinki haa o waylito , o acca Allah geeto .
58003013	Mballindire caka mooɗon balɗe fuu nde " hande " maajum ɗon , ngam taa hakke esta on , taa on cattina ko'e mooɗon .
58003014	Ngam en fuu en laati yimɓe Almasiihu , to en accaay jogaago hoolaare nde en njogino diga fuɗɗam .
58003015	Ndaa ko deftere Allah wi'i :
58003016	Ɓeye nani sawtu Allah , tuurtani mo ? Yimɓe ɓe Muusa wurtini Misra fuu .
58003017	Ɓeye Allah ɓernani duuɓi cappanɗe nayi ? O ɓernani waɗooɓe hakke , do''iiɓe , maayɓe nder ladde .
58003018	Nde Allah huni hunayeere nde'e : " Ɓe keɓataa nastugo siwtaare am " , dow ɓeye o wolwi ? O wolwi dow tuurtuɓe go .
58003019	En ngi'i ɓe keɓaay nastugo siwtaare man ngam ɓe nuɗɗinaay .
58004001	Yoo , Allah wi'no hokkan en laawol nastugo siwtaare muuɗum . Sey en kula , ngam taa gooto mooɗon tampa nastugo siwtaare man .
58004002	Ngam enen boo en nani kubaruwol ceynoowol bana yimɓe nder ladde go . Ɓe nani ngol , ammaa ngol nafaay ɓe , ngam ɓe njaɓaay ngol bee nuɗɗinki .
58004003	Ammaa enen en nuɗɗini , ngam maajum en keɓan nastugo siwtaare Allah . Bana no Allah wi'i :
58004004	Fakat , ndaa ko winda dow nyande joweeɗiɗawre :
58004005	Haala ka'a winda haa nokkuure feere boo :
58004006	Aartuɓe nanugo koŋgol Allah nastaay siwtaare maako ngam ɓe nuɗɗinaay , ammaa woodi woɗɓe heɓanɓe nastugo siwtaare man .
58004007	Ngam maajum Allah waɗi nyande wonde wi'eteende " hande " . O wolwi haala maare ɓaawo duuɓi ɗuuɗɗi bee hunduko Daawuda , o wi'i :
58004008	Ngam to Yosuwa yahrino yimɓe haa siwtaare Allah , Allah wolwataano haala nyande feere ɓaawoɗon .
58004009	To non kam , wakkati siwtaare ngam yimɓe Allah tammi warugo tawon . Siwtaare man nandi bee siwtaare Allah nyande joweeɗiɗawre .
58004010	Ngam koomoy nasti siwtaare man , siwtoto e kuuɗe muuɗum bana no Allah siwtori e kuuɗe muuɗum .
58004011	Ngam maajum sey en kaɓda bee tiinaare ngam haa en keɓa nastugo siwtaare Allah . Taa koomoy meeɗen tuurtana mo bana ɓeya go tuurtiri , ngam taa laato en keɓaay nastugo siwtaare man .
58004012	Ngam wolde Allah ɗon yeeɗi , ɗon huuwa . Nde ɓuri kaafahi kookiye marki mbeldiiji ɗiɗi ta''ugo . Nde ɗon ta''a haa yotto kawtirɗe i'e e mbosam , waato yoŋki e ruuhu . Nde ɗon hiito suunooji e numooji ɓerɗe yimɓe .
58004013	Walaa ko nyukkanto Allah . Kooɗume fuu ɗon waŋgi haa gite maako . Doole en fuu en njaabano ko'e meeɗen yeeso maako .
58004014	Ngam maajum sey en njogo nuɗɗinki ki en ceedoto bee ɓernde woore . Ngam en ngoodi hooreejo liman'en mo yotti haa joonde Allah fakat , ɗum Yeesu , Ɓiɗɗo Allah .
58004015	Hooreejo liman'en meeɗen waawi yurmingo tampe meeɗen , ngam kaŋko o nani estooji kal kal bee meeɗen , ammaa o waɗaay hakke .
58004016	Ngam maajum taa en kula ɓaditaago leeso laamu Allah haa mo''ere tawete . En keɓan enɗam e mo''ere ton , koondey en tampi fuu .
58005001	Hooreejo liman'en fuu laati cuɓaaɗo nder yimɓe , o huuwana Allah ngam maɓɓe , o lii'o dokke e kirsaaɗi ngam ittugo hakkeeji .
58005002	O waawan yurmingo sooya-anndal'en , waɗooɓe aybe , ngam kaŋko bee hoore maako o ɗon tampa nder kuuje ɗuuɗɗe .
58005003	Ngam maajum sey o wadda kirsaaɗi ngam ittugo hakkeeji , naa ngam yimɓe tan , ammaa ngam hoore maako boo .
58005004	Walaa mo hoosanta hoore muuɗum tedduŋgal haa o laato hooreejo liman'en . Sey bee ewnaandu Allah tan goɗɗo laatorto hooreejo liman'en , bana no Haruna laatorino .
58005005	Koo Almasiihu boo teddinaay hoore muuɗum ngam haa o laato hooreejo liman'en . Ammaa Allah wi'i mo :
58005006	Haa aayaare feere o wi'i :
58005007	Yaake Yeesu ɗonno haa duniyaaru , o waɗi do'a , o tori Allah bee bojji e gonɗi , ngam Allah waawi hisnugo mo diga maayde . Allah boo nani tornde maako ngam o ɗowtani ɗum , o mawninaay hoore maako .
58005008	Ammaa koo nde o Ɓiɗɗo Allah , o ekkitori ɗowtaare bee yarugo bone .
58005009	Nde o laati timmidiɗɗo , o laati baaba kisndam nduumiiɗam ngam koomoy ɗowtani mo .
58005010	Allah boo darni mo hooreejo liman'en fodde limanku Malkisadaka .
58005011	Lutti haala ɗuuɗka ka mi wolwaay , ammaa caɗɗum tindingo on ka , ngam on paamataa law .
58005012	Wakkati he'i haa on laato anndinooɓe , ammaa haa jonta on mari haaje goɗɗo anndina on kuuje ɓurɗe hoyugo nder habaru Allah . Haani on nyaama nyaamdu sembindu , ammaa on ɗon musina kosam tawon .
58005013	Koomoy musinta kosam , o ɓiŋgel tawon , o anndaa sendindirgo gooŋga bee fewre .
58005014	Mawɓe ke'i nyaamdu tiindu , ngam ɓe elti hakkiilooji maɓɓe , ɓe anndi sendindirgo booɗɗum bee kalluɗum .
58006001	Ngam maajum njehen yeeso haa anndinol mawɓe , taa en tokko jooɗaago haa anndinol fuɗɗanɓe nder nuɗɗinki Almasiihu . Taa en puɗɗita wallingo caɓɓawal nuɗɗinki , bana haala accugo kuuɗe meereeje , e nuɗɗingo Allah ,
58006002	e ekkitingo ngiiwamji baptisma feere feere , e wallingo juuɗe , e ummitaaki maayɓe , e kiita nduumiika .
58006003	Aa'a , njehen yeeso ! En mbaɗan ɗum , to Allah muuyi .
58006004	Noy loriiɓe ɓaawo ngartata haa ɓe tuuba fahin ? Ɓe meeɗi jooɗaago haa annoora Allah , ɓe metti dokkal asama , ɓe njaɓi geɗal maɓɓe haa Ruuhu Ceniiɗo .
58006005	Ɓe anndi fakat wolde Allah wooɗi , ɓe maati baawɗe jamanuuru waranndu .
58006006	Nden ɓe lori ɓaawo ! Waɗataako ɓe ngarta ɓe tuuba . Ngam to goɗɗo lorake ɓaawo , ɗum laati bana to o ɓili Ɓiɗɗo Allah haa leggal gaafaaŋgal fahin , o jambi mo yeeso yimɓe .
58006007	Allah ɗon barkiɗina lesdi , ndi ɗon yara iyeende nde Allah toɓnata dow maari tum , ndi ɗon fuɗna haakooji ngam haa ɗi nafa remooɓe .
58006008	Ammaa to ndi fuɗni gi'e e geene meere tan , ndi nafataa kooɗume . Neeɓataa , Allah naalan ndi , haa yiite halka ndi .
58006009	Ammaa koo to min ɗon mbolwa bana ni , onon yiɗaaɓe , min ɗon kooli on . Min anndi on ɗon dow laawol booɗŋgol , waato laawol kisndam .
58006010	Allah o gooŋgaajo , o yejjitittaa kuuɗe mooɗon , malla yiide nde on kolli mo bee wallugo nuɗɗinɓe , bandiraaɓe mon , on ɗon mballa ɓe jonta boo .
58006011	Min ngiɗi koomoy mooɗon tokko bee tiinaare muuɗum haa timmoode , ngam haa on keɓa ko on tammoto .
58006012	Min ngiɗaa on laato mbaateendam'en , ammaa on tokko aartuɓe on nuɗɗingo bee munyal , heɓɓe ko Allah wi'i hokkan en .
58006013	Nde Allah waɗi alkawal bee Ibrahiima , o huni o waɗan bana o wi'i . Nde walaa ɓurɗo mo , o huni ɗum bee innde maako .
58006014	O wi'i : " Mi ɗon haɓɓa alkawal bee maaɗa , mi barkiɗinan ma , mi hokkan ma ɓiɓɓe ɗuuɗɓe . "
58006015	Ibrahiima reeni bee munyal , ngam maajum o heɓi ko Allah wi'no mo .
58006016	To neɗɗo hunake , o ɗon hunoro bee innde ɓurannde nde maako , hunayeere man ɗon timmina haalaaji caka yimɓe .
58006017	Allah boo tabitini alkawal muuɗum bee hunayeere . Bana ni o faamtiniri jaɓanɓe alkawal man , o fistataa anniya maako .
58006018	Woodi kuuje ɗiɗi ɗe pistataake , waato alkawal e hunayeere . Waɗataako Allah fewa nder maaje . Kanjum ɗum ɗon tiɗɗina en , haa en njogo tammunde tabinde nde o hokki en .
58006019	Tammunde nde'e laatani en bana tiggirgal yoŋki , nde dimbataako , nde laati hisrude , nde ɗon saalo gaɗa wirndallo haykaliiru asama haa yotto nder yeɓre maaru ɓurnde senaago .
58006020	Yeesu aarti en nastugo ton , o nasti ton ngam meeɗen . O laati hooreejo liman'en haa foroy bana Malkisadaka .
58007001	Malkisadaka oo , o laamiiɗo Saliima , o limanjo Allah Ɓaŋgiiɗo . Nde Ibrahiima ɗonno warta konu mbarki laamiiɓe , Malkisadaka fotti bee maako , barkiɗini mo .
58007002	Ibrahiima hokki Malkisadaka yeɓre woore nder sappo haa ko o heɓi fuu . Maana innde maako woni Laamiiɗo-gooŋgaaku . Kadiboo o laamiiɗo Saliima , bana wi'ugo Laamiiɗo-salaaman .
58007003	Walaa mo anndi baaba maako malla daada maako malla kaakaaji maako . Walaa mo anndi haala danyeeki maako malla maayde maako . O laati bana Ɓiɗɗo Allah , o laati limanjo haa foroy .
58007004	Ndaare maŋgu Malkisadaka ! Ibrahiima , kaaka meeɗen aartuɗo hokki mo yeɓre woore nder sappo haa keɓal konu muuɗum fuu .
58007005	Tawreeta umri ɓiɓɓe Lewi laatiiɓe liman'en , ɓe njaɓa yeɓre woore nder sappo haa jawdi yimɓe Isra'iila , waato ɓe ɗon njaɓa ɗum haa bandiraaɓe maɓɓe , koo nde kamɓe boo ɓe asŋgol Ibrahiima .
58007006	Malkisadaka laataaki nder lenyol Lewi , ammaa o jaɓi yeɓre woore nder sappo haa Ibrahiima , o barkiɗini keɓɗo alkawal Allah .
58007007	Walaa seko , barkiɗinɗo ɓuri barkiɗinaaɗo tedduŋgal .
58007008	Nder limanku Lewi'en , maayanɓe njaɓan yeɓre woore nder sappo . Ammaa nder limanku Malkisadaka , goɗɗo mo maayataa jaɓi yeɓre woore nder sappo . Kanjum woni seedamku deftere .
58007009	Bana wi'ugo : Nde Ibrahiima hokki yeɓre woore nder sappo haa kuuje muuɗum , Lewi boo hokki ɗum , koo nde ɓiɓɓe muuɗum tammi jaɓugo yeɓre man .
58007010	Saa'i maajum Lewi danyaaka tawon , ammaa o ɗonno nder ɓandu kaaka maako Ibrahiima nde Malkisadaka fotti bee Ibrahiima .
58007011	Allah hokki yimɓe Isra'iila tawreeta , darni ka dow limanku Lewi'en . To kuugal liman'en Lewi'en laatino timmuŋgal , haaje walaa limanjo goɗɗo waŋga , nanduɗo bee Malkisadaka , naa goɗɗo asŋgol Haruna .
58007012	To limanku waylake , doole umroore boo waylo .
58007013	Kuuje ɗe'e mbolwaama dow Jawmiraawo meeɗen . Kaŋko o laati mo lenyol feere . Walaa goɗɗo nder lenyol maako meeɗi laataago limanjo haa hirsirde .
58007014	Koomoy fuu anndi o danyaama nder lenyol Yahuuda . Muusa meeɗaay wolwugo haala lenyol ngo'ol , nde o wolwi haala liman'en .
58007015	Haala ka'a ɓesdan laaɓugo maa : Limanjo goɗɗo waŋgi , mo nandi bee Malkisadaka .
58007016	O laataaki limanjo bee umrooje yimɓe , ammaa o laati limanjo bee baawɗe ngeendam ɗam timmataa .
58007017	Ngam deftere wi'i :
58007018	Umroore ɓooymaare wudinaama , ngam nde tampi , nde nafaay .
58007019	Ngam tawreeta Muusa waawaay timmidingo kooɗume . Jonta en keɓi tammunde ɓurnde mawnugo , kayre ɓadinta en bee Allah .
58007020	Dow maajum boo woodi hunayeere Allah . Limanku naane darnaama bilaa hunayeere bana nde'e .
58007021	Ammaa Yeesu laati limanjo bee hunayeere nde Allah wi'i mo :
58007022	Ngam maajum en anndi fakat , Yeesu waddi alkawal ɓurŋgal ngal naane .
58007023	Woodi huunde feere boo : Liman'en naane ɓe ɗuuɗɓe , ngam maayde haɗi ɓe tokkaago kuuɗe maɓɓe .
58007024	Ammaa Yeesu ɗon yeeɗi haa foroy , limanku maako timmataa .
58007025	Ngam maajum o waawan hisnugo yimɓe ɓe o yahri haa Allah jonta e haa foroy , ngam o ɗon yeeɗi haa foroy ngam o torano ɓe Allah .
58007026	Yeesu woni hooreejo liman'en baawɗo humtango en haaje meeɗen fuu . O ceniiɗo , walaa aybe koo tis haa maako . O sendaama bee marɓe hakke , o ɓaŋgtaama dow asamanji .
58007027	O nandaay bee luttuɓe hoore'en liman'en , o walaa haaje hokkugo kirseteeɗi balɗe fuu , aran ngam hakkeeji maako , nden ngam hakkeeji yimɓe . Ammaa nde o hokki yoŋki maako sadaka , ki laati sadaka ngoota , nde woore , ka he'i haa foroy .
58007028	Tawreeta Muusa suɓi tampuɓe ngam ɓe laato hoore'en liman'en . Ammaa hunayeere Allah warnde ɓaawo tawreeta , suɓi Ɓiɗɗo mo laati timmidiɗɗo haa foroy .
58008001	Ndaa laaɓɗum haala ka'a fuu : En ngoodi hooreejo liman'en bana oo , jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu haa nyaamo Allah , mawɗo asamanji .
58008002	O laati hooreejo liman'en haa nokkuure ɓurnde senaago nder laymaaru gooŋgaaru ndu Jawmiraawo waɗi , naa neɗɗo .
58008003	Hoore'en liman'en fuu cuɓaama ngam ɓe lii'ano Allah dokke e kirsaaɗi . Ngam maajum sey hooreejo liman'en meeɗen boo wadda ko o lii'oto .
58008004	To o ɗonno haa duniyaaru , o laatataakono limanjo sam , ngam woodi liman'en lii'otooɓeno dokke fodde tawreeta Yahuudu'en .
58008005	Kuugal limanku ngal ɓe kuuwata , laati misaalu tan haa ko woni nder asama . Non ɗum laati bee Muusa boo . Nde o ɓadake waɗugo laymaaru , Allah wi'i mo : " Sey a waɗa ɗum fuu fodde misaalu mo mi holli ma dow hooseere . "
58008006	Ammaa jonta Yeesu heɓi kuugal limanku ɓurŋgal ngal maɓɓe . Bana non boo alkawal ngal o haɓɓi hakkunde Allah bee yimɓe , ɓuri ngal naane saman , ngam ngal ɗon dari dow koŋguɗi Allah ɓurɗi ɗi naane tabitgo .
58008007	To alkawal aranal walaano aybe , walaa haaje alkawal ɗiɗaɓal .
58008008	Ammaa Allah tawi aybe haa yimɓe muuɗum , ngam o wi'i :
58008009	" Ngal nandataa bee alkawal ngal kaɓɓumi bee kaakaaji maɓɓe ,
58008010	" Ammaa ɓaawo nyalɗe ɗe'e ,
58008011	Walaa haaje goɗɗo anndina keeddiɗɗum malla deerɗum ,
58008012	Ngam mi yaafoto aybeeji maɓɓe ,
58008013	Nde o wolwi haala alkawal kesal , Allah hiiɗini aranal . Ammaa ko hiiɗi , ɗum ɓadake jinnugo .
58009001	Alkawal aranal woodino farillaaji dow cujidanki Allah . Ngal woodino nokkuure seniinde boo nde yimɓe mbaɗi .
58009002	Yimɓe mbaɗi laymaaji ɗiɗi . Laymaaru arandu ewnaama nokkuure seniinde . Nder maaru woodi jo''inirɗum pittirlaaji e teebur bee tamseeje jo''inaaɗe yeeso Allah .
58009003	Ɓaawo wirndallo ɗiɗaɓo , woodi laymaaru wi'eteendu nokkuure ɓurnde senaago .
58009004	Nder maaru woodi gulduɗum urle ɗum kaŋgeeri , e sundukru alkawal suddaandu bee kaŋgeeri . Nder sundukru man woodi taasawo kaŋgeeri bee mannu nder maago , e sawru Haruna wilitiindu , e alluhaaje kaa'e ɗiɗi bee bolle alkawal bindaaɗe dow maaje .
58009005	Dow sundukru man woodi fotooji keruba'en laatiiɓe misaalu joonde Allah . Ɓe mbeeɗi bileeji maɓɓe dow nokkuure haa hakkeeji njaafaama . Ammaa jonta min mbaawataa tindingo kuuje ɗe'e fuu .
58009006	Nde kuuje fuu ndari bana ni , liman'en tokki nastugo laymaaru arandu balɗe fuu , ngam haa ɓe kuuwa kuuɗe maɓɓe .
58009007	Ammaa laymaaru ɗiɗawru , sey hooreejo liman'en tan nastata ton , kaŋko boo hitaande fuu nde woore . O ɗon nasta bee ?i?am ɗam o lii'anto Allah ngam hoore maako e ngam hakkeeji ɗi yimɓe mbaɗi bilaa anniya .
58009008	Ndaa ko Ruuhu Ceniiɗo anndinta bee kuuje ɗe'e : Yaake laymaaru arandu ɗon dari tawon , laawol nastugo laymaaru ɗiɗawru maɓɓitaaki tawon .
58009009	Suudu arandu woni misaalu ngam hollugo en ko laati jonta . Ɗum yiɗi wi'ugo : Dokke e kirsaaɗi lii'anaaɗi Allah mbaawataa mo''ingo ɓernde cujidoowo haa o laato timmidiɗɗo .
58009010	Dokke man laati haala nyaamdu e njaram e laɓɓinki kuuje bee laabi feere feere . Ɗum fuu ɗum haala yaasi , ɗum nafi haa warugo saa'iire nde Allah wayli ɗum fuu .
58009011	Ammaa jonta Almasiihu wari . Kaŋko woni hooreejo liman'en dow kuuje booɗɗe ɗe ngarani en jonta . O ɗon huuwa nder laymaaru ɓurndu ndu naane mawnugo e wooɗugo . Juuɗe yimɓe mbaɗaay ndu , waato ndu iwaay haa duniyaaru ndu .
58009012	Almasiihu saali nder laymaaru arandu , o nasti nde woore tan haa nokkuure ɓurnde senaago , ɗum he'i haa foroy . O nastaay bee ?i?am jawɗi be'i e ga'i kalhali boo , ammaa o nasti bee ?i?am hoore maako . Bana ni o heɓrani en kisndam nduumiiɗam .
58009013	?i?am jawɗi be'i e ga'i e ndoondi wiige mbiccaama dow yimɓe soɓɓe , kanjum ɗum laɓɓini ɓe , itti coɓki maɓɓe .
58009014	Nde non kam , ?i?am Almasiihu ɓuran nafugo piw . Bee Ruuhu nduumiiŋgu o hokkiri yoŋki maako haa Allah bana sadaka ka walaa aybe koo tis . ?i?am maako laɓɓinan ɓerɗe meeɗen , ittan aybeeji meeɗen , ngam taa en mbaɗa ko yahrata en haa maayde , ammaa en keɓa huuwango Allah , dokkoowo ngeendam .
58009015	Ngam maajum Almasiihu woni kaɓɓuɗo alkawal kesal , ngam haa ewnaaɓe Allah keɓa barkaaji duumiiɗi ɗi Allah wi'no hokkan . Ɗum waɗoto ngam gooto maayi , rimɗini yimɓe diga aybeeji ɗi ɓe mbaɗno yaake ɓe ɗonno nder alkawal ɓooymawal .
58009016	Haa ɗereewol wasuye woni , sey tammiiɓe ronugo ngooŋɗina gasiiɗo ngol maayi .
58009017	Ngam ɗereewol wasuye nafataa kooɗume to gasiiɗo ngol ɗon bee yoŋki tawon , sey ɓaawo maayde maako ngol nafata .
58009018	Kanjum waɗi , koo alkawal ɓooymawal boo tabitaay , sey nde ɓe tabitini ngal bee ?i?am .
58009019	Aran , Muusa waŋgini umrooje fuu bana ɗe mbinda nder tawreeta . Nden o hoo'i ?i?am ga'i kalhali hawtaade bee ndiyam , o wicci ɗam dow deftere tawreeta e yimɓe fuu bee haako isop e uuluuji boɗeejum .
58009020	O wi'i : " ?i?am ɗa'am ɗon tabitina alkawal ngal Allah umri on on ɗowtano . "
58009021	Bana non boo , Muusa wicci ?i?am dow laymaaru e dow kuuje kuugal diina fuu .
58009022	Fodde tawreeta ɓurna kuuje fuu laɓɓinaama bee ?i?am . Walaa yaafuye hakkeeji , sonaa to ?i?am rufi .
58009023	Kuuje ɗe'e , laatiiɗe misaaluuji haa ko woni nder asama , doole ɗe laato cenaaɗe bana non . Ammaa kuuje haa asama mari haaje sadakaaji ɓurɗi ɗi duniyaaru .
58009024	Ngam Almasiihu nastaay nokkuure seniinde nde yimɓe mbaɗi , waato misaaluwol meere . Ammaa o nasti nder asama , ngam haa o seetto en yeeso Allah .
58009025	Hooreejo liman'en haa Yahuudu'en ɗon nasta nokkuure seniinde hitaande fuu bee ?i?am ndabbaawa . Ammaa Almasiihu nastataa tum ngam o hokka yoŋki maako .
58009026	To o waɗino non , diga fuɗɗam tageeki duniyaaru o torrotono nde ɗuuɗɗum . Aa'a , o waŋgi jonta haa timmoode jamanuuji fuu , o waŋgi nde woore ngam foroy , ngam haa o itta hakkeeji bee hokkugo yoŋki maako .
58009027	Koomoy fuu maayan nde woore , ɓaawoɗon Allah hiitoto mo .
58009028	Bana non Almasiihu boo hokki yoŋki muuɗum nde woore ngam o itta hakkeeji ɗuuɗɓe . O waŋgan ɗiɗawre , naa ngam o itta hakkeeji , ammaa ngam o hisna reenɓe mo .
58010001	Tawreeta Yahuudu'en maraay kuuje gooŋgaaje , sey misaalu maaje tan . Ɗe laati bana ɗowdi kuuje booɗɗe ɗe tammi warugo . Duuɓi fuu ɓe tokki lii'anaago Allah kirseteeɗi . Kadi bee kirseteeɗi bana ɗi'i , noy tawreeta waawri timmidingo waddanɓe ɗi haa Allah ?
58010002	To sujidanooɓe Allah laɓɓinaamano e hakkeeji maɓɓe fakat , hakkeeji man naawataano ɓerɗe maɓɓe fahin , walaa haaje lii'aago kirseteeɗi fahin .
58010003	Ammaa kirseteeɗi ɗon ciftinora yimɓe hakkeeji muuɗum'en hitaande fuu .
58010004	Ngam ?i?am ga'i e be'i waawataa ittugo hakkeeji .
58010005	Ngam maajum , nde Almasiihu ɓadi warugo nder duniyaaru , o wi'i Allah :
58010006	A seyortaako dabbaaji guleteeɗi ,
58010007	Nden mbi'mi : Ndaa yam , mi huuwan ko ngiɗɗa , ya Allah ,
58010008	Aran o wi'i : " A yiɗaa kirsaaɗi e dokke , a seyortaako dabbaaji guleteeɗi malla kirseteeɗi ngam ittuki hakke . " O wi'i ɗum koo nde dokke ɗe'e fuu lii'aama fodde tawreeta .
58010009	Nden o wi'i : " Ya Allah , ndaa yam , mi huuwan ko ngiɗɗa . " Bana ni Allah wili sadakaaji ɓooymaaji , o waɗi sadaka Almasiihu mbattudi maaji .
58010010	Yeesu huuwi ko Allah yiɗi , ngam maajum en laɓɓinaama e hakkeeji bee sadaka ɓandu maako ka o waɗi nde woore , ka he'i haa foroy .
58010011	Liman'en fuu ɗon kuuwa kuuɗe muuɗum'en balɗe fuu , ɓe ɗon tokki lii'aago kirseteeɗi . Kirseteeɗi man mbaawataa ittugo hakkeeji .
58010012	Ammaa Almasiihu waɗi sadaka ngoota ngam hakkeeji , ka he'i haa foroy . Ɓaawoɗon o jooɗi haa juŋŋgo Allah nyaamo .
58010013	Ton o ɗon reena haa Allah laatina konne'en maako jaaɓruɗum kosɗe maako .
58010014	Non bee sadaka ngoota o timmidini laɓɓinaaɓe e hakke , o laatini ɓe timmidiɗɓe haa foroy .
58010015	Ruuhu Ceniiŋgu boo ɗon seedano en ɗum . Aran ngu wi'i :
58010016	" Jawmiraawo wi'i : Ɓaawo nyalɗe ɗe'e
58010017	Nden o wi'i : " Mi meetataa siftorgo hakkeeji maɓɓe e kuuɗe maɓɓe kalluɗe . "
58010018	Ngam maajum , nde Allah yaafi ɗum , walaa haaje lii'aago kirseteeɗi ngam ittugo hakke fahin .
58010019	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , ngam daliila ?i?am Almasiihu ndufaaɗam en keɓi laawol nastugo nokkuure ɓurnde senaago .
58010020	O maɓɓitani en laawol kesol , jahranŋgol en haa ngeendam , gaɗa wirndallo , kaŋgo woni ɓandu maako .
58010021	En ngoodi hooreejo liman'en laatiiɗo mawɗo saare Allah .
58010022	Ngam maajum sey en ɓadito Allah bee ɓerɗe gooŋgaaje , bee nuɗɗinki cembiɗki , bee ɓerɗe laɓɓinaaɗe diga hakke , ɓalli boo giiwaaɗi bee ndiyam ceniiɗam .
58010023	Sey en njogo tammunde nde en ceedoto , ngam Allah o koolniiɗo , o waɗan ko o wi'i .
58010024	Sey koomoy meeɗen cuklano deerɗum'en , tiɗɗina ɓe haa en mbaŋgina yiide , haa en kuuwa kuuɗe booɗɗe .
58010025	Taa en acca mooɓtaago bee nuɗɗinɓe bana woɗɓe mbaɗata . Ammaa sey en cembiɗindira , sakkoma nde on anndi nyande Jawmiraawo ɓadake warugo .
58010026	En anndi gooŋga . To en ɗon tokko waɗugo hakke bee anniya , walaa sadaka waawata ittugo hakke meeɗen .
58010027	To non kam , walaa ko luttata , sey hulugo kiita e yiite nge tammi halkugo konne'en Allah !
58010028	Koomoy yawi tawreeta Muusa , o mbareteeɗo bilaa enɗam , to seedooɓe ɗiɗo malla tato tabitini aybe maako .
58010029	Sakkoma to goɗɗo yawake Ɓiɗɗo Allah , to o laari ?i?am alkawal Allah ɗam laɓɓini mo bana huunde meere , to o huɗi Ruuhu mo''ere ! Fakat , kaŋko o heɓan kiita ɓurka hallugo .
58010030	Ngam en anndi mo wi'i :
58010031	Yanugo haa juŋŋgo Allah geeto ɗum kulniiɗum masin !
58010032	Ciftore no on njooɗori naane . Nder balɗe man , ɓaawo Allah yaynani on bee annoora muuɗum , on njari boneeji ɗuuɗɗi , ammaa ɗi ɓuraay on sembe .
58010033	Ɓe kuɗi woɗɓe mooɗon , ɓe toonyi ɓe , ammaa luttuɓe mooɗon boo tiɗɗini huɗaaɓe go .
58010034	Ɓerɗe mooɗon naawi ngam daliila haɓɓaaɓe . Nde wuyɓe ngujji jawdi mooɗon , on munyi asar man , ngam on anndi luttani on kuuje ɓurɗe wooɗugo , ɗe timmataa .
58010035	Taa njoofe dartaare mooɗon , ngam nde waddanan on mbarjaari mawndi .
58010036	On mari haaje munyal ngam haa on kuuwa muuyo Allah , on keɓa ko o wi'i o hokkan .
58010037	Ngam deftere wi'i :
58010038	Ammaa yimɓe am gooŋga'en nuɗɗinan , ɓe ngeeɗan .
58010039	Enen kam en laataaki nder loriiɓe ɓaawo , halkanɓe . Ammaa en ɗon tabiti nder nuɗɗinki , en kisan .
58011001	Hooliiɓe Allah anndi fakat o hokkan ɓe ko ɓe tammoto , ɓe anndi fakat , kuuje ɗe ɓe ngi'aay tawon , ɗe ɗon tabiti .
58011002	Bee hoolaare bana ni yimɓe jamanuuji ɓooymaaji laati yerdaaɓe Allah .
58011003	En ɗon kooli Allah , ngam maajum en anndi wolde Allah tagi duniyaaru e asama . Ko en ngi'ata fuu , ɗum iwi haa ko yi'ataake .
58011004	Habila hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o hokki Allah dokkal ɓurŋgal ngal Kayinu . Nde o ɗon hooli Allah , o heɓi yerduye Allah ngam Allah bee hoore muuɗum jaɓi dokkal maako . Koo nde o maayi , o ɗon wolwana en bee hoolaare maako .
58011005	Anuhu hooli Allah . Ngam maajum Allah eeŋgtini mo , o maayaay . Walaa mo heɓti Anuhu , ngam Allah eeŋgtini mo . Deftere wi'i , diga o eeŋgtinaaka , o fottani Allah .
58011006	Bilaa hoolaare goɗɗo waawataa fottango Allah . Koomoy yiɗi warugo haa Allah , sey nuɗɗina Allah ɗon , o ɗon warjo ɗaɓɓitanɓe mo boo .
58011007	Nuuhu hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o nani ko Allah wi'i dow asar ko tammi warugo koo nde o yi'aay ɗum . O ɗowtani mo , o sehi koombowalfe . Nder maagal kaŋko bee yimɓe saare maako fuu ɓe kisi . Hoolaare maako hiiti duniyaaru fuu . Nuuhu nuɗɗini Allah , heɓi yerduye maako .
58011008	Ibrahiima hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o ɗowtani Allah nde Allah ewni mo o yaha haa lesdi ndi Allah wi'no hokkan mo . O acci lesdi maako bilaa anndugo haa o yahata .
58011009	O hooli Allah , o jooɗi bana jananno nder lesdi ndi Allah wi'i hokkan mo . O jooɗi nder laymaaji , kaŋko e Isiyaaku e Yakubu , jaɓɓe ko Allah wi'i bana kaŋko o jaɓri ɗum .
58011010	Ngam Ibrahiima ɗonno reena berniwol ngol Allah diidi , mahi , berniwol marŋgol caɓɓaaje tabitɗe .
58011011	Ibrahiima hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o heɓi baawɗe danyugo ɓiŋgel koo nde duuɓi maako caali , Saratu boo laatino dimaro . O hooli Allah waɗan ko o wi'i .
58011012	Koo nde o laati bana maayɗo , o laati kaaka yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe bana koode asama , malla bana njaareendi maayo ndi limataako .
58011013	Yimɓe ɓe'e fuu maayi bee hoolaago Allah . Ɓe keɓaay ko Allah wi'no hokkan ɓe , ammaa diga daayiiɗum ɓe eewi ɗum , ɓe ceyori ɗum . Ɓe cemtaay wi'ugo ɓe jananɓe e hoɗɓe haa duniyaaru .
58011014	Wi'ɓe ɗum ngiɗi wi'ugo ɓe ɗon ɗaɓɓita lesdi halal maɓɓe .
58011015	Ɓe numaay lesdi ndi ɓe acci . To naa non , ɓe keɓanno loraago ton .
58011016	Aa'a , ɓe ngenwi lesdi ɓurdundi , waato asama . Ngam maajum Allah semtiraay ewneego Allah maɓɓe , ngam o waɗani ɓe berniwol .
58011017	Ibrahiima hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o lii'ani mo ɓiɗɗo maako Isiyaaku bana kirseteeŋga , nde Allah jarribi mo . Koo nde Allah wi'i hokkan mo danygol , o yerdi hokkugo ɓiɗɗo maako bajjo bana kirseteeŋga .
58011018	Allah wi'no mo : " Bee Isiyaaku keɓrata danygol . "
58011019	Ibrahiima numi Allah waawan ummitingo Isiyaaku diga maayde . Non o heɓti Isiyaaku bana diga maayde .
58011020	Isiyaaku hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o barkiɗini Yakubu e Isuwa ngam balɗe garanɗe .
58011021	Yakubu hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o barkiɗini ɓiɓɓe Yusufu hiddeko o maaya . O tuggi sawru maako , o sujidani Allah .
58011022	Yusufu hooli Allah . Ngam maajum nde o ɓadi maayugo , o wolwi haala egguki Isra'iila'en diga Misra , o tindini ɓe ko ɓe mbaɗata bee i'e maako .
58011023	Saarooji Muusa kooli Allah . Ngam maajum ɓe kulaay luutugo umroore laamiiɗo , ɓe nyukkini Muusa lebbi tati ɓaawo danyeeki muuɗum ngam ɓe ngi'i o ɓiŋgel booɗŋgel .
58011024	Muusa hooli Allah . Ngam maajum , nde o mawni , o sali laataago ɓii ɓiɗɗo Firawna debbo .
58011025	O ɓuri yiɗugo o yara bone bee yimɓe Allah dow mettaago seyo hakkeeji baakin seɗɗa .
58011026	O numi yarugo bone yawaare ngam Almasiihu ɓuri ndesaaji Misra fuu saman , ngam o accaay numugo mbarjaari ndi o tammi heɓugo .
58011027	Muusa hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o hulaay tikkere laamiiɗo , ammaa o wurti Misra . O dimbaaki sam , bana o laari Allah mo yi'ataake .
58011028	O hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o waɗi juulde Paska , o umri Isra'iila'en ɓe mbicca ?i?am dow dammuɗe , ngam taa malaa'ikaajo maayde mbara ɓiɓɓe maɓɓe afɓe .
58011029	Yimɓe Isra'iila kooli Allah . Ngam maajum ɓe keɓi eeraago maayo Maaliya bana dow lesdi njoorndi . Nde Misra'en ɗaɓɓi tokkaago ɓe , maayo moɗi ɗum'en .
58011030	Yimɓe Isra'iila kooli Allah . Ngam maajum ɓe ngaanci , ɓe taari wuro Yeriko balɗe joweeɗiɗi , haa mahol maago yibbi .
58011031	Rahab , debbo daakaareejo , hooli Allah . Ngam maajum o jaɓɓi Isra'iila'en horooɓe bee seyo . Ngam man o mbaraaka bee luttuɓe ɓe ɗowtanaaki Allah .
58011032	Ɗume ɓesdanmi limtugo ? Wakkati he'aay mi wolwa haala Gedeyon , Barak , Samson , Yefta , Daawuda , Samuyila e annabo'en .
58011033	Ɓe fuu ɓe kooli Allah . Ngam maajum ɓe kaɓi bee laamuuji , ɓe njaali . Ɓe mbaɗi ko Allah yiɗi , ɓe keɓi boo ko Allah wi'no hokkan . Ɓe cukki kunduɗe barooɗe ,
58011034	ɓe nyifi yiite huɓɓanŋge , ɓe kisi mbareego bee kaafahi . Ɓe tampi , ammaa ɓe keɓi sembe . Ɓe laati waawɓe nder konu , ɓe njaali sooje'en jananɓe .
58011035	Rewɓe kooli Allah . Ngam maajum ɓe keɓti maayɓe maɓɓe , waato ɓe ummitinaama , ɓe ngeeɗiti fahin .
58011036	Yimɓe duniyaaru njanci woɗɓe maɓɓe , ɓocci ɓe , kaɓɓi woɗɓe , cakkini ɓe nder fursina ,
58011037	piɗi ɓe bee kaa'e haa ɓe maayi , ta''i ɓalli maɓɓe geɓe ɗiɗi , mbari ɓe bee kaafahi . Ɓe ngiili ɓe ɗon ɓorni lare be'i e baali , ɓe talkiɗi , ɓe torraama , ɓe toonyaama .
58011038	Duniyaaru haananaay ɓe . Ɓe ngiili nder laɗɗe e kooseeje bana riiwaaɓe , ɓe njooɗi nder lowi e nder gasɗe .
58011039	Yimɓe ɓe'e fuu ɓe nuɗɗini Allah , ɓe keɓi yerduye maako . Ammaa ɓe keɓaay ko o wi'no hokkan ,
58011040	ngam o waɗi anniya hokkugo en ko ɓuri wooɗugo . Allah yiɗaa ɓe laato timmidiɗɓe , sonaa hawtaade bee meeɗen .
58012001	Ummaatoore ɗuunde , seedooɓe hoolaare maɓɓe , ɗon taari en bana ruuldere . Ngam maajum , sey en ngudina kooɗume ko teddanta en , sey en ngudina dooŋgal hakke ɗakkotooŋgal en bee sembe . Sey en tiino timmitingo daɗadaɗa meeɗen .
58012002	Taa en acca laarugo Yeesu , ngam hoolaare meeɗen ɗon dari dow maako diga fuɗɗoode haa timmoode . Nde ɓe mbari mo haa leggal gaafaaŋgal , o munyi ɗum . O hakkilanaay mbustu maayde nde'e , ngam daliila seyo ngo Allah sigani mo . Jonta o ɗon jooɗi dow leeso laamu haa nyaamo Allah .
58012003	Nume boneeji ɗi o yari , no o munyiri yawaare marɓe hakke ! Kanjum ɗum wallan on ngam taa on tampa , taa on njoofa hoolaare mooɗon sam .
58012004	Ngam nder haɓre mooɗon bee hakke on kaɓaay haa yotti maayde tawon .
58012005	On ngejjiti bolle cembiɗinooje ɗe Allah wolwani on , onon ɓiɓɓe maako na ? O wi'i :
58012006	Ngam Jawmiraawo ɗon elta yiɗaaɓe muuɗum ,
58012007	Munye torra mooɗon bana elto baaba , ngam torra mooɗon ɗon waŋgina Allah ɗon huuwana on bana ɓiɓɓe muuɗum . Woodi ɓiŋgel ngel baaba muuɗum eltataa na ?
58012008	To Allah eltaay on bana o eltirta ɓiɓɓe maako fuu , nden kam naa on ɓiɓɓe maako , ammaa on njaalu'en .
58012009	Ciftoren baabiraaɓe meeɗen haa duniyaaru . Ɓe elti en , ammaa en ɗon teddina ɓe . Sakkoma Baabiraawo meeɗen haa asama , sey en ɗowtano mo haa en ngeeɗa !
58012010	Baabiraaɓe meeɗen haa duniyaaru elti en wakkati seɗɗa , bana ɗum fottani ɓe . Ammaa Allah ɗon elta en ngam mbooɗeeŋga meeɗen , ngam haa en kawta bee maako nder senaare .
58012011	Yaake o ɗon elta en , en ɗon maata naawɗum , naa seyo . Ammaa ɓaawoɗon jaɓɓe elto man paaman ngo wooɗi , ngo laatini ɓe huuwooɓe ko fotti , ngo waddani en jam .
58012012	Kadi ɓaŋgte juuɗe mooɗon comɗe , cembiɗine koppi mooɗon tampuɗi !
58012013	Tokke laabi darnuɗi , ngam taa kosŋgal naawanŋgal tullita , ammaa ngal yamɗita .
58012014	Tiine jooɗaago jam bee koomoy . Tiine ɓesdaago nder senaare , ngam bilaa maare walaa mo yi'ata Jawmiraawo .
58012015	Kakkile ngam taa koo gooto mooɗon loro ɓaawo , acca mo''ere Allah . Kakkile taa koomoy mooɗon laato bana haako haaɗko ko ɗon mawna , ko ɗon torra yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe bee tooke maako .
58012016	Kakkile ngam taa koomoy mooɗon halla bana Isuwa . Ngam Isuwa ɗowtanaaki Allah , o soorri daraja afaaku maako ngam o heɓa o nyaama nde woore tan .
58012017	On anndi ɓaawoɗon nde o yiɗi heɓugo barka baaba maako , o heɓaay . O heɓaay waylugo ko o waɗno boo , koo nde o tefi ɗum bee bojji .
58012018	Onon on ngaraay bana no Isra'iila'en ngarno , haa ko on mbaawi meemugo , waato haa hooseere Sina bee yiite huɓɓanŋge , malla haa nyiɓre , malla haa naargewol ,
58012019	malla haa hoolo algaytaaru , malla haa hoolo sawtu . Nde yimɓe nani sawtu man , ɓe tori taa ɓe meeta nanugo koo wolde woore ,
58012020	ngam ɓe mbaawaay munyugo umroore nde'e : " Koo to ndabbaawa meemi hooseere , sey nga mbare bee kaa'e . "
58012021	Laarugo ɗum hulni koo Muusa boo haa o wi'i : " Mi ɗon diwna ngam kulol ! "
58012022	Ammaa onon on ngari haa hooseere Siyona , haa berniwol Allah geeto , waato Urusaliima ngol asama , bee mooɓtorde juulde nde malaa'ika'en ujine ujineeje .
58012023	On ngari haa mooɓtorde ɓiɓɓe Allah afɓe , ɓe inɗe muuɗum'en mbinda haa asama . On ngari haa Allah , kiitoowo yimɓe fuu , on ngari haa yoŋkiiji gooŋga'en laatiiɓe timmidiɗɓe .
58012024	On ngari haa Yeesu , kaɓɓuɗo alkawal kesal , on ngari haa ?i?am mbiccaaɗam mbaŋginanɗam kuuje booɗɗe ko ɓuri ?i?am Habila .
58012025	Ngam maajum kakkile , taa cale nanugo bolwanɗo jonta . Saliiɓe nanugo bolwuɗo haala Allah haa duniyaaru , kisaay . Kadi noy enen en tammi hisugo , to en ɗoyli bolwanɗo diga asama !
58012026	Ɓooyma sawtu maako dimbi duniyaaru , ammaa jonta o wi'i : " Nde woore fahin mi dimban naa duniyaaru tan , ammaa asama boo . "
58012027	Bolle " nde woore fahin " ɗon kolla en laaɓɗum no tagaaɗum fuu dimboto , ittete ngam haa ko dimbataako tabita .
58012028	Ngam maajum ngetten Allah , ngam en keɓan laamu ngu dimbataako . Cujidanen Allah bana ɗum fottanta mo , bee kulol boo ,
58012029	ngam fakat Allah meeɗen woni yiite nyaamooye .
58013001	Tokke yiɗindirgo ngam on deerɗiraaɓe .
58013002	Taa ngejjite weernugo hoɗɓe . Woɗɓe mbaɗi ɗum , njaɓɓi malaa'ika'en bilaa anndugo ɓe malaa'ika'en .
58013003	Ciftore haɓɓaaɓe nder fursina , bana on haɓɓaaɓe bee maɓɓe . Ciftore toonyaaɓe , bana on toonyaaɓe bee maɓɓe .
58013004	Sey yimɓe fuu camɗina teegal , te'aaɓe boo taa mbaɗa njeenu . Allah hiitoto daakaare'en e jeenooɓe .
58013005	Taa cuune ceede , ammaa ceye bee ko on mari . Ngam Allah wi'i : " Mi accataa ma , mi yeebataako ma sam . "
58013006	Ngam maajum en ɗon mbi'a bee dartaare :
58013007	Taa ngejjite ardiiɓe on naane , wolwanɓe on haala Allah . Nume no ɓe njooɗori , no ɓe maayri , tokke nuɗɗinki maɓɓe .
58013008	Yeesu Almasiihu o tabitɗo keenya e hande e haa foroy .
58013009	Taa acce anndinol feere malla janannol selna on laawol gooŋga . Ɗum wooɗi to yoŋkiiji meeɗen keɓi sembe nder mo''ere Allah , naa bee tokkaago farillaaji dow nyaamdu . Tokkiiɓe irin farillaaji ɗi'i keɓaay nafuda .
58013010	Liman'en huuwooɓe nder laymaaru Yahuudu'en keɓataa nyaamugo kirseteeɗi haa hirsirde meeɗen .
58013011	Hooreejo liman'en ɗon wadda ?i?am dabbaaji nder nokkuure ɓurnde senaago haa o lii'o ɗam ngam ittuki hakkeeji , ammaa ɓe ɗon ngula dabbaaji man haa yaasi saŋgeere .
58013012	Ngam maajum Yeesu boo maayi yaasi dammugal berniwol , ngam haa o laɓɓina yimɓe diga hakke muuɗum'en bee ?i?am maako .
58013013	Sey en njaha haa maako yaasi saŋgeere ngam en kawta bee maako munyango semteende man .
58013014	Ngam en ngalaa joonde tabinde haa duniyaaru ndu , en ɗon ngenwa joonde warannde .
58013015	Barka Yeesu sey en lii'ano Allah maŋgtoore bana dokkal , waato en ceedo innde maako tum bee kunduɗe meeɗen .
58013016	Taa ngejjite huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga . Mballindire , ngam kanjum woni sadakaaji pottananɗi Allah .
58013017	Ɗowtane ardiiɓe on , tokke umrooje maɓɓe . Ɓe ɗon ayna yoŋkiiji mooɗon bilaa siwtaare , ngam ɓe njaaboto Allah dow kuuɗe maɓɓe . To on ɗowtanake ɓe , ɓe kuuwan bee seyo . To naa non , ɓe kuuwan bee mone , kanjum boo ɗum waddanan on sarru .
58013018	Tokke toraago Allah ngam meeɗen . En anndi fakat ɓerɗe meeɗen laaɓi , ngam foroy en ngiɗi huuwugo ko fotti .
58013019	Mi ɗon ɓesda toraago on , on toro Allah ngam am , ngam haa o lornammi haa mooɗon bee jaawal .
58013020	Allah ummitini Jawmiraawo meeɗen Yeesu diga maayde , kaŋko o laati gaynaako baali mawɗo ngam daliila maayde maako . Bee ?i?am maako o tabitini alkawal duumiiŋgal .
58013021	Allah dokkoowo en jam , walla on huuwugo kuuɗe booɗɗe fuu ɗe o ɗaɓɓata haa mooɗon . Kaŋko bee hoore maako huuwan nder meeɗen ko fottanta mo . O waɗan ɗum bee Yeesu Almasiihu . Tedduŋgal laatano Almasiihu haa abada abadin . Aamiina !
58013022	Onon deerɗiraaɓe , mi ɗon toro on : Njaɓe bolle am ɗe'e bee seyo , haa ɗe tiɗɗina ɓerɗe mooɗon . Bataakewol am ngo'ol juutaay .
58013023	Mi yiɗi anndingo on , deerɗiraawo meeɗen Timote yoofaama nder fursina . To o yottake ɗo law , mi yahdan bee maako to mi ɗo yaha laarugo on .
58013024	Koofne ardiiɓe on fuu , koofne yimɓe Allah fuu . Deerɗiraaɓe haa Italiya koofni on .
58013025	Mo''ere Allah laatano on fuu .
59001001	Bataakewol ngol iwi haa Yakuba , maccuɗo Allah e Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
59001002	Deerɗam'en , ceye masin to caɗeele feere feere keɓi on .
59001003	Ngam on anndi to nuɗɗinki mooɗon ɗon tabiti koo nder saɗeende , ɗum ɓesdan munyal .
59001004	Ammaa kakkile ngam haa on laato munyɓe haa timmoode , on laato timmuɓe ɓe ngalaa feloore nder kooɗume .
59001005	Ammaa to hikma goɗɗo mooɗon ngakki , sey o toro Allah . Kaŋko o hokkan mo ka , ngam o hokkan koomoy bee yiide , o tampataa .
59001006	Ammaa sey o toro bee nuɗɗinki , bilaa sekugo sam , ngam mo seki nandi bee ?uuge weendu ɗe hendu soggata bana yiɗi .
59001007	Taa irin goɗɗo man tammo heɓugo kooɗume haa Jawmiraawo ,
59001008	ngam o tabitaay , o anndaa ko o tammi waɗugo .
59001009	Sey laafuɗo juro to Allah ɓaŋgti mo ,
59001010	diskuɗo boo juro to Allah leesni mo . Ngam riskuɓe njinnan bana pindi ladde .
59001011	To naaŋge wuli , fuɗŋgo ɗaylan , pindi mum saaman , wooɗugo man fuu halkan . Bana non diskuɗo boo halkan yaake o ɗon suklano kuuɗe maako .
59001012	Barka laatanto koomoy munyani caɗeele , ngam to o jaalake ɗe , o heɓan ngeendam ɗam Allah wi'i hokkan yiɗɓe mo .
59001013	To goɗɗo jarribaama , taa o wi'a : " Allah jarribake yam . " Ngam Allah jarribataake bee halleende , kaŋko boo o jarribataako koomoy .
59001014	Ammaa jarraba ɗon naŋga goɗɗo to suuno maako esti mo , naŋgi mo .
59001015	To suuno man rimi , ɗum warti hakke . To hakke mawni , ɗum riman maayde .
59001016	Deerɗam'en , taa esto naŋga on !
59001017	Caahu mbooɗŋgu e dokkal timmuŋgal fuu iwi dow , ɗum iwi haa Allah , tagɗo jayli asama . O waylataako , nyiɓɓuki laatataako haa maako bana haa jayli manfa .
59001018	Nder muuyo maako o hokkiri en ngeendam bee wolde maako gooŋgaare , ngam haa joonde meeɗen ɓura joole tagle maako fuu .
59001019	Deerɗam'en yiɗaaɓe , ciftore ɗu'um : Sey koomoy fuu yaawa nanugo , ammaa taa o yaawa wolwugo , taa o yaawa tikkugo boo .
59001020	Ngam tikkanɗo huuwataa ko fotti yeeso Allah .
59001021	Ngam maajum ngudine halleende e kuuɗe kalluɗe fuu . Tuubane Allah , njaɓe wolde nde o aawata nder ɓerɗe mooɗon , ngam nde waawan hisnugo on .
59001022	Taa on numa nanugo wolde Allah tan he'i . Aa'a , sey on mbaɗa ko nde wi'i on .
59001023	Koomoy nani wolde Allah , ammaa waɗaay ko nde wi'i , kaŋko o nandi bee daarɗo ɓandu muuɗum nder daarorgal , yi'i no wa'i ,
59001024	dilli , yejjiti no wa'no .
59001025	Ammaa Allah barkiɗinan kuuɗe goɗɗo kuuwanɗo ko umroore wi'i mo , ngam o ɗon hakkilana nde , o ɗon tokko hakkilango nde tum , naa nanugo meere , law o yejjita . Kayre woni umroore timmunde , nde ɗon rimɗina yimɓe .
59001026	Woodi mo numi o goɗɗo diina na ? To o hakkilanaay ko o wolwata , diina maako laati meere , o fewani hoore maako .
59001027	Ndaa ko woni diina gooŋgaha , laaɓka haa Allah Baabiraawo : Hakkilango atiime'en e rewɓe yurumɓe nder ɓillaare maɓɓe , aynugo hoore muuɗum ngam taa haala duniyaaru nasta ɓernde mum , wonna nde .
59002001	Deerɗam'en ! Nde on laati nuɗɗinɓe Jawmiraawo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo tedduɗo , taa on cendindira yimɓe sam ngam daliila maral .
59002002	To diskuɗo nasti mooɓtorde mooɗon , ɗon ɓorni limce booɗɗe , halagaare woonde boo ɗon haa hoondu . Nden laafuɗo boo nasti , ɗon ɓorni tekkaaje .
59002003	On teddini ɓorniiɗo booɗɗe , on mbi'i mo : " Jooɗa dow koromwal . " Ammaa on mbi'i laafuɗo boo : " Dara ɗo , malla jooɗa haa lesdi . "
59002004	To on mbaɗi non , nden kam on mbaɗi aybe bee sendindirgo yimɓe . On mbaɗi haala ka bee numooji kalluɗi .
59002005	Deerɗam'en yiɗaaɓe , nananeeɗam ! Allah suɓi laafuɓe duniyaaru ngam haa ɓe ndiska nder nuɗɗinki , ɓe mara laamu ngu Allah wi'i hokkan yiɗɓe mo .
59002006	Ammaa onon on ɗon leesna laafuɓe . Kadi moy ɓillata on ? Moy yahrata on yeeso hiitooɓe ? Naa riskuɓe na ?
59002007	Kamɓe kallinta innde woonde nde Allah hokki on .
59002008	Fakat on mbaɗi booɗɗum to on ɗowtanake umroore mawnde tawaande haa deftere Allah : " Yiɗ keeddiɗɗa bana hoore ma . "
59002009	Ammaa to on cendindiri yimɓe fodde maral maɓɓe , on nasti hakke , umroore man hiitoto on ngam on njawi nde .
59002010	Ngam koo to goɗɗo ɗowtanake umrooje fuu , ammaa o ɗowtanaaki woore , o kiiteteeɗo bana luutɗo tawreeta fuu .
59002011	Ngam mo wi'i : " Taa waɗ njeenu " , o wi'i boo : " Taa mbar hoore . " Koo to a waɗaay njeenu , ammaa a waɗi mbar-hoore , a luuti tawreeta fuu .
59002012	Mbolwe , kuuwe bana hiiteteeɓe bee umrooje dimɗinooje yimɓe .
59002013	Ngam to goɗɗo walaa enɗam , Allah hiitoto mo bilaa enɗam . Ammaa enɗam jaaloto kiita .
59002014	Deerɗam'en ! Ɗume ɗum nafata to goɗɗo wi'i : " Mi woodi nuɗɗinki " , ammaa kuuɗe maako ngooŋɗinaay ɗum ? Nuɗɗinki man hisnan mo na ?
59002015	To woodi deerɗiraaɓe ɓe ngalaa limce , ɓe ngalaa nyaamdu ,
59002016	to a wi'i ɓe : " Allah barkiɗina on ! Kolte , nyaame , kaare . " Ko ɗum nafata to a hokkaay ɓe kooɗume ngam haaje maɓɓe ?
59002017	Non nuɗɗinki boo laati , to ki hawtaay bee kuuɗe , ki nafataa .
59002018	Ammaa to goɗɗo wi'i : " An a woodi nuɗɗinki , min boo mi woodi kuuɗe " , mi jaaboto : " Hollam nuɗɗinki bilaa kuuɗe , min boo mi holle nuɗɗinki am bee kuuɗe . "
59002019	A nuɗɗini Allah o gooto na ? Booɗɗum ! Ginnaaji boo nuɗɗini , ammaa ɗi ɗon ndiwna ngam kulol .
59002020	Paataaɗo ! A yiɗi holleego nuɗɗinki bilaa kuuɗe nafataa sam na ?
59002021	Noy kaaka meeɗen Ibrahiima heɓri yerduye Allah ? Bee kuuɗe o heɓi ɗum , nde o yahri Isiyaaku haa hirsirde .
59002022	A faamataa na ? Nuɗɗinki maako hawti bee kuuɗe maako . Ki laati timmuki ngam kuuɗe maako .
59002023	Bana non ko deftere Allah wi'no gooŋɗiri : " Ibrahiima nuɗɗini Allah , Allah boo limani mo ɗum gooŋgaaku . " Allah ewni mo soobaajo muuɗum .
59002024	Kadi na on paami , neɗɗo heɓan yerduye Allah bee kuuɗe , naa bee nuɗɗinki tan .
59002025	Non boo Rahab , daakaareejo . O heɓi yerduye Allah ngam kuuɗe maako , nde o jaɓɓi nelaaɓe Yahuudu'en , o walli ɓe wurtaago bee laawol feere .
59002026	Bana no ɓandu bilaa yoŋki walaa nafuda , non nuɗɗinki bilaa kuuɗe nafataa sam .
59003001	Deerɗam'en ! Taa ɗuuɗɓe mooɗon laato anndinooɓe , ngam on anndi minin anndinooɓe , kiita boofi amin ɓuran kiita luttuɓe fuu saatugo .
59003002	En fuu en ɗon mboofa tum . Mo woofataa nder bolle muuɗum , kaŋko woni timmuɗo , baawɗo naŋgtugo ɓandu fuu .
59003003	En ɗon nastina laɓaŋge haa kunduɗe pucci ngam ɗi ɗowtano en , bana ni en keɓan yahrugo ɗi haa en ngiɗi fuu .
59003004	Nume boo haala koombowal . No ngal mawniri fuu , no hendu yahrata ngal fuu , laanyoowo ɗon laanya ngal bee laanyirgel peetel , ɗon yahra ngal haa yiɗi fuu .
59003005	Non boo ɗemŋgal . No ngal famɗiri fuu , ngal ɗon juroro wolwugo haalaaji mawɗi .
59003006	Ɗemŋgal boo bana yiite . Ngal mooɓi halleende fuu , ngal jooɗi nder ɓandu , ngal ɗon saŋkita halleende haa ɓandu fuu . Bee yiite iwŋge haa jahannama ngal jamnan balɗe meeɗen fuu , diga danyeeki haa yotto maayde .
59003007	Neɗɗo waawi eltugo tagle fuu : kuuje ladde e colli e ladooji e liɗɗi fuu .
59003008	Ammaa walaa meeɗɗo eltugo ɗemŋgal . Ngal halli , ngal eltataake , ngal heewi tooke barooje .
59003009	Bee maagal en ɗon ngetta Jawmiraawo meeɗen e Baabiraawo meeɗen , bee maagal boo en ɗon kuɗa yimɓe , tagaaɓe dow nandal bee Allah .
59003010	Bolle gettooje e bolle kuɗooje haa hunduko wooto ngurtoto . Deerɗam'en , kanjum ɗum haanaay sam .
59003011	Walaa seeɓoore ɓulata ndiyam mbelɗam e ndiyam kaaɗɗam haa ɓuldude woore .
59003012	Deerɗam'en , ibbi rimataa ngalbiije , inabohi boo rimataa ibbe , non boo ndiyam kaaɗɗam laatataako mbelɗam .
59003013	Woodi hikmaajo , marɗo faamu caka mooɗon na ? Sey o waŋgina ɗum bee joonde woonde , bee huuwugo kuuɗe booɗɗe bee yaŋkinaare e hikma .
59003014	Ammaa to on ngoodi kaajal caatuŋgal e jokkirgol nder ɓerɗe mooɗon , nden kam taa on mawnito , taa on pewa , on luuta gooŋga .
59003015	Irin hikma ka'a iwaay haa dow , ka iwi haa duniyaaru , ka iwi haa ɗabiya neɗɗo , ka iwi haa Sayɗaanu .
59003016	Ngam haa kaajal e jokkirgol ngoni , ton sooynde narral e halleende fuu ngoni boo .
59003017	Ammaa hikma iwka haa dow laaɓi saray . Kadiboo ka ɗon wadda jam e neɗɗaaku e soobaaku , ka heewi enɗam , ka riman kuuɗe booɗɗe , ka sendindirtaa yimɓe , ka waɗataa tufle .
59003018	Narrinooɓe yimɓe ɗon mbaɗa jam , nafuda maɓɓe ɗum kuuɗe ɗe Allah yerdoto .
59004001	Haa toy kaɓe e jokkirli caka mooɗon iwata ? Ɗum iwi haa suunooji mooɗon kaɓanɗi nder ɓalli mooɗon foroy .
59004002	On ngiɗi heɓugo kuuje goɗɗe , ammaa on keɓataa ɗe , ngam maajum on taaski mbarugo woɗɓe , on ɗon kaaja boo . On ɗon ɗaɓɓa kuuje , ammaa on keɓataa ɗe , ngam maajum on ɗon njokkira , on ɗon kaɓa . On keɓaay ko on ngiɗi , ngam on toraaki ɗum haa Allah .
59004003	Koo to on ɗon toro mo , on keɓataa ngam numooji mooɗon kalli , on ɗon toro ngam seynugo ɓalli mooɗon .
59004004	Onon tuurtanooɓe Allah ! On anndaa soobaaku bee duniyaaru ɗum konnaagu bee Allah na ? To on coobri bee duniyaaru , nden kam on laati konne'en Allah .
59004005	Taa nume ko deftere wolwi ɗum meere , nde wi'i : " Hakkiilo ngo o hokki en haaji masin . "
59004006	Ammaa mo''ere nde Allah mo''ani en , ɓuri mawnugo . Ngam deftere wi'i : " Allah ɗon leesna mawnitiiɓe , ammaa o ɗon mo''ana leesɓe . "
59004007	Ngam maajum tuubane Allah . To on ndartake Sayɗaanu , o doggan on .
59004008	Ɓadite Allah , kaŋko boo o ɓadititto on . Laɓɓine juuɗe mooɗon , onon marɓe hakke . Laɓɓine ɓerɗe mooɗon , onon naafiki'en .
59004009	Cune , ngooke , mboye . Jaleeɗe mooɗon laato bojji , seyo mooɗon laato suno .
59004010	Leestine ko'e mooɗon yeeso Jawmiraawo , nden kam o ɓaŋgtan on .
59004011	Deerɗam'en , taa on mbolwa kalluka dow deerɗiraaɓe . Koomoy wolwi kalluka dow deerɗum , malla hiiti mo , wolwi kalluka dow tawreeta , hiiti ka . To a hiiti tawreeta , a laataaki ɗowtaniiɗo ka , ammaa a laati kiitoowo ka .
59004012	Allah feere muuɗum hokki en tawreeta , kaŋko hiitoto ka ngam kaŋko feere maako mari baawɗe hisnugo malla halkugo . An a moy , haa a hiito deerɗiraawo ?
59004013	Nananeeɗam , onon wi'anɓe : " Hande malla jaŋgo min ndillan haa wuro kaja , min nduuma ton , min mbaɗa filu , min nyaama riba ɗuuɗka . "
59004014	On anndaa ko waɗata jaŋgo . Ngam on laati bana cuurɗe pamare , ɗe mbaŋgi seɗɗa , law ɗe majji .
59004015	Haani on mbi'a : " To Allah muuyi , to o yahri yoŋki , min mbaɗan ni bee ni . "
59004016	Ammaa jonta on ɗon mawnito , on ɗon njuro . Irin juro ngo'o wooɗaay .
59004017	Koomoy anndi huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga , huuwaay ɗum , waɗi aybe .
59005001	Nananeeɗam jonta , onon riskuɓe ! Mboye , ngooke ngam boneeji tammiiɗi warugo dow mooɗon .
59005002	Jawdi mooɗon nyoli , moo?u nyaami limseeji mooɗon .
59005003	Kaŋgeeri e cardi mooɗon fuuni . Ɗum laatoto seedamku dow mooɗon , ɗum nyaaman ɓalli mooɗon bana yiite . On mbaagi jawdi nder balɗe ragareeje ɗe'e .
59005004	On njoɓaay ngeenaari huuwooɓe gese mooɗon . Nane bojji maɓɓe ! Bojji sodooɓe ?aamle mooɗon njottake haa Allah Jawmiraawo , baawɗo kooɗume .
59005005	Joonde mooɗon haa duniyaaru ndu'u heewi neeminaare e pijirle . On payni ko'e mooɗon ngam nyalaade kirsol .
59005006	On kiiti mo walaa aybe , on mbari mo . Kaŋko o dartanaaki on .
59005007	Deerɗam'en , munye haa to Jawmiraawo wari . Ndaare no demoowo munyrata , o ɗon reena haa gese maako ɓenda booɗɗum . O ɗon reena iyeende arande e ɓaawoore .
59005008	Onon boo , sey munyon ! Taa come , ngam nyande garki Jawmiraawo ɓadake .
59005009	Deerɗam'en , taa ngullotire , ngam taa Allah hiito on . Kiitoowo ɗon dari haa dammugal , yiɗi nastugo .
59005010	Deerɗam'en , ciftore annabo'en wolwuɓe bee innde Jawmiraawo . Munye nder bone bana kamɓe boo ɓe munyiri .
59005011	En ɗon mbi'a ɓe barkiɗinaaɓe ngam ɓe accaay munyugo . On nani haala munyal Ayuba , on anndi boo no Allah humtiri haaje maako haa ragare . Ngam Jawmiraawo o keewɗo enɗam e mbooɗeeŋga .
59005012	Deerɗam'en , taa kune sam , to on mbi'i on mbaɗanan goɗɗo huunde feere . Taa kunore bee asama , taa kunore bee lesdi , taa kunore bee kooɗume . Wi'ugo " ooho " malla " aa'a " he'i , taa ɓura non ngam taa Allah hiito on .
59005013	Woodi jaroowo bone caka mooɗon na ? O waɗa do'a . Woodi ceyiiɗo na ? O yima gime gettooje .
59005014	Woodi nyawɗo caka mooɗon na ? O ewno dawrooɓe jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe . Ɓe toro Allah ngam maako , ɓe moytira mo nebbam bee innde Jawmiraawo .
59005015	Tornde nde'e , to hawti bee nuɗɗinki , hisnan nyawɗo . Jawmiraawo yamɗitinan mo , yaafanto mo hakkeeji ɗi o waɗno .
59005016	Mbaŋgine hakkeeji mooɗon hakkunde mooɗon , tore Allah ngam koomoy mooɗon , ngam haa on njamɗita . Tornde gooŋgaajo woodi baawɗe , nafan masin .
59005017	Eliya o goɗɗo bana meeɗen . O tori Allah bee tiinaare ngam taa iyeende toɓa . Duuɓi tati bee reeta nde toɓaay .
59005018	O tori mo fahin , asama yoofi iyeende , lesdi waɗi ?aamnde .
59005019	Deerɗam'en ! To gooto mooɗon seli laawol gooŋga , sey goɗɗo lorna mo .
59005020	Ciftore ɗu'um : Koomoy lorni marɗo hakke diga laabi kalluɗi , hisni yoŋki marɗo hakke oo , suddan hakkeeji ɗuuɗɗi .
60001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Piyer , nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu , yahugo haa suɓaaɓe Allah , laatiiɓe jananɓe saŋkitiiɓe haa lesɗe Pontus e Galaatiya e Kappadosiya e Asiya e Bitiniya .
60001002	On laati suɓaaɓe ngam daliila muuyo Allah Baabiraawo . Ruuhu maako seni on , haa on ɗowtano Yeesu Almasiihu , haa ?i?am maako laɓɓina on .
60001003	Ngetten Allah , Baabiraawo Jawmiraawo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu ! O enɗi en , o hokki en ngeendam kesam bee ummitingo Yeesu Almasiihu diga maayde . Ɗum hebbini ɓerɗe meeɗen bee tammunde gooŋgaare .
60001004	En ɗon tammo heɓugo barkaaji Allah mawɗi ɗi o sigani yimɓe maako . O sigani on ɗi haa asama . Ton ɗi nyolataa , ɗi mbonnataako , ɗi ustataako boo .
60001005	On ɗon nuɗɗini mo . Ngam maajum o ɗon ayna on bee baawɗe maako . Nder balɗe ragareeje on keɓan kisndam taaskitinaaɗam diga jonta .
60001006	Ceyore ɗum , koo to boneeji feere-feereeji keɓanɗi on jonta ɗon cuna on seɗɗa .
60001007	Boneeji man poondan nuɗɗinki mooɗon , to ki gooŋgahi . Koo kaŋgeeri maa , wonnoto , ammaa ɓe ɗon poonda ndi bee yiite . Sakko nuɗɗinki mooɗon , ki ɓuri kaŋgeeri saman piw , sey ki foonde ngam taa ki jinna . Ɓaawo poondol man , on keɓan gettooje e tedduŋgal e maŋgu , nyande Yeesu Almasiihu waŋganta yimɓe fuu .
60001008	Koo nde on ngi'aay mo , on ngiɗi mo . Koo nde on ngi'ataa mo jonta , on nuɗɗini mo . Ngam maajum on ɗon ceyo bee seyo tedduŋgo , ɗuuɗŋgo , ngo ɓuri wolweego ,
60001009	ngam on keɓan ko on tammoto nder nuɗɗinki mooɗon , kanjum woni kisndam yoŋkiiji mooɗon .
60001010	Annabo'en mbaɗi annabaaku dow barkaaji ɗi Allah tammi hokkugo on , ngam Ruuhu Allah wondi bee maɓɓe , holli ɓe Almasiihu tammi yarugo bone , ɓaawoɗon o tammi heɓugo tedduŋgal . Annabo'en go tefi haala ka , linyi ka bee hakkiilo ngam ɓe keɓta ndey ka waɗata , e noy ka laatorto .
60001011	
60001012	Allah waŋginani ɓe kubaruwol ngo'ol , ngol laataaki ngam ko'e maɓɓe , ammaa o halfinani ɓe ngol ngam mooɗon . Nelaaɓe waajinɓe on linjiila ngecci on gooŋgaaji ɗi'i . Ɓe ngaaji on ɗi bee baawɗe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo iwŋgu haa asama . Malaa'ika'en maa , ngiɗi faamugo haala ka .
60001013	Ngam maajum , sey numooji mooɗon taaskano kuugal ! Kakkile , njo''ine tammunde mooɗon fuu haa barka ka keɓoton saa'i Yeesu Almasiihu waŋgi .
60001014	Ɗowtane Allah , taa tokke suunooji mooɗon ɗi tokkinooɗon yaake on anndaa gooŋga .
60001015	Ammaa bana Allah ewniiɗo on o Ceniiɗo , laate onon boo on seniiɓe nder ko mbaɗoton fuu .
60001016	Ngam Allah wi'i : " Laate seniiɓe ngam min mi Ceniiɗo . "
60001017	To on ɗon mbaɗa do'a , on ɗon ewno Allah , Baabiraawo . To o ɗon hiito yimɓe , o sendindirtaa ɓe , ammaa o ɗon hiito ɓe deydey kuuɗe maɓɓe . Ngam maajum timmine balɗe ngeendam mooɗon luttuɗe haa duniyaaru bee ɗowtanaago mo .
60001018	Ngam on anndi saman ko coottiraaɗon ngam taa on njooɗo bilaa tammunde bana kaakaaji mooɗon . Saman coottaari mooɗon ustataako bana saman kaŋgeeri malla cardi .
60001019	Ammaa on keɓi ndimu bee ?i?am caɗɗam ɗam Almasiihu , mo laati bana jawgel laaɓŋgel ngel walaa aybefa .
60001020	Allah suɓi mo diga duniyaaru tagaaka tawon , o waŋgini mo haa mooɗon nder balɗe ragareeje ɗe'e .
60001021	Ngam barka maako on nuɗɗini Allah mo ummitini mo diga maayde , teddini mo . Bana non nuɗɗinki mooɗon e tammunde mooɗon haa Allah tabitirta .
60001022	Jonta nde on ceni ko'e mooɗon bee ɗowtanaago gooŋga , on ngiɗi deerɗiraaɓe nder nuɗɗinki . Ngam maajum ngiɗindire bee ɓerɗe laaɓɗe , bilaa naafikaare .
60001023	Ngam on laati danyaaɓe hesɓe bee wolde Allah yeere nde timmataa . On danyaaɓe haa Baabiraawo mo maayataa .
60001024	Bana ko winda :
60001025	Ammaa wolde Jawmiraawo re'ataa . "
60002001	Ngam maajum ngudine halleende fuu : Fewre , tufle , kaajal bee kuudi fuu !
60002002	Bana no ɓikkoy keccoy ngiɗiri kosam tum , onon boo ngiɗe wolde Allah gooŋgaare bana non , haa on mawna bee maare , on kisa .
60002003	Ngam bana deftere wi'i : " On metti mbooɗeeŋga Jawmiraawo . "
60002004	Ngare haa maako . O laati hayre yeere nde yimɓe meeriɗini , ammaa nde Allah suɓi ngam ɗuuɗugo saman maare .
60002005	Ngare , laate kaa'e geete , mahruɗe haykaliiru Ruuhu Ceniiɗo . Acce Yeesu Almasiihu hokka on baawɗe laataago liman'en seniiɓe lii'anooɓe Allah sadakaaji pottananɗi mo .
60002006	Ngam deftere wi'i :
60002007	Hayre nde'e mari saman ɗuuɗɗo haa onon nuɗɗinɓe , ammaa haa sooyɓe nuɗɗinki :
60002008	Fahin deftere feere wi'i :
60002009	Ammaa onon ngoni asŋgol cuɓaaŋgol , liman'en laamiiɗo , yimɓe seniiɓe , halal Allah mo wurtini on nyiɓre , yahri on haa annoora maako kayɗiniika , suɓi on haa on ngaajina kuuɗe maako booɗɗe .
60002010	Naane on laataaki yimɓe Allah , ammaa jonta on laati yimɓe maako . Naane on anndaa enɗam Allah , ammaa jonta on njaɓi enɗam maako .
60002011	Soobiraaɓe am , on laati hoɗɓe e jananɓe haa duniyaaru ndu . Ngam maajum mi tori on taa on accana suunooji ɓandu laawol , ngam tum ɗi ɗon ɗaɓɓa halkugo yoŋkiiji mooɗon .
60002012	Sey joonde mooɗon caka heefeerɓe wooɗa masin , ngam koo to ɓe ngulli on bee wi'ugo on halluɓe , doole ɓe anndita kuuɗe mooɗon booɗɗe , ɓe teddina Allah nyande garki maako .
60002013	Ngam daliila Jawmiraawo , ɗowtane mawɓe duniyaaru . Ɗowtane mawɗo lesdi ngam o ɓuri luttuɓe maŋgu .
60002014	Ɗowtane ngomna'en , ngam ɓe nelaaɓe mawɗo lesdi haa ɓe kiito halluɓe , ɓe teddina wooɗɓe .
60002015	Ngam ndaa ko woni muuyo Allah : Bee kuuɗe booɗɗe ɗe on kuuwata , on nje''ina faataaɓe wolwanɓe bolle meereeje .
60002016	Bee Yeesu Almasiihu on keɓi ndimu . Taa cudde halleende koondeye bee ndimu ngu , ammaa laate maccuɓe Allah .
60002017	Teddine yimɓe fuu , ngiɗe deerɗiraaɓe nuɗɗinɓe , kule Allah , teddine mawɗo lesdi .
60002018	Onon huuwooɓe , ɗowtane jaagorɓe mooɗon , on teddina ɓe . Taa mbaɗe ɗum haa wooɗɓe e ɗelma-gikku'en tan , ammaa koo haa saatuɓe boo .
60002019	Ɗum booɗɗum to on munyi naawɗum bone ko ukkanto on meere ngam daliila Allah .
60002020	Ɗume munyal mooɗon nafata to on munyi piyɗe ɗe ɓe piyi on ngam aybeeji mooɗon ? Ammaa to on munyi boneeji ɗi on njari ngam huuwugo gooŋga , Allah barkiɗinan on .
60002021	Ngam irin man Allah ewni on . Ngam Almasiihu bee hoore mum yari bone ngam mooɗon , o holli on laawol yarugo bone ngam haa on tokko mo .
60002022	O meeɗaay waɗugo hakke , walaa meeɗɗo nanugo fewre haa hunduko maako .
60002023	Nde ɓe kuɗi mo o huutaaki , nde o yari bone , o jeeɗi , ammaa o jo''ini tammunde maako haa Allah , kiitoowo gooŋgaajo .
60002024	Almasiihu bee hoore muuɗum roondi hakkeeji meeɗen haa ɓandu muuɗum dow leggal gaafaaŋgal , ngam haa en laato maayɓe hedi hakke , ammaa yeeɗɓe hedi mbooɗeeŋga .
60002025	On laatino bana baali majjuɗi , ammaa jonta Allah lorni on ngam haa on tokko gaynaako aynoowo yoŋkiiji mooɗon .
60003001	Bana non boo onon rewɓe , ɗowtane worɓe mooɗon . Ngam to woɗɓe maɓɓe nuɗɗinaay wolde Allah , ɗowtaare mooɗon yahran ɓe haa nuɗɗinki . Ɗum waɗan koo to on mbolwaay koo tis ,
60003002	ngam ɓe ndaaran no joonde mooɗon laaɓrata , no on cujidiranta Allah bee gooŋga .
60003003	Taa kuuwtinire pawne ngam wo''ingo ɓalli mooɗon , bee moorugo gaasa , koo bee pawne jamɗe caɗɗe coggu , koo bee ɓornuce booɗɗe .
60003004	Ndikka wooɗugo mooɗon iwa diga nder ɓerɗe mooɗon , waato hakkiilo de'iiŋgo ngo jinnataa , ɗum mari saman masin haa yeeso Allah .
60003005	Bana ni rewɓe seniiɓe ɓooyma laatiniri ko'e maɓɓe ɓe wooɗɓe , ɓe jo''ini tammunde maɓɓe haa Allah . Ɓe ɗowtaniiɓe worɓe maɓɓe .
60003006	Saratu waɗi ɗum , o ɗowtani Ibrahiima , o ewni mo jaagorɗo maako . Onon ngoni ɓikkoy maako to on kuuwi mbooɗeeŋga , to on kulaay kooɗume .
60003007	Onon worɓe boo : Anndite no sembe rewɓe yottaaki sembe mooɗon , sey on teddina ɓe , ngam kamɓe boo Allah hokkan ɓe ngeendam bana o hokkata on ɗam . Mbaɗe ɗum ngam taa kooɗume haɗa do'aaji mooɗon .
60003008	Dow ko mi wolwi fuu , mi wi'i fahin : Sey on fuu on mara numo wooto , njurmindire , ngiɗindire bana deerɗiraaɓe , mballindire , taa kolle deerɗiraaɓe maŋgu .
60003009	Taa lorne halleende bee halleende , malla kuudi bee kuudi . Ndikka on mbarkiɗina , ngam nde Allah ewni on o wi'i o barkiɗinan on .
60003010	Bana deftere wi'i :
60003011	o acca halleende , o waɗa mbooɗeeŋga ,
60003012	Ngam Jawmiraawo ɗon hakkilana gooŋga'en ,
60003013	Moy waɗata on halleende to on tiini waɗugo mbooɗeeŋga ?
60003014	Ammaa koo to on njari bone ngam huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga , on ceyoto masin . Taa kule yimɓe , taa hakkiilooji mooɗon njiiɓo .
60003015	Ammaa teddine Almasiihu nder ɓerɗe mooɗon , o laato Jawmiraawo mooɗon . Laate taaskiiɓe koondey haa on mbaawa jaabaago koomoy to ?ami on haala tammunde mooɗon .
60003016	Ammaa njaabe ?amɓe on bee yaŋkinaare e teddingo . Numooji ɓerɗe mooɗon laato laaɓɗi , ngam to ɓe kuɗi on , ɓe mbolwi kalluka dow joonde mooɗon woonde nder kawtal bee Almasiihu , ɓe cemtan .
60003017	To ɗum laatake muuyo Allah , ndikka yarugo bone ngam kuuɗe booɗɗe dow yarugo bone ngam kuuɗe kalluɗe .
60003018	Ngam Almasiihu bee hoore muuɗum maayi nde woore ngam hakkeeji yimɓe , nafuda man jinnataa haa foroy . O walaa hakke , ammaa o maayi ngam marɓe hakke , ngam o yahra on haa Allah . Yimɓe mbari mo , ammaa Ruuhu Ceniiɗo yeeɗitini mo .
60003019	Bee baawɗe Ruuhu ngu , o jippi haa yoŋkiiji maɓɓaaɗi , o waajini ɗi .
60003020	Waato yoŋkiiji ɗi ɗowtanaakino Allah , koo nde o holli ɓe munyal nder jamanu Nuuhu , yaake Nuuhu ɗonno seha koombowal . Yimɓe njoweetato tan nasti koombowal man , kisi ndiyam .
60003021	Ndiyam ɗa'am laati misaalu sappingo on ngiiwam baptisma , ɗam ɗon hisna on naa bee lootugo tuundi ɓandu , ammaa bee waɗango Allah alkawal bee numo ɓernde laaɓŋgo . Ngiiwam baptisma hisni on bee ummitineeki Yeesu Almasiihu
60003022	mo eeŋgi haa asama , jooɗi haa nyaamo Allah . O ɗon laamano malaa'ika'en , e mawɓe e baawɗeeji asama fuu .
60004001	On anndi Almasiihu yari bone nder ɓandu muuɗum . Cembiɗine ko'e mooɗon bee numo bana ngo Almasiihu , ngam koomoy to ɗon yara bone , faalataa hakkeeji .
60004002	Diga jonta , haa luttuɗum balɗe mooɗon haa duniyaaru , sey on njooɗo nder muuyo Allah , naa nder suunooji ɓandu .
60004003	Joonde nde on njooɗino nder ko heefeerɓe kuuwata , he'i . On njooɗino nder halleende , suunooji , nguyka , pijirle kalluɗe , on cujidanino labbi karminaaɗi .
60004004	Jonta heefeerɓe ɗon kayɗina ngam on kawtataa bee maɓɓe nder joonde maɓɓe hallunde e pijirle maɓɓe kalluɗe . Ngam maajum ɓe nasti huɗugo on .
60004005	Ammaa sey ɓe njaabo Allah , taaskiiɗo hiitaago yeeɗɓe e maayɓe .
60004006	Kanjum waɗi Almasiihu waajini maayɓe boo kubaruwol ceynoowol , waato haa hiitaaɓeno nder ɓandu bana yimɓe fuu kiitorte . O waajini ɓe ngol ngam haa Ruuhu Ceniiɗo hokka ɓe baawɗe jooɗaago jam bana Allah jooɗori .
60004007	Kuuje fuu ɓadake timmugo . Naŋgte ko'e mooɗon , kakkile haa on mbaawa waɗugo do'a .
60004008	Ko ɓuri fuu , ngiɗindire bee yiide gooŋgaare , ngam yiide suddan hakkeeji ɗuuɗɗi .
60004009	Ewnindire haa ci'e mooɗon bee seyo .
60004010	Koomoy mooɗon hakkilana dokkal ngal Allah hokki mo , woonana woɗɓe bee man . Bana ni on laatorto aynooɓe dokke Allah feere feere , wooɗɓe .
60004011	Koomoy waaji , sey o waajo wolde Allah . Koomoy huuwani goɗɗo , sey o huuwana mo bee sembe ɗe Allah hokkata mo . Nder ko en mbaɗata fuu , sey en teddina Allah bee Yeesu Almasiihu . Kaŋko jeyi tedduŋgal e baawɗe haa foroy ! Aamiina .
60004012	Soobiraaɓe am , taa kayɗine boneeji ɗi on njarata , bana ɗi kayɗiniiɗi .
60004013	Ndikka seyaago ngam on ɗon kawta nder bone Almasiihu ngam haa on keewa seyo yaake tedduŋgal maako waŋgi .
60004014	On laatake barkiɗinaaɓe to ɓe kuɗi on ngam on tokki Almasiihu , ngam ɗum waŋgini Ruuhu Allah tedduŋgu jippi haa mooɗon .
60004015	Taa gooto mooɗon yara bone ngam o laati mbaroowo hoore , malla gujjo , malla pasoowo , malla naatalmaajo .
60004016	Ammaa to on njari bone ngam on tokki Almasiihu , taa cemte ɗum . Sey on ngetta Allah ngam on njogi innde Almasiihu .
60004017	Wakkati kiita yottake , Allah boo aartan hiitaago yimɓe muuɗum . To ka fuɗɗi haa meeɗen , noy ɗum laatorto haa ɓe njaɓaay kubaruwol ceynoowol ngol Allah ?
60004018	Bana no deftere wi'i :
60004019	Ngam maajum , koomoy yari bone ngam Allah muuyani mo ɗum , taa o acca huuwugo mbooɗeeŋga , ammaa o hoolo tagɗo mo , mo yoofataa mo sam .
60005001	Jonta , mi ɗon toro dawrooɓe jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe wonɓe caka mooɗon . Min boo mi dawroowo bana mooɗon , mi seedi boneeji ɗi Almasiihu yari , mi nastan tedduŋgal ngal Allah tammi waŋginango en . Mi ɗon toro on :
60005002	Ayne tokkere nde Allah hokki on , ayne nde bee yiide bana no Allah yiɗi , naa bee doole . Kuuwe , naa ngam heɓugo ceede meere , ammaa ngam on ngiɗi ɗum .
60005003	Taa laamane yimɓe ɓe Allah hokki on , ammaa laatane ɓe misaalu haa ɓe tokko on .
60005004	To gaynaako mawɗo waŋgi , on keɓan meetaleewol marŋgol tedduŋgal ngal jinnataa .
60005005	Onon derke'en boo , ɗowtane mawɓe bana non . On fuu , laate yaŋkiniiɓe , mballindire ngam deftere wi'i :
60005006	Ngam maajum njaŋkine ko'e mooɗon haa Allah baawɗo , haa o ɓaŋgta on yaake o yiɗi .
60005007	Ndokke mo numooji mooɗon fuu , ngam o ɗon hakkilana on .
60005008	Kakkile , ayne ! Ngam konneejo mooɗon , waato Iblisa , ɗon halli bana mbarooga mbeelaaŋga tefanŋga mo o nyaama .
60005009	Tabite nder nuɗɗinki mooɗon , kaɓe bee maako ngam on anndi yimɓe nuɗɗinɓe bana mooɗon nder duniyaaru fuu ɗon njara bone bana ni .
60005010	Ammaa to on njari bone wakkati seɗɗa , marɗo mo''ere fuu , waato Allah bee hoore muuɗum laatinan on on timmuɓe . O darnan on , o sembiɗinan on , haa on ndaro booɗɗum bana dow tapaare . Nder Yeesu Almasiihu , o ɗon ewno on haa on kawta bee maako nder tedduŋgal maako duumiiŋgal .
60005011	Baawɗe laatano mo haa foroy ! Aamiina .
60005012	Silas mo kooliimi ɗum bana deerɗiraawo gooŋgaajo , walli yam windango on bataakewol ngol . Mi yiɗi sembiɗingo on , mi yiɗi seedaago on mo''ere nde laati mo''ere Allah fakat . Tabite nder maare .
60005013	Jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe haa Baabila nde Allah suɓi bana o suɓiri on , hoofni on . Ɓiŋgel am Markus boo hoofni on .
60005014	Koofnindire booɗɗum bana deerɗiraaɓe .
61001001	Bataakewol ngo'ol iwi haa Simon Piyer , maccuɗo e nelaaɗo Yeesu Almasiihu , yahugo haa heɓɓe nuɗɗinki booɗki bana ki amin . On keɓi ki bee yerduye Allah meeɗen e bee Yeesu Almasiihu .
61001002	Mo''ere e jam ɗuuɗana on bee anndugo Allah e Yeesu , Jawmiraawo meeɗen .
61001003	Allah hokki en baawɗe maako mawɗe ngam taa kooɗume tampana en haa joonde meeɗen nder nuɗɗinki . O hokkiri en ɗe bee anndugo mo , nde o ewni en haa en kawta bee maako nder tedduŋgal e mbooɗeeŋga maako .
61001004	Bana ni ko o wi'i o hokkan en , laatani en huunde mawnde , woonde masin . To on njaɓi ko o wi'i on , on kisan suunooji kalkooji gonɗi nder duniyaaru , on keɓan nastugo ɗabiya Allah .
61001005	Ngam maajum , ɗaɓɓite ngam haa nuɗɗinki mooɗon waŋgina mbooɗeeŋga e anndal e
61001006	naŋgtaare e tiinaare e ɗowtanaago Allah ,
61001007	yiide deerɗiraaɓe e yiide Allah .
61001008	Haani on mara ɗum . To ɗum ɗuuɗi haa mooɗon , ɗum laatinan on tiiɗɓe haa on njaha yeeso bee anndugo Jawmiraawo men Yeesu Almasiihu .
61001009	Koomoy mo walaa ɗum , yi'ataa daayiiɗum , laati bana bumɗo , yejjiti hakkeeji muuɗum lootanooma .
61001010	Ngam maajum , deerɗam'en , njoge ewnaandu Allah e cuɓki muuɗum bee sembe . To on mbaɗi non , on nastataa halleende .
61001011	Bana non on keɓan baawɗe nastugo laamu nduumiiŋgu ngu Jawmiraawo e Kisnoowo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu .
61001012	Ngam maajum , tum mi ɗon siftinora on haala ka , koo to on anndi ka , koo to on ndari bee sembe nder gooŋga ka on njaɓi .
61001013	Ammaa mi numi ɗum haani mi findina on bee ciftinorki ki nde mi ɗon bee yoŋki tawon .
61001014	Ngam mi anndi yeeso seɗɗa mi accan ɓandu nyolooru ndu , bana Jawmiraawo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu yecci yam bee laaɓɗum .
61001015	Ngam maajum mi haɓdan waɗugo ko mi waawi fuu ngam on ciftora haala ka ɓaawo maayde am .
61001016	Naa bee taarihaaji yimɓe min anndiniri on garki Yeesu Almasiihu bee baawɗe . Ammaa bee gite amin min ngi'i maŋgu maako !
61001017	Min ɗonno ton yaake Allah Baabiraawo hokki mo tedduŋgal e maŋgu . Allah marɗo tedduŋgal maŋgal wi'no mo : " Kaŋko woni Ɓiɗɗo am giɗaaɗo , mo mi seyorto . "
61001018	Minin bee noppi amin min nani sawtu man iwi haa asama nde min ɗonno bee maako haa hooseere seniinde .
61001019	Ɗum hokki min sembe nuɗɗingo habaru annabo'en . Sey on kakkilana ɗum , ngam ɗum laati bana pittirla njaynanka nder nyiɓre haa nyalawma waɗa , haa jayŋgol horre fajiri yayna nder ɓerɗe mooɗon .
61001020	Ammaa nume ɗu'um : Walaa baawɗo faamtingo annabaaku ko woni nder defte bee hoore muuɗum .
61001021	Ngam walaa annabaaku iwŋgu haa muuyo neɗɗo . Ammaa Ruuhu Ceniiŋgu nasti hakkiilo annabo'en haa ɓe mbolwi ko Allah wi'i ɓe .
61002001	Bana no annabo'en fewooɓe ngardi caka yimɓe naane , non jaŋginooɓe fewooɓe boo ngardata caka mooɗon . Ɓe ngaddan anndinol fewre , kalkoowol , ɓe ngeddan Jawmiraawo mo hisni ɓe . Ngam maajum halkere heɓan ɓe .
61002002	Koo non , ɗuuɗɓe tokkoto laabi maɓɓe kalluɗi . Ngam daliila kuuɗe maɓɓe , yimɓe kallinan laawol gooŋga .
61002003	Jaŋginooɓe fewooɓe ɓe'e ɓe ɗon cuuna ceede haa ɓe pewana on bee habaruuji meereeji ngam nyaamugo riba . Diga naane , kiitoowo ɓe taaskake , kalkoowo ɓe ɗaanataako !
61002004	Koo malaa'ika'en waɗɓe hakke maa , Allah sakkini ɓe haa yiite jahannama . Ɓe kaɓɓaama ton bee callalluuji , ɓe ɗon ndeena nyande kiita .
61002005	Allah hisnaay duniyaaru naane , ammaa o waddi ilam tuufaana dow duniyaaru halluɓe . Sey Nuuhu , gaajoowo gooŋgaaku tan hisi , bee yimɓe muuɗum njoweeɗiɗo .
61002006	Allah hiiti wuro Sodoma e wuro Gomorra , o halki ɗe bee yiite ngam halluɓe fuu ndaara ko tammi heɓugo ɓe .
61002007	O hisni Ludu , goɗɗo booɗɗo . Nder jamanu Ludu , halluɓe njarni mo bone bee joonde maɓɓe hallunde .
61002008	Ngam booɗɗo oo o jooɗi caka maɓɓe , o yi'i , o nani halleende maɓɓe , ɗum torri ɓernde maako masin .
61002009	Jawmiraawo anndi no hisnirta tokkiiɓe mo diga torra maɓɓe . O anndi boo no o aynirta halluɓe ngam haa o hiito ɓe nyande kiita ,
61002010	sakkonta tokkiiɓe suunooji ɓandu kalluɗi , yawiiɓe maŋgu Allah .
61002011	Koo malaa'ika'en ɓuranɓe ɓe maŋgu e baawɗe maa , ngullataako mawɓe asama bee kuudi yeeso Jawmiraawo .
61002012	Ammaa yimɓe ɓe'e , ɓe tokki ɗabiya maɓɓe bana kuuje ladde dimaaɗe ngam naŋgeego e mbareego , ɓe ɗon kuɗa ɗum ko ɓe paamataa . Allah halkan ɓe bana kuuje ladde ,
61002013	o waatanan ɓe torra bana ka ɓe torriri woɗɓe bee man . Ɓe ɗon ceyo hebbingo suunooji ɓalli kalluɗi haa gite yimɓe . Ɓe ɗon nyaamda bee mooɗon , ɓe ɗon ceyo waɗugo jamba maɓɓe . Kayya ! Ɗum cemtuɗum masin !
61002014	Sey rewɓe daakaare'en tan ɓe ngiɗi laarugo , ɓe comataa waɗugo hakke sam . Ɓe ɗon njahra tampuɓe haa tuufnorɗum . Ɓerɗe maɓɓe mboowi suuno . Ɓe ɗon nder naaloore Allah !
61002015	Ɓe acci laawol gooŋga , ɓe nasti ladde , ɓe tokki laawol ngol Balaama ɓii Be'or , giɗɗo ceede ɗe o heɓata bee waɗugo halleende ,
61002016	ammaa o telɓanaama ngam boofol maako . Ngam wamnde muukaare wolwani mo bee sawtu neɗɗo , haɗi paataaku annaboojo oo .
61002017	Yimɓe ɓe'e , ɓe nandi bee ɓulndu yoorndu , ɓe nandi bee duule ɗe hendu soggata . Allah taaskani ɓe nokkuure nder nyiɓre ɓurdunde nyiɓɓugo .
61002018	Ɓe ɗon mbolwa bolle mantooje bee faataare , ɓe ɗon kuuwtinira suunooji ɓalli kalluɗi ngam ɓe naŋga wurtiiɓe jonta caka jooɗiiɓe nder aybefa .
61002019	Ɓe mbi'i yimɓe ɓe'e ɓe laatoto rimɓe , ammaa kamɓe maa , ɓe maccuɓe kuuɗe kalkooje . Ngam ko jaali goɗɗo fuu , laatini mo maccuɗo maajum .
61002020	Bee anndugo Jawmiraawo e Kisnoowo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu ɓe kisino baawɗeeji duniyaaru kalkooji . Ammaa ɓe ndokki ɗi laawol fahin , ɗi njaalake ɓe . Ngam man timmoode maɓɓe ɓuri fuɗɗoode maɓɓe hallugo .
61002021	Ndikkano ɓe to ɓe meeɗaayno anndugo laawol Allah dow anndugo ngol , acca umroore maako nde o umri ɓe !
61002022	Ko waɗi ɓe , gooŋɗini balndol ngol : " Rawaandu lorake haa tuure mum . " Kadiboo : " Gaduuru yiiwaandu lorake , talli nder loope . "
61003001	Yiɗaaɓe am , kaŋgol woni bataakewol am ɗiɗaɓol haa mooɗon . Nder bataakeeji ɗiɗi fuu mi ɗaɓɓiti ummingo numooji booɗɗi nder mooɗon bee siftinorgo on ko on ekkitino .
61003002	Mi yiɗi on ciftora bolle ɗe annabo'en seniiɓe mbolwi diga ɓooyma , bee umroore Jawmiraawo e Kisnoowo , nde nelaaɓe haa mooɗon ngaddani on .
61003003	Aran , paame , nder balɗe ragareeje tokkiiɓe suunooji ɓalli maɓɓe ngaran . Ɓe njalan on ,
61003004	ɓe mbi'an : " O wi'no o waran , naa non na ? Toy mo ? Kaakaaji meeɗen maayi jonta , ammaa walaa ko wayliti diga fuɗɗam duniyaaru haa jonta ! "
61003005	Ɓe njawi gooŋga ka : Diga ɓooyma Allah tagri asama e lesdi bee bolle . O tagri lesdi bee ndiyam , nder ndiyam o jogoto ndi ,
61003006	kadiboo o halki duniyaaru naane bee ndiyam , waato ilam tuufaana .
61003007	Ngam asama e lesdi ko en ndaarata jonta , njooɗi ngam Allah yiɗi non tawon . Ammaa ɗum tammi halkugo bee yiite . Allah jogi ɗum haa nyande o hiitoto halluɓe , o halka ɓe .
61003008	Soobiraaɓe am , taa ngejjite huunde woore : Jawmiraawo sendataa nyalaade woore bee duuɓi ujineere . Haa maako ɗum fuu ɗum gootum .
61003009	Woɗɓe ɗon numa Jawmiraawo ɗon neeɓa waɗugo ko o wi'no . Ammaa naa non , o neeɓataa . Ammaa o ɗon munyana on ngam o yiɗaa koomoy halka , o yiɗi yimɓe fuu tuuba , acca hakkeeji maɓɓe .
61003010	Koo non fuu , nyalaade Jawmiraawo waran bana gujjo . Nyande man , asamanji majjan bee hoolo hulniiŋgo , koode asama boo kalkan bee yiite , lesdi boo bee ko woni ton fuu majjan .
61003011	Nde kuuje ɗe fuu kalkan bana ni , on anndi no njooɗortooɗon . Sey on njooɗo nder senaare , on tokko Allah bee gooŋga ,
61003012	bee reenugo nyalaade maako . Kuuwe haa nde wara law , waato nyalaade nde asamanji ngulata , ɗi kalka , koode boo ɓolwa bee yiite .
