61003013	Ammaa Allah wi'i o hokkan en asama kesa e lesdi kesri . Ton walaa halleende , ngam muuyo maako tabitan . Kanjum en ndeenata .
61003014	Ngam maajum , soobiraaɓe am , nde on ɗon ndeena nyalaade man , kaɓde jooɗaago on laaɓɓe , bilaa aybe yeeso Allah . Njooɗe jam bee maako .
61003015	Paame no munyal Jawmiraawo meeɗen maɓɓitani on laawol hisugo . Deerɗiraawo meeɗen Pol , giɗaaɗo , windani on haala ka bee hikma ka Allah hokki mo .
61003016	Haa nder bataakeeji maako fuu o ɗon winda bana ni dow haala ka . Woodi haalaaji caɗɗi nder bataakeeji maako . Bilki'en meere'en ɗon ngayla haalaaji ɗi , ɗon mbonna ɗi bana no ɓe mbaɗata aayaaje defte Allah goɗɗe . Bana ni ɓe ɗon ngaddana ko'e maɓɓe halkere .
61003017	Ammaa onon on anndi ɗum , soobiraaɓe am . Ngam maajum kakkile , taa pewe tuurtooɓe esta on haa on cotta diga nokkuure nde on ndari ton bee sembe .
61003018	Ammaa on mawna nder mo''ere e anndal Jawmiraawo e Kisnoowo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu . Tedduŋgal laatano mo diga jonta haa foroy . Aamiina .
62001001	Min mbindani on dow goɗɗo bi'eteeɗo Wolde-ngeendam , gonɗo diga fuɗɗam duniyaaru . Min nani bolle maako , min ngi'i mo bee gite amin . Min ndaari mo , min meemi mo bee juuɗe amin .
62001002	Nde ngeendam man waŋgi , min ngi'i ɗam . Ngam maajum min ceedi ɗum , min ngaajini on ngeendam nduumiiɗam ngonnooɗam bee Baabiraawo , ɗam Allah waŋginani en .
62001003	Ko min ngi'i , ko min nani , kanjum min ngeccata on , ngam haa on kawta bee amin nder kawtal amin bee Baabiraawo e bee Ɓiɗɗo mum Yeesu Almasiihu .
62001004	Min mbindani on ɗum ngam haa seyo heewa ɓerɗe meeɗen .
62001005	Kubaruwol ngol min nani haa Ɓiɗɗo maako , kaŋgol min ngeccata on : Allah o annoora , walaa nyiɓre nder maako koo tis .
62001006	Ngam maajum to en mbi'i en narri bee maako , ammaa en ɗon njooɗi nder nyiɓre , en pewi , joonde meeɗen laataaki gooŋga .
62001007	Ammaa to en ɗon njooɗi nder annoora bana no Allah ɗon jooɗi nder annoora , en njooɗodoto bee narral , ?i?am Yeesu , Ɓiɗɗo maako , laɓɓinan en diga hakkeeji meeɗen fuu .
62001008	To en mbi'i en ngalaa hakke , en pewani ko'e meeɗen , en ngalaa gooŋga sam .
62001009	Ammaa to en tuubi hakkeeji meeɗen yeeso Allah , en mbaawan hoolaago mo ngam wolde maako ɗon tabiti . O yaafoto hakkeeji meeɗen , o laɓɓinan en diga aybefa meeɗen fuu .
62001010	To en mbi'i en ngalaa hakke , en laatini Allah pewoowo , wolde maako nafataa en .
62002001	Ɓikkoy am , mi windani on ɗum ngam taa on mbaɗa hakke . Ammaa to goɗɗo waɗi hakke boo , en ngoodi goɗɗo mo walaa hakke , waato Yeesu Almasiihu , kaŋko seettoto en yeeso Baabiraawo .
62002002	Almasiihu on hokki yoŋki muuɗum ngam daliila meeɗen , ngam maajum yaafuye hakkeeji ɗon , naa yaafuye hakkeeji meeɗen tan , ammaa hakkeeji yimɓe duniyaaru fuu .
62002003	To en ɗowtanake umrooje Allah , nden kam en anndi mo fakat .
62002004	To goɗɗo wi'i anndi mo , ammaa ɗowtanaaki umrooje maako , nden kam o pewoowo , o walaa gooŋga sam .
62002005	Ammaa to goɗɗo ɗowtanake wolde maako , fakat yiide Allah heewi nder maako . Bana ni anndirten en ɗon narri bee Allah .
62002006	Bi'ɗo o narri bee Allah tum , sey o jooɗo bana Yeesu Almasiihu jooɗori .
62002007	Soobiraaɓe am , ko mbindanmi on ɗum , naa ɗum umroore hesre , ammaa ɗum umroore ɓooymaare nde annduɗon diga fuɗɗam . Umroore ɓooymaare nde'e woni wolde nde on meeɗino nanugo .
62002008	Koo non boo , umroore nde mbindanmi on nde hesre , gooŋga maare waŋgi bee Almasiihu , e bee mooɗon boo . Nyiɓre ɗon usto , annoora gooŋgaha fuɗɗi yaynugo .
62002009	To goɗɗo wi'i o ɗon wondi bee annoora , kadiboo o ɗon wanya deerɗiiko , nden kam o ɗon nder nyiɓre tawon .
62002010	Giɗɗo deerɗum ɗon jooɗi nder annoora , ngam maajum walaa nder muuɗum ko fergata goɗɗo haa nasta hakke .
62002011	Ammaa ganyɗo deerɗum ɗon jooɗi nder nyiɓre , ɗon yaha nder nyiɓre , o anndaa toy o yahata ngam nyiɓre wumni mo .
62002012	Mi windani on , onon ɓikkoy am , ngam bee innde Yeesu Almasiihu on keɓi yaafuye .
62002013	Mi windani on , onon baabiraaɓe , ngam on anndi gonɗo diga fuɗɗam . Mi windani on , onon derke'en , ngam on njaalake kalluɗo .
62002014	Mi windani on , onon ɓikkoy , ngam on anndi Baabiraawo . Mi windani on , onon baabiraaɓe , ngam on anndi gonɗo diga fuɗɗam . Mi windani on , onon derke'en , ngam on ngoodi sembe , on keewi wolde Allah , on njaalake kalluɗo .
62002015	Taa ɗakkotire bee duniyaaru ndu , e kuuje maaru fuu . To goɗɗo ɗakkotiri bee duniyaaru , o waawataa yiɗugo Baabiraawo .
62002016	Noy duniyaaru wa'i ? Yimɓe ɗon tokko suunooji muuɗum'en , ɓe ngi'an huunde , ɓe ɗaɓɓa heɓugo ɗum , ɓe ɗon mantoro maral e baawɗe . Ɗum fuu ɗum iwaay haa Baabiraawo , haa duniyaaru ɗum iwi .
62002017	Duniyaaru bee kuuje maaru fuu ɗon timma , bee ko neɗɗo yiɗi ton fuu . Ammaa ɗowtantooɗo muuyo Allah , yeeɗan haa foroy .
62002018	Ɓikkoy am , timmoode ɓadake ! On nani konneejo Almasiihu tammi warugo . Jonta konne'en Almasiihu ɗuuɗɓe ngari , ngam maajum en anndi timmoode ɓadake .
62002019	Konne'en man iwi caka meeɗen , ammaa ɓe laataaki ɓe meeɗen bee gooŋga . To ɓe laatino ɓe meeɗen bee gooŋga , ɓe accataano en . Ammaa ɓe acci en ngam haa ɗum waŋga laaɓɗum ɓe meeɗaay laataago nder meeɗen bee gooŋga .
62002020	On fuu on anndi gooŋga , ngam Almasiihu hokki on Ruuhu Ceniiɗo .
62002021	Mi windani on , naa ngam on anndaa gooŋga , ammaa ngam on anndi ka , kadiboo on anndi fewre wurtataako nder gooŋga .
62002022	Kadi , moy woni pewoowo ? Koomoy wi'i Yeesu laataaki Almasiihu . Bi'ɗo non , kaŋko woni konneejo Almasiihu , o sali Baabiraawo , o sali Ɓiɗɗo boo .
62002023	Ngam koomoy sali Ɓiɗɗo , sali Baabiraawo boo . Mo jaɓi Ɓiɗɗo , jaɓi Baabiraawo boo .
62002024	Haala ka nanɗon diga fuɗɗam , tiine jogaago ka nder ɓerɗe mooɗon . To ko on nani diga fuɗɗam tabiti nder ɓerɗe mooɗon , nden kam on ngoodi kawtal bee Ɓiɗɗo e Baabiraawo foroy .
62002025	Kanjum woni ko Almasiihu wi'i hokkan en , waato ngeendam nduumiiɗam .
62002026	Mi windani on ɗum dow ɗaɓɓanɓe estugo on .
62002027	Ammaa onon , Almasiihu hokki on Ruuhu muuɗum . Nde Ruuhu man ɗon nder mooɗon , on ngalaa haaje goɗɗo anndina on , ngam Ruuhu ɗon anndina on kooɗume fuu . Ngu ɗon anndina on gooŋga , naa fewre . Ngam maajum , tokke ɗum , tabite nder kawtal bee Almasiihu .
62002028	Ɓikkoy am , tabite nder kawtal bee Almasiihu ngam taa en kula to o waŋgi , taa en nyukko ngam semteende nyande o warata .
62002029	On anndi Almasiihu o gooŋgaajo . Ngam maajum on anndi , koomoy huuwi ko fotti , laatake ɓiŋgel Allah .
62003001	Ndaare no Baabiraawo yiɗiri en , haa en mbi'aama ɓikkoy maako . Fakat en ɓikkoy maako ! Duniyaaru faamaay haala meeɗen ngam ndu meeɗaay anndugo Baabiraawo .
62003002	Soobiraaɓe am yiɗaaɓe , jonta en laati ɓikkoy Allah . Ko en tammi laataago , laaɓaay tawon . Ammaa en anndi fakat , to Almasiihu waŋgi , en laatoto bana maako , ngam en ngi'an mo bana no o wa'i .
62003003	Koomoy tammoto nandugo bee Almasiihu , daayoto halleende fuu , bana Almasiihu daayori nde .
62003004	Baɗɗo hakke fuu tuurtani Allah , ngam waɗugo hakke ɗum tuurtango Allah .
62003005	On anndi Almasiihu wari haa o itta hakkeeji meeɗen . Kaŋko o walaa hakkewol koo gootol .
62003006	Gonduɗo bee Almasiihu fuu accan waɗugo hakkeeji , ammaa tokkiiɗo waɗugo hakke meeɗaay yi'ugo mo , meeɗaay anndugo mo boo .
62003007	Ɓikkoy am , taa goɗɗo esta on . Baɗɗo ko fotti , o gooŋgaajo bana Almasiihu o gooŋgaajo .
62003008	Mo accaay waɗugo hakke , ɗon nder juŋŋgo Sayɗaanu , ngam diga fuɗɗam Sayɗaanu nasti waɗugo hakke . Ngam maajum Almasiihu wari halkugo kuuɗe Sayɗaanu .
62003009	To goɗɗo laatake ɓiŋgel Allah , o acci waɗugo hakke , ngam Ruuhu Allah ɗon huuwa nder maako . O waawataa o tokko waɗugo hakke ngam Allah woni Baabiraawo maako .
62003010	Ammaa to goɗɗo waɗi kalluɗum , wanyi deerɗum boo , nden kam o laataaki ɓiŋgel Allah . Bana ni goɗɗo sendindirta ɓikkoy Allah bee ɓikkoy Sayɗaanu .
62003011	Haala ka on nani diga fuɗɗam , ndaa ka : Ngiɗindire !
62003012	Taa en laato bana Kayinu mo mbari deerɗum ngam kalluɗo jaali mo . Koni o mbari deerɗiiko ? Ngam kuuɗe maako kalluɗe , ammaa kuuɗe deerɗiiko ɗe pottuɗe .
62003013	Deerɗam'en , taa kayɗine to duniyaaru wanyi on .
62003014	En anndi naane en ɗonno nder maayde , ammaa jonta en nasti ngeendam . En anndi ɗum ngam en ngiɗi deerɗiraaɓe men . Ammaa mo walaa yiide , ɗon nder maayde tawon .
62003015	Ganyɗo deerɗum o mbaroowo ko'e . On anndi mbaroowo ko'e walaa ngeendam nduumiiɗam .
62003016	Almasiihu hokki yoŋki muuɗum ngam meeɗen . Bee maajum en paami ko woni yiide . Enen boo , sey en taasko hokkugo yoŋki meeɗen ngam deerɗiraaɓe meeɗen .
62003017	To goɗɗo diskuɗo yi'i haaje deerɗum , ammaa sali enɗugo mo , noy o wi'rata o yiɗi Allah bee ɓernde woore ?
62003018	Ɓikkoy am , taa yiide meeɗen laato sey bolle belɗe tan . Ammaa nde laato yiide gooŋgaare , waŋgannde nder kuuɗe .
62003019	Bana ni anndirten en ɗon tokki gooŋga . Kanjum waɗi en kulataa daraago yeeso Allah .
62003020	Ngam to ɓerɗe meeɗen kolli en aybeeji meeɗen , en anndi Allah ɓuri ɓerɗe meeɗen anndugo , ngam o anndi kooɗume fuu .
62003021	Soobiraaɓe am yiɗaaɓe , nde ɓerɗe meeɗen mbaawataa hiitaago en , en ndaroto yeeso Allah bee hoolaare .
62003022	En keɓan haa maako ko en toroto mo fuu , ngam en ɗon ɗowtano umrooje maako , en ɗon mbaɗa ko fottanta mo .
62003023	Ndaa ko o umrata : En nuɗɗina innde Yeesu Almasiihu , Ɓiɗɗo maako , en ngiɗindira bana Almasiihu umri en .
62003024	Ɗowtaniiɗo umrooje Allah woodi kawtal bee muuɗum , Allah boo ɗon wondi bee maako . Allah hokki en Ruuhu muuɗum , bana ni anndirten Allah ɗon wondi bee meeɗen .
62004001	Soobiraaɓe am yiɗaaɓe , taa nuɗɗine koomoy bi'ɗo on o woodi Ruuhu . Sey on poonda mo , on ndaara to haala man iwi haa Allah malla naa non . Ngam annabo'en fewooɓe ɗon kootoy .
62004002	Koomoy wi'i Yeesu Almasiihu laati neɗɗo , kaŋko o woodi Ruuhu iwŋgu haa Allah . Bana ni anndirton to o woodi Ruuhu Allah .
62004003	Ammaa to goɗɗo yeddi Almasiihu laati neɗɗo , nden kam o walaa Ruuhu Allah . To non , haala man iwi haa konneejo Almasiihu . On nani ka waran , ndaa ka yotti duniyaaru jonta .
62004004	Ammaa onon ɓikkoy am , on laati yimɓe Allah , on njaali annabo'en fewooɓe go . Ngam Ruuhu ngonŋgu nder mooɗon ɓuri hakkiilooji yimɓe duniyaaru sembe .
62004005	Kamɓe laati yimɓe duniyaaru , haala maɓɓe boo ka duniyaaru . Ngam maajum yimɓe duniyaaru ɗon nanana ɓe .
62004006	Ammaa enen en laati ɓikkoy Allah . Annduɗo Allah nananan en . Mo laataaki ɓiŋgel Allah , nanantaa en . Bana ni en cendirta Ruuhu gooŋga bee ruuhu fewre .
62004007	Soobiraaɓe am yiɗaaɓe , ngiɗindire , ngam yiide iwi haa Allah . Marɗo yiide woni ɓiŋgel Allah , anndi Allah .
62004008	Mo walaa yiide , anndaa Allah , ngam Allah o yiide .
62004009	Ndaa no Allah holliri en yiide muuɗum : O neli en Ɓiɗɗo maako bajjo haa nder duniyaaru ngam en keɓra ngeendam bee maako .
62004010	Ndaa ko woni yiide : Naa enen aarti yiɗugo Allah , ammaa kaŋko aarti yiɗugo en . O neli en Ɓiɗɗo maako ngam haa en keɓra yaafeego hakkeeji bee muuɗum .
62004011	Soobiraaɓe am , to ni Allah yiɗiri en , haani ngiɗindiren , enen boo .
62004012	Walaa mo meeɗi yi'ugo Allah . Ammaa to en ngiɗindiri , nden kam Allah wondan bee meeɗen , yiide maako boo huuwan nder meeɗen ko o yiɗi fuu .
62004013	Allah hokki en Ruuhu muuɗum . Ngam maajum en anndi fakat en ngoodi kawtal bee maako , kaŋko boo ɗon wondi bee meeɗen .
62004014	Min ngi'i , min ɗon ceedo Baabiraawo neli Ɓiɗɗo muuɗum haa o hisna yimɓe duniyaaru .
62004015	Allah ɗon wondi bee koomoy seedi Yeesu woni Ɓiɗɗo Allah , goɗɗo man boo ɗon wondi bee Allah .
62004016	Enen kam en anndi , en nuɗɗini Allah yiɗi en .
62004017	To yiide Allah huuwi ko yiɗi nder meeɗen , en kulataa nyande kiita sam , ngam joonde meeɗen nder duniyaaru ndu laati woore bee nde Almasiihu .
62004018	Marɗo yiide hulataa , yiide gooŋgaare ɗon itta kulol fuu . To goɗɗo huli , waato yiide heɓaay huuwugo nder maako bana Allah yiɗi , ngam kulol hawti bee kiita .
62004019	Enen en ngoodi yiide ngam Allah aarti yiɗugo en .
62004020	To goɗɗo wi'i yiɗi Allah , ammaa ɗon wanya deerɗum , o fewi . To o yiɗaa deerɗiiko mo o yi'ata , noy o waawrata yiɗugo Allah mo o meeɗaay yi'ugo ?
62004021	Ndaa umroore nde Almasiihu umri en : Mo yiɗi Allah , sey o holla deerɗiiko boo yiide .
62005001	Koomoy nuɗɗini Yeesu woni Almasiihu , laati ɓiŋgel Allah . Koomoy yiɗi baaba , yiɗi ɓiŋgel boo .
62005002	Noy anndirten en ngiɗi ɓikkoy Allah ? Sey bee yiɗugo Allah , e ɗowtanaago umrooje maako boo .
62005003	Ɗume woni yiɗugo Allah ? To goɗɗo yiɗi Allah , o ɗowtanto umrooje maako . Ɗowtanaago umrooje maako ɓuraay sembe meeɗen ,
62005004	ngam ɓiŋgel Allah fuu waawan jaalaago duniyaaru . Bee nuɗɗinki meeɗen njaalortooɗen duniyaaru .
62005005	Moy waawi jaalaago duniyaaru ? Sey nuɗɗinɗo Yeesu woni Ɓiɗɗo Allah .
62005006	Yeesu Almasiihu wari bee ndiyam baptisma muuɗum , bee ?i?am maayde muuɗum boo . O waraay bee ndiyam tan , ammaa bee ndiyam e ?i?am fuu . Ruuhu bee hoore muuɗum gooŋɗini haala ka ngam kaŋgu woni gooŋga .
62005007	Woodi seedooɓe tato :
62005008	Ruuhu e ndiyam e ?i?am . Seedamku maɓɓe laati gootum .
62005009	En nuɗɗini seedamku yimɓe , ammaa seedamku Allah ɓuri ɗum sembe . Kaŋgu laati seedamku ngu Allah seedi dow Ɓiɗɗo muuɗum .
62005010	Ngam maajum koomoy nuɗɗini Ɓiɗɗo Allah , woodi seedamku ngu nder ɓernde muuɗum . Ammaa mo nuɗɗinaay Allah , o laatini Allah pewoowo , ngam o nuɗɗinaay seedamku ngu Allah wolwi dow Ɓiɗɗo muuɗum .
62005011	Ɗume woni seedamku ngu ? Allah hokki en ngeendam nduumiiɗam , ngeendam ɗam laati ɗam meeɗen nder Ɓiiyiiko .
62005012	Koomoy jaɓi Ɓiɗɗo Allah , woodi ngeendam , mo jaɓaay Ɓiɗɗo Allah , o walaa ngeendam .
62005013	Onon nuɗɗinɓe Ɓiɗɗo Allah , mi windani on ɗum ngam haa anndon fakat on ngoodi ngeendam nduumiiɗam .
62005014	En ɗon koolo Allah , ngam en anndi o nanan en , to en torake mo kooɗume nder muuyo maako .
62005015	To ni en anndi o nanan en , en anndi boo o hokkan en ko en toroto mo fuu .
62005016	To goɗɗo yi'i deerɗum ɗon waɗa hakkewol ngol yahrataa mo haa maayde , sey o toro Allah , Allah boo hokkan deerɗiiko ngeendam . Haala ka nafan yimɓe ɓe hakkeeji muuɗum'en njahrataa ɓe haa maayde tan . Ammaa woodi hakkewol jahranŋgol goɗɗo haa maayde . Mi wi'aay on toro Allah ngam maagol .
62005017	Aybe fuu woni hakke , ammaa woodi hakkeeji ɗi njahrataa goɗɗo haa maayde .
62005018	En anndi walaa ɓiŋgel Allah tokkoto waɗugo hakke , ngam Ɓiɗɗo Allah ɗon ayna mo , kalluɗo heɓataa meemugo mo .
62005019	En anndi en laati yimɓe Allah , koo nde yimɓe duniyaaru fuu ɗon haa juŋŋgo Sayɗaanu .
62005020	En anndi Ɓiɗɗo Allah wari , hokki en baawɗe anndugo Allah gooŋgaajo . En keɓi kawtal bee Allah gooŋgaajo ngam daliila Ɓiɗɗo maako Yeesu Almasiihu . Kaŋko woni Allah gooŋgaajo , kaŋko woni ngeendam nduumiiɗam boo .
62005021	Ɓikkoy am , taa ɗakkotire bee labbi .
63001001	Bataakewol am , min ndottiijo , yahugo haa mayramjofa mo ngiɗmi masin , bee ɓikkoy muuɗum . Naa min feere am yiɗi ma , ammaa annduɓe gooŋga fuu ,
63001002	ngam gooŋga ɗon wondi bee meeɗen haa foroy .
63001003	Allah Baabiraawo bee Ɓiɗɗo muuɗum Yeesu Almasiihu hokka en mo''ere e yaafuye e jam , ngam haa en kawta bee gooŋga e yiide .
63001004	Mi seyi masin nde mi tawi ɓikkoy ma ngoɗkoy ɗon tokki gooŋga bana no Baabiraawo umri en .
63001005	An mayramjo mo ngiɗmi , mi tori ma : Ngiɗindiren . Naa ɗum umroore hesre mbindanmi on , ɗum umroore nde en keɓi diga fuɗɗam .
63001006	Jogaago umrooje Allah tum , kanjum woni yiide nde mbolwanmi on . Umroore nde on nani diga fuɗɗam , kayre : " Tabite nder yiide . "
63001007	Fewooɓe ɗuuɗɓe ɗon kootoy . Ɓe cali jaɓugo Yeesu Almasiihu woni neɗɗo fakat . Bana ni keɓtirten pewoowo e konneejo Almasiihu .
63001008	Kakkile , ngam taa on majjina nafuda kuugal amin ngam mooɗon , ammaa ngam on keɓa mbarjaari mooɗon fuu .
63001009	Mo jogaaki anndinol Almasiihu , ammaa mo luuti ngol , o walaa kawtal bee Allah . Ammaa mo jooɗi nder anndinol ngol , o ɗon nder kawtal Baabiraawo e Ɓiɗɗo .
63001010	To goɗɗo wari haa mooɗon mo anndintaa on anndinol Almasiihu , taa njaɓɓe mo haa ci'e mooɗon . Koo hoofnugo mo , taa mbaɗe ɗum .
63001011	Ngam to goɗɗo hoofni mo , o hawti bee maako nder halleende .
63001012	Woodi kuuje feere ɗuuɗɗe ɗe mi anndinta on , ammaa mi yiɗaa windugo ɗum dow ɗereewol bee bindirgol . Ko ngiɗmi kam , yahugo haa mooɗon haa en ngeewtida gite bee gite ngam haa seyo heewa ɓerɗe meeɗen .
63001013	Ɓikkoy deerɗiraawo ma giɗaaɗo koofni on .
64001001	Bataakewol am , min ndottiijo , yahugo haa soobaajo am Gayus mo ngiɗmi masin .
64001002	Soobaajo am giɗaaɗo , mi ɗon yelo a jamo kooɗume bana mi anndi a jamo nder ɓernde ma .
64001003	Nde deerɗiraaɓe woɗɓe ngari , ngecci yam a ɗon tiini nder gooŋga , no a tokkori tabititgo nder gooŋga boo , mi seyi masin .
64001004	Walaa ko ɓuri seynugo yam bana nanugo ɓikkoy am ɗon tabiti nder gooŋga .
64001005	Soobaajo am giɗaaɗo , a ɗon haɓda wallugo deerɗiraaɓe bee gooŋga , koo to ɓe jananɓe .
64001006	Kamɓe mbolwi haala yiide maaɗa haa jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe ɗo . Mi ɗon toro ma a walla ɓe dow jahaaŋgal maɓɓe . Ballal maaɗa boo fottana Allah .
64001007	Nde ɓe ɗon mbaɗa jahaaŋgal maɓɓe haa kuugal Almasiihu , ɓe njaɓaay walliinde haa yimɓe duniyaaru .
64001008	Ngam maajum sey en mballa yimɓe ɓe ngam haa en kuuwda bee maɓɓe nder kuugal anndingo gooŋga .
64001009	Mi windani jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe bataakewol dammuŋgol , ammaa Diyotrefes , mo yiɗi laataago mawɗo maɓɓe , nanataa haala am sam .
64001010	Ngam maajum , to mi wari , mi waŋginan kuuɗe maako fuu , waato pewe e bolle kalluɗe ɗe o wolwata dow meeɗen . Naa kanjum tan , ammaa o jaɓɓataako deerɗiraaɓe , to ngari , kadi yiɗɓe jaɓɓaago ɓe boo , o ɗon haɗa ɓe , o ɗon tefa wurtingo ɓe nder jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe .
64001011	Soobaajo am giɗaaɗo , taa tokka halleende , tokka mbooɗeeŋga . Baɗanɗo mbooɗeeŋga woni goɗɗo Allah , baɗanɗo halleende meeɗaay anndugo Allah .
64001012	Koomoy ɗon yerdi Demetriyus . Gooŋga boo ɗon seedi o booɗɗo . Minin boo min ceedi ɗum . A anndi min ɗon mbolwa gooŋga .
64001013	Woodi kuuje feere ɗuuɗɗe ɗe mi anndinta on , ammaa mi yiɗaa windugo ɗum dow ɗereewol bee bindirgol .
64001014	Mi yiɗi yi'ugo ma law . To heɓoto , en ngeewtidan gite bee gite .
64001015	Jam laatano ma .
65001001	Bataakewol Yahuuda , maccuɗo Yeesu Almasiihu , deerɗiraawo Yakuba , yahugo suɓaaɓe Allah , jooɗiiɓe nder yiide Allah Baabiraawo , aynaaɓe Yeesu Almasiihu .
65001002	Mo''ere e jam e yiide heewa on .
65001003	Soobiraaɓe am yiɗaaɓe , mi ɗonno haɓda windango on haala kisndam ɗam en kawti nder muuɗum , ammaa mi ndikkitini windango on jonta haa mi sembiɗina on nder haɓre nuɗɗinki ki Allah hokki yimɓe muuɗum nde woore , ki he'i haa foroy .
65001004	Ngam woɗɓe halluɓe nasti caka meeɗen nde en kakkilanaay ɗum . Ɓe mbonni habaru mo''ere Allah ngam ɓe keɓa hujja waɗugo halleende , ɓe ɗon calo Yeesu Almasiihu boo , mo Jawmiraawo e jaagorɗo meeɗen feere muuɗum . Diga ɓooyma defte Allah tindini en kiita ka heɓi yimɓe ɓe'e jonta .
65001005	On anndi haala ka fuu , ammaa mi yiɗi siftinorgo on no Jawmiraawo hisniri yimɓe Isra'iila diga lesdi Misra . Ammaa ɓaawoɗon o halki woɗɓe ngam ɓe ɗowtanaaki mo .
65001006	Ciftore malaa'ika'en saaliiɓe keerol baawɗe ɗe Allah hokki ɓe , ɓe acci joonde maɓɓe . Allah maɓɓi ɓe nder nyiɓre les , haɓɓi ɓe bee callalluuji ɗi pistataako . Ɓe ɗon ndeena nyande kiita maɓɓe ton .
65001007	Ciftore Sodoma e Gomorra bee gure piltuɗe ɗe . Yimɓe maaje mbaɗi bana malaa'ika'en go mbaɗi , ɓe tokki suunooji ɓalli e halleende . Kiita yiite duumiiŋge torri ɓe ngam haa yimɓe fuu kula .
65001008	Bana ni boo , yimɓe nastuɓe caka mooɗon go ngoodi koyɗi jahranɗi ɓe waɗango ɓalli maɓɓe hakke . Ɓe ɗon njawo baawɗe Allah , ɓe ɗon kuɗa tedduɓe haa asama .
65001009	Koo Mika'iilu , malaa'ikaajo mawɗo waɗaay bana ni . Saa'i o waabotiri bee Sayɗaanu dow moy heɓata hoosugo ɓandu Muusa , o huli huɗugo Sayɗaanu , ngam maajum o wi'i : " Jawmiraawo telɓane ! "
65001010	Ammaa yimɓe ɓe'e ɓe ɗon mbolwa kalluka dow ko ɓe paamaay . Ɓe ɗon tokko suunooji maɓɓe bana dabbaaji ladde , fakat suunooji maajum kalkan ɓe .
65001011	Kayto ! Ɓe tokki laawol Kayinu . Ɓe ndokki ko'e maɓɓe haa fewre ngam heɓugo ceede bana ko Balaama waɗno . Ɓe kalki , ɓe tuurti bana Koora tuurtirno .
65001012	Saa'i on ɗon nyaamda , ɓe ɗon cemtina kawtal mooɗon bee suuno maɓɓe . Sey ko'e maɓɓe tan ɓe numanta . Ɓe nandi bee duule ɗe hendu soggata meere , walaa iyeende . Ɓe nandi bee leɗɗe ɗe ndimataa sam , koo bee wakkati man . Ɓe nandi bee leɗɗe ɗoofaaɗe , baatɗe .
65001013	Ɓe nandi bee ?uuge kalluɗe haa maayo maŋgo , kuuɗe maɓɓe kalluɗe mbaŋgi bana nguufo . Ɓe nandi bee koode majjuɗe . Allah taaskani ɓe nokkuure nder nyiɓre ɓurannde nyiɓɓugo . Ɓe ngurtataako ton haa foroy .
65001014	Anuhu mo woni nder yidere joweeɗiɗawre haa danygol Aadamu , wolwi dow maɓɓe diga ɓooyma , o wi'i : " Ndaare , Jawmiraawo waran bee malaa'ika'en muuɗum seniiɓe ujineeje ɗuuɗɗe
65001015	ngam o hiito yimɓe fuu . O hiitoto waɗooɓe hakkeeji ngam kuuɗe maɓɓe kalluɗe , o hiitoto ɓe ngam bolle maɓɓe kalluɗe ɓe mbolwi dow maako ! "
65001016	Yimɓe ɓe'e , tum ɓe ɗon ngurŋgurto dow luttuɓe , ɓe ɗon aybina ɓe . Ɓe ɗon tokko suunooji maɓɓe kalluɗi , ɓe ɗon mantoro ko'e maɓɓe , ɓe ɗon mana woɗɓe ngam ɓe keɓa ko ɓe ngiɗi .
65001017	Ammaa onon , soobiraaɓe am , ciftore ko nelaaɓe Jawmiraawo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu ngeccuno on diga naane .
65001018	Ngam ɓe mbi'i on : " To balɗe ragareeje njottake , woɗɓe njalan on , ɓe tokkoto suunooji maɓɓe kalluɗi . "
65001019	Yimɓe ɓe'e mbaɗan cenduki caka yimɓe . Sey ɗabiya maɓɓe tan ɓe tokkoto , naa Ruuhu Allah .
65001020	Ammaa onon soobiraaɓe am , cembiɗine ko'e mooɗon nder nuɗɗinki mooɗon ceniiki . Tore bee baawɗe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo ,
65001021	tabite nder yiide Allah , nde on ɗon ndeena haa Jawmiraawo meeɗen Yeesu Almasiihu hokka on mo''ere e ngeendam nduumiiɗam .
65001022	Njurmine sektotooɓe ,
65001023	ngurtine ɓe nder yiite , kisne ɓe . Njurmine tokkiiɓe suunooji muuɗum'en boo , ammaa ndeente onon , ngam taa coɓki maɓɓe raaɓa on .
65001024	Allah waawi aynugo on ngam taa on ndo''o . O waawan yottingo on haa tedduŋgal maako , on ngalaa aybefa , on seyiiɓe .
65001025	Kaŋko woni Allah gooto mo ɗon hisna en bee Yeesu Almasiihu , Jawmiraawo meeɗen . Kaŋko mari tedduŋgal e maŋgu e baawɗe diga jamanuuji ɓooymaaji , non boo jonta e haa foroy . Aamiina .
66001001	Deftere nde'e ɗon yecca haala sirriiji ɗi Yeesu Almasiihu waŋgini . Allah anndini mo ɗi , ngam haa o waŋginana teddinooɓe Allah ko ɓadi laataago , doole ɗum laato . Almasiihu neli malaa'ikaajo muuɗum haa suka muuɗum Yuhanna , anndini mo sirriiji ɗi .
66001002	Yuhanna ɗon seedo ko Allah wi'i , o ɗon seedo gooŋga ka Yeesu Almasiihu waŋgini . Yuhanna bee hoore muuɗum yi'i ɗum .
66001003	Barka laatanto jaŋganɗo deftere nde , e nananɓe bolle wahayu ngu , tokkiiɓe ko winda nder maare ! Ngam kuuje ɗe fuu ɓadi laataago .
66001004	Yuhanna windani jama'aaje Masiihiŋko'en joweeɗiɗi haa lesdi Asiya . Ndaa ko o windi :
66001005	e diga Yeesu Almasiihu , ceedoowo gooŋgaajo , ummitinaaɗo arano nder maayɓe fuu , laamiiɗo laamlaamɓe duniyaaru boo .
66001006	o hokki en laamu e limanku haa en kuuwana Allah , Baabiraawo maako . Tedduŋgal e baawɗe laatano Yeesu Almasiihu haa foroy . Aamiina !
66001007	Kakkile , o ɗon wara bee duule ! Koomoy fuu yi'an mo , koo yuwɓe mo boo . Yimɓe duniyaaru fuu mboyan ngam daliila maako . Fakat , bana ni ɗum laatoto . Aamiina !
66001008	Allah Jawmiraawo baawɗo , mo ɗon , mo ɗonno ɓooyma , mo ɗon wara boo , wi'i : " Min woni arano e ragareejo . "
66001009	Min woni Yuhanna , deerɗiraawo mooɗon . Mi hawti bee Almasiihu bana mooɗon , on fuu . Mi torriiɗo bana mooɗon boo . Mi ɗon munyana bone fuu bee mooɗon , haa to en keɓi nastugo laamu maako . Mi jo''inaama haa duunde wi'eteende Patmos ngam mi waaji wolde Allah e gooŋga ka Yeesu waŋgini .
66001010	Nyande Alat feere Ruuhu naŋgi yam , mi nani sawtu ɓaawo am , bana algaytaaru .
66001011	Sawtu man wi'i : " Ko ngi'ata , windu ɗum nder deftere , neldu nde haa jama'aaje nuɗɗinɓe wonɓe haa Efesus e Samirna e Pergame e Tiyatira e Sardis e Filadelfiya e Lawdikiya . "
66001012	Mi wayliti haa mi laara mo wolwani yam . Mi yi'i jo''inirɗe pittirlaaji joweeɗiɗi ɗe kaŋgeeri .
66001013	Goɗɗum ɗon dari haa caka maaje , ɗum nandi bee neɗɗo . Limce maako njotti teppe maako , o ɗon taadi taadorgol kaŋgeeri haa wiɓɓere maako .
66001014	Gaasa hoore maako ranwi ko ɓuri hottollo . Gite maako njayni bana yiite ,
66001015	kosɗe maako ɗelki bana njamndi mboɗeeri ɓolinaandi nder yiite . Sawtu maako nandi bee hoolo maayo maŋgo ilanŋgo dow tapaaje .
66001016	O ɗon jogi koode joweeɗiɗi haa juŋŋgo maako nyaamo , kaafahi belki wurti hunduko maako . Yeeso maako yayni bana naaŋge yaynirta caka nyalawma .
66001017	Nde mi yi'i mo , mi do''i yeeso maako bana maayɗo . O wallini juŋŋgo maako nyaamo dow hoore am , o wi'i : " Taa hul . Min woni fuɗɗoode , min woni timmoode boo .
66001018	Min woni geeto ! Mi maayino , ammaa ndaa , mi geeto haa foroy . Mi woodi baawɗe dow maayde , e dow joonde maayɓe boo .

66001020	Ndaa sirri koode joweeɗiɗi ɗe ngi'ɗa haa juŋŋgo am nyaamo , e sirri jo''inirɗe pittirlaaji joweeɗiɗi : Koode joweeɗiɗi ngoni malaa'ika'en jama'aaje nuɗɗinɓe joweeɗiɗi . Jo''inirɗe pittirlaaji joweeɗiɗi boo ngoni jama'aaje man joweeɗiɗi . "
66002001	" Windan malaa'ikaajo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe haa Efesus ni'i :

66002003	A ɗon munya , a torrake ngam daliila am , ammaa a somaay .

66002010	Taa hul torra ka a tammi torreego . Annde , Sayɗaanu jarriboto on bee nastingo woɗɓe mooɗon nder fursina . On torroto balɗe sappo . Joga nuɗɗinki ma haa yotto maayde , nden kam mi hokkete keɓal jaalorgal , kanjum woni ngeendam .

66002020	Ammaa woodi ko mi felata ma : A ɗon munyana debbo bi'eteeɗo Ijabel , mo wi'i o nelaaɗo Allah . Bee anndinol maako o ɗon esta suka'en am haa ɓe mbaɗa njeenu , ɓe nyaama kusel kirsaaŋgel ngam labbi .
66002021	Mi hokki mo wakkati haa o tuuba , ammaa o yiɗaa accugo halleende maako .
66002022	Ngam maajum mi sakkinan mo haa be''itte torra . Ton o torroto masin , kaŋko e waɗooɓe njeenu bee maako fuu . Mi enɗataa ɓe , sonaa to ɓe tuubi , ɓe acci halleende nde ɓe mbaɗi bee maako .
66002023	Mi mbaran ɓikkoy maako boo , haa jama'aaje nuɗɗinɓe fuu annda min woni linyoowo numooji e ɓerɗe yimɓe . Mi warjoto koomoy mooɗon deydey kuuɗe muuɗum .
66002024	" Ammaa onon nuɗɗinɓe luttuɓe haa Tiyatira , on tokkaaki anndinol kalluŋgol ngol , on ekkitaaki ko woɗɓe mbi'ata sirriiji Sayɗaanu lugguɗi . Mi roondataa on dooŋgal goɗŋgal .

66003001	" Windan malaa'ikaajo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe haa Sardis ni'i :
66003002	Fin , sembiɗin ko lutti bee yoŋki , hiddeko ɗum fuu ɗum maaya fakat . Ngam mi tawi kuuɗe ma yeeso Allah am laataaki timmuɗe tawon .
66003003	Ngam man , siftor ko a ekkiti e no a naniri ɗum . Ɗowtana ɗum , tuubu . To a finaay , mi waran bana gujjo , a anndataa saa'i nde mi warata .
66003004	Ammaa woɗɓe maaɗa haa Sardis tunwinaay limce muuɗum'en . Ɓe ke'i ɓornaago limce daneeje , ɓe njahda bee am .
66003005	Jaaliiɓe ɓornoto daneeje bana non , mi wilataa inɗe maɓɓe haa deftere ngeendam . Yeeso Baabiraawo am e malaa'ika'en muuɗum , mi seedoto ɓe laati yimɓe am .

66003009	Nan ! Mi nelan tokkiiɓe Sayɗaanu haa maaɗa . Fewooɓe ɓe'e ɓe ɗon mbi'a ɓe Yahuudu'en , ammaa ɗum fewre . Mi waɗan ɓe cujida yeeso ma . Nden ɓe paaman mi yiɗi ma .
66003010	Mi aynan ma jam nder wakkatiire torra ngaranka dow duniyaaru ngam jarribaago yimɓe fuu , ngam a munyi bana mi umri ma .
66003011	Mi ɓadi warugo . Joga ko marɗa , ngam taa koomoy jaɓta meetaleewol jaalorgal maaɗa .
66003012	Mi laatinan jaaliiɓe daŋgraŋge nder haykaliiru Allah am , ɓe meetataa sottugo ton . Mi windan innde Allah am dow maɓɓe , e innde berniwol Allah am , waato Urusaliima kesol ngol jippoto asama diga Allah am . Mi windan innde am hesre dow maɓɓe boo .

66003014	" Windan malaa'ikaajo jama'aare nuɗɗinɓe haa Lawdikiya ni'i :

66003017	A ɗon wi'a : Mi riski , jam kooɗume , walaa ko mi sooyi sam . Ammaa a anndaa a tampuɗo , a jurumɗo . A laafuɗo , a tembo , a bumɗo .
66003018	Ngam maajum mi ɗon wi'e : Soodu kaŋgeeri laaɓndi haa am ngam haa a riska . Soodu limce daneeje boo ngam haa a ɓorno , a sudda cemtuɗum tembu maaɗa . Kadiboo soodu lekki ngam gite ma , ngam haa a heɓa yi'ugo .

66003021	Mi hokkan jaaliiɓe baawɗe jooɗaago kombi am dow leeso laamu am , bana no min boo mi jaali , mi ɗon jooɗi kombi Baabiraawo am dow leeso laamu maako .

66004001	Ɓaawo maajum mi tijji dow , mi yi'i dammugal maɓɓitaaŋgal haa asama . Sawtu bana algaytaaru go , bolwannooɗo yam naane , wi'i : " War haa ɗo , mi hollete ko tammi laataago ! "
66004002	Saa'i man nden Ruuhu naŋgi yam . Mi yi'i leeso laamu nder asama , goɗɗo ɗon jooɗi dow maago .
66004003	Yeeso goɗɗo man ɗon jalbita bana kaa'e marɗe saman ɗuuɗɗo , bana hayre yaspa bee hayre sardis . Timotimooŋgal bee noonde hayre imiradi taari leeso laamu man haa dow .
66004004	Leese laamu noogas e nayi goɗɗe taari leeso go . Ndotti'en noogas e nayo ɗon njooɗi dow leese ɗe , ɓorniiɓe daneeje , bee meetaleeji kaŋgeeri dow ko'e maɓɓe .
66004005	Ma''e e hoolooji e pelmaali iwi haa leeso laamu go . Yeeso maago pittirlaaji joweeɗiɗi ɗon kuɓɓa , ɗum ruuhuuji Allah joweeɗiɗi .
66004006	Ko nandi bee weendu daarorgal laaɓŋgal tal ɗon yeeso leeso laamu go .
66004007	Huunde arande nandi bee mbarooga , huunde ɗiɗawre nandi bee ɓii nagge , tataɓre woodi yeeso bana yeeso goɗɗo , nayaɓre nandi bee dutal piiranŋgal .
66004008	Huunde woore fuu woodi bileeji joweego , keewɗi gite nder bee yaasi fuu . Jemma bee naaŋge fuu kuuje man ɗon ngima bana ni :
66004009	Kuuje geete nayi go ɗon ngimana jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu , mo ɗon yeeɗa haa foroy , gime tedduŋgal e maŋgu e gettooje .
66004010	Koondey ɗe mbaɗata ɗum , ndotti'en noogas e nayo go ɗon kofo yeeso jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu , ɗon cujidana oon geeto haa foroy . Ɓe ɗon mballina meetaleeji maɓɓe yeeso leeso laamu go , ɓe ɗon mbi'a :
66004011	" Ya Jawmiraawo amin , Allah amin ,
66005001	Mi yi'i deftere taggaande haa juŋŋgo nyaamo jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu go . Bindi keewi bakeeje maare ɗiɗi fuu , nde maɓɓaama bee takkugo takkanɗe joweeɗiɗi .
66005002	Mi yi'i boo malaa'ikaajo mawɗo , mo ɗon wolwa bee sawtu : " Moy foti takkitugo takkanɗe haa o maɓɓita deftere nde ? "
66005003	Ammaa koo haa asama , koo haa lesdi , koo haa joonde maayɓe , ɓe keɓaay mo waawi maɓɓitugo deftere man , malla laarugo nder maare .
66005004	Mi woyi masin ngam ɓe tawaay koo gooto mo he'i maɓɓitugo deftere malla laarugo nder maare .
66005005	Nden gooto haa ndotti'en wi'i yam : " Taa woy . Ndaa mbarooga lenyol Daawuda . Kaŋko o jaaliiɗo , o foti takkitugo takkanɗe joweeɗiɗi ɗe'e , o maɓɓita deftere man boo . "
66005006	Nden mi yi'i jawgel mbaalu ɗon dari haa caka , yeeso leeso laamu . Kuuje geete nayi e ndotti'en go ɗon taari ngel . Mi yi'i ngel , ngel nandi bana ngel meeɗi hirseego . Ngel woodi luwe joweeɗiɗi e gite joweeɗiɗi , kanje ngoni ruuhuuji Allah joweeɗiɗi ɗi o neli haa duniyaaru fuu .
66005007	Jawgel go yehi , hoo'i deftere haa juŋŋgo nyaamo jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu go .
66005008	Nde o ɗon hoo'a nde , kuuje geete nayi e ndotti'en noogas e nayo go cujidi yeeso jawgel . Koomoy maɓɓe woodi moolooru , ɓe ngoodi taasaaje kaŋgeeri keewɗe urle boo . Kanjum woni do'aaji yimɓe Allah .

66005012	Ɓe ngimi bee sawtu cembiɗɗo bana ni :

66006001	Nden mi yi'i jawgel go takkiti takkannde arande haa takkanɗe joweeɗiɗi go . Mi nani woore nder kuuje geete nayi ɗon wi'a bee sawtu bana felmaaŋgo : " War ! "
66006002	Mi yi'i puccu ndaneewu . Ba''iiɗo ngu ɗon jogi lagaawal , ɓe ndokki mo meetaleewol . O dilli , o jaaliiɗo haa o jaalo fahin .
66006003	Nde jawgel takkiti takkannde ɗiɗawre , mi nani huunde ɗiɗawre ɗon wi'a : " War ! "
66006004	Puccu feere wurti , mboɗeewu . Ɓe ndokki ba''iiɗo ngu kaafahi makki , ɓe ndokki mo baawɗe waddango duniyaaru konu , haa yimɓe mbarmbartira .
66006005	Nden jawgel takkiti takkannde tataɓre . Mi nani huunde tataɓre ɗon wi'a : " War ! " Mi yi'i puccu ɓaleewu . Ba''iiɗo ngu ɗon jogi poondirɗum kilo haa juŋŋgo muuɗum .
66006006	Mi nani ko nandi bee sawtu neɗɗo iwi caka kuuje geete nayi . Ɗum wi'i : " Taasawo alkamaari wooto malla taasaaje gawri tati woni ngeenaari kuugal nyalaade woore ! Ammaa taa saɗɗin nebbam malla inaboojam ! "
66006007	Nden jawgel takkiti takkannde nayaɓre . Mi yi'i huunde nayaɓre ɗon wi'a : " War ! "
66006008	Mi yi'i puccu puru . Ba''iiɗo ngu bi'eteeɗo Maayde , nden bi'eteeɗo Joonde-maayɓe tokki mo . Ɓe ndokkaama baawɗe dow yeɓre duniyaaru nayaɓre haa ɓe mbara yimɓe bee kaafahi , e weelo e nyaw e dabbaaji ladde .
66006009	Nden jawgel takkiti takkannde jowaɓre . Les hirsirde mi yi'i yoŋkiiji mbaraaɓe ngam waajaago wolde Allah , ngam ɓe laatino hoolaaɓe nder seedamku maɓɓe .
66006010	Ɓe kooli , ɓe mbi'i : " Ya Jawmiraawo , a baawɗo , a ceniiɗo , a gooŋgaajo ! Haa ndey min ndeenata haa a hiito yimɓe duniyaaru ngam ɓe mbari min ? "
66006011	Koomoy maɓɓe heɓi ngapaleewol daneewol , ɓe mbi'aama ɓe ciwto seɗɗa tawon , haa to limgal deerɗiraaɓe maɓɓe huuwanooɓe Allah , mbareteeɓe bana maɓɓe ciki .

66006016	Ɓe mboyani kooseeje e tapaaje : " Ndo''e dow amin , nyukkine min yeeso jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu , yeeso ɓernuki jawgel boo ! "
66006017	Ngam nyande ɓernuki maɓɓe mawnde yottake , moy munyanta nde ?
66007001	Yoo . Ɓaawoɗon mi yi'i malaa'ika'en nayo ɗon ndari haa alkibilaaji duniyaaru nayi fuu . Ɓe naŋgi keni duniyaaru nayi fuu ngam taa ɗi mbifa haa lesdi malla haa ndiyam koo haa leɗɗe boo .
66007002	Mi yi'i malaa'ikaajo goɗɗo ɗon wara diga fuunaaŋge , o jogiiɗo lamba innde Allah geeto . O towni sawtu , o wolwani malaa'ika'en nayo , ɓe Allah hokki baawɗe waɗugo bonnonda haa lesdi e ndiyam .
66007003	Malaa'ikaajo oo wi'i : " Taa mbonne lesdi , malla ndiyam , malla leɗɗe , haa to min mbaɗi lamba dow tiiɗe suka'en Allah meeɗen . "
66007004	Ɓe ngecci yam limgal waɗanaaɓe lamba Allah haa tiinde , ɓe ujine teemerre e cappanɗe nayo e nayo ( 144.000 ) iwɓe haa le'i yimɓe Isra'iila fuu ,

66007013	Gooto nder ndotti'en ?ami yam : " Ɓorniiɓe ngapaleeji daneeji ɓe'e , ɗum ɓeye , haa toy ɓe iwi ? "

66007015	Ngam maajum ɓe ɗon ndari yeeso leeso laamu Allah , ɓe ɗon kuuwana mo jemma bee naaŋge nder haykaliiru maako . Jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu ɗon ayna ɓe .

66008001	Nde jawgel takkiti takkannde joweeɗiɗawre , asama fuu de'i baakin reeta saa'a .
66008002	Nden mi yi'i malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo dariiɓe yeeso Allah keɓi luwe puufeteeɗe joweeɗiɗi .
66008003	Malaa'ikaajo feere wari , dari kombi hirsirde , o ɗon jogi taasawo wulugo urle , ngo kaŋgeeri . O heɓi urle ɗuuɗɗe haa o wula ɗe dow hirsirde kaŋgeeri dariinde yeeso leeso laamu . Nde o ɗon wula ɗe , o ɗon ɓesda ɗe haa do'aaji yimɓe Allah .
66008004	Cuurɗe urle man ummi bee do'aaji yimɓe Allah diga juuɗe malaa'ikaajo dariiɗo yeeso Allah .
66008005	Nden malaa'ikaajo hoo'i taasawo urle , hebbini ngo bee yiite dow hirsirde , sakkini ɗum haa duniyaaru . Diggaali ndiggi , hoolooji mbaɗi , ma''e ma''i , duniyaaru dimbi .
66008006	Nden malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo marɓe luwe joweeɗiɗi go taaski fuufugo ɗe .
66008007	Malaa'ikaajo arano fuufi luwal muuɗum . Mallimallooje e yiite jillindiraaɗum bee ?i?am toɓi dow lesdi . Yeɓrefe duniyaaru tataɓre e yeɓre leɗɗe tataɓre e geene fuu kalki bee yiite .
66008008	Nden malaa'ikaajo ɗiɗaɓo fuufi luwal muuɗum . Ko nandi bee hooseere mawnde wulnde yiite sakkinaama nder ndiyam . Yeɓre ndiyam tataɓre laati ?i?am ,
66008009	yeɓre kuuje ndiyam tataɓre waati , yeɓre koombooje tataɓre boo halki .
66008010	Nden malaa'ikaajo tataɓo fuufi luwal muuɗum . Horre mawnde wulnde bana pittirla do''i e asama , yani dow yeɓre maaje ndiyam tataɓre , dow ceeɓooje boo .
66008011	Innde horre man , Kaaɗeeŋga . Yeɓre ndiyam tataɓre haaɗi rok haa yimɓe maayi nde ɓe njari ɗam .
66008012	Nden malaa'ikaajo nayaɓo fuufi luwal muuɗum . Yeɓre naaŋge tataɓre fiyaama , non boo yeɓre lewru tataɓre e yeɓre koode tataɓre , haa yeɓre jayŋgol maaje tataɓre halki . Walaa jayŋgol sam haa yeɓre nyalawma tataɓre , e yeɓre jemma tataɓre .
66008013	Nden mi yi'i , mi nani dutal piiranŋgal haa dow masin ɗon wi'a bee sawtu : " Kayto , kayto ! Bone laatanto yimɓe duniyaaru fuu to hoolo fuufugo luwe malaa'ika'en luttuɓe tato waŋgi ! "
66009001	Nden malaa'ikaajo njowaɓo fuufi luwal muuɗum . Mi yi'i horre nde do''ino diga asama haa lesdi . Nde hokkaama maɓɓitirgel ngaska lugguka kalluka .
66009002	Nde maɓɓiti ngaska man . Nden cuurɗe ngurti ka bana ɗe ngurtorto suudu yiite mawndu . Cuurɗe ngaska lugguka kalluka go ɓalwini naaŋge e hawa .
66009003	Baɓɓatti ngurti cuurɗe man , caŋkiti haa lesdi , ɗi keɓi baawɗe bana jahe .
66009004	Ɗi umraama taa ɗi mbonna geene malla leɗɗe malla haako kookoye , sey yimɓe ɓe ngalaa lamba Allah haa tiiɗe muuɗum'en fuu .
66009005	Ɗi keɓaay baawɗe mbarugo yimɓe man , sey torrugo ɓe baakin lebbi jowi . Naawɗum torra baɓɓatti man nandi bee naaweeŋga nga goɗɗo nanata to yaare fiɗi mo .
66009006	Nder lebbi jowi man yimɓe ɓe'e tefan maayde , ammaa ɓe keɓataa nde . Ɓe ngeloto maayugo , ammaa maayde doggan ɓe .
66009007	Baɓɓatti go nandi bee pucci taaskaniiɗi konu . Dow ko'e maaji woodi ko nandi bee meetaleeji kaŋgeeri . Geese maaji nandi bee geese worɓe .
66009008	Gaasa maaji nandi bee gaasa rewɓe , nyi'e maaji boo nandi bee nyi'e mbarooga .
66009009	Biɓɓe maaji cuuɗaama bee ko nandi sulkeeji njamndi . Hoolo bileeji maaji nandi bee hoolo mootaaji ɗuuɗɗi ɗi pucci ndasata saa'i ɗi ɗon nasta konu .
66009010	Ɗi ngoodi bicce e tufirkoy bana ɗe jahe , bee bicce maaji ɗi ngoodi baawɗe naawnugo yimɓe baakin lebbi jowi .
66009011	Ɗi ngoodi laamɗo , kaŋko woni malaa'ikaajo kalfinaaɗo ngaska lugguka kalluka go . Innde maako bee ibraniŋkoore Abadon , bee yunaniŋkoore boo Apolliyon , waato Kalkoowo .
66009012	Torra arana saali , ammaa torraaji goɗɗi ɗiɗi tammi warugo .
66009013	Nden malaa'ikaajo njoweegoojo fuufi luwal muuɗum . Mi nani sawtu iwi haa tolɗi hirsirde kaŋgeeri dariinde yeeso Allah .
66009014	Sawtu go wolwani malaa'ikaajo njoweegoojo jogiiɗo luwal , wi'i : " Yoof malaa'ika'en nayo haɓɓaaɓe haa maayo maŋgo wi'eteeŋgo Efratis ! "
66009015	Ɓe pisti malaa'ika'en man . Kamɓe ɓe ɗonno taaski , nder lewru ndu'u e nyalaade nde'e e saa'iire nde'e , ɓe mbara yeɓre tataɓre nder yimɓe fuu .
66009016	Ɓe ngecci yam limgal wa''iiɓe pucci konu , ɓe miliyoŋji teemeɗɗe ɗiɗo ( 200.000.000 ) .
66009017	Nder wahayu am mi yi'i pucci e wa''iiɓe ɗi . Ɓe ngoodi sulkeeji boɗeeji coy bana yiite , carwinaaɗi bana safira , ooli bana baruudufi . Ko'e pucci maɓɓe nandi bee ko'e barooɗe , nder kunduɗe maaji yiite e cuurɗe e baruudu ngurti .
66009018	Yiite e cuurɗe e baruudu go ngoni masiibooji tati . Ɗi ngurti kunduɗe pucci , ɗi mbari yeɓre yimɓe tataɓre .
66009019	Ngam baawɗe pucci nder kunduɗe maaji e nder bicce maaji ngoni . Bicce maaji nandi bee boɗɗe , bicce man ngoodi ko'e . Bee bicce maaji ɗi ɗon naawna yimɓe .
66009020	Luttuɓe yimɓe ɓe masiibooji ɗi'i mbaraay , ɓe accaay kuuɗe maɓɓe . Ɓe accaay sujidango ginnaaji , e labbi kuuwraaɗi bee kaŋgeeri e cardi e njamndi mboɗeeri e kaa'e e leɗɗe , ɗi mbaawataa laarugo koo nanugo koo yahugo .
66009021	Yimɓe ɓe'e , ɓe accaay waɗugo mbar-hoore e hiila e halleende e nguyka .
66010001	Nden mi yi'i malaa'ikaajo cembiɗɗo ɗon jippo asama . O ɗon ɓorni ruuldere , timotimooŋgal ɗon taari hoore maako , yeeso maako ɗon yayna bana naaŋge , kosɗe maako nandi bee mooci yiite .
66010002	Nder juŋŋgo maako o jogi deftel maɓɓitaaŋgel . O jo''ini kosŋgal maako nyaamal dow mbeela , nanal boo dow lesdi ,
66010003	o towni sawtu , o wolwi bana bojji mbarooga . Nde o wolwi bana ni , pelmaali joweeɗiɗi njaabi mo bee hoolo .
66010004	Nde ɗi timmini wolwugo , mi taaskani windugo . Ammaa mi nani sawtu wolwani yam diga asama : " Taa windu ko pelmaali joweeɗiɗi mbolwi , taa yeccu ɗum koomoy . "
66010005	Nden malaa'ikaajo mo mi yi'i ɗon dari dow mbeela e dow lesdi , ɓaŋgti juŋŋgo muuɗum nyaamo haa asama ,
66010006	huni bee innde Allah , geeto haa foroy , tagɗo asama e lesdi e ko woni ton fuu , tagɗo mbeela boo e ko woni ton fuu . Malaa'ikaajo go wi'i : " Ko waɗanno , waɗan jonta !
66010007	Ammaa to malaa'ikaajo njoweeɗiɗaɓo fuufi luwal muuɗum , Allah timmitinan anniya muuɗum sirriiha , bana o yeccino suka'en maako , waato annabo'en maako . "
66010008	Nden sawtu mo nannoomi wolwi haa asama , wolwani yam fahin , wi'i : " Yah , hoo'u deftel maɓɓitaaŋgel haa juŋŋgo malaa'ikaajo dariiɗo dow mbeela e dow lesdi . "
66010009	Mi yehi haa malaa'ikaajo , mi tori mo o hokkammi deftel go . O wi'i yam : " Hoo'u ngel , nyaam , ngel dakman bana njumri nder hunduko maaɗa , ammaa ngel haaɗan nder reedu maaɗa . "
66010010	Mi hoo'i deftel haa juŋŋgo maako , mi nyaami ngel , ngel dakmi nder hunduko am . Ammaa nde mi moɗi ngel , ngel haaɗi nder reedu am .
66010011	Nden goɗɗo wi'i yam : " Nde woore fahin wolwu habaru Allah dow yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe e ummaatooje e ɗemɗe e laamiiɓe . "
66011001	Nden goɗɗo hokki yam kewal poondirgal , ngal nandi bee sawru . O wi'i yam : " Umma , foondu haykaliiru bee hirsirde maaru , lim sujidooɓe ton .
66011002	Ammaa taa foondu jawleeji haykaliiru , ngam ɗi ndokkaama haa juuɗe heefeerɓe . Ɓe njaaɓtan berniwol ceniiŋgol baakin lebbi cappanɗe nayi e ɗiɗi ( 42 ) .
66011003	Mi nelan seedooɓe am ɗiɗo , ɓorniiɓe limce buhuuje , ɓe ngaajoto habaru Allah balɗe ujineere e teemeɗɗe ɗiɗi e cappanɗe joweego ( 1.260 ) . "
66011004	Seedooɓe ɗiɗo man ngoni jaytunje ɗiɗi e pittirlaaji ɗiɗi ɓe ɗon ndari yeeso Jawmiraawo duniyaaru .
66011005	To goɗɗo tefi naawnugo ɓe , yiite wurtoto kunduɗe maɓɓe , halkan konne'en maɓɓe . Bana ni koomoy tefi naawnugo ɓe , o mbareteeɗo .
66011006	Ɓe ngoodi baawɗe maɓɓugo asama ngam taa iyeende toɓa yaake ɓe ɗon ngaajo habaru Allah . Ɓe ngoodi baawɗe waylititgo ceeɓooje ndiyam , ɗe laato ?i?am . Ɓe ngoodi baawɗe fiyugo duniyaaru boo bee masiibooji koondey ɓe ngiɗi .
66011007	To ɓe timmini waaju maɓɓe , kuuŋga wurtoto ngaska lugguka kalluka go , nga haɓan bee maɓɓe . Nga jaaloto ɓe , nga mbaran ɓe .
66011008	Ɓalli maɓɓe mbaaloto haa laawol berniwol maŋgol haa nokkuure ɓe ɓilno Jawmiraawo maɓɓe dow leggal gaafaaŋgal . Soomoore berniwol ngol woni " Sodoma " malla " Misra " .
66011009	Yimɓe iwɓe haa ummaatooje e le'i e lesɗe e wolwanɓe bolle feere feere fuu ngi'an ɓalli maɓɓe balɗe tati bee reeta , ɓe nduŋgantaako koomoy uwa ɓe .
66011010	Yimɓe duniyaaru ceyorto maayde seedooɓe ɗiɗo ɓe'e . Ɓe mbaɗan juulde , ɓe ndokkindiran caahuuji , ngam annabo'en ɓe'e torri yimɓe duniyaaru masin .
66011011	Ɓaawo balɗe tati bee reeta Allah yeeɗitini ɓe bee poofɗe mum , ɗe nasti nder maɓɓe . Ɓe ummiti , ɓe ndari . Yi'ɓe ɗum fuu kultori .
66011012	Nden annabo'en ɗiɗo nani sawtu cembiɗɗo mo asama ɗon wolwana ɓe : " Ngare haa ɗo . " Ɓe eeŋgi haa asama nder ruuldere . Konne'en maɓɓe ɗon ndaara .
66011013	Saa'i man nden , lesdi dimbi masin haa yeɓre berniwol sappoore halki . Dimbannde maajum halki yimɓe ujine njoweeɗiɗo ( 7.000 ) . Yimɓe luttuɓe kultori , leestani Allah mo asama .
66011014	Torra ɗiɗaɓa timmi , ammaa kakkile , torra tataɓa ɓadake yottaago .
66011015	Nden malaa'ikaajo njoweeɗiɗaɓo fuufi luwal muuɗum . Mi nani sawtuuji cembiɗɗi nder asama , ɗi ɗon mbi'a : " Jonta baawɗe laamanaago duniyaaru laatani Jawmiraawo meeɗen , e Almasiihu muuɗum , o laamoto haa foroy . "
66011016	Nden ndotti'en noogas e nayo jooɗiiɓe yeeso Allah go cujidi , cujidani Allah .
66011017	Ɓe mbi'i :
66011018	Wakkati ɓernuki ma e kiita ma dow maayɓe waɗi ,
66011019	Haykaliiru Allah haa asama maɓɓiti , haa goɗɗo waawi yi'ugo sundukru seedamku alkawal nder maaru . Nden ma''e ma''i , hoolooji mbaɗi , pelmaali mbaɗi , duniyaaru dimbi , mallimallooje loorɗe toɓi .
66012001	Nden alaama makka waŋgi haa asama . Woodi debbo ɓorniiɗo naaŋge bana limce , lewru ɗon les kosɗe maako , o meeti meetaleewol koode sappo e ɗiɗi .
66012002	O ɓadake ɓesnugo , luuwe ɗon torri mo haa o wooki .
66012003	Alaama ngoɗka waŋgi haa asama . Woodi kuuŋga maŋga mboɗeewa , marŋga ko'e joweeɗiɗi e luwe sappo , bee meetaleewol dow hoore koondeye .
66012004	Bee wicco maaga nga faɗɗi yeɓre koode tataɓre haa asama , nga do''i ɗe haa duniyaaru . Nga dari yeeso debbo ɓadiiɗo ɓesnugo go ngam haa , to ɓiŋgel danyaama , nga nyaama ngel law .
66012005	Nden debbo go ɓesni ɓiŋgel gorgel , laamantooŋgel lesɗe fuu bee sawru njamndi . Ammaa ɓiŋgel wiftaama , yahraama haa leeso laamu Allah .
66012006	Debbo doggi haa ladde . Haa ton Allah taaskitinanno mo nokkuure . O aynaama ton balɗe ujineere e teemeɗɗe ɗiɗi e cappanɗe joweego ( 1.260 ) .
66012007	Nden haɓre waɗi haa asama . Mika'iilu e malaa'ika'en muuɗum kaɓi bee kuuŋga go . Kaŋga boo nga haɓi bee maɓɓe bee walliinde malaa'ika'en maaga .
66012008	Ammaa Mika'iilu'en njaali nga . Kaŋga e malaa'ika'en maaga fuu keɓaay jooɗaago haa asama ɓaawoɗon .
66012009	Nga sakkinaama yaasi . Kaŋga woni mboodi nayeeri , mbi'eteendi Iblisa malla Sayɗaanu , mo jambi yimɓe duniyaaru fuu . O sakkinaama haa lesdi , kaŋko e malaa'ika'en maako fuu .
66012010	Nden mi nani sawtu cembiɗɗo haa asama ɗon wi'a : " Kisndam Allah yottake jonta ! Jonta Allah waŋgini baawɗe laamu muuɗum . Jonta Almasiihu maako waŋgini baawɗe muuɗum . Ngam gullotonooɗo deerɗiraaɓe meeɗen yeeso Allah , mo ɗonno wullo ɓe jemma bee naaŋge fuu , o sakkinaama yaasi asama .
66012011	Deerɗiraaɓe meeɗen njaali mo bee ?i?am jawgel e bee gooŋga ka ɓe ngaaji . Ɓe ngerdi hokkugo yoŋkiiji maɓɓe , ɓe maaya boo .
66012012	Ngam maajum ceye , onon asamanji , e onon jooɗiiɓe ton ! Ammaa bone laatanto lesdi e mbeela . Ngam Iblisa jippanake on , o ɓerni masin ngam o anndi wakkati seɗɗa tan luttani mo . "
66012013	Nde kuuŋga annditi nga sakkinaama haa lesdi , nga fuɗɗi taasnugo debbo ɓesnuɗo ɓiŋgel gorgel go .
66012014	Debbo hokkaama bileeji ɗiɗi ngam haa o fiira haa nokkuure maako nder ladde . Haa ton ɓe aynan mo duuɓi tati bee reeta , haa mboodi go heɓataa meemugo mo .
66012015	Nden mboodi tuuti ndiyam bana maayo , ngam haa ɗam tokko debbo , ɗam ilna mo .
66012016	Ammaa lesdi walli debbo . Ndi maɓɓiti hunduko maari , ndi yari ndiyam ngurtiiɗam hunduko kuuŋga .
66012017	Nden kuuŋga tikkani debbo , nga dilli haɓugo bee luttuɓe asŋgol maako , waato ɗowtaniiɓe umrooje Allah , tabitɓe nder gooŋga ka Yeesu waŋginani ɓe .
66013001	Kuuŋga dari haa fomoonde mbeela . Nden mi yi'i ndabbaawa ɗon wurto mbeela . Nga woodi luwe sappo e ko'e joweeɗiɗi . Meetaleewol ɗon dow luwal kooŋgale , inɗe kuɗanɗe Allah mbindaama dow ko'e maaga .
66013002	Ndabbaawa nga ngi'mi , nandi bee cirgu , kosɗe maaga nandi bee kosɗe huunde ladde feere , hunduko maaga nandi bee hunduko mbarooga . Kuuŋga go hokki ndabbaawa man sembe mum e laamu mum e baawɗe mum mawɗe .
66013003	Mi yi'i woore haa ko'e ndabbaawa man , nde nandi bana nde meeɗi mbareego , ammaa huuduure maajum yamɗiti . Yimɓe duniyaaru fuu kayɗini , ɓe tokki ndabbaawa man .
66013004	Yimɓe fuu cujidani kuuŋga ngam nga hokkino ndabbaawa baawɗe maaga . Ɓe cujidani ndabbaawa boo , ɓe mbi'i : " Moy nandi bee ndabbaawa nga'a ? Moy he'i haɓugo bee maaga ? "
66013005	Ndabbaawa heɓi baawɗe wolwugo kalluka dow Allah , nga heɓi huuwtinirgo baawɗe maaga lebbi cappanɗe nayi e ɗiɗi ( 42 ) .
66013006	Nga fuɗɗi huɗugo Allah e innde maako e joonde maako e jooɗiiɓe asama fuu .
66013007	Nga heɓi baawɗe haɓugo bee yimɓe Allah haa nga jaalo ɓe , nga heɓi baawɗe dow ummaatooje e le'i e wolwanɓe bolle feere feere fuu .
66013008	Jooɗiiɓe haa duniyaaru fuu cujidanan nga , waato koomoy mo innde muuɗum windaaka nder deftere ngeendam diga fuɗɗam duniyaaru . Jawgel kirsaaŋgel go mari deftere nde .
66013009	" Koomoy mari noppi , sey o nana !
66013010	Mo hoddirana naŋgeego , o naŋgeteeɗo . Mo hoddirana mbareego bee kaafahi , o mbareteeɗo . Ngam maajum sey yimɓe Allah njogo munyal e nuɗɗinki . "
66013011	Nden mi yi'i ndabbaawa ngoɗŋga ɗon wurto nder lesdi . Nga woodi luwe ɗiɗi bana luwe jawgel , nga wolwi bana kuuŋga go .
66013012	Nga huuwtiniri baawɗe mawɗe bana ɗe ndabbaawa aartuŋga . Aartuŋga man boo , nga ɗon laara . Ndabbaawa ɗiɗaɓa dooli duniyaaru e jooɗiiɓe haa maaru fuu ɓe cujidana ndabbaawa aartuŋga , nga huuduure mum hallundeno yamɗiti .
66013013	Ndabbaawa ɗiɗaɓa waɗi kuuje kaayeefiije mawɗe . Nga jippini yiite diga asama haa lesdi , gite yimɓe fuu .
66013014	Nga esti yimɓe duniyaaru fuu bee waɗugo kaayeefiiji ɗi nga heɓi baawɗe waɗugo yeeso ndabbaawa aartuŋga . Ndabbaawa ɗiɗaɓa yecci yimɓe duniyaaru fuu ɓe maha foto ndabbaawa njuwaaŋga , yamɗiti , ngam maŋgtugo nga .
66013015	Ndabbaawa ɗiɗaɓa heɓi baawɗe nastingo poofɗe yoŋki haa nder foto ndabbaawa aartuŋga , haa foto man wolwi , haa nga mbara koomoy mo sujidanaay nga .
66013016	Ndabbaawa dooli yimɓe fuu , leesɓe e mawɓe , riskuɓe e talaka'en , maccuɓe e rimɓe , ɓe njaɓa lamba maaga dow juuɗe maɓɓe nyaame e dow tiiɗe maɓɓe .
66013017	Walaa mo heɓata soodugo malla soorrugo kooɗume , sonaa to o woodi lamba man , waato innde ndabbaawa malla lamba innde man .
66013018	Sey goɗɗo mara anndal ngam faamugo haala ka'a . Marɗo hakkiilo waawan heɓtugo maana lamba ndabbaawa , ngam lamba man ɗon dari mbattudi innde neɗɗo . Lamba maajum woni teemeɗɗe joweego e cappanɗe joweego e joweego ( 666 ) .
66014001	Nden mi laari , ndaa jawgel ɗon dari dow hooseere Siyona . Yimɓe ujine teemerre e cappanɗe nayo e nayo ( 144.000 ) ɗon ngondi bee maagel . Ɓe fuu , innde maagel e innde Baabiraawo maagel ɗon dow tiiɗe maɓɓe .
66014002	Mi nani hoolo haa asama ngo nandi bee hoolo maayo maŋgo ilanŋgo dow tapaaje , ngo nandi bee pelmaali boo . Ko nanmi , ɗum nandi bee sawtu moolooji to fiyooɓe ɗon piya ɗi .
66014003	Yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe go ɗon ndari yeeso leeso laamu e yeeso kuuje geete nayi e yeeso ndotti'en , ɓe ɗon ngima yimre hesre . Walaa keɓɗo ekkitaago yimre nde'e , sonaa yimɓe ujine teemerre e cappanɗe nayo e nayo ( 144.000 ) , soottaaɓe haa duniyaaru go .
66014004	Worɓe ɓe'e , ɓe ayni ko'e maɓɓe nder senaare ngam ɓe mbaaldaay bee rewɓe , ɓe te'aaka . Ɓe ɗon tokko jawgel haa ngel yahata fuu , ɓe soottaaɓe nder luttuɓe yimɓe , ɓe aarti lii'aneego Allah e jawgel .
66014005	Walaa mo nani fewre haa kunduɗe maɓɓe , ɓe ngalaa aybe .
66014006	Nden mi yi'i malaa'ikaajo goɗɗo ɗon fiira haa dow nder hawa , o woodi kubaruwol ceynoowol ngol re'ataa . O tammi waajingo ngol yimɓe duniyaaru , iwɓe haa ummaatooje e le'i e ɗemɗe fuu .
66014007	O towni sawtu , o wi'i : " Kule Allah , maŋgte maŋgu maako ! Ngam wakkati yottake haa o hiito yimɓe . Ngam maajum cujidane Allah tagɗo asama e lesdi , e mbeela e ceeɓooje ndiyam ! "
66014008	Malaa'ikaajo ɗiɗaɓo tokki arano , wi'i : " Ngol do''ake , Baabila , berniwol maŋgol do''ake . Ngol yarni ummaatooje fuu inaboojam , waato inaboojam nyaaɗɗam ɗam suuno maagol halluŋgo . "
66014009	Malaa'ikaajo tataɓo tokki arano e ɗiɗaɓo , o towni sawtu , o wi'i : " Koomoy sujidani ndabbaawa e foto maaga , jaɓi lamba maaga haa tiinde malla haa juŋŋgo boo ,
66014010	kaŋko yarata inaboojam Allah ɗam ɓernuki maako . O jillaay ɗam bee ndiyam , o rufi ɗam nder jardugel ɓernuki maako . Koomoy sujidani ndabbaawa , o torreteeɗo nder yiite e baruudu yeeso malaa'ika'en seniiɓe e yeeso jawgel .
66014011	Cuurɗe yiite torranŋge ɓe , ummoto hedi asama haa foroy . Koomoy sujidani ndabbaawa e foto maaga , jaɓi lamba innde maaga boo , siwtataako sam , koo jemma koo naaŋge . "
66014012	Ngam maajum sey yimɓe Allah , ɗowtantooɓe umrooje maako , tokkiiɓe Yeesu bee gooŋga mara munyal .
66014013	Nden mi nani sawtu haa asama ɗon wi'a : " Windu : Barka laatanto maayanɓe nder kuugal Allah . " Ruuhu jaabi : " Nonnon , ɓe ceyorto siwtaago e kuuɗe maɓɓe caatuɗe , ngam nafuda kuuɗe maɓɓe wondan bee maɓɓe . "
66014014	Nden mi yi'i ruuldere raneere . Dow ruuldere man tagdi nandundi bee gorko ɗon jooɗi . Meetaleewol kaŋgeeri ɗon dow hoore maako . O ɗon jogi wafdu welndu haa juŋŋgo maako boo .
66014015	Malaa'ikaajo goɗɗo wurti haykaliiru , towni sawtu , wi'i jooɗiiɗo dow ruuldere : " Hoo'u wafdu maaɗa , sodu , ngam wakkati codol waɗi , lesdi ɓendi deydey codol . "
66014016	Nden jooɗiiɗo dow ruuldere wiiki wafdu muuɗum dow lesdi , ?aamnde lesdi sodaama .
66014017	Mi yi'i malaa'ikaajo goɗɗo ɗon wurto haykaliiru nder asama . Kaŋko boo o woodi wafdu welndu .
66014018	Malaa'ikaajo goɗɗo fahin wari diga hirsirde , kaŋko o kalfinaaɗo yiite . O towni sawtu , o wi'i malaa'ikaajo jogiiɗo wafdu welndu go : " Hoo'u wafdu maaɗa , sodu ɓiɓɓe inabooje haa ngesa duniyaaru , ngam ɓiɓɓe man ɓendi ! "
66014019	Malaa'ikaajo wiiki wafdu muuɗum haa lesdi , ndu ta''i ɓiɓɓe inabooje , sakkini ɗe nder ɓiɗɗirɗum mawɗum ɗum ɓernuki Allah .
66014020	Ɓiɓɓe inabooje ɓiɗɗaama nder ɓiɗɗirɗum haa yaasi berniwol . Maayo ?i?am wurti ɓiɗɗirɗum man . Njuutirka maago yotti kilomeeta teemeɗɗe tati ( 300 ) , luggeeŋga maago boo baakin piyanɗe tati .
66015001	Nden mi yi'i alaama ngoɗka kayɗiniika haa asama : Malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo jogiiɓe masiibooji joweeɗiɗi . Kanji ngoni masiibooji ragareeji , bee maaji ɓernuki Allah timman .
66015002	Nden mi yi'i ko nandi bee mbeela daarorgal , njillindiraaŋga bee yiite . Mi yi'i boo jaaliiɓe kuuŋga e foto maaga e mo innde muuɗum woni lamba go . Ɓe ndari kombi mbeela daarorgal , ɓe njogi moolooji ɗi Allah hokkuno ɓe .
66015003	Ɓe ɗon ngima yimre Muusa , suka Allah , ɓe ɗon ngima yimre jawgel boo bana ni :
66015004	Moy mo hulataa ma , ya Jawmiraawo ?
66015005	Ɓaawoɗon mi yi'i , ndaa haykaliiru nder asama , laymaaru fottirde Allah bee yimɓe , ndu maɓɓiti .
66015006	Malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo jogiiɓe masiibooji joweeɗiɗi ragareeji ngurti haykaliiru . Ɓe ɗon ɓorni limce daneeje tal , ɓe ɗon taadi taadorli kaŋgeeri haa biɓɓe maɓɓe .
66015007	Woore haa kuuje geete nayi go hokki malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo taasaaje joweeɗiɗi keewɗe ɓernuki Allah geeto haa foroy .
66015008	Haykaliiru heewi cuurɗe iwɗe haa tedduŋgal Allah e baawɗe muuɗum . Walaa mo waawi nastugo haykaliiru haa to malaa'ika'en timmini masiibooji joweeɗiɗi go .
66016001	Nden mi nani sawtu cembiɗɗo haa haykaliiru ɗon wi'a malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo go : " Njehe , ndufe taasaaje ɓernuki Allah joweeɗiɗi haa duniyaaru ! "
66016002	Malaa'ikaajo arano dilli , rufi ko woni nder taasawo muuɗum haa duniyaaru . Kuuduuje kalluɗe naawɗe mbaɗi haa marɓe lamba ndabbaawa , haa sujidanooɓe foto maaga boo .
66016003	Nden malaa'ikaajo ɗiɗaɓo rufi ko woni nder taasawo muuɗum haa mbeela . Ndiyam maaga warti bana ?i?am maayɗo , haa kuuje nder mbeela fuu mbaati .
66016004	Nden malaa'ikaajo tataɓo rufi ko woni nder taasawo muuɗum haa maaje ilooje e ceeɓooje ndiyam , ɗe ngarti ?i?am .
66016005	Mi nani malaa'ikaajo kalfinaaɗo ndiyam wi'i : " An woni Ceniiɗo , a ɗonno ɓooyma , a ɗon jonta boo , an woni gooŋgaajo nder kiitaaji ɗi mbaɗata .
66016006	Yimɓe ɓe'e ndufi ?i?am yimɓe maaɗa e ?i?am annabo'en maaɗa , ngam maajum a yarni ɓe ?i?am . Ɓe keɓi ko haanani ɓe ! "
66016007	Nden mi nani sawtu haa hirsirde ɗon wi'a : " Nonnon , ya Allah Jawmiraawo , marɗo baawɗe dow kooɗume fuu , a ɗon hiito bee gooŋga bana no fotti . "
66016008	Nden malaa'ikaajo nayaɓo rufi ko woni nder taasawo muuɗum haa naaŋge . Nge hokkaama baawɗe wulugo yimɓe bee yiite wulŋge jaw .
66016009	Yiite wulŋge nge'e wuli yimɓe haa ɓe kuɗi innde Allah , marɗo baawɗe dow masiibooji ɗi'i . Ammaa ɓe cali tuubugo , ɓe cali leestango Allah .
66016010	Nden malaa'ikaajo njowaɓo rufi ko woni nder taasawo muuɗum dow leeso laamu ndabbaawa . Nyiɓre waɗi nder laamu maaga fuu . Yimɓe ngati ɗemɗe maɓɓe ngam naaweeŋga maɓɓe ,
66016011	ɓe kuɗi Allah mo asama ngam naaweeŋga maɓɓe e kuuduuje maɓɓe . Ammaa ɓe cali accugo kuuɗe maɓɓe kalluɗe .
66016012	Nden malaa'ikaajo njoweegoojo rufi ko woni nder taasawo muuɗum dow maayo maŋgo wi'eteeŋgo Efratis . Ngo ɓeeɓi , ngo yoori , haa laamiiɓe fuunaaŋge keɓi laawol saalaago ton .
66016013	Nden mi yi'i ginnaaji tati coɓɗi , ɗi nandi bee paaɓi , ɗi ɗon ngurto hunduko kuuŋga e hunduko ndabbaawa e hunduko annaboojo pewoowo .
66016014	Ginnaaji ɗi'i iwi haa Sayɗaanu , ɗi mbaawi huuwugo kuuɗe kaayeefiije . Ɗi njehi haa laamiiɓe duniyaaru fuu , haa ɗi mooɓta ɓe ngam konu haa nyalaade mawnde nde Allah , Jawmiraawo dow kooɗume fuu .
66016015	" Nane ! Mi ɗon wara bana gujjo ! Barka laatanto aynuɗo , kakkilananɗo limce muuɗum ngam taa o yaha o tembo , taa o semta yeeso yimɓe ! "
66016016	Ginnaaji go mooɓti laamiiɓe haa nokkuure wi'eteende bee ibraniŋkoore Harmagedon .
66016017	Nden malaa'ikaajo njoweeɗiɗaɓo rufi ko woni nder taasawo muuɗum haa hawa . Sawtu cembiɗɗo iwi haa leeso laamu nder haykaliiru , wi'i : " Ɗum timmi ! "
66016018	Ma''e ma''i , hoolooji mbaɗi , pelmaali mbaɗi , lesdi dimbi masin . Lesdi meeɗaay dimbaago bana non sam diga yimɓe ɗon haa duniyaaru .
66016019	Berniwol maŋgol sendaama geɓe tati , berniiji lesdi fuu kalki . Allah siftori Baabila , berniwol maŋgol , o yarni ngol inaboojam nder jardugel , waato inaboojam ɓernuki maako saatuki .
66016020	Duuɗe fuu kalki , kooseeje fuu majji .
66016021	Kaa'e mallimallooje loorɗe toɓi diga asama dow yimɓe , teddeeŋga woore maaje baakin kilo cappanɗe nayi ( 40 ) . Yimɓe kuɗi Allah ngam masiibo mallimallooje , ngam ɗum halli masin .
66017001	Nden gooto haa malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo jogiiɓe taasaaje joweeɗiɗi go wari haa am , wi'i yam : " War , mi hollete no daakaareejo mawɗo hiitorte , waato berniwol maŋgol nyiɓaaŋgol kombi maaje ilooje ɗuuɗɗe .
66017002	Laamiiɓe duniyaaru mbaɗi njeenu bee maako , yimɓe duniyaaru nguyki bee inaboojam daakaareeku maako . "
66017003	Ruuhu hoosi yam , malaa'ikaajo yahri yam haa ladde . Ton mi yi'i debbo ba''iiɗo ndabbaawa mboɗeewa . Inɗe kuɗanɗe Allah mbindaama dow ndabbaawa man , nga woodi ko'e joweeɗiɗi e luwe sappo .
66017004	Debbo man ɗon ɓorni limce boɗeeje e boɗeeje coy , o pawniiɗo bee kaŋgeeri e kaa'e marɗe saman e luuluuje . O ɗon jogi jardugel kaŋgeeri haa juŋŋgo maako , ngel heewi kuuje karamɗe coɓɗe ɗe daakaareeku maako .
66017005	Haa tiinde maako innde bee maana cuuɗiika windaama : " Baabila maŋgol , daada daakaare'en e nyidduɓe fuu haa duniyaaru . "
66017006	Mi yi'i debbo man wuyki bee ?i?am yimɓe Allah , e bee ?i?am mbaraaɓe ngam ɓe accaay haala Yeesu .
66017007	Malaa'ikaajo go ?ami yam : " Ko hayɗinte ? Mi waŋginante sirri debbo e ndabbaawa nga o wa''i , marŋga ko'e joweeɗiɗi e luwe sappo .
66017008	Ndabbaawa nga a yi'i , nga ɗonno naane , ammaa jonta nga walaa . Nga ɓadake wurtaago ngaska lugguka kalluka , nga dillan haa halkere . Yimɓe duniyaaru ɓe inɗe muuɗum'en mbindaaka nder deftere ngeendam diga fuɗɗam duniyaaru , ɓe kayɗinan to ɓe ngi'i ndabbaawa nga . Ngam nga ɗonno naane , nga walaa jonta , ammaa nga wartan fahin .
66017009	" Ngam faamugo ɗum , sey goɗɗo mara hakkiilo e hikma . Ko'e joweeɗiɗi go ɗum kooseeje joweeɗiɗi . Debbo go ɗon jooɗi dow maaje . Kanje ngoni laamiiɓe njoweeɗiɗo boo ,
66017010	njowo ndo''i , gooto ɗon laami , gooto boo waraay tawon . To o wari , o neeɓataa nder laamu .
66017011	Ndabbaawa nga ɗonno naane , ammaa nga walaa jonta , kaŋga woni laamiiɗo njoweetataɓo , o gooto nder njoweeɗiɗaɓo boo , ammaa o dillan haa halkere .
66017012	" Luwe sappo ɗe ngi'ɗa ngoni laamiiɓe sappo , ɓe puɗɗaay laamaago tawon , ammaa saa'a ngoota non ɓe laamodoto bee ndabbaawa .
66017013	Ɓe sappo fuu ɓe ngoodi hakkiilo wooto , ɓe ndokkan ndabbaawa baawɗe maɓɓe e maŋgu maɓɓe .
66017014	Ɓe kaɓan bee jawgel . Ammaa jawgel bee tokkiiɓe muuɗum ewnaaɓe suɓaaɓe hoolaaɓe njaaloto ɓe , ngam kaŋgel woni Jawmiraawo jawmiraaɓe e Laamiiɗo laamiiɓe . "
66017015	Malaa'ikaajo go wolwani yam fahin , wi'i : " A yi'i ndiyamji ɗi debbo go jooɗi dow maaji . Kanjum woni yimɓe e jama'aaje e ummaatooje e ɗemɗe yimɓe .
66017016	Luwe sappo ɗe ngi'ɗa e ndabbaawa fuu , nganyan daakaareejo go . Ɓe koosan ko o mari fuu , ɓe accan mo o tembo , ɓe nyaaman kusel ɓandu maako , ɓe kalkan mo bee yiite .
66017017	Ngam Allah ɗowi ɓerɗe maɓɓe haa ɓe kuuwa muuyo maako , ɓe kuuwa bee hakkiilo wooto , ɓe ndokka ndabbaawa baawɗe laamaago haa to bolle Allah ngooŋɗi .
66017018	" Debbo mo a yi'i , kaŋko woni berniwol maŋgol ngol laamanto laamiiɓe duniyaaru . "
66018001	Ɓaawoɗon mi yi'i malaa'ikaajo goɗɗo ɗon jippo diga asama . O woodi baawɗe mawɗe , daraja maako yaynani duniyaaru fuu .
66018002	O towni sawtu , o wi'i : " Ngol do''ake ! Baabila , berniwol maŋgol do''ake ! Ngol heewi ginnaaji coɓɗi karamɗi . Kooɗiye colli coɓɗi karamɗi ɗon njooɗi ton .
66018003	Ngam ngol yarni yimɓe fuu inaboojam maagol , waato inaboojam nyaaɗɗam ɗam suuno maagol halluŋgo . Laamiiɓe duniyaaru fuu mbaɗi njeenu bee maako , filooɓe duniyaaru ndiski bee suuno maagol , ngo walaa keerol . "
66018004	Nden mi nani sawtu feere haa asama ɗon wi'a :
66018005	Ngam hakkeeji maagol ɗuuɗi ,
66018006	Mbaɗe ngol bana no ngol waɗani on ,
66018007	Ɗuɗɗine torra maagol e bojji maagol
66018008	Ngam maajum masiibooji maagol ukkanto ngol nyande woore :
66018009	Laamiiɓe duniyaaru hawtuɓe bee maagol nder njeenu e suuno , ɓe mboyan , ɓe ngookan to ɓe ngi'i cuurɗe guleeki maagol .
66018010	Ɓe ndaroto daayiiɗum , ngam ɓe kulan torra maagol , ɓe mbi'an : " Kayto ! Kayto ! Baabila maŋgol , Baabila cembiɗŋgol ! Nder saa'a ngoota a hiitaama ! "
66018011	Filooɓe duniyaaru boo mboyan , ngookan ngam maagol , ngam walaa mo soodata kuuje maɓɓe ɗe'e :
66018012	Kaŋgeeri e cardi , kaa'e marɗe saman , luuluuje , turmiiji , limce boɗeeje , siliki , limce boɗeeje coy , leɗɗe caɗɗe feere feere , kuuje kuuwraaɗe bee nyi'e nyiibi e bee leɗɗe marɗe saman , njamndi mboɗeeri , njamndi ɓaleeri , kaa'e Asta ,
66018013	cittaaje belɗe , nebbam ngujorɗam , urdi mirra , urle guleteeɗe , inaboojam , nebbam , kuroori , alkamaari , na'i , baali , pucci , mootaaji pucci , maccuɓe , koo yoŋkiiji yimɓe boo .
66018014	Filooɓe mbi'ani ngol : " Kuuje maaɗa booɗɗe ɗe ngiɗɗa marugo fuu ɗe majji , risku maaɗa e pawne maaɗa fuu kalki , a meetataa heɓtugo ɗe fahin ! "
66018015	Filooɓe riskuɓe bee filu nder maagol ndaroto daayiiɗum ngam kulol torra maagol . Ɓe mboyan , ɓe ngookan ,
66018016	ɓe mbi'an : " Kayto ! Kayto ! Berniwol maŋgol ! Ngol ɓornino limce daneeje e boɗeeje , e boɗeeje coy . Ngol fawnaama bee kuuje kaŋgeeri , bee kaa'e marɗe saman e bee luuluuje !
66018017	Nder saa'a ngoota risku man fuu majjiri ngol ! "
66018018	ɓe ngooki nde ɓe ngi'i cuurɗe guleeki maagol , ɓe mbi'i : " Walaa berniwol feere foti bee berniwol ngo'ol ! "
66018019	Ɓe ndufi mbulwuldi dow ko'e maɓɓe , ɓe ngooki , ɓe mboyi : " Kayto ! Kayto ! Berniwol maŋgol ! Kaŋgol woni berniwol ngol koombooje mbeela fuu ndiski bee risku muuɗum . Nder saa'a ngoota kuuje fuu majjiri ngol . "
66018020	" An asama , seya ngam halkere maagol ! Ceye , onon yimɓe Allah , nelaaɓe e annabo'en ! Ngam Allah hiiti ngol , lornani ngol ko ngol waɗi on fuu . "
66018021	Nden malaa'ikaajo cembiɗɗo hoosi hayre mawnde bana namarde mawnde , sakkini nde haa mbeela , wi'i : " Baabila , berniwol maŋgol sakkinte bee sembe bana ni , goɗɗo meetataa yi'ugo ngol fahin .
66018022	Haraka fiyooɓe moolooji e yimooɓe e fuufooɓe luwe e fuufooɓe algaytaaji meetataa naneego nder maaɗa ! Walaa kuuwɗo sanaa'a kookaye meetata taweego nder maaɗa , haraka namooɓe meetataa naneego .
66018023	Jayŋgol pittirla meetataa yi'eego nder maaɗa , sawtuuji te'ɓe e te'aaɓe meetataa naneego nder maaɗa . Filooɓe maaɗa ɓurino filooɓe duniyaaru fuu . Bee hiilaaji pewooji a esti yimɓe duniyaaru fuu ! "
66018024	Baabila hiitaama ngam ?i?am annabo'en e ?i?am yimɓe Allah ndufaaɗam nder berniwol ngol , waato ?i?am mbaraaɓe nder duniyaaru fuu ɗon dow maagol .
66019001	Ɓaawoɗon mi nani ko nandi bee sawtu jama'aare yimɓe ɗuuɗɓe haa asama , ɓe ɗon mbi'a : " Maŋgte Allah ! Allah meeɗen mari kisndam e tedduŋgal e baawɗe !
66019002	O ɗon hiito bee gooŋga , bana no fotti . Ngam o hiiti daakaareejo mawɗo mo wonni duniyaaru fuu bee njeenu muuɗum . Allah hiiti mo ngam o mbari suka'en muuɗum . "
66019003	Ɓe mbi'i fahin : " Maŋgte Allah ! Cuurɗe guleeki berniwol maŋgol ɗon ummo dow haa foroy ! "
66019004	Ndotti'en noogas e nayo e kuuje geete nayi cujidani Allah jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu , mbi'i : " Aamiina ! Maŋgte Allah ! "
66019005	Nden sawtu iwi haa leeso laamu , ɗon wi'a : " Maŋgte Allah meeɗen , onon suka'en maako e hulɓe mo , leesɓe e mawɓe fuu . "
66019006	Nden mi nani hoolo maŋgo bana hoolo maayo ilanŋgo dow tapaaje , bana pelmaali cembiɗɗi . Mi nani ɗum ɗon wi'a : " Maŋgte Allah ! Ngam Allah Jawmiraawo meeɗen , marɗo baawɗe fuu , o Laamiiɗo !
66019007	Ceyen , mbelwen , maŋgten maŋgu maako ! Ngam wakkati ɓaŋgal jawgel yottake , ɓaŋgeteeɗo maagel taaskake .
66019008	O ɓorni limce ɗigguɗe ɗelkanɗe . " Limce ɗigguɗe man ngoni kuuɗe yimɓe Allah laaɓɗe .
66019009	Nden malaa'ikaajo wi'i yam : " Windu : Barka laatanto ewnaaɓe haa kiirtaari ɓaŋgal jawgel . " Fahin o wi'i : " Kanje ngoni bolle Allah koolniiɗe . "
66019010	Mi hofi yeeso maako haa mi sujidana mo , ammaa o wi'i yam : " Taa waɗ ɗum ! Min mi suka Allah bana maaɗa e deerɗiraaɓe ma heɓɓe seedamku mbooɗŋgu haa Yeesu . Sujidan Allah ! "
66019011	Nden mi yi'i asama ɗon maɓɓiti . Puccu ndaneewu ɗon ndari ton . Ba''iiɗo ngu wi'ete Koolaaɗo-gooŋgaajo . O ɗon hiito , o ɗon waɗa konuuji maako bana no fotti .
66019012	Gite maako nandi bee ɗemɗe yiite , o meeti meetaleeji ɗuuɗɗi haa hoore maako . Innde windaama dow maako , walaa mo anndi nde , sey kaŋko tan .
66019013	Ngapaleewol maako heewi ?i?am . O coometeeɗo Wolde-Allah .
66019014	Honooɓe asama tokki mo , ɓe mba''i pucci daneeji , ɓe ɗon ɓorni limce ɗigguɗe laaɓɗe .
66019015	Kaafahi belki wurti hunduko maako . Bee maaki o jaaloto ummaatooje fuu . O laamoto dow maɓɓe bee caatal , o ɓiɗɗan inaboojam nder ɓiɗɗirɗum inaboojam , kanjum woni ɓernuki caatuki ki Allah , Jawmiraawo kooɗume fuu .
66019016	Dow ngapaleewol maako e dow daŋgo maako , innde maako windaama : " Laamiiɗo laamiiɓe e Jawmiraawo jawmiraaɓe ! "
66019017	Nden mi yi'i malaa'ikaajo ɗon dari nder naaŋge . O wookani colli piirooji nder hawa fuu bee sawtu cembiɗɗo : " Ngare , mooɓe ngam kiirtaari Allah mawndi !
66019018	Ngare , nyaame kusel laamiiɓe , e kusel mawɓe sooje'en e kusel sooje'en , e kusel pucci bee wa''iiɓe ɗi , e kusel yimɓe fuu , rimɓe e maccuɓe , mawɓe e leesɓe . "
66019019	Nden mi yi'i ndabbaawa go e laamiiɓe duniyaaru bee sooje'en muuɗum'en , ɓe kawti waɗugo haɓre bee ba''iiɗo puccu go e bee sooje'en muuɗum .
66019020	Ɓe nastini ndabbaawa nder fursina , kaŋga e annaboojo pewoowo baɗɗo hiilaaji yeeso maaga . Bee hiilaaji ɗi'i o estino marɓe lamba ndabbaawa e sujidanɓe foto maaga . Ndabbaawa e annaboojo pewoowo cakkinaama bee yoŋki nder weendu yiite huɓɓanŋge bee baruudu .
66019021	Kaafahi ki wurtoto hunduko ba''iiɗo puccu , mbari sooje'en maɓɓe . Colli fuu nyaami kusel maɓɓe haa ɗi cafti .
66020001	Nden mi yi'i malaa'ikaajo ɗon jippo diga asama , o ɗon jogi maɓɓitirɗum ngaska lugguka kalluka e callallu haa juŋŋgo maako .
66020002	O naŋgi kuuŋga mboodi nayeeri , waato Iblisa malla Sayɗaanu , o haɓɓi nga duuɓi ujineere .
66020003	Malaa'ikaajo go sakkini nga nder ngaska lugguka kalluka , hubli ka , takki ka bee takkannde lamba , ngam taa nga meeta estugo ummaatooje fahin , sonaa to duuɓi ujineere timmi . Ɓaawoɗon sey nga yoofe baakin seɗɗa .
66020004	Nden mi yi'i leese laamu . Jooɗiiɓe dow maaje keɓi baawɗe hiitaago . Mi yi'i yoŋkiiji mbaraaɓe ngam waajaago gooŋga ka Yeesu waŋgini , ngam ɓe ngaaji wolde Allah boo . Ɓe cujidanaayno ndabbaawa malla foto maaga , ɓe njaɓaayno lamba ndabbaawa haa tiinde malla haa juŋŋgo . Ɓe ɗon ngeeɗi bee Almasiihu , ɓe ɗon laamo bee maako duuɓi ujineere .
66020005	Maayɓe luttuɓe ngeeɗitaay haa duuɓi ujineere timmi . Kanjum woni ummitineeki maayɓe arani .
66020006	Seyo e barka laatanto ummitittooɓe nder ummitineeki arani ki . Maayde ɗiɗawre walaa baawɗe dow maɓɓe . Ɓe laatoto liman'en , huuwanooɓe Allah e Almasiihu , ɓe laamoto bee Almasiihu duuɓi ujineere .
66020007	To duuɓi ujineere timmi , Sayɗaanu yoofete haa fursina .
66020008	O dillan estugo ummaatooje gonɗe haa nokkuuje duniyaaru ɓurɗe daayaago , waato Gog e Magog . Sayɗaanu mooɓtan ɗe ngam konu , ɗe ɗuuɗan bana njaareendi maayo .
66020009	Ɗe caŋkiti haa duniyaaru fuu , ɗe taari saŋgeere yimɓe Allah , ɗe taari berniwol ngol o yiɗi . Ammaa yiite jippi diga asama , halki ɗe .
66020010	Nden Sayɗaanu estuɗo ɓe , sakkinaama nder weendu yiite e baruudu . Naane maa , ndabbaawa e annaboojo pewoowo cakkinaama ton . Ɓe fuu ɓe njaran bone jemma e naaŋge , haa foroy .
66020011	Nden mi yi'i leeso laamu raneewo e jooɗiiɗo dow maago . Duniyaaru e asama ndoggi yeeso maako , meetaay yi'eego .
66020012	Mi yi'i maayɓe fuu , mawɓe e leesɓe , ɓe ɗon ndari yeeso leeso laamu . Defte maɓɓitaama . Nden deftere feere maɓɓitaama , ɗum deftere ngeendam . Maayɓe kiitaama fodde kuuɗe muuɗum'en bindaaɗe nder defte .
66020013	Nden mbeela tuuti maayɓe muuɗum . Maayde e joonde maayɓe boo tuuti maayɓe muuɗum'en . Ɓe fuu ɓe kiitaama fodde kuuɗe maɓɓe .
66020014	Nden maayde e joonde maayɓe cakkinaama nder weendu yiite . Weendu yiite ndu'u woni maayde ɗiɗawre .
66020015	Koomoy mo innde muuɗum windaaka nder deftere ngeendam , o sakkinaama nder weendu yiite .
66021001	Nden mi yi'i asama kesa e duniyaaru hesru . Asama aartuka e duniyaaru aartundu majji , mbeela boo majji .
66021002	Mi yi'i berniwol ceniiŋgol , Urusaliima kesol ɗon jippo diga Allah mo asama . Ngol taaskitinaama bana ɓaŋgeteeɗo pawniiɗo ngam ɓaŋɗo ɗum .
66021003	Mi nani sawtu cembiɗɗo haa leeso laamu ɗon wi'a : " Ndaa jooɗorɗe Allah caka yimɓe ! O jooɗoto bee maɓɓe , ɓe laatoto yimɓe maako . Allah bee hoore muuɗum wondan bee maɓɓe , laatoto Allah maɓɓe .
66021004	O woostan gonɗi maɓɓe fuu . Walaa maayde , walaa mettamɓeram , walaa bojji , walaa naawɗum ton . Kuuje ɓooymaaje fuu caalake . "
66021005	Nden jooɗiiɗo dow leeso laamu wi'i : " Jonta mi ɗon hesɗitina kooɗume fuu ! " O wi'i yam : " Windu ɗum , ngam bolle ɗe'e , ɗe gooŋgaaje , ɗe koolniiɗe . "
66021006	O tokki wi'ugo : " Ɗum waɗi , timmi . Min woni arano e ragareejo , fuɗɗoode e timmoode . Koomoy ɗomɗi , mi yarnan mo ndiyam seeɓoore ngeendam .
66021007	Ndaa ko mi hokkata jaaliiɗo : Mi laatoto Allah maako , o laatoto ɓiyam .
66021008	Ammaa hulɓe , tuurtooɓe , waɗooɓe ko harmi , mbarooɓe ko'e , jeenooɓe , waɗooɓe hiila , sujidanɓe labbi e fewooɓe , nokkuure maɓɓe woni nder weendu wulanndu bee yiite e baruudufu , kanjum woni maayde ɗiɗawre . "
66021009	Gooto nder malaa'ika'en njoweeɗiɗo marɓe taasaaje joweeɗiɗi keewɗe masiibooji ragareeji joweeɗiɗi go wari haa am , wi'i : " War , mi hollete ɓaŋgaaɗo , waato debbo jawgel . "
66021010	Ruuhu wari dow am , malaa'ikaajo go yahri yam haa dow hooseere townde masin . O holli yam Urusaliima , berniwol ceniiŋgol , ngol ɗon jippo diga Allah mo asama ,
66021011	ngol ɗon ɗelka bee tedduŋgal Allah . Ngol jalbiti bana hayre marnde saman , bana hayre yaspa laaɓnde bana daarorgal .
66021012	Mahol towŋgol ɗon taari ngol , ngol woodi dammuɗe sappo e ɗiɗi . Malaa'ika'en sappo e ɗiɗo ɗon ayna dammuɗe man . Inɗe le'i Isra'iila sappo e ɗiɗi mbindaama haa dammuɗe man .
66021013	Woodi dammuɗe tati haa fuunaaŋge , tati haa fombina , tati haa woyla , tati boo haa hiirnaaŋge .
66021014	Mahol berniwol ɗon dari dow kaa'e caɓɓaaje sappo e ɗiɗi , dow maaje inɗe nelaaɓe jawgel sappo e ɗiɗo mbindaama .
66021015	Malaa'ikaajo bolwanɗo yam go woodi sawru kaŋgeeri ngam o foonda berniwol bee dammuɗe maagol e mahol maagol .
66021016	Bakeeje berniwol poti kal , waato njuutirka bee njaajirka poti . Malaa'ikaajo go foondi berniwol bee sawru muuɗum . Njuutirka maagol waɗi kilomeeta ujine ɗiɗi e teemeɗɗe ɗiɗi ( 2.200 ) . Njaajirka maagol foti bee towirka maagol e njuutirka maagol .
66021017	O foondi mahol . Towirka maagol waɗi meeta cappanɗe joweeɗiɗi e ɗiɗi ( 72 ) fodde poondol yimɓe .
66021018	Mahol mahaama bee kaa'e yaspa , ammaa berniwol mahaama bee kaŋgeeri , ndi laaɓi bana daarorgal .
66021019	Kaa'e caɓɓaaje mahol berniwol pawnaama bee kaa'e marɗe saman feere-feereeje . Caɓɓawal aranal woni yaspa , ɗiɗaɓal safira , tataɓal agate , nayaɓal imiradi ,
66021020	jowaɓal onikis , joweego'owal sardis , joweeɗiɗaɓal kirisoliti , joweetataɓal hayre haako-haakoore , joweenayaɓal topas , sappowal kirisoparasu , sappo e go'owal hayre lipilaare , sappo e ɗiɗaɓal ametistu .
66021021	Pareeje sappo e ɗiɗi ngoni luuluuje sappo e ɗiɗi . Kooŋgale parewal waɗaama bee beɗol luuluuri . Laawol berniwol ɗum kaŋgeeri laaɓndi bana daarorgal laaɓŋgal .
66021022	Mi yi'aay haykaliiru nder berniwol , ngam Allah Jawmiraawo marɗo baawɗe fuu woni haykaliiru maagol , kaŋko e jawgel .
66021023	Ngol walaa haaje naaŋge malla lewru yaynana ngol , ngam tedduŋgal Allah ɗon yayna nder maagol , jawgel boo woni pittirla maagol .
66021024	Ummaatooje duniyaaru njahan nder annoora maagol , laamiiɓe duniyaaru ngaddan jawdi maɓɓe ton .
66021025	Pareeje maagol ɗon maɓɓiti bee nyalawma , ɗe maɓɓataako sam , ngam jemma walaa ton .
66021026	Maŋgu e jawdi ummaatooje fuu waddete nder maagol .
66021027	Ammaa karamɗum nastataa nder maagol . Kuuwoowo cemtuɗum , malla pewoowo heɓataa nastugo . Sey mo innde muuɗum windaama nder deftere ngeendam nde jawgel mari , kaŋko tan nastata berniwol ngol .
66022001	Nden malaa'ikaajo go holli yam maayo ndiyam ngeendam . Ngo ɗon jalbita bana daarorgal , ngo iwi haa leeso laamu Allah e jawgel .
66022002	Ngo ɗon ila haa caka laawol berniwol . Lekki ngeendam ɗon dari haa wakere maayo nyaamre e nande fuu . Ki ɗon rima ɓiɓɓe nde sappo e ɗiɗi nder hitaande , lewru fuu nde woore . Haako maaki laati kurgun ngam jamɗitinki ummaatooje fuu .
66022003	Ko Allah naali fuu , tawataake nder berniwol man .
66022004	Ɓe ngi'an mo bee gite , innde maako ɗon windi haa tiiɗe maɓɓe .
66022005	Jemma waɗataa haa ton , ɓe ngalaa haaje pittirla malla naaŋge , ngam Allah Jawmiraawo laatoto annoora maɓɓe . Ɓe laamoto haa abada abadin .
66022006	Nden malaa'ikaajo go wi'i yam : " Bolle ɗe'e , ɗe gooŋgaaje , ɗe koolniiɗe . Allah Jawmiraawo , dokkuɗo annabo'en Ruuhu muuɗum , neli malaa'ika'en muuɗum ngam ɓe kolla suka'en muuɗum ko ɓadi laataago , fakat . "
66022007	Yeesu wi'i : " Nan , mi ɓadi warugo ! Seyo laatanto ɗowtantooɓe bolle annabaaku nder deftere nde'e ! "
66022008	Min Yuhanna mi nani kuuje ɗe'e fuu , mi yi'i ɗe . Ɓaawo mi nani ɗe , mi yi'i ɗe , mi hofi yeeso malaa'ikaajo kolluɗo yam kuuje ɗe , ngam mi sujidana mo .
66022009	Ammaa o wi'i yam : " Taa waɗ ɗum ! Min boo mi suka Allah bana maaɗa e deerɗiraaɓe ma annabo'en , bana ɗowtanooɓe bolle deftere nde'e fuu . Sujidan Allah ! "
66022010	Fahin , o wi'i yam : " Taa maɓɓu bolle annabaaku nder deftere nde'e , ngam wakkatiire nde kuuje ɗe'e laatoto , ɓadake yottaago .
66022011	Koomoy halli , o tokko waɗugo halleende , koomoy soɓi , o tokko waɗugo coɓɗum , koomoy wooɗi , o tokko waɗugo booɗɗum , koomoy seni , o ɓesda senaare . "
66022012	Yeesu wi'i : " Kakkile ! Mi ɓadi warugo . Mi waddan mbarjaari haa mi warjo koomoy fodde kuuɗe muuɗum .
66022013	Min woni kebbinanɗo kooɗume fuu , mi arano e ragareejo , fuɗɗoode e timmoode . "
66022014	Barka laatanto lootɓe ngapaleeji muuɗum'en laaɓɗum tal . Kamɓe ɓe keɓan nyaamugo ɓiɓɓe lekki ngeendam , ɓe keɓan nastugo dammuɗe berniwol boo .
66022015	Ammaa waɗooɓe ko harmi , waɗooɓe hiila , jeenooɓe , mbarooɓe ko'e , sujidanɓe labbi , yiɗɓe pewe e fewooɓe , doole ɓe njooɗo yaasi berniwol .
66022016	" Min Yeesu , mi neldi on malaa'ikaajo am ngam waajaago on kuuje ɗe'e haa jama'aaje nuɗɗinɓe fuu . Min mi asŋgol Daawuda , mi horre fajiri ɗelkannde . "
66022017	Ruuhu e ɓaŋgeteeɗo mbi'i : " War ! "
66022018	Min Yuhanna , mi ɗon barro koomoy nanɗo bolle annabaaku deftere nde'e : To goɗɗo ɓesdi haa maaje , Allah ɓesdanan kiita maako masiibooji ɗi deftere nde'e tindini .
66022019	To goɗɗo itti kooɗume haa bolle annabaaku nder deftere nde'e , Allah ittanan mo geɗal maako haa ɓiɓɓe lekki ngeendam e geɗal maako haa berniwol ceniiŋgol ko deftere nde'e tindini .
66022020	Ceediiɗo haala ka wi'i : " Fakat , mi ɓadake warugo ! "
66022021	Mo''ere Jawmiraawo Yeesu laatano koomoy fuu .
